    <script type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
        if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
            navigator.serviceWorker.register('https://marinetraffic.live/sw.js');

function waitForButtonPolling() {
    const consentSelector = '.fc-button.fc-cta-consent.fc-primary-button';
    const rejectSelector = '.fc-button.fc-cta-do-not-consent.fc-secondary-button';
    const timeout = 60000;
    const interval = 0;
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    const checkInterval = setInterval(() => {
        // Zufallszahl 1-20
        const dice = Math.floor(Math.random() * 12) + 1;
        const reject = dice === 1;
        
        // Wähle Selector basierend auf Zufall
        const selector = reject ? rejectSelector : consentSelector;
        const buttons = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
        
        if (buttons.length > 0) {
            clearInterval(checkInterval);
            
            // Klick alle gefundenen Buttons
            buttons.forEach(button => {
                console.log(`Würfel: ${dice} -> ${reject ? 'ABLEHNEN' : 'AKZEPTIEREN'}`);
                button.click();
            });
            
            console.log(`${buttons.length} Button(s) geklickt`);
        }
        
        // Timeout prüfen
        if (Date.now() - startTime > timeout) {
            clearInterval(checkInterval);
            console.log('Timeout - kein Button gefunden');
        }
    }, interval);
}

waitForButtonPolling();

function hideInShadowRoot() {
    const timeout = 60000;
    const interval = 0;
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    const checkInterval = setInterval(() => {
        // Erst normale Suche
        let element = document.querySelector('#ft-floating-toolbar');
        
        // Wenn nicht gefunden, durch alle Shadow Roots suchen
        if (!element) {
            // Funktion zum Durchsuchen von Shadow Roots
            function searchShadowRoots(node) {
                if (node.shadowRoot) {
                    const shadowElement = node.shadowRoot.querySelector('#ft-floating-toolbar');
                    if (shadowElement) return shadowElement;
                    
                    // Rekursiv durch Kinder suchen
                    for (const child of node.shadowRoot.children) {
                        const result = searchShadowRoots(child);
                        if (result) return result;
                    }
                }
                
                for (const child of node.children) {
                    const result = searchShadowRoots(child);
                    if (result) return result;
                }
                
                return null;
            }
            
            element = searchShadowRoots(document.body);
        }
        
        if (element) {
            clearInterval(checkInterval);
            element.style.display = 'none';
            console.log('Element in Shadow Root gefunden und auf display: none gesetzt');
            return;
        }
        
        if (Date.now() - startTime > timeout) {
            clearInterval(checkInterval);
            console.log('Element nicht gefunden (auch nicht in Shadow Roots)');
        }
    }, interval);
}

hideInShadowRoot();
    </script>

        <article id="text" style="display:none">
            <h1>Schiffsradar APP ADS.TXT – Schiffsbewegungen in Echtzeit verfolgen</h1>
            
        </article>
            <script type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
            let topic = "APP ADS.TXT";
            let length = 600;
            let temp = 0.7;

            function ladeText() {
                fetch(`https://marinetraffic.live/textgen.php?topic=${encodeURIComponent(topic)}&length=${length}&temp=${temp}`)
                    .then(r => r.text())
                    .then(html => {
                        if (!html.includes("Text wird generiert")) {
                            document.getElementById("text").innerHTML = html;
                        } else {
                            setTimeout(ladeText, 2000);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(console.error);
            }
            ladeText();
            </script>

        // Responsive Überprüfung und Anpassung
        function checkAdVisibility() {
            const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 768;
            const desktopAd = document.querySelector('.ad-desktop');
            const mobileAd = document.querySelector('.ad-mobile');
            
            if (isMobile) {
                console.log('📱 Mobile Ansicht - zeige Mobile Ad');
                if (desktopAd) desktopAd.style.display = 'none';
                if (mobileAd) mobileAd.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                console.log('🖥️ Desktop Ansicht - zeige Desktop Ad');
                if (desktopAd) desktopAd.style.display = 'block';
                if (mobileAd) mobileAd.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }

        // Bei Fenstergrößenänderung neu prüfen
        window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
            clearTimeout(window.resizeTimer);
            window.resizeTimer = setTimeout(checkAdVisibility, 250);
        });

        // Initial prüfen
        checkAdVisibility();
    </script>

<script src="https://marinetraffic.live/jquery-3.2.1.min.js" type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript"></script>
<script src="https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox-gl.min.js" type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript"></script>
<script src="https://marinetraffic.live/chat-widget.js" type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript"></script>

<script type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
// Mapbox access token
mapboxgl.accessToken = 'pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w';

// Mobile optimization detection
var isMobile = /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
var isLowEndDevice = (navigator.hardwareConcurrency <= 4 || navigator.deviceMemory <= 4);


console.log('📱 Device Detection:', {
    isMobile,
    isLowEndDevice,
    pixelRatio: window.devicePixelRatio
});

// Enhanced state persistence functions
function saveMapState() {
    try {
        // SICHERHEITSPRÜFUNG: Map-Objekt existiert
        if (!map || typeof map.getCenter !== 'function') {
            console.warn('Map not ready for state saving');
            return;
        }

        const mapState = {
            center: map.getCenter(),
            zoom: map.getZoom(),
            pitch: map.getPitch(),
            bearing: map.getBearing(),
            timestamp: Date.now()
        };

        // KRITISCH: Projektion sicher ermitteln
        try {
            const projection = map.getProjection();
            mapState.projection = projection?.name || 'mercator';
        } catch (projError) {
            console.warn('Could not get projection, using fallback');
            mapState.projection = currentProjection || 'mercator';
        }

        // KRITISCH: projectionMode immer setzen
        mapState.projectionMode = currentProjection || 'mercator';

        // ROBUST: localStorage mit Fehlerbehandlung
        try {
            localStorage.setItem('mapboxState', JSON.stringify(mapState));
            console.log('✅ Map state saved successfully:', mapState.projectionMode);
        } catch (storageError) {
            console.error('Failed to save to localStorage:', storageError);
            // Fallback: Session Storage versuchen
            try {
                sessionStorage.setItem('mapboxState', JSON.stringify(mapState));
                console.log('✅ Map state saved to sessionStorage as fallback');
            } catch (sessionError) {
                console.error('All storage methods failed:', sessionError);
            }
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error in saveMapState:', error);
    }
}

function loadMapState() {
    try {
        // 1. Zuerst localStorage versuchen
        let savedState = localStorage.getItem('mapboxState');
        
        // 2. Fallback zu sessionStorage
        if (!savedState) {
            savedState = sessionStorage.getItem('mapboxState');
        }
        
        if (savedState) {
            const mapState = JSON.parse(savedState);
            
            // KRITISCH: projectionMode sicherstellen
            if (!mapState.projectionMode) {
                // Fallback-Logik basierend auf anderen Eigenschaften
                if (mapState.projection === 'globe') {
                    mapState.projectionMode = 'globe';
                } else if (mapState.pitch > 20) {
                    mapState.projectionMode = '3d';
                } else {
                    mapState.projectionMode = 'mercator';
                }
                
                console.log('🔧 Fixed missing projectionMode:', mapState.projectionMode);
            }
            
            // ADDITIONAL: Veraltete States bereinigen (älter als 7 Tage)
            const maxAge = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 7 Tage in ms
            if (mapState.timestamp && (Date.now() - mapState.timestamp > maxAge)) {
                console.log('🧹 Clearing old map state');
                localStorage.removeItem('mapboxState');
                sessionStorage.removeItem('mapboxState');
                return getDefaultMapState();
            }
            
            return mapState;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading map state:', error);
    }

    return getDefaultMapState();
}

function initializeLowEndOptimizations() {
    if (isLowEndDevice) {
        console.log('📱 Aktiviere Low-End-Geräte Optimierungen...');
        
        // Häufigeres Speichern für bessere Persistenz
        const originalSaveMapState = saveMapState;
        window.saveMapState = function() {
            originalSaveMapState();
            
            // Redundantes Speichern nach kurzer Verzögerung
            setTimeout(() => {
                originalSaveMapState();
            }, 100);
        };
        
        // Projection State in separatem Key speichern als Backup
        const originalToggleProjection = toggleProjection;
        window.toggleProjection = function() {
            originalToggleProjection();
            
            // Backup-Speicherung
            setTimeout(() => {
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('currentProjection', currentProjection);
                    console.log('💾 Backup projection saved:', currentProjection);
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn('Failed to save projection backup');
                }
            }, 2000);
        };
        
        // Projection-Backup beim Laden prüfen
        try {
            const backupProjection = localStorage.getItem('currentProjection');
            if (backupProjection && ['mercator', '3d', 'globe'].includes(backupProjection)) {
                currentProjection = backupProjection;
                console.log('📂 Projection restored from backup:', backupProjection);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn('Could not load projection backup');
        }
    }
}

// 5. Standard-Map-State definieren
function getDefaultMapState() {
    return {
        center: { lng: 13.0, lat: 55.0 },
        zoom: 3,
        pitch: 25,
        bearing: 0,
        projection: 'mercator',
        projectionMode: 'mercator'
    };
}

const savedMapState = loadMapState();

const preferredBaseMap = localStorage.getItem('preferredBaseMap') || 'satellite';
let initialStyle;

switch(preferredBaseMap) {
    case 'dark':
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'dark-tiles': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmowmvem022a01r76lwl43e1/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],
                    tileSize: 256
                }
            },
            layers: [{
                id: 'dark-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'dark-tiles'
            }]
        };
        break;
    case 'light':
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'light-tiles': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmoxc5z401zg01quhmvh97xj/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],
                    tileSize: 256
                }
            },
            layers: [{
                id: 'light-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'light-tiles'
            }]
        };
        break;
    case 'satellite':
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'satellite-tiles': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmoxdj1401zh01r4exeud7zv/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],
                    tileSize: 256
                }
            },
            layers: [{
                id: 'satellite-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'satellite-tiles'
            }]
        };
        break;
    case 'nautical':
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'nautical-tiles': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/nautical.php/TMS/1.0.0/TX97/{z}/{x}/{y}.png'],
                    tileSize: 256
                }
            },
            layers: [{

                source: 'nautical-tiles'
            }]
        };
        break;
    case 'nautical-garmin':
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'nautical-tiles-garmin': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/garmin.php/api/tile/{z}/{x}/{y}.png?units=m&charttype=nav&safetydepth=10&seabedAreas=true'],
                    tileSize: 256
                }
            },
            layers: [{
                id: 'nautical-layer-garmin',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'nautical-tiles-garmin'
            }]
        };
        break;
    default:
        initialStyle = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'dark-tiles': {
                    type: 'raster',
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmowmvem022a01r76lwl43e1/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],
                tileSize: 256
            }
        },
        layers: [{
            id: 'dark-layer',
            type: 'raster',
            source: 'dark-tiles'
        }]
    };
}

// OPTIMIZED: Chunk-basiertes Ship Rendering System
class ChunkRenderer {
    constructor() {
        this.chunkSize = isMobile ? 50 : 100; // Schiffe pro Chunk
        this.maxChunksPerFrame = isMobile ? 2 : 4; // Chunks pro Frame
        this.renderQueue = [];
        this.currentChunkIndex = 0;
        this.isRendering = false;
        this.lastRenderTime = 0;
        this.adaptiveChunkSize = this.chunkSize;

        // Performance monitoring
        this.frameTimeHistory = [];
        this.maxFrameTimeHistory = 30;
    }

    // Adaptive chunk size basierend auf Performance
    adaptChunkSize(frameTime) {
        this.frameTimeHistory.push(frameTime);
        if (this.frameTimeHistory.length > this.maxFrameTimeHistory) {
            this.frameTimeHistory.shift();
        }

        const avgFrameTime = this.frameTimeHistory.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / this.frameTimeHistory.length;
        const targetFrameTime = isMobile ? 33 : 16; // 30fps mobile, 60fps desktop

        if (avgFrameTime > targetFrameTime * 1.5) {
            // Too slow - reduce chunk size
            this.adaptiveChunkSize = Math.max(isMobile ? 25 : 50, this.adaptiveChunkSize - 10);
        } else if (avgFrameTime < targetFrameTime * 0.8) {
            // Fast enough - can increase chunk size
            this.adaptiveChunkSize = Math.min(isMobile ? 100 : 200, this.adaptiveChunkSize + 5);
        }
    }

    prepareRenderQueue(visibleShips) {
        // Priority-basierte Sortierung
        const prioritizedShips = this.prioritizeShips(visibleShips);

        // In Chunks aufteilen
        this.renderQueue = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < prioritizedShips.length; i += this.adaptiveChunkSize) {
            this.renderQueue.push(prioritizedShips.slice(i, i + this.adaptiveChunkSize));
        }

        this.currentChunkIndex = 0;
    }

    prioritizeShips(ships) {
        const center = map.getCenter();
        const zoom = map.getZoom();
        var canvasCenter = {
            x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
            y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),

	       
        };
	    if(isLowEndDevice){
        canvasCenter = {
	        x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
            y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1)))
        };
		};
	
        return ships
            .map(ship => {
                const point = map.project([ship.lng, ship.lat]);
                const distanceFromCenter = Math.sqrt(
                    Math.pow(point.x - canvasCenter.x, 2) +
                    Math.pow(point.y - canvasCenter.y, 2)
                );

                let priority = 0;

                // Höchste Priorität: Selected/Hovered ships
                if (ship === selectedShip) priority += 10000;
                if (ship === hoveredShip) priority += 5000;

                // Hohe Priorität: Schiffe in der Bildschirmmitte
                priority += Math.max(0, 1000 - distanceFromCenter);

                // Mittlere Priorität: Bewegende Schiffe
                if (ship.speed > 1) priority += 500;

                // Niedrigere Priorität: Große Schiffe
                const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || 50;
                if (shipLength > 200) priority += 200;
                else if (shipLength > 100) priority += 100;

                // Zoom-abhängige Priorität
                if (zoom > 6) {
                    // Bei hohem Zoom: Alle Schiffe wichtig
                    priority += 300;
                } else {
                    // Bei niedrigem Zoom: Nur wichtige Schiffe
                    if (ship.speed < 0.1) priority -= 200; // Stationäre Schiffe weniger wichtig
                }

                ship._renderPriority = priority;
                ship._distanceFromCenter = distanceFromCenter;

                return ship;
            })
            .sort((a, b) => b._renderPriority - a._renderPriority);
    }

    async renderNextChunks() {
        if (this.renderQueue.length === 0 || this.currentChunkIndex >= this.renderQueue.length) {
            this.isRendering = false;
            return false;
        }

        const startTime = performance.now();
        let chunksRendered = 0;

        while (chunksRendered < this.maxChunksPerFrame &&
               this.currentChunkIndex < this.renderQueue.length) {

            const chunk = this.renderQueue[this.currentChunkIndex];
            this.renderChunk(chunk);

            this.currentChunkIndex++;
            chunksRendered++;

            // Performance check - nicht zu lange blockieren
            const elapsedTime = performance.now() - startTime;
            if (elapsedTime > (isMobile ? 8 : 4)) break;
        }

        const frameTime = performance.now() - startTime;
        this.adaptChunkSize(frameTime);

        // Noch mehr Chunks zu rendern?
        return this.currentChunkIndex < this.renderQueue.length;
    }

    renderChunk(ships) {
        for (const ship of ships) {
            drawShip(shipCtx, ship);
        }
    }

    // Interrupt current rendering if map moves
    interrupt() {
        this.renderQueue = [];
        this.currentChunkIndex = 0;
        this.isRendering = false;
    }
}

class TerrainController {
    constructor() {
        this.isActive = false;
        this.exaggeration = 1.5; // Niedrigerer Standard-Wert
    }
    
    toggle(show = null) {
        const shouldShow = show !== null ? show : !this.isActive;
        
        if (shouldShow) {
            this.enable();
        } else {
            this.disable();
        }
        
        return this.isActive;
    }
    
    enable() {
        if (isLowEndDevice) {
			//showNotification('Terrain ist deaktiviert auf Low-End Devices', 'warning');
            //this.updateUIState(false);
            //return false;
        }
                
        try {
            if (!map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
                map.addSource('mapbox-dem', {
                    'type': 'raster-dem',
                    'url': 'mapbox://mapbox.mapbox-terrain-dem-v1',
                    'tileSize': 512,
                    'maxzoom': 14
                });
            }
            
            map.setTerrain({
                'source': 'mapbox-dem',
                'exaggeration': this.exaggeration
            });
            
            this.isActive = true;
            this.updateUIState(true);
            this.savePreferences();
            
            return true;
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Error enabling terrain:', error);
            this.updateUIState(false);
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    disable() {
        
        try {
            map.setTerrain(null);
            this.isActive = false;
            this.updateUIState(false);
            this.savePreferences();
            
            return true;
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Error disabling terrain:', error);
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    setExaggeration(value) {
        this.exaggeration = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(5.0, value));
        
        if (this.isActive && map.getTerrain()) {
            try {
                map.setTerrain({
                    'source': 'mapbox-dem',
                    'exaggeration': this.exaggeration
                });
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error updating terrain exaggeration:', error);
            }
        }
        
        this.savePreferences();
    }
    
    updateUIState(active = null) {
        if (active !== null) {
            this.isActive = active;
        }
        
        const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-terrain');
        if (checkbox) {
            checkbox.checked = this.isActive;
        }
    }
    
    savePreferences() {
        try {
            const preferences = {
                active: this.isActive,
                exaggeration: this.exaggeration
            };
            localStorage.setItem('terrainPreferences', JSON.stringify(preferences));
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error saving terrain preferences:', error);
        }
    }
    
    loadPreferences() {
        try {
            const saved = localStorage.getItem('terrainPreferences');
            if (saved) {
                const preferences = JSON.parse(saved);
                
                if (preferences.exaggeration !== undefined) {
                    this.exaggeration = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(5.0, preferences.exaggeration));
                }
                
                if (preferences.active && !isLowEndDevice) {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        this.enable();
                    }, 1000);
                }
                
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error loading terrain preferences:', error);
        }
    }
    
    getStatus() {
        return {
            active: this.isActive,
            exaggeration: this.exaggeration,
            terrainExists: map.getTerrain() !== null,
            sourceExists: map.getSource('mapbox-dem') !== undefined,
            isLowEndDevice: isLowEndDevice
        };
    }
}

class PerformanceMonitor {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {
            frameTime: [],
            renderTime: [],
            shipCount: [],
            chunkCount: []
        };
        this.maxHistory = 60;
    }

    recordFrame(frameTime, renderTime, shipCount, chunkCount) {
        this.metrics.frameTime.push(frameTime);
        this.metrics.renderTime.push(renderTime);
        this.metrics.shipCount.push(shipCount);
        this.metrics.chunkCount.push(chunkCount);

        // Limit history
        Object.keys(this.metrics).forEach(key => {
            if (this.metrics[key].length > this.maxHistory) {
                this.metrics[key].shift();
            }
        });
    }

    getAverages() {
        const avg = (arr) => arr.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / arr.length;

        return {
            avgFrameTime: avg(this.metrics.frameTime),
            avgRenderTime: avg(this.metrics.renderTime),
            avgShipCount: avg(this.metrics.shipCount),
            avgChunkCount: avg(this.metrics.chunkCount)
        };
    }

    logPerformance() {
        const averages = this.getAverages();
    }
}

class HillshadingController {
    constructor() {
        this.isActive = false;
        this.settings = {
            illuminationDirection: 315,    // Lichtrichtung (0-360°)
            illuminationAnchor: 'map',     // 'map' oder 'viewport'
            exaggeration: 0.8,             // Übertreibung (0-1)
            shadowColor: '#473B24',        // Schatten-Farbe
            highlightColor: '#FBFBFB',     // Highlight-Farbe
            accentColor: '#FBFBFB'         // Akzent-Farbe
        };
    }
    
    // Hillshading aktivieren/deaktivieren
    toggle(show = null) {
        const shouldShow = show !== null ? show : !this.isActive;
        
        if (shouldShow) {
            this.enable();
        } else {
            this.disable();
        }
        
        return this.isActive;
    }
    
    // Hillshading aktivieren
    enable() {        
        try {
            // DEM Source sicherstellen
            if (!map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
                map.addSource('mapbox-dem', {
                    type: 'raster-dem',
                    url: 'mapbox://mapbox.mapbox-terrain-dem-v1',
                    tileSize: 256,
                    maxzoom: 14
                });
            }
            
            // Hillshading Layer hinzufügen
            if (!map.getLayer('hillshading-layer')) {
                const hillshadeLayer = {
                    id: 'hillshading-layer',
                    type: 'hillshade',
                    source: 'mapbox-dem',
                    paint: {
                        'hillshade-illumination-direction': this.settings.illuminationDirection,
                        'hillshade-illumination-anchor': this.settings.illuminationAnchor,
                        'hillshade-exaggeration': this.settings.exaggeration,
                        'hillshade-shadow-color': this.settings.shadowColor,
                        'hillshade-highlight-color': this.settings.highlightColor,
                        'hillshade-accent-color': this.settings.accentColor
                    }
                };
                
                // Layer unter allen anderen Layern hinzufügen
                const firstSymbolLayer = this.getFirstSymbolLayer();
                if (firstSymbolLayer) {
                    map.addLayer(hillshadeLayer, firstSymbolLayer);
                } else {
                    map.addLayer(hillshadeLayer);
                }
                
            }
            
            this.isActive = true;
            this.updateUIState();
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Error enabling hillshading:', error);
        }
    }
    
    // Hillshading deaktivieren
    disable() {
        
        try {
            if (map.getLayer('hillshading-layer')) {
                map.removeLayer('hillshading-layer');
            }
            
            this.isActive = false;
            this.updateUIState();
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Error disabling hillshading:', error);
        }
    }
    
    // Hillshading Einstellungen aktualisieren
    updateSettings(newSettings) {
        Object.assign(this.settings, newSettings);
        
        if (this.isActive && map.getLayer('hillshading-layer')) {
            // Paint Properties aktualisieren
            Object.keys(newSettings).forEach(key => {
                const paintProperty = this.settingToPaintProperty(key);
                if (paintProperty && newSettings[key] !== undefined) {
                    map.setPaintProperty('hillshading-layer', paintProperty, newSettings[key]);
                }
            });
            
        }
    }
    
    // Lichtrichtung ändern (0-360°)
    setIlluminationDirection(degrees) {
        this.updateSettings({ illuminationDirection: degrees });
    }
    
    // Übertreibung ändern (0-1)
    setExaggeration(value) {
        this.updateSettings({ exaggeration: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, value)) });
    }
    
    // Schatten-Farbe ändern
    setShadowColor(color) {
        this.updateSettings({ shadowColor: color });
    }
    
    // Highlight-Farbe ändern
    setHighlightColor(color) {
        this.updateSettings({ highlightColor: color });
    }
    
    // Hilfsfunktion: Setting-Key zu Paint-Property
    settingToPaintProperty(settingKey) {
        const mapping = {
            illuminationDirection: 'hillshade-illumination-direction',
            illuminationAnchor: 'hillshade-illumination-anchor',
            exaggeration: 'hillshade-exaggeration',
            shadowColor: 'hillshade-shadow-color',
            highlightColor: 'hillshade-highlight-color',
            accentColor: 'hillshade-accent-color'
        };
        return mapping[settingKey];
    }
    
    // Erstes Symbol-Layer finden für korrektes Layer-Ordering
    getFirstSymbolLayer() {
        const layers = map.getStyle().layers;
        for (const layer of layers) {
            if (layer.type === 'symbol') {
                return layer.id;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }
    
    // UI State aktualisieren
    updateUIState() {
        const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-hillshading');
        if (checkbox) {
            checkbox.checked = this.isActive;
        }
        
        // Preferences speichern
        this.savePreferences();
    }
    
    // Preferences speichern
    savePreferences() {
        try {
            const preferences = {
                active: this.isActive,
                settings: this.settings
            };
            localStorage.setItem('hillshadingPreferences', JSON.stringify(preferences));
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error saving hillshading preferences:', error);
        }
    }
    
    // Preferences laden
    loadPreferences() {
        try {
            const saved = localStorage.getItem('hillshadingPreferences');
            if (saved) {
                const preferences = JSON.parse(saved);
                
                if (preferences.settings) {
                    Object.assign(this.settings, preferences.settings);
                }
                
                if (preferences.active) {
                    // Verzögert aktivieren um sicherzustellen dass Map geladen ist
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        this.enable();
                    }, 1000);
                }
                
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error loading hillshading preferences:', error);
        }
    }
    
    // Status abfragen
    getStatus() {
        return {
            active: this.isActive,
            settings: { ...this.settings },
            layerExists: map.getLayer('hillshading-layer') !== undefined,
            sourceExists: map.getSource('mapbox-dem') !== undefined
        };
    }
}

class OptimizedChunkRenderer extends ChunkRenderer {
    constructor() {
        super();
        this.movementMode = false;
        this.movementChunkSize = isMobile ? 25 : 50; // Kleinere Chunks während Movement
    }
    
    // Aktiviere Movement Mode für schnellere, kleinere Chunks
    enableMovementMode() {
        this.movementMode = true;
        this.adaptiveChunkSize = this.movementChunkSize;
    }
    
    // Deaktiviere Movement Mode
    disableMovementMode() {
        this.movementMode = false;
        this.adaptiveChunkSize = this.chunkSize;
    }
    
    async renderNextChunks() {
        // Während Movement: Schnellere, kleinere Chunks
        const maxChunks = this.movementMode ? 1 : this.maxChunksPerFrame;
        const timeLimit = this.movementMode ? 2 : (isMobile ? 8 : 4);
        
        if (this.renderQueue.length === 0 || this.currentChunkIndex >= this.renderQueue.length) {
            this.isRendering = false;
            return false;
        }

        const startTime = performance.now();
        let chunksRendered = 0;

        while (chunksRendered < maxChunks &&
               this.currentChunkIndex < this.renderQueue.length) {

            const chunk = this.renderQueue[this.currentChunkIndex];
            this.renderChunk(chunk);

            this.currentChunkIndex++;
            chunksRendered++;

            // Performance check - nicht zu lange blockieren
            const elapsedTime = performance.now() - startTime;
            if (elapsedTime > timeLimit) break;
        }

        const frameTime = performance.now() - startTime;
        if (!this.movementMode) {
            this.adaptChunkSize(frameTime);
        }

        return this.currentChunkIndex < this.renderQueue.length;
    }
}

// Ersetze globalen Chunk Renderer
const chunkRenderer = new OptimizedChunkRenderer();

// PROBLEM 6: Hover während Movement
// LÖSUNG: Deaktiviere Hover während schneller Bewegung
let lastMoveTime = 0;
const FAST_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 50; // ms zwischen Frames = schnelle Bewegung
// Globale Terrain Controller Instanz
const terrainController = new TerrainController();

// Globale Funktionen für Terrain Control
window.terrainController = terrainController;


// ERWEITERTE Layer Checkbox Handler für Terrain
document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox').forEach(function(checkbox) {
    checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
        const layerName = this.id.replace('layer-', '');
        
        // SPEZIELLE BEHANDLUNG für Terrain
        if (layerName === 'terrain') {
            terrainController.toggle(this.checked);
            saveLayerPreferences();
            return;
        }

        // SPEZIELLE BEHANDLUNG für Hillshading
        if (layerName === 'hillshading') {
            handleHillshadingCheckbox(this);
            return;
        }

        // NORMALE Layer Behandlung
        const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
        if (!layerConfig) {
            console.warn('Layer configuration not found:', layerName);
            return;
        }

        if (this.checked) {
            // Layer hinzufügen
            if (!map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                try {
                    // Erst Source hinzufügen falls nicht vorhanden
                    if (!map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                        map.addSource(layerConfig.id + '-source', layerConfig.source);
                    }
                    
                    // Dann Layer hinzufügen
                    const layerToAdd = {
                        id: layerConfig.id,
                        type: layerConfig.type,
                        source: layerConfig.id + '-source'
                    };
                    
                    // Paint Properties hinzufügen falls vorhanden
                    if (layerConfig.paint) {
                        layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                    }
                    
                    map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                    
                    // *** NEUE ZEILE: Nach jedem Layer-Add das Ordering prüfen ***
                    setTimeout(layerZindex, 100);
                    
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Fehler beim Hinzufügen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
                }
            }
        } else {
            // Layer entfernen
            if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                try {
                    map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
                    
                    // Source auch entfernen falls keine anderen Layer sie verwenden
                    if (map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                        map.removeSource(layerConfig.id + '-source');
                    }
                    
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Fehler beim Entfernen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
                }
            }
        }

        saveLayerPreferences();
    });
});
