const performanceMonitor = new PerformanceMonitor();

function createShipCanvas() {
    shipCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    shipCanvas.id = 'ship-canvas';
    shipCanvas.style.position = 'fixed';
    shipCanvas.style.top = '0';
    shipCanvas.style.left = '0';
    shipCanvas.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    shipCanvas.style.zIndex = '-1';
    
    // Look for the maplibre-overlay container first
    const overlayContainer = document.getElementById('maplibre-overlay');
    
    if (overlayContainer) {
        overlayContainer.appendChild(shipCanvas);
        console.log('🚢 Ship Canvas in maplibre-overlay erstellt');
    } else {
        // Fallback to original behavior if overlay doesn't exist
        document.getElementById('map').appendChild(shipCanvas);
        console.log('🚢 Ship Canvas in map erstellt (Fallback)');
    }
    
    shipCtx = shipCanvas.getContext('2d');
    
    // Mobile optimizations
    if (isLowEndDevice) {
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
    } else {
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
    }
    
    resizeShipCanvas();
}

function resizeShipCanvas() {
    if (!shipCanvas) return;
    
    const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
    
    // MOBILE FIX: Einfache PixelRatio ohne Komplexität
    const pixelRatio = isMobile ? 1 : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    
    // Ship Canvas resizing
    shipCanvas.width = mapContainer.offsetWidth * pixelRatio;
    shipCanvas.height = mapContainer.offsetHeight * pixelRatio;
    shipCanvas.style.width = mapContainer.offsetWidth + 'px';
    shipCanvas.style.height = mapContainer.offsetHeight + 'px';
    
    shipCtx.setTransform(pixelRatio, 0, 0, pixelRatio, 0, 0);
    
    if (isLowEndDevice) {
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
    } else {
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
        shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
    }
    
    // Handle other canvases if they exist
    const otherCanvases = ['measurementCanvas', 'routingCanvas'];
    
    otherCanvases.forEach(canvasId => {
        const canvas = window[canvasId];
        if (canvas) {
            canvas.width = mapContainer.offsetWidth * pixelRatio;
            canvas.height = mapContainer.offsetHeight * pixelRatio;
            canvas.style.width = mapContainer.offsetWidth + 'px';
            canvas.style.height = mapContainer.offsetHeight + 'px';
            
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            if (ctx) {
                ctx.setTransform(pixelRatio, 0, 0, pixelRatio, 0, 0);
                
                if (isLowEndDevice) {
                    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
                    ctx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
                } else {
                    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
                    ctx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
                }
            }
        }
    });
    
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function hasMapChanged() {
    if (!lastMapCenter || !lastMapZoom) return true;
    
    const currentCenter = map.getCenter();
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    const currentBearing = map.getBearing();
    const currentPitch = map.getPitch();
    
    // Größere Schwellenwerte für weniger Updates
    const centerThreshold = 0.001;
    const zoomThreshold = 0.1;
    const angleThreshold = 2.0;
    
    const centerChanged = 
        Math.abs(currentCenter.lng - lastMapCenter.lng) > centerThreshold ||
        Math.abs(currentCenter.lat - lastMapCenter.lat) > centerThreshold;
        
    const zoomChanged = Math.abs(currentZoom - lastMapZoom) > zoomThreshold;
    const bearingChanged = Math.abs(currentBearing - lastMapBearing) > angleThreshold;
    const pitchChanged = Math.abs(currentPitch - lastMapPitch) > angleThreshold;
    
    return centerChanged || zoomChanged || bearingChanged || pitchChanged;
}

let movementRAF = null;
let isInMovementCycle = false;
let lastMovementFrame = 0;
let movementFrameCount = 0;

function optimizedMovementHandler() {
    if (isInMovementCycle) {
        return; // Verhindere überlappende Cycles
    }
    
    isInMovementCycle = true;
    
    // Benutze requestAnimationFrame für smoothe Updates
    if (movementRAF) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(movementRAF);
    }
    
    movementRAF = requestAnimationFrame((timestamp) => {
        const now = performance.now();
        
        // Throttle auf 30fps während Movement für bessere Performance
        if (now - lastMovementFrame < 33) { // ~30fps
            isInMovementCycle = false;
            return;
        }
        
        lastMovementFrame = now;
        movementFrameCount++;
        
        try {
            // NUR zeichnen wenn wirklich nötig
            if (hasMapChanged() || needsRedraw) {
                // KRITISCH: Canvas Sync vor dem Zeichnen
                syncCanvasPositions();
                
                drawShips();
                needsRedraw = false;
                
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Movement handler error:', error);
        } finally {
            isInMovementCycle = false;
        }
    });
}

function syncCanvasPositions() {
    if (!shipCanvas) return;
    
    const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
    const containerRect = mapContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
    
    // Ship Canvas Position sync
    const shipCanvasRect = shipCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const mapContainerRect = mapContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
    
    // Prüfe ob Canvas Position abweicht
    const positionDrift = Math.abs(shipCanvasRect.left - mapContainerRect.left) > 1 ||
                         Math.abs(shipCanvasRect.top - mapContainerRect.top) > 1;
    
    if (positionDrift) {
        shipCanvas.style.left = '0px';
        shipCanvas.style.top = '0px';
        shipCanvas.style.position = 'fixed';
    }
    
    // Measurement Canvas sync falls vorhanden
    if (measurementCanvas) {
        measurementCanvas.style.left = '0px';
        measurementCanvas.style.top = '0px';
        measurementCanvas.style.position = 'fixed';
    }
    
    // Routing Canvas sync falls vorhanden
    if (routingCanvas) {
        routingCanvas.style.left = '0px';
        routingCanvas.style.top = '0px';
        routingCanvas.style.position = 'fixed';
    }
}

// ===== ERWEITERTE VIEWPORT-BASIERTE SHIP CANVAS FUNKTIONEN =====

/**
 * Erweiterte getVisibleShips Funktion mit Viewport-Optimierung und Pitch-Berücksichtigung
 */
function getVisibleShips() {
    if (ships.length === 0) return [];

    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    if(isLowEndDevice){
        pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    }
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    const projection = map.getProjection();
    const mapPitch = map.getPitch();

    // ===== STRENGE VIEWPORT BOUNDS (OHNE EXPANSION) =====
    const bounds = map.getBounds();
    const strictViewport = {
        north: bounds.getNorth(),
        south: bounds.getSouth(), 
        east: bounds.getEast(),
        west: bounds.getWest()
    };

    const visibleShips = [];
    let skippedOutside = 0;
    let skippedGlobe = 0;
    let skippedCanvas = 0;

    // Performance limits
    let MaxShips = calculateMaxShipsForPitch(zoom, mapPitch);
    const maxProcessShips = Math.min(ships.length, MaxShips * 1.5);

    for (let i = 0; i < ships.length && visibleShips.length < MaxShips && i < maxProcessShips; i++) {
        const ship = ships[i];

        // ===== 1. STRIKTE VIEWPORT BOUNDS CHECK (KEIN MARGIN) =====
        if (ship.lat < strictViewport.south || ship.lat > strictViewport.north ||
            ship.lng < strictViewport.west || ship.lng > strictViewport.east) {
            skippedOutside++;
            continue; // Skip ship - definitiv außerhalb
        }

        // ===== 2. GLOBE PROJEKTION HANDLING =====
        if (projection && projection.name === 'globe') {
            const center = map.getCenter();
            const shipLng = ship.lng;
            const centerLng = center.lng;

            let lngDiff = Math.abs(shipLng - centerLng);
            if (lngDiff > 180) {
                lngDiff = 360 - lngDiff;
            }

if (zoom < 5) {
    if (lngDiff > 90) {
        skippedGlobe++;
        continue;
    }
} else if (zoom < 6) {
    const transitionProgress = (zoom - 3) / 2;
    const cutoffAngle = 90 + (transitionProgress * 90);
    
    if (lngDiff > cutoffAngle) {
        skippedGlobe++;
        continue;
    }
}
        }

        // ===== 3. PROJEKTION FÜR CANVAS CHECK =====
        const point = map.project([ship.lng, ship.lat]);
        
        // SEHR STRIKTE Canvas Bounds (kleiner Margin nur für Rendering-Edge-Cases)
        const margin = 10; // Sehr klein!
        
        if (point.x < -margin || point.x > canvasWidth + margin ||
            point.y < -margin || point.y > canvasHeight + margin) {
            skippedCanvas++;
            continue; // Skip ship - außerhalb Canvas
        }

        // ===== SCHIFF IST SICHTBAR - HINZUFÜGEN =====
        ship._projectedPoint = {
            x: Math.round(point.x * 10) / 10,
            y: Math.round(point.y * 10) / 10
        };
        ship._pitchScale = calculatePitchScale(ship, point.y, mapPitch, canvasHeight);
        visibleShips.push(ship);
    }

    console.log(`🎯 STRICT Filtering: ${visibleShips.length} visible, ${skippedOutside} outside viewport, ${skippedGlobe} globe-culled, ${skippedCanvas} outside canvas`);
    return visibleShips;
}

/**
 * Berechnet Pitch-basierte Skalierung für Schiffe
 */
function calculatePitchScale(ship, canvasY, mapPitch, canvasHeight) {
    if (mapPitch <= 0) return 1.0;
    
    const pitchRadians = mapPitch * Math.PI / 180;
    const screenCenterY = canvasHeight / 2;
    
    // Normalisierte Y-Position (-1 bis +1)
    const normalizedY = (canvasY - screenCenterY) / screenCenterY;
    
    // Basis-Skalierung durch Pitch
    let baseScale = Math.cos(pitchRadians);
    
    // Perspektivische Korrektur basierend auf Y-Position
    let perspectiveScale = 1.0;
    
    if (mapPitch > 30) {
        // Schiffe weiter oben (negativer Y) erscheinen kleiner (weiter weg)
        // Schiffe weiter unten (positiver Y) erscheinen größer (näher)
        const perspectiveFactor = Math.min(mapPitch / 55, 1.0); // 0.0 bis 1.0
        perspectiveScale = 1.0 - (normalizedY * perspectiveFactor * 0.3);
    }
    
    const finalScale = baseScale * perspectiveScale;
    
    // Minimum/Maximum Grenzen
    return Math.max(0.1, Math.min(2.0, finalScale));
}

/**
 * Berechnet maximale Schiffsanzahl basierend auf Pitch
 */
function calculateMaxShipsForPitch(zoom, mapPitch) {
    let baseMaxShips = 1000;
    if (isMobile) 
        baseMaxShips = 800;
    if (isLowEndDevice)
        baseMaxShips = 300;

    // Pitch-Anpassung: Bei hohem Pitch werden mehr Schiffe sichtbar
    if (mapPitch > 30) {
        const pitchBonus = (mapPitch - 30) / 25; // 0.0 bis 1.0 für 30° bis 55°
        baseMaxShips = Math.floor(baseMaxShips * (1.0 + pitchBonus * 0.3)); // Bis zu 30% mehr
    }
    
    return baseMaxShips;
}

// 3. Verbesserte calculateGlobeOrientation für sanfteren Übergang
function calculateGlobeOrientation(ship) {
    const projection = map.getProjection();
    const zoom = map.getZoom();

    if (!projection || projection.name !== 'globe') {
        return (ship.heading || ship.course || 0) * Math.PI / 180;
    }

    const { lng, lat } = ship;
    const courseRad = (ship.heading || ship.course || 0) * Math.PI / 180;

    // ÜBERGANGSBEREICH: Zwischen Zoom 5 und 6
    if (zoom >= 5 && zoom < 6) {
        const transitionProgress = (zoom - 5); // 0 bis 1
        
        // Standard-Orientierung für flache Karte
        const flatOrientation = courseRad;
        
        // Globe-Orientierung berechnen
        const shipPoint = map.project([lng, lat]);
        const northPoint = map.project([lng, Math.min(89, lat + 0.1)]);
        const eastPoint = map.project([Math.min(179, lng + 0.1), lat]);

        const surfaceNorth = {
            x: northPoint.x - shipPoint.x,
            y: northPoint.y - shipPoint.y
        };

        const northLength = Math.sqrt(surfaceNorth.x * surfaceNorth.x + surfaceNorth.y * surfaceNorth.y);

        if (northLength > 0) {
            surfaceNorth.x /= northLength;
            surfaceNorth.y /= northLength;
        }

        const surfaceNorthAngle = Math.atan2(surfaceNorth.y, surfaceNorth.x) - Math.PI / 2;
        const globeOrientation = courseRad + surfaceNorthAngle;
        
        // Zwischen den Orientierungen überblenden
        return flatOrientation * transitionProgress + globeOrientation * (1 - transitionProgress);
    }
    
    // Standard Globe-Verhalten für Zoom < 5
    const shipPoint = map.project([lng, lat]);
    const northPoint = map.project([lng, Math.min(89, lat + 0.1)]);
    const eastPoint = map.project([Math.min(179, lng + 0.1), lat]);

    const surfaceNorth = {
        x: northPoint.x - shipPoint.x,
        y: northPoint.y - shipPoint.y
    };

    const northLength = Math.sqrt(surfaceNorth.x * surfaceNorth.x + surfaceNorth.y * surfaceNorth.y);

    if (northLength > 0) {
        surfaceNorth.x /= northLength;
        surfaceNorth.y /= northLength;
    }

    const surfaceNorthAngle = Math.atan2(surfaceNorth.y, surfaceNorth.x) - Math.PI / 2;

    return courseRad + surfaceNorthAngle;
}

let currentlyRendering = false;

function drawShips() {
    if (currentlyRendering || !shipCanvas || !shipCtx) return;

    currentlyRendering = true;
    
    try {
        var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
        if(isLowEndDevice){
            pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
        }
        
        const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
        const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;

        // Canvas clearing
        shipCtx.save();
        shipCtx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
        shipCtx.clearRect(0, 0, shipCanvas.width, shipCanvas.height);
        shipCtx.restore();
        shipCtx.setTransform(pixelRatio, 0, 0, pixelRatio, 0, 0);
        
        if (isLowEndDevice) {
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
	} else {
            shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
            shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
        }

        // Spezielle Modi (unverändert)
        if (typeof isTrackVisible !== 'undefined' && isTrackVisible) {
            if (!window.tempShipsBackupTrack && ships.length > 0) {
                window.tempShipsBackupTrack = [...ships];
                ships = [];
            }
            drawSearchPositionMarker();
        if (typeof drawGPSMarker === 'function') {
            drawGPSMarker();
        }
            drawTrackMarker();
            return;
        }

        if (typeof isForecastVisible !== 'undefined' && isForecastVisible) {
            if (!window.tempShipsBackupForecast && ships.length > 0) {
                window.tempShipsBackupForecast = [...ships];
                ships = [];
            }
            drawSearchPositionMarker();
        if (typeof drawGPSMarker === 'function') {
            drawGPSMarker();
        }
            drawTrackMarker();
            return;
        }

        if (typeof isDistanceMeasureActive !== 'undefined' && isDistanceMeasureActive) {
            drawSearchPositionMarker();
        if (typeof drawGPSMarker === 'function') {
            drawGPSMarker();
        }
            drawTrackMarker();
        }

        if (typeof isRoutingMode !== 'undefined' && isRoutingMode) {
            drawSearchPositionMarker();
        if (typeof drawGPSMarker === 'function') {
            drawGPSMarker();
        }
            drawTrackMarker();
        }

        // Ship backups wiederherstellen
        if (window.tempShipsBackupTrack && ships.length === 0) {
            ships = [...window.tempShipsBackupTrack];
            window.tempShipsBackupTrack = null;
        }
        
        if (window.tempShipsBackupForecast && ships.length === 0) {
            ships = [...window.tempShipsBackupForecast];
            window.tempShipsBackupForecast = null;
        }
		
        const zoom = map.getZoom();
        const mapPitch = map.getPitch();

        // SCHIFFE IMMER ZEICHNEN - KEIN MOVEMENT CHECK!
        if (ships.length === 0 && persistentShips.length === 0) {
            drawSearchPositionMarker();
        if (typeof drawGPSMarker === 'function') {
            drawGPSMarker();
        }
            drawTrackMarker();
            return;
        }

        if (persistentShips && persistentShips.length > 0) {
            const visiblePersistentShips = getVisibleShipsInViewport(persistentShips.map(ship => {
                // Auch für persistentShips smooth animation
                if (ship.displayLat !== undefined && ship.displayLng !== undefined) {
                    return {
                        ...ship,
                        lat: ship.displayLat,
                        lng: ship.displayLng
                    };
                }
                return ship;
            }), viewportBounds);
            
            if (visiblePersistentShips.length > 0) {
                renderShipsDirectly(visiblePersistentShips);
                drawShipNames(visiblePersistentShips, zoom);
            }
        }

        const viewportBounds = calculateViewportBounds(canvasWidth, canvasHeight, mapPitch);
        const visibleShips = getVisibleShipsInViewport(ships, viewportBounds);

		if (typeof isFleetFilterActive !== 'undefined' && isFleetFilterActive && showOtherShips === false) {
			visibleShips = visibleShips.filter(ship => {
				return ship.fleetId && visibleFleets.has(ship.fleetId);
			});
		}

        if (visibleShips.length > 0) {
            var MaxShips = 1000;
            if (isMobile) MaxShips = 800;
            if (isLowEndDevice) MaxShips = 300;
            
            const shipsToRender = visibleShips.slice(0, Math.min(MaxShips, visibleShips.length));
            
            renderShipsDirectly(shipsToRender);
            drawShipNames(shipsToRender, zoom);
        }

        if (persistentShips && persistentShips.length > 0) {
            const visiblePersistentShips = getVisibleShipsInViewport(persistentShips, viewportBounds);
            if (visiblePersistentShips.length > 0) {
                renderShipsDirectly(visiblePersistentShips);
                drawShipNames(visiblePersistentShips, zoom);
            }
        }

        drawSearchPositionMarker();
        drawGPSElements();
        drawTrackMarker();
		
		if (map.getZoom() > 8 && Object.values(poiFilters).some(active => active)) {
			drawStaticAssets();
		}
		
        if (typeof fleetTrackingActive !== 'undefined' && fleetTrackingActive) {
            drawFleetShips();
        }
        
    } catch (error) {

    } finally {
        currentlyRendering = false;
    }
}

function calculateViewportBounds(canvasWidth, canvasHeight, mapPitch) {
    // Basis-Bounds vom aktuellen Map View
    const bounds = map.getBounds();
    
    // Pitch-Korrektur: Bei hohem Pitch wird der "sichtbare" Bereich größer
    // da Schiffe am Horizont weiter entfernt, aber noch sichtbar sind
    let pitchExpansionFactor = 1.0;
    
    if (mapPitch > 0) {
        // Progressive Expansion basierend auf Pitch (0° bis 55°)
        const pitchNormalized = Math.min(mapPitch, 55) / 55; // 0.0 bis 1.0
        
        // Bei max Pitch (55°) erweitere Viewport um 50%
        pitchExpansionFactor = 1.0 + (pitchNormalized * 0.5);
        
    }
    
    // Erweiterte Bounds berechnen
    const latRange = bounds.getNorth() - bounds.getSouth();
    const lngRange = bounds.getEast() - bounds.getWest();
    
    const latExpansion = (latRange * (pitchExpansionFactor - 1)) / 2;
    const lngExpansion = (lngRange * (pitchExpansionFactor - 1)) / 2;
    
    return {
        north: bounds.getNorth() + latExpansion,
        south: bounds.getSouth() - latExpansion,
        east: bounds.getEast() + lngExpansion,
        west: bounds.getWest() - lngExpansion,
        expansion: pitchExpansionFactor
    };
}

function getVisibleShipsInViewport(shipList, viewportBounds) {
    if (shipList.length === 0) return [];

    const visibleShips = [];
    const projection = map.getProjection();
    const zoom = map.getZoom();

    for (const ship of shipList) {
        // 1. VIEWPORT BOUNDS CHECK (Hauptfilter)
        if (!isShipInViewportBounds(ship, viewportBounds)) {
            continue; // Skip ship - nicht im Viewport
        }

        // 2. GLOBE PROJECTION SPEZIAL-BEHANDLUNG
        if (projection && projection.name === 'globe') {
            if (!isShipVisibleOnGlobe(ship, map.getCenter(), zoom)) {
                continue; // Skip ship - auf Rückseite des Globus
            }
        }

        // 3. PROJEKTION BERECHNEN (nur für sichtbare Schiffe)
        const point = map.project([ship.lng, ship.lat]);
        
        // 4. CANVAS BOUNDS CHECK (Feinfilter)
        // Erweiterte Canvas-Bounds für edge cases
        var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
        if(isLowEndDevice){
            pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
        }
        const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
        const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
        
        const margin = zoom > 10 ? 20 : 50; // Kleinerer Margin bei hohem Zoom
        
        if (point.x >= -margin && point.x <= canvasWidth + margin &&
            point.y >= -margin && point.y <= canvasHeight + margin) {
            
            // PROJEKTION CACHEN für Performance
            ship._projectedPoint = {
                x: Math.round(point.x * 10) / 10,
                y: Math.round(point.y * 10) / 10
            };
            
            visibleShips.push(ship);
        }
    }

    return visibleShips;
}

/**
 * Prüft ob Schiff in Viewport Bounds liegt
 */
function isShipInViewportBounds(ship, bounds) {
    return ship.lat >= bounds.south && 
           ship.lat <= bounds.north && 
           ship.lng >= bounds.west && 
           ship.lng <= bounds.east;
}

async function renderShipsInChunks(visibleShips) {

    // Interrupt laufendes Rendering
    chunkRenderer.interrupt();

    // Neue Render Queue vorbereiten
    chunkRenderer.prepareRenderQueue(visibleShips);
    chunkRenderer.isRendering = true;

    // Erste Chunks sofort rendern (wichtigste Schiffe)
    const hasMoreChunks = await chunkRenderer.renderNextChunks();

    // Restliche Chunks asynchron rendern
    if (hasMoreChunks) {
        scheduleAsyncChunkRendering();
    }
}

function renderShipsDirectly(visibleShips) {
    // Sortiere nach Priorität für besseres Rendering
    const prioritizedShips = prioritizeShipsForRendering(visibleShips);

    for (const ship of prioritizedShips) {
        drawShip(shipCtx, ship);
    }
}

function prioritizeShipsForRendering(ships) {
    const center = map.getCenter();
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    var canvasCenter = {
        x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
        y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
    };
    
    if(isLowEndDevice){
        canvasCenter = {
            x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
            y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1)))
        };
    }

    return ships
        .map(ship => {
            const point = ship._projectedPoint || map.project([ship.lng, ship.lat]);
            const distanceFromCenter = Math.sqrt(
                Math.pow(point.x - canvasCenter.x, 2) +
                Math.pow(point.y - canvasCenter.y, 2)
            );

            let priority = 0;

            // Höchste Priorität: Selected/Hovered ships
            if (ship === selectedShip) priority += 10000;
            if (ship === hoveredShip) priority += 5000;

            // Hohe Priorität: Schiffe in der Bildschirmmitte
            priority += Math.max(0, 1000 - distanceFromCenter);

            // Mittlere Priorität: Bewegende Schiffe
            if (ship.speed > 1) priority += 500;

            // Niedrigere Priorität: Große Schiffe
            const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || 50;
            if (shipLength > 200) priority += 200;
            else if (shipLength > 100) priority += 100;

            // Zoom-abhängige Priorität
            if (zoom > 6) {
                priority += 300; // Bei hohem Zoom: Alle Schiffe wichtig
            } else {
                if (ship.speed < 0.1) priority -= 200; // Stationäre Schiffe weniger wichtig
            }

            ship._renderPriority = priority;
            ship._distanceFromCenter = distanceFromCenter;

            return ship;
        })
        .sort((a, b) => b._renderPriority - a._renderPriority);
}

function scheduleAsyncChunkRendering() {
    if (!chunkRenderer.isRendering) return;

    requestIdleCallback(async () => {
        if (!chunkRenderer.isRendering || isMapMoving) return;

        const hasMoreChunks = await chunkRenderer.renderNextChunks();

        if (hasMoreChunks && !isMapMoving) {
            scheduleAsyncChunkRendering();
        }
    }, { timeout: isMobile ? 32 : 16 });
}

function getMaxShipNamesForViewport(zoom, visibleShipsCount) {
    let maxNames;
    
    if (isMobile && window.innerWidth <= 480) {
	if (zoom >= 9)
	maxNames = 50;
	if (zoom >= 13) 
	return visibleShipsCount;
	return Math.min(maxNames, visibleShipsCount);	
	} else {
	if (zoom >= 9)
	maxNames = 50
	if (zoom >= 14)
	return visibleShipsCount;	
	return Math.min(maxNames, visibleShipsCount);	
	}
}

let stableShipNames = [];
let lastNameUpdate = 0;
let lastZoomForNames = 0;
let lastShipCount = 0;

// Namen nur alle X Sekunden oder bei wichtigen Änderungen updaten
const NAME_UPDATE_INTERVAL = 3000; // 3 Sekunden
const ZOOM_THRESHOLD = 0.5; // Namen neu berechnen bei 0.5 Zoom-Unterschied

function shouldUpdateNames(visibleShips) {
    const now = Date.now();
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    const currentShipCount = visibleShips.length;
    
    // Gründe für Namen-Update:
    
    // 1. Noch nie berechnet
    if (stableShipNames.length === 0) {
        return true;
    }
    
    // 2. Zeit abgelaufen
    if (now - lastNameUpdate > NAME_UPDATE_INTERVAL) {
        return true;
    }
    
    // 3. Signifikante Zoom-Änderung
    if (Math.abs(currentZoom - lastZoomForNames) > ZOOM_THRESHOLD) {
        return true;
    }
	
    return false;
}

function updateStableNames(visibleShips, maxNames) {
    const now = Date.now();
    
    // Einfache Namen-Auswahl (ohne Zentrum-Bias)
    const importantShips = visibleShips.filter(ship => 
        ship === selectedShip || ship === hoveredShip
    );
    
    const normalShips = visibleShips.filter(ship => 
        ship !== selectedShip && ship !== hoveredShip
    );
    
    // Normale Schiffe: Nur große und bewegende bevorzugen
    const filteredNormalShips = normalShips
        .filter(ship => {
            const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || parseFloat(ship.vsl_length) || 50;
            const speed = ship.speed || 0;
            return shipLength > 80 || speed >= 0.1; // Große oder bewegende Schiffe
        })
        .slice(0, maxNames - importantShips.length);
    
    // Falls nicht genug: Mit allen anderen auffüllen
    if (filteredNormalShips.length < maxNames - importantShips.length) {
        const remainingSlots = maxNames - importantShips.length - filteredNormalShips.length;
        const usedShips = new Set([...importantShips, ...filteredNormalShips]);
        
        const additionalShips = normalShips
            .filter(ship => !usedShips.has(ship))
            .slice(0, remainingSlots);
        
        filteredNormalShips.push(...additionalShips);
    }
    
    stableShipNames = [...importantShips, ...filteredNormalShips].slice(0, maxNames);
    
    // Update Tracking-Variablen
    lastNameUpdate = now;
    lastZoomForNames = map.getZoom();
    lastShipCount = visibleShips.length;  
}

// NEUE prioritizeShipsForNames mit Stabilität
function prioritizeShipsForNames(visibleShips, maxNames) {
    if (!visibleShips || visibleShips.length === 0) {
        return [];
    }
    
    // Prüfe ob Namen-Update nötig ist
    if (shouldUpdateNames(visibleShips)) {
        updateStableNames(visibleShips, maxNames);
    }
    
    // Filtere stabile Namen nach aktuell sichtbaren Schiffen
    const currentlyVisibleNames = stableShipNames.filter(stableShip => {
        return visibleShips.some(visibleShip => {
            // Match by MMSI, shipId oder Name+Position
            if (stableShip.mmsi && visibleShip.mmsi) {
                return stableShip.mmsi === visibleShip.mmsi;
            }
            if (stableShip.shipId && visibleShip.shipId) {
                return stableShip.shipId === visibleShip.shipId;
            }
            // Fallback: Name + ungefähre Position
            return stableShip.name === visibleShip.name &&
                   Math.abs(stableShip.lat - visibleShip.lat) < 0.01 &&
                   Math.abs(stableShip.lng - visibleShip.lng) < 0.01;
        });
    });
    
    // Falls zu wenige: Mit aktuellen Schiffen auffüllen
    if (currentlyVisibleNames.length < maxNames) {
        const usedShips = new Set(currentlyVisibleNames);
        const additionalShips = visibleShips
            .filter(ship => !usedShips.has(ship))
            .slice(0, maxNames - currentlyVisibleNames.length);
        
        currentlyVisibleNames.push(...additionalShips);
    }
    
    return currentlyVisibleNames.slice(0, maxNames);
}

// Movement-Handler: Namen NICHT während Bewegung updaten
let isMapMovingForNames = false;
let moveTimeoutForNames = null;

// Modifiziere shouldUpdateNames für Movement
const originalShouldUpdateNames = shouldUpdateNames;
window.shouldUpdateNames = function(visibleShips) {
    // Während Movement: KEINE Namen-Updates außer bei Selected/Hovered
    if (isMapMovingForNames) {
        const hasSelectedInNames = stableShipNames.some(ship => ship === selectedShip);
        const hasHoveredInNames = stableShipNames.some(ship => ship === hoveredShip);
        
        return (selectedShip && !hasSelectedInNames) || (hoveredShip && !hasHoveredInNames);
    }
    
    return originalShouldUpdateNames(visibleShips);
};

function drawShipNames(visibleShips, zoom) {
    if (!nameRenderingEnabled || !shipCanvas || !shipCtx) return;
    
    const maxNames = getMaxShipNamesForViewport(zoom, visibleShips.length);
    if (maxNames === 0 && zoom < 11) return;
    
    const shipsWithNames = prioritizeShipsForNames(visibleShips, maxNames);
    if (shipsWithNames.length === 0) return;
    
    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    if(isLowEndDevice){
        pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    }
    
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    
    let namesInViewport = 0;
    
    for (const ship of shipsWithNames) {
        // KORRIGIERT: Konsistente Position-Verwendung
        const actualLat = (ship.displayLat !== undefined && ship.displayLng !== undefined && 
                          map.getZoom() >= 11) ? ship.displayLat : ship.lat;
        const actualLng = (ship.displayLat !== undefined && ship.displayLng !== undefined && 
                          map.getZoom() >= 11) ? ship.displayLng : ship.lng;
        
        const point = map.project([actualLng, actualLat]);
        const x = point.x;
        const y = point.y;
        
        // ULTRA-STRIKTE PRÜFUNG: Exakt 0 bis Canvas-Größe
        if (x <= 0 || x >= canvasWidth || y <= 0 || y >= canvasHeight) {
            continue; // Skip komplett alles außerhalb
        }
        
        // ZUSÄTZLICH: Prüfe ob genug Platz für Text ist
        const textHeight = 20; // Geschätzte Text-Höhe
        if (y < textHeight || y > canvasHeight - textHeight) {
            continue; // Skip wenn kein Platz für Text
        }
        
        var shipName = ship.name || 'N/A Ship';
        
        // NEUE LOGIK: Signal-Label Position berechnen
        let nameOffsetY = -37; // Standard-Offset für Namen
        let showSignalLabel = false;
        let signalLabelText = '';
        
        // Prüfe ob Signal-Label angezeigt werden soll (ab Zoom 8)
        if (zoom >= 11) {
			var effectiveElapsed = ship.elapsed;

            // Label Text basierend auf effectiveElapsed bestimmen
            showSignalLabel = true;
            
            if (effectiveElapsed !== undefined && effectiveElapsed !== null && effectiveElapsed !== 'N/A') {
                const minutes = parseInt(effectiveElapsed);
                
                if (!isNaN(minutes)) {
                    if (minutes <= 2.1) {
                        signalLabelText = 'LIVE';
                    } else if (minutes <= 60) {
                        signalLabelText = `${minutes}min`;
                    } else {
                        signalLabelText = '60min+';
                    }
                } else {
                    signalLabelText = '60min+';
                }
            } else {
                signalLabelText = '60min+';
            }
            if(map.getZoom() >=8)
            nameOffsetY = -37;
		if(map.getZoom() >=11)
			 nameOffsetY = -45;
        }
		
        // Schiffsname zeichnen (eventuell mit angepasstem Offset)
        if (zoom >= 11) {
		drawPOILabel(shipCtx, x, y, shipName.toUpperCase(), nameOffsetY);	
		}
        
        // Signal-Label zeichnen (falls vorhanden)
        if (zoom >= 11) {
            if (showSignalLabel && signalLabelText) {
                drawSignalLabel(shipCtx, x - 22, y, signalLabelText);
				drawSpeedLabel(shipCtx, x +22, y, ship);
            }
        }
        
        namesInViewport++;
    }
}

function drawSignalLabel(ctx, x, y, signalText, ship, offsetY = -8) {
    ctx.save();
    
    if (ship && ship.elapsed !== undefined && ship.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
        const minutes = parseInt(ship.elapsed);
        if (!isNaN(minutes)) {
            if (minutes <= 2.1) {
                signalText = 'LIVE';
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.8)'; // Grün
            } else if (minutes <= 60) {
                signalText = `${minutes}min`;
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.8)'; // Gelb
            } else {
                signalText = '60min+';
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.8)'; // Rot
            }
        }
    }
	
    // NEU: Verwende interpolierte Position falls verfügbar
    if (ship && ship.displayLat !== undefined && ship.displayLng !== undefined) {
        const point = map.project([ship.displayLng, ship.displayLat]);
        x = point.x;
        y = point.y;
    }
    
    // Deklariere labelY Variable korrekt
    let labelY;
    
    if(map.getZoom() >= 8)
        labelY = y - 25;

    if(map.getZoom() >= 11)
        labelY = y - 30;
    
    ctx.font = isMobile ? '10px system-ui' : '10px system-ui';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    
    const metrics = ctx.measureText(signalText);
    const boxWidth = metrics.width + 10;
    const boxHeight = 16;
    
    localStorage.setItem('metrics', metrics.width);
    
    // GEÄNDERT: Abgerundetes Rechteck statt normales Rechteck
    const borderRadius = 5;
    const rectX = x - boxWidth/2;
    const rectY = labelY - boxHeight/2;
    
    // Hintergrund mit abgerundeten Ecken
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(rectX + borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + boxWidth - borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY, rectX + boxWidth, rectY + borderRadius);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY + boxHeight - borderRadius);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY + boxHeight, rectX + boxWidth - borderRadius, rectY + boxHeight);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + borderRadius, rectY + boxHeight);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX, rectY + boxHeight, rectX, rectY + boxHeight - borderRadius);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX, rectY + borderRadius);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX, rectY, rectX + borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.closePath();
    
    // Fülle Hintergrund
    if (signalText === 'LIVE') {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.8)';
    } else {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.8)';
    }
    ctx.fill();
    
    // Rahmen mit abgerundeten Ecken
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.stroke();
    
    // Text
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    ctx.fillText(signalText, x, labelY + 4);
    
    ctx.restore();
}

function drawSpeedLabel(ctx, x, y, ship, offsetY = -8) {
    ctx.save();
    
	if(map.getZoom() >=8)
		labelY = y - 25;

	if(map.getZoom() >=11)
		labelY = y - 30;
    
    ctx.font = isMobile ? '10px system-ui' : '10px system-ui';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    
    // NEU: Verwende interpolierte Speed falls verfügbar
    var displaySpeed = ship.speed || 0;

    // Speed Text und Größe
    const speedText = `${displaySpeed.toFixed(1)}kn`;
    const metrics = ctx.measureText(speedText);
    const boxWidth = metrics.width + 10;
    const boxHeight = 16;
    const borderRadius = 5;
    const rectX = x - boxWidth/2;
    const rectY = labelY - boxHeight/2;
    
    // Helper für Speed-Farbe
    function getSpeedColor(speedInKnots) {
        const speed = speedInKnots || 0;
        if (speed <= 0.5) return 'rgba(107, 114, 128, 0.8)';
        else if (speed <= 5) return 'rgba(220, 38, 38, 0.8)';
        else if (speed <= 10) return 'rgba(249, 115, 22, 0.8)';
        else if (speed <= 15) return 'rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.8)';
        else if (speed <= 20) return 'rgba(132, 204, 22, 0.8)';
        else if (speed <= 25) return 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.8)';
        else return 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.8)';
    }
    
    // Abgerundetes Rechteck zeichnen
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(rectX + borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + boxWidth - borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY, rectX + boxWidth, rectY + borderRadius);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY + boxHeight - borderRadius);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX + boxWidth, rectY + boxHeight, rectX + boxWidth - borderRadius, rectY + boxHeight);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX + borderRadius, rectY + boxHeight);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX, rectY + boxHeight, rectX, rectY + boxHeight - borderRadius);
    ctx.lineTo(rectX, rectY + borderRadius);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(rectX, rectY, rectX + borderRadius, rectY);
    ctx.closePath();
    
    // Fülle mit Speed-Farbe
    ctx.fillStyle = getSpeedColor(displaySpeed);
    ctx.fill();
    
    // Rahmen
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.stroke();
    
    // Text
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    ctx.fillText(speedText, x, labelY + 4);
    
    ctx.restore();
}

// Optimierte Animationsschleife mit korrekter Synchronisation
let animationId = null;
let isAnimationRunning = false;

function animate(currentTime = 0) {
    // KRITISCH: Stoppe alte Animation bevor neue startet
    if (animationId) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationId);
        animationId = null;
    }
    
    // Verhindere mehrfache parallele Animations-Loops
    if (isAnimationRunning) {
        return;
    }
    
    isAnimationRunning = true;
    
    // Frame Count erhöhen
    frameCount++;
    
    // Frame-Rate-Kontrolle
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    const targetFPS = isMobile ? (zoom > 15 ? 20 : zoom > 12 ? 25 : 30) : (zoom > 15 ? 40 : 60);
    const frameInterval = 1000 / targetFPS;
    
    if (currentTime - lastFrameTime < frameInterval) {
        isAnimationRunning = false;
        animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        return;
    }
    
    // Prüfe auf Kartenänderungen
    if (hasMapChanged() || needsRedraw) {
        drawShips();
        needsRedraw = false;
    }
    
    lastFrameTime = currentTime;
    isAnimationRunning = false;
    animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}

let lastFrameTime = 0;
const zoom = map.getZoom();
const targetFPS = isMobile ? (zoom > 15 ? 20 : zoom > 12 ? 25 : 30) : (zoom > 15 ? 40 : 60);
const frameInterval = 1000 / targetFPS;

function animate(currentTime = 0) {
    // KRITISCH: Stoppe alte Animation bevor neue startet
    if (animationId) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationId);
        animationId = null;
    }
    
    // Verhindere mehrfache parallele Animations-Loops
    if (isAnimationRunning) {
        return;
    }
    
    isAnimationRunning = true;
    
    // Frame Count erhöhen
    frameCount++;
    
    // Frame-Rate-Kontrolle
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    const targetFPS = isMobile ? (zoom > 15 ? 20 : zoom > 12 ? 25 : 30) : (zoom > 15 ? 40 : 60);
    const frameInterval = 1000 / targetFPS;
    
    if (currentTime - lastFrameTime < frameInterval) {
        isAnimationRunning = false;
        animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        return;
    }
    
    // Prüfe auf Kartenänderungen
    if (hasMapChanged() || needsRedraw) {
        drawShips();
        needsRedraw = false;
    }
    
    lastFrameTime = currentTime;
    isAnimationRunning = false;
    animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}

function stopAnimation() {
    if (animationId) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationId);
        animationId = null;
    }
    isAnimationRunning = false;
}

function resetFPSCounter() {
    frameCount = 0;
    fpsStartTime = Date.now();
    lastFPSUpdate = Date.now();
    currentFPS = 0;
    
    const fpsDisplay = document.getElementById('fpsDisplay');
    if (fpsDisplay) {
        fpsDisplay.textContent = '0';
        fpsDisplay.style.color = '#10b981';
        fpsDisplay.title = 'FPS Counter wurde zurückgesetzt';
    }
    
}

// Zoom Handler mit Canvas-Cleanup
let zoomTransitionTimeout = null;

function clearAllCanvases() {
    const canvasesToClear = [
        { canvas: shipCanvas, ctx: shipCtx, name: 'Ship Canvas' },
    ];
    
    canvasesToClear.forEach(({ canvas, ctx, name }) => {
        if (canvas && ctx) {
            try {
                const pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
                const canvasWidth = canvas.width / pixelRatio;
                const canvasHeight = canvas.height / pixelRatio;
                
                // KRITISCH: Vollständiges Löschen mit mehreren Methoden
                ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvasWidth, canvasHeight);
                ctx.save();
                ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
                ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                ctx.restore();
                
            } catch (error) {
                console.warn(`⚠️ ${name} clearing failed:`, error);
            }
        }
    });
}

// VERBESSERTE Pitch-Projektion für Canvas mit realistischerer Perspektive
function calculateSurfaceScale(ship) {
    const projection = map.getProjection();
    const mapPitch = map.getPitch();
    const zoom = map.getZoom();

    if (!projection || projection.name !== 'globe') {
        if (mapPitch > 0) {
            const pitchRadians = mapPitch * Math.PI / 180;
            const basePitchFactor = Math.cos(pitchRadians);

            // VERBESSERT: Progressive Skalierung je nach Pitch-Grad
            let correctedFactor;
            if (mapPitch <= 30) {
                // Sanfte Korrektur bei niedrigem Pitch
                correctedFactor = Math.pow(basePitchFactor, 0.3);
            } else if (mapPitch <= 60) {
                // Mittlere Korrektur
                correctedFactor = Math.pow(basePitchFactor, 0.5);
            } else if (mapPitch <= 75) {
                // Stärkere Korrektur bei hohem Pitch
                correctedFactor = Math.pow(basePitchFactor, 0.7);
            } else {
                // Sehr starke Korrektur bei extremem Pitch
                const excessPitch = (mapPitch - 75) / 15;
                correctedFactor = Math.pow(basePitchFactor, 0.7 + (excessPitch * 2.5));
            }

            return Math.max(0.1, correctedFactor); // Minimum 10% Größe
        }

        return 1.0;
    }

    // VERBESSERT: Sanfterer Übergang für Globe-Projektion
    const { lat, lng } = ship;
    const mapCenter = map.getCenter();
    
    // Berechne Entfernung vom Zentrum
    const distFromCenter = Math.sqrt(
        Math.pow(lng - mapCenter.lng, 2) +
        Math.pow(lat - mapCenter.lat, 2)
    );
    
    const pitchFactor = Math.cos(mapPitch * Math.PI / 180);
    
    // SANFTER ÜBERGANG: Zwischen Zoom 5 und 6
    let distanceFactor;
    
    if (zoom < 5) {
        // Standard Globe-Verhalten für niedrigen Zoom
        distanceFactor = Math.max(0.3, 1 - distFromCenter * 0.01);
    } else if (zoom < 6) {
        // ÜBERGANGSBEREICH: Zoom 5-6
        const transitionProgress = (zoom - 5); // 0 bis 1
        
        // Zwei Faktoren berechnen und mischen
        const globeFactor = Math.max(0.3, 1 - distFromCenter * 0.01);
        const flatFactor = 1.0; // Normale Projektion
        
        // Zwischen den Faktoren überblenden
        distanceFactor = globeFactor * (1 - transitionProgress) + flatFactor * transitionProgress;
    } else {
        // Normale Projektion ab Zoom 6
        distanceFactor = 1.0;
    }

    return pitchFactor * distanceFactor;
}

// NEUE FUNKTION: Verbesserte Y-Skalierung basierend auf Bildschirmposition
function calculatePitchYScale(ship, canvasY) {
    const mapPitch = map.getPitch();
    if (mapPitch <= 0) return 1.0;

    const pitchRadians = mapPitch * Math.PI / 180;
    const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
    const screenCenterY = mapContainer.offsetHeight / 2;
    
    // VERBESSERT: Normalisierte Position (-1 bis +1)
    const normalizedY = (canvasY - screenCenterY) / screenCenterY;
    
    // VERBESSERT: Perspektivische Korrektur basierend auf Position
    let perspectiveFactor;
    
    if (mapPitch <= 30) {
        // Sanfte Perspektive bei niedrigem Pitch
        perspectiveFactor = 1 + (normalizedY * 0.1);
    } else if (mapPitch <= 60) {
        // Mittlere Perspektive
        perspectiveFactor = 1 + (normalizedY * 0.2);
    } else {
        // Starke Perspektive bei hohem Pitch
        perspectiveFactor = 1 + (normalizedY * 0.3);
    }
    
    // VERBESSERT: Basis Y-Skalierung mit progressiver Formel
    let baseYScale;
    if (mapPitch <= 45) {
        baseYScale = Math.pow(Math.cos(pitchRadians), 0.3);
    } else if (mapPitch <= 70) {
        baseYScale = Math.pow(Math.cos(pitchRadians), 0.5);
    } else {
        // Extremer Pitch: Sehr aggressive Skalierung
        const excessPitch = (mapPitch - 70) / 20;
        baseYScale = Math.pow(Math.cos(pitchRadians), 0.5 + (excessPitch * 3));
    }
    
    // VERBESSERT: Kombiniere Basis-Skalierung mit Perspektive
    const finalYScale = baseYScale * perspectiveFactor;
    
    return Math.max(0.05, finalYScale); // Minimum 5% Höhe
}

var searchSelectedPosition = null;

// ============================================================================
// KOMPLETTE INTEGRATION DER SCHIFFSNAMEN-PERFORMANCE-OPTIMIERUNG
// Füge diesen Code in dein bestehendes Script ein (nach den globalen Variablen)
// ============================================================================

// SCHRITT 1: NEUE GLOBALE VARIABLEN FÜR NAMEN-OPTIMIERUNG
let nameRenderingEnabled = true;
let lastNameRenderTime = 0;
let shipNamesCache = new Map(); // Cache für berechnete Namen-Positionen

// SCHRITT 2: HILFSFUNKTIONEN FÜR NAMEN-OPTIMIERUNG
function shouldShowShipName(ship, zoom, shipPixelLength) {
    if (zoom < 9) return false;
    
    if (zoom > 16) {
        const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || parseFloat(ship.vsl_length) || 50;
        return shipLength > 100;
    }
    
    if (zoom > 14) {
        const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || parseFloat(ship.vsl_length) || 50;
        const isMoving = (ship.speed || 0) >= 0.1;
        return isMoving || shipLength > 80;
    }
    
    return true;
}

function drawShip(ctx, ship) {
    ctx.save();
    const projectedPoint = ship._projectedPoint;
    const x = projectedPoint.x;
    const y = projectedPoint.y;
    ctx.translate(x, y);

    const shipCourse = ship.heading || ship.course || 0;
    const mapBearing = map.getBearing();
    const rotationRadians = (shipCourse - 180 - mapBearing) * Math.PI / 180;
    
    ctx.rotate(rotationRadians);
    ctx.scale(1, -1);
    
    // NEUE: Verwende bereits berechnete Pitch-Scale
    const pitchScale = ship._pitchScale || calculateSurfaceScale(ship);
    const projection = map.getProjection();
    const mapPitch = map.getPitch();

    // Erweiterte Pitch-Skalierung
    if ((!projection || projection.name !== 'globe') && mapPitch > 0) {
        const yScaleFactor = calculatePitchYScale(ship, y);
        
        let depthScale = 1.0;
        if (mapPitch > 45) {
            const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
            const screenCenterY = mapContainer.offsetHeight / 2;
            const distanceFromCenter = Math.abs(y - screenCenterY) / screenCenterY;
            depthScale = Math.max(0.3, 1 - (distanceFromCenter * 0.2));
        }
        
        ctx.scale(pitchScale * depthScale, pitchScale * yScaleFactor * depthScale);
    } else {
        ctx.scale(pitchScale, pitchScale);
    }

    var zoom = map.getZoom();
	var shipLength = Math.max(parseFloat(ship.length) || parseFloat(ship.vsl_length) || 50, 100);
	if(shipLength == '511') shipLength = '20';
	if(ship.name == '[SAT-AIS]') shipLength = '250';
	if(ship.name == '[SAT-AIS]' && ship.type == 0) shipLength = '200';	
	if(ship.name == '[SAT-AIS]' && ship.type == 2) shipLength = '150';	

    // Ship size calculation (unverändert)
    let sizeMultiplier = 3.0;
    let zoomFactor = 100;
    let basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 24) * 0.2;
    
    // Zoom-spezifische Anpassungen (bestehender Code)
	if(zoom >=1.0 && zoom <=2.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 12) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=2.0 && zoom <=3.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 12) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=3.0 && zoom <=4.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 13) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=4.0 && zoom <=5.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 14) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=5.0 && zoom <=6.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 15) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=6.0 && zoom <=7.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 16) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=7.0 && zoom <=8.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 17) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=8.0 && zoom <=9.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 18) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=9.0 && zoom <=10.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 19) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=10.0 && zoom <=11.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 20) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=11.0 && zoom <=12.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 20) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=12.0 && zoom <=13.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 20) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=13.0 && zoom <=14.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 20) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=14.0 && zoom <=15.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 20) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=15.0 && zoom <=16.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 21) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=16.0 && zoom <=17.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 21) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=17.0 && zoom <=18.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 21) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=18.0 && zoom <=19.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 21) * 0.2;
	if(zoom >=19.0) basePixelsPerMeter = Math.pow(2, zoom - 21) * 0.2;

    const shipPixelLength = Math.max(4, Math.min(60, shipLength * basePixelsPerMeter * zoomFactor * sizeMultiplier));
    const shipPixelWidth = Math.max(2, Math.min(20, shipPixelLength * 0.3));

    const color = getShipColor(ship);

    // Highlight rendering (unverändert)
    if (ship === selectedShip) {
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffff00';
        ctx.lineWidth = 2;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(0, 0, Math.max(shipPixelLength * 0.6, 12), 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.stroke();
    }

    if (ship === hoveredShip) {
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(0, 0, Math.max(shipPixelLength * 0.5, 10), 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.stroke();
    }

    // Draw ship (unverändert)
    ctx.fillStyle = color;
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#000';
    ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(0.5, shipPixelLength / 25);

    const isStationary = (ship.speed || 0) < 0.1;
    const shouldDrawAsCircle = isStationary;

    if (shouldDrawAsCircle) {
        const radius = Math.max(3, shipPixelLength * 0.25);
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(0, 0, radius, 0, 2 * Math.PI);
        ctx.fill();
        ctx.stroke();
    } else {
        const noseLength = shipPixelLength * 0.4;
        const bodyLength = shipPixelLength * 0.6;
        const halfWidth = shipPixelWidth / 2;

        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, -noseLength);
        ctx.lineTo(-halfWidth, 0);
        ctx.lineTo(-halfWidth, bodyLength);
        ctx.lineTo(0, bodyLength * 0.8);
        ctx.lineTo(halfWidth, bodyLength);
        ctx.lineTo(halfWidth, 0);
        ctx.closePath();
        ctx.fill();
        ctx.stroke();
    }

    ctx.restore();
}

var searchSelectedShip = null;

function drawSearchPositionMarker() {
    // Prüfe ob wir überhaupt was zu zeichnen haben
    const markerPosition = searchSelectedPosition;
    const markerShip = searchSelectedShip || clickedShip;
    
    if (!markerPosition || !shipCanvas || !shipCtx) return;
    
    // Position updaten wenn ein Schiff getrackt wird
    if (markerShip) {
        updateSearchMarkerToShipPosition();
    }
    
    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    
    // WICHTIG: IMMER markerPosition verwenden - wird in updateSearchMarkerToShipPosition dynamisch aktualisiert!
    const point = map.project([markerPosition.lng, markerPosition.lat]);
    
    // Prüfen ob Position sichtbar ist
    if (point.x < -100 || point.x > canvasWidth + 100 || 
        point.y < -100 || point.y > canvasHeight + 100) {
        return; // Position nicht sichtbar
    }
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    
    // Zoom-abhängige Kreisgröße
    let markerRadius;
    if (zoom <= 5) {
        markerRadius = 25;
    } else if (zoom <= 8) {
        markerRadius = 20;
    } else if (zoom <= 12) {
        markerRadius = 15;
    } else {
        markerRadius = 12;
    }
    
    shipCtx.save();
    
    // Gelber Kreis mit pulsierendem Effekt
    const time = Date.now() / 1000;
    const pulseScale = 1 + Math.sin(time * 3) * 0.2; // Pulsiert zwischen 0.8 und 1.2
    const currentRadius = markerRadius * pulseScale;
    
    // Äußerer gelber Kreis (transparenter)
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#ffff00';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 3;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.8;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, currentRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    // Innerer gelber Kreis (heller)
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#ffff00';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, currentRadius * 0.6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    // Zentrum-Punkt
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffff00';
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.9;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    shipCtx.restore();
    
    // FIX: Forciere Canvas-Update auf Low-End-Geräten
    if (isLowEndDevice) {
        // Mehrere Methoden um Canvas-Update zu forcieren
        
        // Methode 1: Canvas kurz unsichtbar/sichtbar machen
        shipCanvas.style.display = 'none';
        shipCanvas.offsetHeight; // Force reflow
        shipCanvas.style.display = 'block';
        
        // Methode 2: Transform ändern und zurücksetzen
        shipCanvas.style.transform = 'translateZ(0)';
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            shipCanvas.style.transform = '';
        });
    }
    
    // Kontinuierliche Animation triggern
    if (markerPosition) {
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
}

function getShipAtPosition(x, y) {
    let nearestShip = null;
    let minDistance = Infinity;

    // FIXED: Zoom-abhängige Hit-Area - größer bei niedrigen Zoom-Levels
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    let hitRadius;

    if (currentZoom <= 3) {
        hitRadius = isMobile ? 35 : 30; // Größere Hit-Area bei Zoom 1-3
    } else if (currentZoom <= 5) {
        hitRadius = isMobile ? 30 : 25; // Mittlere Hit-Area bei Zoom 4-5
    } else {
        hitRadius = isMobile ? 25 : 20; // Normale Hit-Area bei Zoom 6+
    }

    // Only check ships that were rendered (have cached projections)
    for (const ship of ships) {
        if (!ship._projectedPoint) continue; // Skip if not in viewport

        const point = ship._projectedPoint;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - point.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - point.y, 2));

        if (distance < hitRadius && distance < minDistance) {
            nearestShip = ship;
            minDistance = distance;
        }
    }

    return nearestShip;
}

function getShipColor(ship) {
    switch(ship.type) {
        case '1': return '#cf7983';
        case '8': return '#ef4444';
        case '7': return '#10b981';
        case '3': return '#22d3ee';
        case '9': return '#8b5cf6';
        case '2': return '#ffd920';
        case '4': return '#ffa000';
        case '6': return '#3b82f6';
        default:  return '#6b7280';
    }
}

function getShipTypeName(type) {
    switch(type) {
        case '1': return 'Navigation';
        case '2': return 'Fischerboot';
        case '3': return 'Schlepper';
        case '4': return 'Speedboot';
        case '6': return 'Passagier';
        case '7': return 'Cargo';
        case '8': return 'Tanker';
        case '9': return 'Yacht';
        default:  return 'N/A';
    }
}

const hillshadingController = new HillshadingController();

// 5. HILLSHADING LAYER CHECKBOX HANDLER
// Diese Funktion in Ihren bestehenden Checkbox Handler integrieren:
function handleHillshadingCheckbox(checkbox) {
    const isChecked = checkbox.checked;
    hillshadingController.toggle(isChecked);
    
    // In Layer Preferences speichern
    saveLayerPreferences();
    
}

function toggleHillshadingLayer(show) {
    
    const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig.hillshading;
    if (!layerConfig) {
        console.error('Hillshading layer configuration not found');
        return;
    }

    if (show) {
        // Hillshading hinzufügen
        if (!map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
            try {
                // 1. Prüfe ob DEM Source bereits existiert
                if (!map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
                    map.addSource('mapbox-dem', layerConfig.source);
                }
                
                // 2. Hillshading Layer hinzufügen
                const hillshadeLayer = {
                    id: layerConfig.id,
                    type: layerConfig.type,
                    source: 'mapbox-dem'
                };
                
                // Paint Properties hinzufügen
                if (layerConfig.paint) {
                    hillshadeLayer.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                }
                
                // Layer vor den Ship Canvas hinzufügen (unter den Schiffen)
                map.addLayer(hillshadeLayer, 'black-background');
                                
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('❌ Error adding hillshading layer:', error);
            }
        } else {
        }
    } else {
        // Hillshading entfernen
        if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
            try {
                map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('❌ Error removing hillshading layer:', error);
            }
        }
    }
}

function layerZindex() {
    // Prüfe ob beide Layer existieren
    const seamarksExists = map.getLayer('seamarks-layer');
    const waterbodyExists = map.getLayer('waterbody-layer');
    const pressureExists = map.getLayer('pressure-layer');
	const tempExists = map.getLayer('temp-layer');
	const windExists = map.getLayer('wind-layer');
	const windBarbsExists = map.getLayer('wind-barbs-layer');
	const precipitationExists = map.getLayer('precipitation-layer');
    const maritimeCurrentsExists = map.getLayer('maritime-currents-layer');
    const maritimeHeightsExists = map.getLayer('maritime-wave-heights-layer');
	const maritimeWindHeightsExists = map.getLayer('maritime-wind-wave-heights-layer');
	const maritimeWavePeriodsExists = map.getLayer('maritime-wave-periods-layer');
	const maritimeSstExists = map.getLayer('maritime-sst-layer');
	const maritimeSurgesExists = map.getLayer('maritime-surges-layer');
    const waterDepthExists = map.getLayer('water-depth-layer');
            
    if (maritimeCurrentsExists && maritimeHeightsExists && waterbodyExists) {
        try { 	
            map.removeLayer('maritime-wave-heights-layer');
            
            map.addLayer({
                id: 'maritime-wave-heights-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'maritime-wave-heights-layer-source',
                paint: {
                    'raster-opacity': 1.0
                }
            });   
			
            map.removeLayer('maritime-currents-layer');
            
            map.addLayer({
                id: 'maritime-currents-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'maritime-currents-layer-source',
                paint: {
                    'raster-opacity': 1.0
                }
            });  			
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Fehler beim Layer-Reordering:', error);
        }
    }

    if (maritimeCurrentsExists && maritimeWindHeightsExists && waterbodyExists) {
        try { 	
            map.removeLayer('maritime-wind-wave-heights-layer');
            
            map.addLayer({
                id: 'maritime-wind-wave-heights-layer',
                type: 'raster',
                source: 'maritime-wind-wave-heights-layer-source',
                paint: {

let lastRedrawCheck = 0;
let redrawCheckInterval = null;

function startContinuousRedrawCheck() {
    if (redrawCheckInterval) return;
    
    redrawCheckInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const now = Date.now();
        
        // Prüfe ob Neuzeichnung nötig ist
        if (needsRedraw && (now - lastRedrawCheck > 1000)) {
            if (!isMapMoving && shipCanvas) {
                drawShips();
                lastRedrawCheck = now;
            }
        }
        
    }, 1000);
}

function moveShipCanvasToMapLibre() {

}

function moveShipCanvasToMainMap() {
    if (!shipCanvas) return;
    
    const mainMapContainer = document.getElementById('map');
    if (!mainMapContainer) return;
    
    // Ship Canvas zurück zum Haupt-Map Container verschieben
    if (shipCanvas.parentElement !== mainMapContainer) {
        mainMapContainer.appendChild(shipCanvas);
        console.log('🚢 Ship Canvas moved BACK to main map container');
    }
    
    resizeShipCanvas();
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function saveLayerPreferences() {
    const preferences = {
        overlays: []
    };

    document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox:checked').forEach(function(checkbox) {
        const layerName = checkbox.id.replace('layer-', '');
        preferences.overlays.push(layerName);
    });

    localStorage.setItem('layerPreferences', JSON.stringify(preferences));
    console.log('💾 Saved layer preferences:', preferences.overlays);
}


function loadLayerPreferences() {
    // KORRIGIERT: Basemap Radio Button korrekt setzen
    const preferredBaseMap = localStorage.getItem('preferredBaseMap') || 'satellite';
    console.log('📂 Loading preferred basemap:', preferredBaseMap);
    
    // ALLE Radio Buttons zurücksetzen
    document.querySelectorAll('input[name="basemap"]').forEach(radio => {
        radio.checked = false;
    });
    
    // Korrekten Radio Button setzen basierend auf gespeicherter Preference
    let radioToCheck;
    switch(preferredBaseMap) {
        case 'dark':
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-streets');
            break;
        case 'light':
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-light');
            break;
        case 'satellite':
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-satellite');
            break;
        case 'nautical':
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-nautical');
            break;
        case 'nautical-garmin':
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-nautical-garmin');
            break;
        default:
            radioToCheck = document.getElementById('layer-streets');
    }
    
    if (radioToCheck) {
        radioToCheck.checked = true;
        console.log('✅ Radio Button gesetzt für:', preferredBaseMap);
    }

    // Overlay Preferences laden
    const preferences = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences') || '{}');
    if (preferences.overlays && preferences.overlays.length > 0) {
        console.log('📂 Loading layer preferences:', preferences.overlays);
        
        preferences.overlays.forEach(function(layerName) {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-' + layerName);
            if (checkbox) {
                checkbox.checked = true;
                
                // Terrain automatisch laden falls in Preferences
                if (layerName === 'terrain') {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        terrainController.enable();
                    }, 800);
                }
                // HILLSHADING automatisch laden falls in Preferences
                else if (layerName === 'hillshading') {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        hillshadingController.enable();
                    }, 1200);
                }
            }
        });

        // Normale Overlay-Layer laden
        setTimeout(() => {
            preferences.overlays.forEach(function(layerName) {
                if (layerName !== 'hillshading' && layerName !== 'terrain') {
                    const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
                    if (layerConfig && !map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                        try {
                            if (!map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                                map.addSource(layerConfig.id + '-source', layerConfig.source);
                            }
                            
                            const layerToAdd = {
                                id: layerConfig.id,
                                type: layerConfig.type,
                                source: layerConfig.id + '-source'
                            };
                            
                            if (layerConfig.paint) {
                                layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                            }
                            
                            map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                            console.log('📂 Loaded preference layer:', layerConfig.id);
                        } catch (error) {
                            console.error('❌ Error loading preference layer:', layerConfig.id, error);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 500);
    }
    
    // Hillshading Preferences separat laden
    hillshadingController.loadPreferences();
    
    // Terrain Preferences laden
    terrainController.loadPreferences();
}

setDefaultLayers();

function setDefaultLayers() {
    // Prüfe ob bereits Layer-Präferenzen existieren
    const hasPreferences = localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences');
    
    if (!hasPreferences) {
		
        // 1. Checkbox aktivieren	
		//const layerwaterbodyCheckbox = document.getElementById('layer-waterbody');
        //if (layerwaterbodyCheckbox) {
        //    layerwaterbodyCheckbox.checked = true;
        //}	
		
		//const maritimecurrentsCheckbox = document.getElementById('layer-maritime-currents');
        //if (maritimecurrentsCheckbox) {
        //    maritimecurrentsCheckbox.checked = true;
        //}	
		
		const seamarksCheckbox = document.getElementById('layer-seamarks');
        if (seamarksCheckbox) {
            seamarksCheckbox.checked = true;
        }
        
        // 2. Standard-Präferenzen speichern
        const defaultPreferences = {
            overlays: ['seamarks']
        };
        localStorage.setItem('layerPreferences', JSON.stringify(defaultPreferences));
    }
}

// EINFACHER FUNKTIONIERENDER Basemap Event Handler
document.querySelectorAll('input[name="basemap"]').forEach(function(input) {
   input.addEventListener('change', function() {
       if (this.checked) {
           console.log('🗺️ Switching to basemap:', this.value);

           const savedCheckboxes = [];
           document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox:checked').forEach(function(checkbox) {
               savedCheckboxes.push(checkbox.id);
           });
           
           // 1. ALLE OVERLAY-CHECKBOXEN DEAKTIVIEREN
           console.log('🔄 Unchecking all overlay checkboxes...');
           document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox').forEach(function(checkbox) {
               if (checkbox.checked) {			   
                   checkbox.checked = false;
                   const event = new Event('change');
                   checkbox.dispatchEvent(event);
               }
           });
		   
            savedCheckboxes.forEach(function(checkboxId) {
				setTimeout(() => {
                     const checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
					if (checkbox) {
						checkbox.checked = true;
						const event = new Event('change');
						checkbox.dispatchEvent(event);
						}
				},100);
            });

           // 2. STYLE DEFINIEREN
           let style;
           switch(this.value) {
               case 'dark':
                   style = {
                       version: 8,
                       sources: {
                           'dark-tiles': {
                               type: 'raster',
                               tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmowmvem022a01r76lwl43e1/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],
                               tileSize: 256
                           }
                       },
                       layers: [{
                           id: 'dark-layer',
                           type: 'raster',
                           source: 'dark-tiles'
                       }]
                   };
                   break;
               case 'light':
                   style = {
                       version: 8,

                               tileSize: 256
                           }

                           source: 'light-tiles'
                       }]
                   };
                   break;
               case 'satellite':
                   style = {

                       sources: {

                               type: 'raster',
                               tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/mapbox.php/styles/v1/mapbox-official/clmoxdj1401zh01r4exeud7zv/tiles/256/{z}/{x}/{y}?access_token=pk.eyJ1IjoiZXhhbXBsZXMiLCJhIjoiY203eXd1a3ZzMGV1ejJrcHRvdnVoYng0NCJ9.NzlqpAcLHejzezQqazzI-w'],

                           }
                       },
                       layers: [{
                           id: 'satellite-layer',

                       }]
                   };
                   break;
               case 'nautical':
                   style = {

                       sources: {

                               tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.com/api.php/TMS/1.0.0/TX97/{z}/{x}/{y}.png'],

                       layers: [{

                       }]
                   };
                   break;
    case 'nautical-garmin':
        style = {
            version: 8,
            sources: {
                'nautical-tiles-garmin': {
                    type: 'raster',
					minZoom: 2,
                    tiles: ['https://marinetraffic.live/garmin.php/api/tile/{z}/{x}/{y}.png?units=m&charttype=nav&safetydepth=10&seabedAreas=true'],

            layers: [{

        break;
               default:
                   style = {
                       version: 8,
                       sources: {
