           // 3. STYLE WECHSELN
           map.setStyle(style);

           // 4. EINFACHE WIEDERHERSTELLUNG NACH STYLE-LOAD
// 4. EINFACHE WIEDERHERSTELLUNG NACH STYLE-LOAD
map.once('style.load', function() {
    console.log('🗺️ Style loaded, basic setup only...');
    
    try {
		
if(document.getElementById('layer-light').checked)
map.addLayer({
	'id': 'light-layer',
	'type': 'raster',
	'source': 'light-tiles'
});

if(document.getElementById('layer-dark').checked)
map.addLayer({
	'id': 'dark-layer',
	'type': 'raster',
	'source': 'dark-tiles'
});
if(document.getElementById('layer-satellite').checked)
map.addLayer({
	'id': 'satellite-layer',
	'type': 'raster',
	'source': 'satellite-tiles'
});
if(document.getElementById('layer-nautical').checked)
map.addLayer({
	'id': 'nautical-layer',
	'type': 'raster',
	'source': 'nautical-tiles'
});
if(document.getElementById('layer-nautical-garmin').checked)
map.addLayer({
	'id': 'nautical-garmin-layer',
	'type': 'raster',
	'source': 'nautical-garmin-tiles'
});
				   
        // DEM Source hinzufügen (für mögliche spätere Nutzung)
        if (!isLowEndDevice && !map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
            try {
                map.addSource('mapbox-dem', {
                    'type': 'raster-dem',
                    'url': 'mapbox://mapbox.mapbox-terrain-dem-v1',
                    'tileSize': 512,
                    'maxzoom': 14
                });
                console.log('✅ DEM source added');
            } catch (demError) {
                console.log('ℹ️ DEM source setup skipped');
            }
        }
        
        // Fog
        try {
            map.setFog({
                'range': [-0.5, 9],
                'horizon-blend': 0.1,
                'color': '#262b2c',
                'high-color': '#000000',
                'space-color': '#000000',
                'star-intensity': 0.5
            });
        } catch (fogError) {
            console.warn('Fog setup failed:', fogError.message);
        }

        console.log('✅ Basemap loaded - all overlays cleared');
        
        // WICHTIG: Warte kurz bevor Layer Preferences wiederhergestellt werden
        setTimeout(() => {
            // Layer Preferences wiederherstellen
            const preferences = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences') || '{}');
            
            if (preferences.overlays && preferences.overlays.length > 0) {
                console.log('📂 Restoring overlay layers after basemap change...');
                
                preferences.overlays.forEach(function(layerName) {
                    // Terrain
                    if (layerName === 'terrain' && typeof terrainController !== 'undefined') {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            terrainController.enable();
                        }, 100);
                    }
                    else if (layerName === 'hillshading' && typeof hillshadingController !== 'undefined') {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            hillshadingController.enable();
                        }, 300);
                    }
                    // Normale Overlay Layer
                    else {
                        const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
                        if (layerConfig && !map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                try {
                                    // Source hinzufügen falls nicht vorhanden
                                    if (!map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                                        map.addSource(layerConfig.id + '-source', layerConfig.source);
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Layer hinzufügen
                                    const layerToAdd = {
                                        id: layerConfig.id,
                                        type: layerConfig.type,
                                        source: layerConfig.id + '-source'
                                    };
                                    
                                    if (layerConfig.paint) {
                                        layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                                    }
                                    
                                    map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                                    console.log('📂 Restored overlay layer:', layerConfig.id);
                                    
                                } catch (error) {
                                    console.error('❌ Error restoring overlay layer:', layerConfig.id, error);
                                }
                            }, 100);
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // Canvas Updates
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (shipCanvas) {
                    resizeShipCanvas();
                    needsRedraw = true;
                }
            }, 500);
            
        }, 300); // Warte 300ms nach Style load

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Error in style.load handler:', error);
    }
});

           // Base map preference speichern
           localStorage.setItem('preferredBaseMap', this.value);
           
           // WICHTIG: Layer Preferences auch leeren da alle Overlays deaktiviert wurden
           const emptyPreferences = { overlays: [] };
           localStorage.setItem('layerPreferences', JSON.stringify(emptyPreferences));
           
           console.log('💾 Saved basemap preference and cleared layer preferences');
       }
   });
});

// HILFSFUNKTION: Alle Controller-States zurücksetzen
function resetAllControllerStates() {
    // Hillshading Controller zurücksetzen
    if (typeof hillshadingController !== 'undefined' && hillshadingController.isActive) {
        hillshadingController.disable();
    }
    
    // Terrain Controller zurücksetzen
    if (typeof terrainController !== 'undefined' && terrainController.isActive) {
        terrainController.disable();
    }
    
    console.log('🔄 All controller states reset');
}

// ERWEITERTE Checkbox Handler (unverändert)
function handleLayerCheckboxChange() {
    const layerName = this.id.replace('layer-', '');
    
    console.log('🎛️ Checkbox changed:', layerName, '=', this.checked);
    
    // SPEZIELLE BEHANDLUNG für Terrain
    if (layerName === 'terrain') {
        terrainController.toggle(this.checked);
        saveLayerPreferences();
        return;
    }
    
    // SPEZIELLE BEHANDLUNG für Hillshading
    if (layerName === 'hillshading') {
        handleHillshadingCheckbox(this);
        return;
    }

    // NORMALE Layer Behandlung
    const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
    if (!layerConfig) {
        console.warn('Layer configuration not found:', layerName);
        return;
    }

    if (this.checked) {
        // Layer hinzufügen
        if (!map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
            try {
                if (!map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                    map.addSource(layerConfig.id + '-source', layerConfig.source);
                }
                
                const layerToAdd = {
                    id: layerConfig.id,
                    type: layerConfig.type,
                    source: layerConfig.id + '-source'
                };
                
                if (layerConfig.paint) {
                    layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                }
                
                map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                console.log('✅ Layer hinzugefügt:', layerConfig.id);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('❌ Fehler beim Hinzufügen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
            }
        }
    } else {
        // Layer entfernen
        if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
            try {
                map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
                
                if (map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                    map.removeSource(layerConfig.id + '-source');
                }
                
                console.log('✅ Layer entfernt:', layerConfig.id);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('❌ Fehler beim Entfernen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
            }
        }
    }

    saveLayerPreferences();
}

// Event Listeners für Checkboxen
document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox').forEach(function(checkbox) {
    checkbox.removeEventListener('change', handleLayerCheckboxChange);
    checkbox.addEventListener('change', handleLayerCheckboxChange);
});

// KORRIGIERTE FUNKTION: Layer in richtiger Reihenfolge wiederherstellen
function restoreAllLayersInCorrectOrder(activeStates) {
    console.log('🔄 Starting layer restoration in correct order...');
    console.log('🔄 Active states to restore:', activeStates);
    
    let delay = 0;
    const STEP_DELAY = 10; // Etwas mehr Zeit zwischen jedem Schritt
    
    // REIHENFOLGE: Von unten nach oben (wie Layer übereinander liegen sollen)
    
    // 1. HILLSHADING (ganz unten, über Basemap)
    if (activeStates.hillshading) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            console.log('🏔️ Step 1: Restoring Hillshading...');
            hillshadingController.enable();
            
            // Checkbox auch setzen
            const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-hillshading');
            if (checkbox) {
                checkbox.checked = true;
            }
        }, delay);
        delay += STEP_DELAY;
    }
    
    // 2. TERRAIN (über Hillshading, modifiziert die Geometrie)
    if (activeStates.terrain) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            console.log('🏔️ Step 2: Restoring Terrain...');
            terrainController.enable();
            
            // Checkbox auch setzen
            const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-terrain');
            if (checkbox) {
                checkbox.checked = true;
            }
        }, delay);
        delay += STEP_DELAY;
    }
    
    // 3. NORMALE OVERLAY-LAYER (in korrekter Reihenfolge)
    const overlayOrder = ['waterbody','density','maritime-currents','waterlevel','seamarks'];

    overlayOrder.forEach(layerName => {
        if (activeStates.overlays.includes(layerName)) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                console.log(`🌊 Step ${3 + overlayOrder.indexOf(layerName)}: Restoring ${layerName}...`);
                restoreOverlayLayer(layerName);
            }, delay);
            delay += STEP_DELAY;
        }
    });
    
    console.log(`✅ All restoration steps scheduled (${delay}ms total)`);
}

// VERBESSERTE FUNKTION: Einzelnen Overlay-Layer korrekt wiederherstellen
function restoreOverlayLayer(layerName) {
    const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
    if (!layerConfig || !layerConfig.source) {
        console.error('❌ Layer config not found:', layerName);
        return;
    }
    
    try {
        const sourceId = layerConfig.id + '-source';
        
        // CLEANUP: Entferne Layer/Source falls bereits vorhanden
        if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
            try {
                map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
                console.log('🧹 Removed existing layer:', layerConfig.id);
            } catch (e) {
                console.log('ℹ️ Layer removal not needed:', layerConfig.id);
            }
        }
        
        if (map.getSource(sourceId)) {
            try {
                map.removeSource(sourceId);
                console.log('🧹 Removed existing source:', sourceId);
            } catch (e) {
                console.log('ℹ️ Source removal not needed:', sourceId);
            }
        }
        
        // WARTEN: Kurz warten bevor wir neu hinzufügen
        setTimeout(() => {
            try {
                // HINZUFÜGEN: Frisch hinzufügen
                map.addSource(sourceId, layerConfig.source);
                console.log('✅ Source added:', sourceId);
                
                const layerToAdd = {
                    id: layerConfig.id,
                    type: layerConfig.type,
                    source: sourceId
                };
                
                if (layerConfig.paint) {
                    layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                }
                
                // KRITISCH: Layer OHNE beforeId hinzufügen (damit er oben ist)
                map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                console.log('✅ Layer restored on top:', layerConfig.id);
                
                // Checkbox sicherstellen
                const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-' + layerName);
                if (checkbox) {
                    checkbox.checked = true;
                }
                
            } catch (addError) {
                console.error('❌ Error adding layer after cleanup:', layerName, addError);
            }
        }, 500); // 100ms Pause nach dem Cleanup
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Error restoring overlay layer:', layerName, error);
    }
}

// NEUE FUNKTION: Alle Layer komplett neu laden
function restoreAllLayers(activeStates) {
    console.log('🔄 Starting complete layer restoration...');
    
    // TERRAIN WIEDERHERSTELLEN (falls aktiv war)
    if (activeStates.terrain && !isLowEndDevice && map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
        try {
            map.setTerrain({
                'source': 'mapbox-dem',
                'exaggeration': 1.5
            });
            console.log('✅ Terrain restored');
        } catch (terrainError) {
            console.error('❌ Terrain restoration failed:', terrainError);
        }
    }
    
    let layerDelay = 0;
    const DELAY_STEP = 150;
    
    // 1. HILLSHADING WIEDERHERSTELLEN
    if (activeStates.hillshading) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            console.log('🏔️ Restoring Hillshading...');
            hillshadingController.enable();
        }, layerDelay);
        layerDelay += DELAY_STEP;
    }
    
    // 2. NORMALE OVERLAY-LAYER WIEDERHERSTELLEN
    activeStates.overlays.forEach((layerName, index) => {
        setTimeout(() => {
            console.log('🔄 Restoring overlay layer:', layerName);
            
            const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
            if (layerConfig && layerConfig.source) {
                try {
                    const sourceId = layerConfig.id + '-source';
                    
                    // Source entfernen falls vorhanden (für saubere Neuladung)
                    if (map.getSource(sourceId)) {
                        try {
                            map.removeSource(sourceId);
                        } catch (e) {
                            // Ignorieren falls Source nicht entfernt werden kann
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Layer entfernen falls vorhanden
                    if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                        try {
                            map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
                        } catch (e) {
                            // Ignorieren falls Layer nicht entfernt werden kann
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // NEU HINZUFÜGEN
                    map.addSource(sourceId, layerConfig.source);
                    
                    const layerToAdd = {
                        id: layerConfig.id,
                        type: layerConfig.type,
                        source: sourceId
                    };
                    
                    if (layerConfig.paint) {
                        layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                    }
                    
                    map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                    console.log('✅ Overlay layer restored:', layerConfig.id);
                    
                    // Checkbox sicherstellen
                    const checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-' + layerName);
                    if (checkbox) {
                        checkbox.checked = true;
                    }
                    
                } catch (layerError) {
                    console.error('❌ Error restoring overlay layer:', layerName, layerError);
                }
            }
        }, layerDelay);
        layerDelay += DELAY_STEP;
    });
    
    console.log(`🔄 All layer restoration scheduled (${layerDelay}ms total)`);
}

function ensureTerrainSetup() {
    if (isLowEndDevice) {
        console.log('⚡ Low-end device - skipping terrain');
        return;
    }
    
    // FIXED: Nur DEM Source hinzufügen, NICHT automatisch Terrain aktivieren
    if (!map.getSource('mapbox-dem')) {
        try {
            map.addSource('mapbox-dem', {
                'type': 'raster-dem',
                'url': 'mapbox://mapbox.mapbox-terrain-dem-v1',
                'tileSize': 512,
                'maxzoom': 14
            });
            console.log('✅ DEM source ensured (terrain not auto-activated)');
        } catch (error) {
            console.warn('DEM source setup failed:', error.message);
        }
    }
    
    // REMOVED: Automatische Terrain-Aktivierung
    // Terrain wird nur aktiviert wenn explizit über Checkbox/Controller gewünscht
}

document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox').forEach(function(checkbox) {
    checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
        const layerName = this.id.replace('layer-', '');
        
        // SPEZIELLE BEHANDLUNG für Hillshading
        if (layerName === 'hillshading') {
            handleHillshadingCheckbox(this);
            return;
        }

        // NORMALE Layer Behandlung
        const layerConfig = overlayLayersConfig[layerName];
        if (!layerConfig) {
            console.warn('Layer configuration not found:', layerName);
            return;
        }

        if (this.checked) {
            // Layer hinzufügen
            if (!map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                try {
                    // Erst Source hinzufügen falls nicht vorhanden
                    if (!map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                        map.addSource(layerConfig.id + '-source', layerConfig.source);
                    }
                    
                    // Dann Layer hinzufügen
                    const layerToAdd = {
                        id: layerConfig.id,
                        type: layerConfig.type,
                        source: layerConfig.id + '-source'
                    };
                    
                    // Paint Properties hinzufügen falls vorhanden
                    if (layerConfig.paint) {
                        layerToAdd.paint = layerConfig.paint;
                    }
                    
                    map.addLayer(layerToAdd);
                    console.log('✅ Layer hinzugefügt:', layerConfig.id);
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Fehler beim Hinzufügen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
                }
            }
        } else {
            // Layer entfernen
            if (map.getLayer(layerConfig.id)) {
                try {
                    map.removeLayer(layerConfig.id);
                    
                    // Source auch entfernen falls keine anderen Layer sie verwenden
                    if (map.getSource(layerConfig.id + '-source')) {
                        map.removeSource(layerConfig.id + '-source');
                    }
                    
                    console.log('✅ Layer entfernt:', layerConfig.id);
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Fehler beim Entfernen des Layers:', layerConfig.id, error);
                }
            }
        }

        saveLayerPreferences();
    });
});

function toggleLayerMenu() {
    const menu = document.getElementById('layerControlMenu');
    const button = document.getElementById('layerControlButton');
    
    if (menu && button) {
        const isActive = menu.classList.toggle('active');
        
        // NUR diesen Button stylen
        if (isActive) {
            button.classList.add('layerButton-active');
        } else {
            button.classList.remove('layerButton-active');
        }
        
        console.log('🗺️ Layer Menu', isActive ? 'geöffnet' : 'geschlossen');
    }
}

// 2. SCHRITT: updateHoverDisplay Funktion erweitern
function updateHoverDisplay(ship) {
    const currentShipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (!currentShipInfo || !ship) {
        return;
    }
    
    const shipName = ship.name || 'N/A Ship';
    const shipSpeed = (ship.speed !== undefined && ship.speed !== null) ? parseFloat(ship.speed).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
    const shipCourse = (ship.course !== undefined && ship.course !== null) ? parseInt(ship.course) : 0;
    const shipType = getShipTypeName(ship.type) || 'N/A';
    const destination = formatDestination(ship.destination) || 'Unbekannt';
    
    // DIREKT elapsed verwenden - OHNE KOMPLIZIERTE LOGIK
    signalAge = 'LIVE';
    if (ship.elapsed !== undefined && ship.elapsed !== null && ship.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
        const minutes = parseInt(ship.elapsed);
        if (!isNaN(minutes)) {
            if (minutes <= 2.1) {
                signalAge = 'LIVE';
            } else if (minutes < 60) {
                signalAge = 'vor ' + minutes + ' min';
            } else {
                const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
                signalAge = 'vor ' + hours + 'h';
            }
        }
    }
    
    currentShipInfo.innerHTML = 
        '<strong>' + shipName + '</strong><br>' +
        'Tempo: ' + shipSpeed + ' kn<br>' +
        'Kurs: ' + shipCourse + '°<br>' +
        'Typ: ' + shipType + '<br>' +
        'Ziel: ' + destination + '<br>' +
        'Signal: ' + signalAge + '';
}

function formatSignalAge(elapsedMinutes) {
    
    // Handle various input types
    if (!elapsedMinutes || elapsedMinutes === 'N/A' || elapsedMinutes === '' || 
        elapsedMinutes === null || elapsedMinutes === undefined || elapsedMinutes === 'Lade...') {
        return 'N/A';
    }
    
    // Convert to number if it's a string
    let minutes;
    if (typeof elapsedMinutes === 'string') {
        minutes = parseFloat(elapsedMinutes);
    } else {
        minutes = parseFloat(elapsedMinutes);
    }
    
    if (isNaN(minutes)) {
        return 'N/A';
    }
        
    if (minutes <= 2.1) {
        return 'LIVE';
    } else if (minutes < 60) {
        return 'vor ' + Math.round(minutes) + ' min';
    } else if (minutes < 1440) { // weniger als 24 Stunden
        const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
        const remainingMinutes = Math.round(minutes % 60);
        if (remainingMinutes === 0) {
            return 'vor ' + hours + 'h';
        } else {
            return 'vor ' + hours + 'h ' + remainingMinutes + 'min';
        }
    } else {
        const days = Math.floor(minutes / 1440);
        const remainingHours = Math.floor((minutes % 1440) / 60);
        if (remainingHours === 0) {
            return 'vor ' + days + ' Tag' + (days > 1 ? 'en' : '');
        } else {
            return 'vor ' + days + ' Tag' + (days > 1 ? 'en' : '') + ' ' + remainingHours + 'h';
        }
    }
}

// 3. SCHRITT: Mousemove Event Handler erweitern
map.on('mousemove', function(e) {
    const now = performance.now();
    const timeSinceLastMove = now - lastMoveTime;
    
    // Deaktiviere Hover bei schneller Bewegung
    if (isMapMoving && timeSinceLastMove < FAST_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD) {
        return;
    }
    
    lastMoveTime = now;
    
    // Rest der Hover-Logik (unverändert)
    if (isMapMoving || isZoomTransition) {
        return;
    }

    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    let REDRAW_THROTTLE = currentZoom <= 3 ? 250 : 150;

    const point = e.point;
    const shipAtPosition = getShipAtPosition(point.x, point.y);

    let newHoveredShipKey = null;
    if (shipAtPosition) {
        newHoveredShipKey = shipAtPosition.mmsi || shipAtPosition.shipId ||
            `${shipAtPosition.name}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lng*1000)}`;
    }

    if (newHoveredShipKey !== lastHoveredShipKey) {
        const previousHoveredShip = hoveredShip;
        hoveredShip = shipAtPosition;
        lastHoveredShipKey = newHoveredShipKey;

        const now = performance.now();
        if (now - lastRedrawTime > REDRAW_THROTTLE) {
            if (hoveredShip !== previousHoveredShip) {
                needsRedraw = true;
                lastRedrawTime = now;
            }
        }

        if (hoveredShip) {
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
        } else {
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';
        }
    }

    const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (shipInfo && hoveredShip && window.innerWidth >= 1200) {
        try {
            // KRITISCH: Aktuellste Schiffsdaten aus masterShipList holen
            const shipKey = hoveredShip.mmsi || hoveredShip.shipId ||
                `${hoveredShip.name}_${Math.round(hoveredShip.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(hoveredShip.lng*1000)}`;
            
            // Hole aktuellste Daten aus masterShipList
            const currentShipData = masterShipList.get(shipKey);
            
            // Verwende aktuellste Daten falls verfügbar, sonst hoveredShip
            const shipDataToShow = currentShipData || hoveredShip;
            
            // Anzeige aktualisieren
            updateHoverDisplay(shipDataToShow);
            
            // Tooltip positionieren
            shipInfo.style.display = 'block';
            shipInfo.style.left = (e.originalEvent.clientX + 10) + 'px';
            shipInfo.style.top = (e.originalEvent.clientY - 10) + 'px';
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error in mousemove hover handling:', error);
            if (shipInfo) {
                shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    } else if (shipInfo) {
        shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
    }
});

let autoRefreshPausedForMovement = false;

function pauseAutoRefreshForMovement() {
    if (!autoRefreshPausedForMovement && autoRefreshEnabled) {
        autoRefreshPausedForMovement = true;
        console.log('⏸️ Auto-Refresh pausiert für Movement');
    }
}

function resumeAutoRefreshAfterMovement() {
    if (autoRefreshPausedForMovement) {
        autoRefreshPausedForMovement = false;
        console.log('▶️ Auto-Refresh wiederaufgenommen nach Movement');
    }
}

// 4. SCHRITT: Verbesserte loadElapsedForShip Funktion (bereits vorhanden, aber optimiert)
async function loadElapsedForShip(ship) {
    // Input validation
    if (!ship || typeof ship !== 'object') {
        console.log('Invalid ship object for elapsed loading');
        return 'N/A';
    }
    
    if (!ship.mmsi && !ship.shipId) {
        console.log('Cannot load elapsed - no MMSI or shipId for:', ship.name || 'unknown ship');
        return 'N/A';
    }
    
    try {
        let shipId = ship.shipId;
        
        // Get shipId from MMSI if needed
        if (!shipId && ship.mmsi) {
            try {
                shipId = await getShipIdFromMMSI(ship.mmsi);
            } catch (error) {
                console.log('Failed to get shipId from MMSI:', error);
                return 'N/A';
            }
        }
        
        if (!shipId) {
            console.log('Cannot get shipId for elapsed loading:', ship.name || 'unknown ship');
            return 'N/A';
        }
        
        const originalUrl = `https://marinetraffic.com/de/ais/get_info_window_json?asset_type=ship&id=${shipId}`;
        const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
        const detailUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
        
        const response = await fetch(detailUrl, {
			headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
            }
        });
        
        if (!response.ok) {
            console.log('Failed to load ship details for elapsed:', response.status, response.statusText);
            return 'N/A';
        }
        
        // JSON parsing mit Validierung
        const responseText = await response.text();
        
        if (!responseText || responseText.trim() === '' || 
            responseText.trim().startsWith('<') || responseText.includes('<!DOCTYPE')) {
            console.log('Invalid response from ship details API');
            return 'N/A';
        }
        
        let apiData;
        try {
            apiData = JSON.parse(responseText);
        } catch (jsonError) {
            console.log('Invalid JSON response from ship details API:', jsonError.message);
            return 'N/A';
        }
        
        // API Response validieren
        if (!apiData || typeof apiData !== 'object' || !apiData.values) {
            console.log('No valid values in ship details response');
            return 'N/A';
        }
        
        const values = apiData.values;
        
        // Elapsed von Timestamp berechnen
        let calculatedElapsed = 'N/A';
        
        if (values.elapsed && values.elapsed !== 'N/A' && values.elapsed !== null) {
            const elapsedTimestamp = parseInt(values.elapsed);
            if (!isNaN(elapsedTimestamp) && elapsedTimestamp > 0) {
                const currentTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                const elapsedMinutes = Math.floor((currentTime - elapsedTimestamp) / 60);
                
                // Sanity check
                if (elapsedMinutes >= 0 && elapsedMinutes < 525600) { // Max 1 Jahr
                    calculatedElapsed = elapsedMinutes;
                    console.log('Calculated elapsed for', ship.name || 'unknown ship', ':', elapsedMinutes, 'minutes');
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Fallback zu last_pos
        if (calculatedElapsed === 'N/A' && values.last_pos && values.last_pos !== 'N/A' && values.last_pos !== null) {
            const lastPosTimestamp = parseInt(values.last_pos);
            if (!isNaN(lastPosTimestamp) && lastPosTimestamp > 0) {
                const currentTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                const elapsedMinutes = Math.floor((currentTime - lastPosTimestamp) / 60);
                
                // Sanity check
                if (elapsedMinutes >= 0 && elapsedMinutes < 525600) {
                    calculatedElapsed = elapsedMinutes;
                    console.log('Using last_pos for elapsed calculation:', ship.name || 'unknown ship', ':', elapsedMinutes, 'minutes');
                }
            }
        }
        
        return calculatedElapsed;
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading elapsed for ship:', ship.name || 'unknown ship', error.message);
        return 'N/A';
    }
}

let SIGNAL_UPDATE_ENABLED = true; // Ändern von false auf true

// 2. SCHRITT: updateHoverDisplay Funktion erweitern
function updateHoverDisplay(ship) {
    if (!ship || typeof ship !== 'object') {
        console.log('updateHoverDisplay: Invalid ship object');
        return;
    }
    
    const currentShipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (!currentShipInfo || currentShipInfo.style.display === 'none') {
        return;
    }
    
    // Prüfe ob das noch das gleiche gehöverte Schiff ist
    if (!hoveredShip || 
        (ship.mmsi && hoveredShip.mmsi !== ship.mmsi) ||
        (ship.shipId && hoveredShip.shipId !== ship.shipId) ||
        (!ship.mmsi && !ship.shipId && hoveredShip.name !== ship.name)) {
        return;
    }
    
    // Basis-Infos ohne API-Call
    var shipName = ship.name || 'N/A Ship';
    const shipSpeed = (ship.speed !== undefined && ship.speed !== null) ? parseFloat(ship.speed).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
    const shipCourse = (ship.course !== undefined && ship.course !== null) ? parseInt(ship.course) : 0;
    const shipType = getShipTypeName(ship.type) || 'N/A';
    const destination = formatDestination(ship.destination) || 'Unbekannt';
    
    // REAKTIVIERT: Elapsed Signal von API holen
    signalAge = 'Lade...'; // Standard während Laden
    
    // Prüfe ob elapsed bereits verfügbar ist
    if (ship.elapsed && ship.elapsed !== 'N/A' && ship.elapsed !== undefined) {
        signalAge = formatSignalAge(ship.elapsed);
    }
    
    try {
        currentShipInfo.innerHTML = 
            '<strong>' + shipName + '</strong><br>' +
            'Tempo: ' + shipSpeed + ' kn<br>' +
            'Kurs: ' + shipCourse + '°<br>' +
            'Typ: ' + shipType + '<br>' +
            'Ziel: ' + destination + '<br>' +
            'Signal: ' + signalAge + '';
            
        console.log('Updated hover display for', shipName, 'with elapsed:', ship.elapsed);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error updating hover display:', error);
    }
}

// 3. SCHRITT: Mousemove Event Handler erweitern
map.on('mousemove', function(e) {
    if (isMapMoving || isZoomTransition) {
        return;
    }

    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    let REDRAW_THROTTLE = currentZoom <= 3 ? 250 : 150;

    const point = e.point;
    const shipAtPosition = getShipAtPosition(point.x, point.y);

    let newHoveredShipKey = null;
    if (shipAtPosition) {
        newHoveredShipKey = shipAtPosition.mmsi || shipAtPosition.shipId ||
            `${shipAtPosition.name}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lng*1000)}`;
    }

    if (newHoveredShipKey !== lastHoveredShipKey) {
        const previousHoveredShip = hoveredShip;
        hoveredShip = shipAtPosition;
        lastHoveredShipKey = newHoveredShipKey;

        const now = performance.now();
        if (now - lastRedrawTime > REDRAW_THROTTLE) {
            if (hoveredShip !== previousHoveredShip) {
                needsRedraw = true;
                lastRedrawTime = now;
            }
        }

        if (hoveredShip) {
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
        } else {
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';
        }
    }

    // HOVER INFO ANZEIGEN - OHNE KOMPLIZIERTE CHECKS
    const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (shipInfo && hoveredShip && window.innerWidth >= 1200) {
        // EINFACH: Verwende hoveredShip direkt
        var shipName = hoveredShip.name || 'N/A Ship';
        const shipSpeed = (hoveredShip.speed !== undefined && hoveredShip.speed !== null) ? parseFloat(hoveredShip.speed).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
        const shipCourse = (hoveredShip.course !== undefined && hoveredShip.course !== null) ? parseInt(hoveredShip.course) : 0;
        const shipType = getShipTypeName(hoveredShip.type) || 'N/A';
        const destination = formatDestination(hoveredShip.destination) || 'Unbekannt';
        
        // DIREKT: elapsed verwenden
			signalAge = 'LIVE';
        if (hoveredShip.elapsed !== undefined && hoveredShip.elapsed !== null && hoveredShip.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
            signalAge = formatSignalAge(hoveredShip.elapsed);
        }

		if(signalAge == 'N/A')
			signalAge = 'LIVE';
        
        shipInfo.innerHTML = 
            '<strong>' + shipName + '</strong><br>' +
            'Tempo: ' + shipSpeed + ' kn<br>' +
            'Kurs: ' + shipCourse + '°<br>' +
            'Typ: ' + shipType + '<br>' +
            'Ziel: ' + destination + '<br>' +
            'Signal: ' + signalAge + '';
        
        shipInfo.style.display = 'block';
        shipInfo.style.left = (e.originalEvent.clientX + 10) + 'px';
        shipInfo.style.top = (e.originalEvent.clientY - 10) + 'px';
        
    } else if (shipInfo) {
        shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
    }
});

// Close menu when clicking outside
document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
    const filterMenu = document.getElementById('filterControlMenu');
    const filterButton = document.getElementById('filterButton');
    
    // Nur Filter Menu behandeln
    if (filterMenu && filterButton && !filterMenu.contains(event.target) && !filterButton.contains(event.target)) {
        filterMenu.classList.remove('active');
        filterButton.classList.remove('filterButton-active');
    }
});

// Event handlers mit korrekter Synchronisation
map.on('click', function(e) {
	
        if (typeof isDistanceMeasureActive !== 'undefined' && isDistanceMeasureActive) {
            return
        }

        if (typeof isRoutingMode !== 'undefined' && isRoutingMode) {
            return;
        }
		
    const point = e.point;
    
    // ZUERST: Prüfe ob ein Port geklickt wurde
    const clickedPort = getPortAtPosition(point.x, point.y);
    
    if (clickedPort) {
        console.log('⚓ Port clicked:', clickedPort.portName, 'ID:', clickedPort.portId);
        
        // Setze selected Port für gelben Kreis
        selectedPort = clickedPort;
        needsRedraw = true; // Trigger redraw für Selection
        
        // Port-Objekt erstellen
        const portFromMap = {
            name: clickedPort.portName,
            id: clickedPort.portId,
            lat: clickedPort.lat,
            lng: clickedPort.lng,
            type: 'Port'
        };
        
        // Port Details anzeigen mit FlyTo
        showPortDetails(portFromMap, true);
        
        // Verhindere dass auch ein Schiff ausgewählt wird
        return;
    }
    
    const clickedMarina = getMarinaAtPosition(point.x, point.y);
    
    if (clickedMarina) {
        console.log('⚓ Marina clicked:', clickedMarina.marinaName, 'ID:', clickedMarina.marinaId);
        
        selectedMarina = clickedMarina;
        selectedPort = null; // Clear port selection
        needsRedraw = true;
        
        // Marina-Objekt für Details erstellen
        const marinaFromMap = {
            name: clickedMarina.marinaName,
            id: clickedMarina.marinaId,
            lat: clickedMarina.lat,
            lng: clickedMarina.lng,
            type: 'Marina'
        };
        
        // Port Details Window für Marina nutzen (oder eigenes erstellen)
        showPortDetails(marinaFromMap, true);
        
        return;
    }
    
    // Wenn kein Port geklickt wurde, clear selection
    if (selectedPort) {
        selectedPort = null;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }

    if (selectedMarina) {
        selectedMarina = null;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
	
    clickedShip = getShipAtPosition(point.x, point.y);


    if (clickedShip) {
        LngLat.push(clickedShip);
        localStorage.setItem('mmsi', clickedShip.mmsi);
        // FIX: Setze auch searchSelectedShip für Marker-Update
        searchSelectedShip = {
            mmsi: clickedShip.mmsi,
            shipId: clickedShip.shipId,
            name: clickedShip.name,
            lat: clickedShip.lat,
            lng: clickedShip.lng,
            speed: clickedShip.speed || 0,
            course: clickedShip.course || 0,
            heading: clickedShip.heading || clickedShip.course || 0,
            destination: clickedShip.destination || 'N/A',
            type: clickedShip.type || 'N/A'
        };
        
        // FIX: Setze searchSelectedPosition für Marker-Anzeige
        searchSelectedPosition = {
            lat: clickedShip.lat,
            lng: clickedShip.lng
        };
        
        // KRITISCH: fromURL = false für Map-Klicks (KEIN FlyTo)
        showShipDetails(clickedShip, false); // FALSE = kein FlyTo
        
        hideShipTrack();
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
    
    const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');
    if (resultsContainer) {
        resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
    }
});

// FIXED: Hover überall aktiviert mit konservativem Throttling
let lastHoveredShipKey = null;
let hoverStabilityTimer = null;
let lastRedrawTime = 0;
let debugHoverCount = 0;
let elapsedLoadingPromises = new Map();

map.on('mousemove', function(e) {
    // ZUERST: Port-Hover prüfen bei entsprechendem Zoom
    if (map.getZoom() > 8) {
        const point = e.point;
        const portAtPosition = getPortAtPosition(point.x, point.y);
        
        if (portAtPosition) {
            // Neuer Hover-Port
            if (!hoveredPort || hoveredPort.portId !== portAtPosition.portId) {
                hoveredPort = portAtPosition;
                needsRedraw = true; // Trigger redraw für Hover-Effekt
            }
            
            // Zeigefinger-Cursor
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
     
            return; // Verhindere Schiff-Hover wenn über Port
        } else if (hoveredPort) {
            // Port-Hover verlassen
            hoveredPort = null;
            needsRedraw = true; // Trigger redraw um Hover zu entfernen
            
            const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
            if (shipInfo) {
                shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
		
const marinaAtPosition = getMarinaAtPosition(point.x, point.y);

if (marinaAtPosition) {
    if (!hoveredMarina || hoveredMarina.marinaId !== marinaAtPosition.marinaId) {
        hoveredMarina = marinaAtPosition;
        hoveredPort = null; // Clear port hover
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
    
    map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
    return;
} else if (hoveredMarina) {
    hoveredMarina = null;
    needsRedraw = true;
}
    }

   // FIXED: Kein mousemove handling während Movement um Flackern zu vermeiden
   if (isMapMoving) {
       return;
   }

   const currentZoom = map.getZoom();

   // FIXED: Hover nur während Zoom-Übergang deaktiviert, sonst überall aktiv
   if (isZoomTransition) {
       return;
   }

   // OPTIMIERT: Größeres Throttling für weniger FPS-Drops
   let REDRAW_THROTTLE = 150; // Größer als vorher (war 50ms)
   if (currentZoom <= 3) {
       REDRAW_THROTTLE = 250; // Noch größer bei niedrigem Zoom
   }

   const point = e.point;
   const shipAtPosition = getShipAtPosition(point.x, point.y);

   let newHoveredShipKey = null;
   if (shipAtPosition) {
       newHoveredShipKey = shipAtPosition.mmsi || shipAtPosition.shipId ||
           `${shipAtPosition.name}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lng*1000)}`;
   }

   if (newHoveredShipKey !== lastHoveredShipKey) {
       if (hoverStabilityTimer) {
           clearTimeout(hoverStabilityTimer);
           hoverStabilityTimer = null;
       }

       const previousHoveredShip = hoveredShip;
       hoveredShip = shipAtPosition;
       lastHoveredShipKey = newHoveredShipKey;

       // OPTIMIERT: Weniger aggressives Throttling
       const now = performance.now();
       if (now - lastRedrawTime > REDRAW_THROTTLE) {
           if (hoveredShip !== previousHoveredShip) {
               needsRedraw = true;
               lastRedrawTime = now;
           }
       }

       if (hoveredShip) {
           map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';

           hoverStabilityTimer = setTimeout(() => {
               const currentShip = findShipByKey(newHoveredShipKey);
               if (!currentShip && hoveredShip) {
                   hoveredShip = null;
                   lastHoveredShipKey = null;
                   needsRedraw = true;
               }
           }, 300);
       } else {
           map.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';
       }
   }

   const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
   if (shipInfo && hoveredShip && window.innerWidth >= 9999999) {
       try {
		   
           if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
		   
           // FIXED: Prüfe ob elapsed geladen werden muss
           if (hoveredShip && (hoveredShip.elapsed === 'N/A' || hoveredShip.elapsed === undefined)) {
               const shipKey = hoveredShip.mmsi || hoveredShip.shipId || hoveredShip.name;
               if (hoveredShip.name == "[SAT-AIS]" && searchSelectedShip)
			   hoveredShip.name = searchSelectedShip.name;
		   
               // Zeige sofort "wird geladen..." - aber nur wenn Schiff noch gültig ist
               if (hoveredShip && hoveredShip.name) {
                   updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip, true);
               }
               
               // Verhindere mehrfache Requests für das gleiche Schiff
               if (shipKey && !elapsedLoadingPromises.has(shipKey)) {
                   console.log('Loading elapsed on-demand for hovered ship:', hoveredShip.name);
                   
                   const loadingPromise = loadElapsedForShip(hoveredShip)
                       .then(elapsed => {
                           // Prüfe ob Schiff noch gehövert wird
                           if (!hoveredShip || !hoveredShip.name) {
                               return;
                           }
                           
                           console.log('Elapsed loaded for', hoveredShip.name, ':', elapsed);
                           
                           // Aktualisiere das Schiff überall
                           hoveredShip.elapsed = elapsed;
                           
                           // Aktualisiere auch in ships array
                           const shipInArray = ships.find(s => 
                               s.mmsi === hoveredShip.mmsi || 
                               s.shipId === hoveredShip.shipId ||
                               s.name === hoveredShip.name
                           );
                           if (shipInArray) {
                               shipInArray.elapsed = elapsed;
                               console.log('Updated ships array elapsed for', shipInArray.name);
                           }
                           
                           // Aktualisiere in masterShipList
                           const masterKey = hoveredShip.mmsi || hoveredShip.shipId || 
                               `${hoveredShip.name}_${Math.round(hoveredShip.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(hoveredShip.lng*1000)}`;
                           const masterShip = masterShipList.get(masterKey);
                           if (masterShip) {
                               masterShip.elapsed = elapsed;
                               console.log('Updated master list elapsed for', masterShip.name);
                           }
                           
                           // CRITICAL: Aktualisiere Hover-Anzeige SOFORT
                           if (hoveredShip && hoveredShip.name) {
                               if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
                           }
                           
                           // Entferne Promise aus Map
                           elapsedLoadingPromises.delete(shipKey);
                       })
                       .catch(error => {
                           console.error('Failed to load elapsed for', hoveredShip?.name || 'unknown ship', ':', error);
                           
                           // Bei Fehler: Zeige "N/A" an - aber nur wenn Schiff noch gültig ist
                           if (hoveredShip && hoveredShip.name) {
                               hoveredShip.elapsed = 'N/A';
                               if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
                           }
                           
                           elapsedLoadingPromises.delete(shipKey);
                       });
                   
                   elapsedLoadingPromises.set(shipKey, loadingPromise);
               } else if (shipKey && elapsedLoadingPromises.has(shipKey)) {
                   // Request läuft bereits - warte auf Ergebnis
                   elapsedLoadingPromises.get(shipKey)
                       .then(() => {
                           // Aktualisiere Anzeige wenn Request fertig ist
                           if (hoveredShip && hoveredShip.name) {
                               if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
                           }
                       })
                       .catch(() => {
                           if (hoveredShip && hoveredShip.name) {
                               if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
                           }
                       });
               }
           } else {
               // Elapsed ist bereits verfügbar
               if (hoveredShip) {updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);}
           }
           
           shipInfo.style.display = 'block';
           shipInfo.style.left = (e.originalEvent.clientX + 10) + 'px';
           shipInfo.style.top = (e.originalEvent.clientY - 10) + 'px';
       } catch (error) {
           console.error('Error in mousemove hover handling:', error);
           // Bei Fehler: Hover-Info ausblenden
           if (shipInfo) {
               shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
           }
       }
   } else if (shipInfo) {
       shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
   }
});

function formatSignalAge(elapsedMinutes) {
    
    // Handle various input types
    if (!elapsedMinutes || elapsedMinutes === 'N/A' || elapsedMinutes === '' || 
        elapsedMinutes === null || elapsedMinutes === undefined || elapsedMinutes === 'Lade...') {
        return 'N/A';
    }
    
    // Convert to number if it's a string
    let minutes;
    if (typeof elapsedMinutes === 'string') {
        minutes = parseFloat(elapsedMinutes);
    } else {
        minutes = parseFloat(elapsedMinutes);
    }
    
    if (isNaN(minutes)) {
        return 'N/A';
    }
        
    if (minutes <= 2.1) {
        return 'LIVE';
    } else if (minutes < 60) {
        return 'vor ' + Math.round(minutes) + ' min';
    } else if (minutes < 1440) { // weniger als 24 Stunden
        const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
        const remainingMinutes = Math.round(minutes % 60);
        if (remainingMinutes === 0) {
            return 'vor ' + hours + 'h';
        } else {
            return 'vor ' + hours + 'h ' + remainingMinutes + 'min';
        }
    } else {
        const days = Math.floor(minutes / 1440);
        const remainingHours = Math.floor((minutes % 1440) / 60);
        if (remainingHours === 0) {
            return 'vor ' + days + ' Tag' + (days > 1 ? 'en' : '');
        } else {
            return 'vor ' + days + ' Tag' + (days > 1 ? 'en' : '') + ' ' + remainingHours + 'h';
        }
    }
}

// NEUE Hilfsfunktion: Schiff anhand Key finden
function findShipByKey(shipKey) {
   if (!shipKey) return null;

   for (const ship of ships) {
       const key = ship.mmsi || ship.shipId ||
           `${ship.name}_${Math.round(ship.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(ship.lng*1000)}`;
       if (key === shipKey) {
           return ship;
       }
   }
   return null;
}

let isFlying = false;
let flyToStartTime = 0;
var pitchandrotation = false;

const originalFlyTo = map.flyTo.bind(map);

map.flyTo = function(options, eventData) {
   console.log('🛫 flyTo started - disabling drawShipsin move');
   
   isFlying = true;
   flyToStartTime = Date.now();
   
   // Optional: Schiffe während flyTo ausblenden
   if (shipCanvas) {
       //ships = [];
   }
   
   // Original flyTo aufrufen
   const result = originalFlyTo(options, eventData);
   
   // flyTo Ende abfangen
   const originalCallback = options?.callback;
   if (options) {
       options.callback = function(error) {
           isFlying = false;
           if (originalCallback) originalCallback(error);
       };
   }
   
   // Fallback: Nach maximaler flyTo-Zeit automatisch Ende
   setTimeout(() => {
       if (isFlying) {
           console.log('🛬 flyTo timeout - re-enabling drawShips');
           isFlying = false;
       }
   }, 5000); // 5 Sekunden Maximum
   
   return result;
};

map.on('pitch', function() {
    pitchandrotation = true;
    
    const currentPitch = map.getPitch();
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    
    // AUTOMATISCHE PROJEKTION ERKENNUNG basierend auf Pitch
    // Wenn Pitch > 0 und wir in Mercator sind -> wechsle zu 3D
    if (currentPitch > 45 && currentProjection === 'mercator') {
        currentProjection = '3d';
        updateProjectionButton();
        console.log('🔄 Automatisch zu 3D gewechselt (Pitch: ' + currentPitch + '°)');
    }
    // Wenn Pitch = 0 und wir in 3D sind -> wechsle zu 2D
    else if (currentPitch === 0 && currentProjection === '3d') {
        currentProjection = 'mercator';
        updateProjectionButton();
        console.log('🔄 Automatisch zu 2D gewechselt (Pitch: 0°)');
    }
    
    clearTimeout(map._pitchTimeout);
    map._pitchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        saveMapState();
    }, 100);
});

let moveTimeout = null;
let moveStartTime = 0;

// FIXED: Movement handler mit sofortigem Redraw für perfekte Sync
map.on('move', function() {
    // Track movement start
    if (!isMapMoving) {
        moveStartTime = performance.now();
    }

    if (window.portClickAreas) {
        window.portClickAreas = [];
    }
	
    if (window.marinaClickAreas) {
        window.marinaClickAreas = [];
    }
    
    isMapMoving = true;
    pitchandrotation = false;
    
    // Menu-Close-Logic (unverändert)
    closeAllMenusOnMove();
    
    // WICHTIG: SCHIFFE SOFORT NEU ZEICHNEN WÄHREND MOVEMENT
    if (!isFlying) {
        // Canvas Position sync
        syncCanvasPositions();
        
        // SOFORT zeichnen - nicht warten!
        drawShips();
        needsRedraw = false; // Verhindere doppeltes Zeichnen
    }
    
    // Cleanup timeout
    if (moveTimeout) {
        clearTimeout(moveTimeout);
    }
    
    // Set moveend detection
    moveTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        isMapMoving = false;
    }, 150);
});

function clearProjectionCache() {
    ships.forEach(ship => {
        delete ship._projectedPoint;
        delete ship._renderPriority;
        delete ship._distanceFromCenter;
    });
    
    if (persistentShips) {
        persistentShips.forEach(ship => {
            delete ship._projectedPoint;
            delete ship._renderPriority;
            delete ship._distanceFromCenter;
        });
    }
    
    console.log('🧹 Projection cache cleared');
}

let reload  = true;
let reload2 = true;
let timeout = null;

let lastZoomLevelForUpdate = null;
let isZoomUpdating = false;
let zoomUpdateQueue = Promise.resolve();

function handleZoomLevelUpdate() {
    if (isZoomUpdating) {
        console.log('🔄 Zoom-Update bereits aktiv, überspringe...');
        return;
    }
    
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    const currentZoomLevel = Math.floor(currentZoom);
    
    // Initialisierung beim ersten Aufruf
    if (lastZoomLevelForUpdate === null) {
        lastZoomLevelForUpdate = currentZoomLevel;
        console.log(`🔍 Zoom-Level Tracking initialisiert: ${currentZoomLevel}`);
        return;
    }
    
    // Prüfe ob wir eine neue Zoom-Stufe erreicht haben
    if (currentZoomLevel !== lastZoomLevelForUpdate) {
        console.log(`🔄 Zoom-Level Wechsel erkannt: ${lastZoomLevelForUpdate} → ${currentZoomLevel}`);
        
        // Updates in Queue abarbeiten
        zoomUpdateQueue = zoomUpdateQueue.then(async () => {
            if (isLoading) return;
            
            try {
                await executeZoomLevelUpdate(lastZoomLevelForUpdate, currentZoomLevel);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Zoom update failed:', error);
            }
        });
        
        lastZoomLevelForUpdate = currentZoomLevel;
    }
}

function executeZoomLevelUpdate(fromLevel, toLevel) {
    if (isZoomUpdating || isLoading) {
        console.log('🔄 Update übersprungen - bereits aktiv oder loading');
        return Promise.resolve();
    }
    
    return new Promise(async (resolve, reject) => {
        isZoomUpdating = true;
        console.log(`📡 Zoom-Level Update: Stufe ${fromLevel} → ${toLevel}`);
        
        // Sichere alte Schiffe als Backup
        const backupShips = [...ships];
        const backupIncomingShips = new Map(incomingShips);
        const backupMasterList = new Map(masterShipList);
        
        try {
            // Prüfe Map-Status vor Update
            if (!map || typeof map.getZoom !== 'function') {
                throw new Error('Map ist nicht verfügbar für Update');
            }
            
            if (typeof loadRealShips !== 'function') {
                throw new Error('loadRealShips Funktion nicht verfügbar');
            }
            
            // Breche laufende Requests ab
            if (currentRequestController) {
                currentRequestController.abort();
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 50));
            }
            
            // Clear incoming ships für sauberen Neustart
            masterShipList.clear();
            incomingShips.clear();
            clearProjectionCache();
            
            // Lade neue Schiffe (mit Timeout)
            const loadPromise = Promise.race([
                loadRealShips(),
                new Promise((_, reject) => 
                    setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Loading timeout')), 5000)
                )
            ]);
            
            await loadPromise;
            
            // Prüfe ob erfolgreich geladen
            const hasNewShips = ships.length > 0 || incomingShips.size > 0;
            
            if (hasNewShips) {
                console.log(`✅ ${ships.length} Schiffe geladen für Zoom ${toLevel}`);
                
                // Nur bei erfolgreicher Ladung neu zeichnen
                if (shipCanvas && shipCtx) {
                    const pixelRatio = isMobile ? 
                        Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : 
                        (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
                    
                    shipCtx.clearRect(0, 0, 
                        shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio, 
                        shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio);
                    
                    needsRedraw = true;
                    if (!isMapMoving) {
                        drawShips();
                    }
                }
                
                resolve(true);
                
            } else {
                console.warn('⚠️ Keine Schiffe geladen - verwende Backup');
                
                // Restore backup - Inhalte aktualisieren statt Neuzuweisung
                ships.length = 0;
                ships.push(...backupShips);
                
                incomingShips.clear();
                backupIncomingShips.forEach((value, key) => {
                    incomingShips.set(key, value);
                });
                
                masterShipList.clear();
                backupMasterList.forEach((value, key) => {
                    masterShipList.set(key, value);
                });
                
                needsRedraw = true;
                if (!isMapMoving) {
                    drawShips();
                }
                
                // Versuche asynchron nochmal zu laden
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (!isLoading && !isZoomUpdating) {
                        loadRealShips().catch(console.error);
                    }
                }, 1000);
                
                resolve(false);
            }
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Fehler bei Zoom-Level Update:', error);
            
            // Bei Fehler: Backup wiederherstellen - Inhalte aktualisieren
            ships.length = 0;
            ships.push(...backupShips);
            
            incomingShips.clear();
            backupIncomingShips.forEach((value, key) => {
                incomingShips.set(key, value);
            });
            
            masterShipList.clear();
            backupMasterList.forEach((value, key) => {
                masterShipList.set(key, value);
            });
            
            if (shipCanvas && typeof drawShips === 'function') {
                needsRedraw = true;
                if (!isMapMoving) {
                    drawShips();
                }
            }
            
            reject(error);
            
        } finally {
            isZoomUpdating = false;
            console.log('✅ Zoom-Level Update abgeschlossen');
        }
    });
}

if (typeof window.handleZoomLevelUpdate === 'undefined') {
    console.log('✅ Definiere handleZoomLevelUpdate erstmalig');
    
    // Variablen für Zoom-Level Tracking
    let lastZoomLevelForUpdate = null;
    let isZoomUpdating = false;

    /**
     * Garantiertes Update bei Zoom-Level Wechsel - ORIGINAL VERSION
     */
    window.handleZoomLevelUpdate = function() {
        // Verhindere mehrfache parallele Updates
        if (isZoomUpdating) {
            console.log('🔄 Zoom-Update bereits aktiv, überspringe...');
            return;
        }
        
        const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
        const currentZoomLevel = Math.floor(currentZoom);
        
        // Initialisierung beim ersten Aufruf
        if (lastZoomLevelForUpdate === null) {
            lastZoomLevelForUpdate = currentZoomLevel;
            console.log(`🔍 Zoom-Level Tracking initialisiert: ${currentZoomLevel}`);
            return;
        }
        
        // Prüfe ob wir eine neue Zoom-Stufe erreicht haben
        if (currentZoomLevel !== lastZoomLevelForUpdate) {
            console.log(`🔄 Zoom-Level Wechsel erkannt: ${lastZoomLevelForUpdate} → ${currentZoomLevel}`);
            
            // SOFORT Update ohne Verzögerung
            executeZoomLevelUpdate(lastZoomLevelForUpdate, currentZoomLevel);
            lastZoomLevelForUpdate = currentZoomLevel;
        }
    };

    /**
     * Führt das eigentliche Update durch - ORIGINAL VERSION
     */
    window.executeZoomLevelUpdate = function(fromLevel, toLevel) {
        if (isZoomUpdating || isLoading) {
            console.log('🔄 Update übersprungen - bereits aktiv oder loading');
            return;
        }
		
		return executeZoomLevelUpdate(fromLevel, toLevel)
        .catch(error => {
            console.error('Zoom update failed, retrying once...', error);
            
            // Ein Retry-Versuch nach kurzer Pause
            return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500))
                .then(() => executeZoomLevelUpdate(fromLevel, toLevel))
                .catch(retryError => {
                    console.error('Retry also failed:', retryError);
                    // Gib auf, aber crashe nicht
                    return false;
                });
        });	
        
        isZoomUpdating = true;
        
        console.log(`📡 SOFORTIGES Zoom-Level Update: Stufe ${fromLevel} → ${toLevel}`);
        
        try {
            // KRITISCH: Prüfe Map-Status vor Update
            if (!map || typeof map.getZoom !== 'function') {
                console.error('❌ Map ist nicht verfügbar für Update');
                return;
            }
            
            // KRITISCH: Prüfe ob loadRealShips existiert
            if (typeof loadRealShips !== 'function') {
                console.error('❌ loadRealShips Funktion nicht verfügbar');
                return;
            }
            
            // Standard Update
            //console.log(`🎯 Standard Update für Zoom-Level ${toLevel}`);
			masterShipList.clear();
			incomingShips.clear();
			clearProjectionCache();
            loadRealShips();
            
            
            // KRITISCH: Prüfe Canvas vor Redraw
            if (typeof drawShips=== 'function' && shipCanvas) {
                needsRedraw = true;
                if (!isMapMoving) {
                    drawShips(); // Sofortiges Neuzeichnen
                }
            } else {
                console.warn('⚠️ drawShipsoder shipCanvas nicht verfügbar');
            }
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ Fehler bei Zoom-Level Update:', error);
            // WICHTIG: Detaillierte Fehlerausgabe für Mobile Debug
            console.error('Error details:', {
                message: error.message,
                stack: error.stack,
                mapExists: !!map,
                shipCanvasExists: !!shipCanvas,
                isLoadingState: isLoading,
                currentZoom: map ? map.getZoom() : 'N/A'
            });
        } finally {
            // Update-Status sofort zurücksetzen
            isZoomUpdating = false;
            console.log('✅ Zoom-Level Update abgeschlossen');
        }
    };
    
} else {
    console.log('⚠️ handleZoomLevelUpdate bereits definiert, überspringe Definition');
}

function stopShipAnimation() {
    if (animationFrame) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrame);
        animationFrame = null;
    }
}

map.on('zoom', function() {
	var zoom = map.getZoom();
		
	handleZoomLevelUpdate();
	
    if (window.portClickAreas) {
        window.portClickAreas = [];
    }
    
    drawShips();
	
    updateZoomDisplay(zoom);
    needsRedraw = true;

    clearTimeout(map._zoomTimeout);
    map._zoomTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        saveMapState();
    }, 100);

    let exaggeration = 1.5;
    if (map.getTerrain()) {
        map.setTerrain({
            'source': 'mapbox-dem',
            'exaggeration': exaggeration
        });
    }
});

});

// Variable für die letzte Bounding Box (außerhalb der Funktion definieren)
	let lastBounds2 = null;

map.on('moveend', function() {
    isMapMoving = false;
    
    if(map.getZoom() > 8 && Object.values(poiFilters).some(active => active))
        loadStaticAssets();
    chunkRenderer.disableMovementMode();
    resumeAutoRefreshAfterMovement();
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    updateZoomDisplay(zoom);
    saveMapState();
    
    // Aktuelle Bounds abrufen
    const currentBounds = map.getBounds();
    
    // Prüfen, ob die aktuelle Position außerhalb der letzten Bounds liegt
    const boundsChanged = !lastBounds2 || !lastBounds2.contains(currentBounds.getCenter());
    
    if (map.getZoom() >= 11 && boundsChanged) {
        if (!isLowEndDevice) {	
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 100);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                drawShips();
            }, 200);
        }
        
        // LOW-END: ZUSÄTZLICHE UPDATES
        if (isLowEndDevice) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 300);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 600);
        }
        
        // Neue Bounds speichern (mit etwas Buffer)
        lastBounds2 = currentBounds;
    } else if (map.getZoom() <= 11 && !boundsChanged || boundsChanged) {
        if (!isLowEndDevice) {	
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 100);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                drawShips();
            }, 200);
        }
        
        // LOW-END: ZUSÄTZLICHE UPDATES
        if (isLowEndDevice) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 300);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                masterShipList.clear();
                incomingShips.clear();
                clearProjectionCache();
                loadRealShips();
            }, 600);
        }		 
        lastBounds2 = currentBounds;		
	}
    
    clearTimeout(moveTimeoutForNames);
    moveTimeoutForNames = setTimeout(() => {
        isMapMovingForNames = false;
    }, 500);
});

// KORRIGIERTE Error-Handler für robusteren Betrieb
map.on('error', function(e) {
    const errorMessage = e.error?.message || '';
    
    // Suppress häufige, harmlose Fehler
    const suppressedErrors = [
        'Source already exists',
        'Layer already exists', 
        'There is already a source',
        'There is already a layer',
        'Terrain source'
    ];
    
    const shouldSuppress = suppressedErrors.some(suppressedError => 
        errorMessage.includes(suppressedError)
    );
    
    if (!shouldSuppress) {
        console.warn('Map error (not suppressed):', errorMessage);
    }
});

function createFPSDisplay() {
   // Check if element already exists
   if (document.getElementById('fpsDisplay')) {
       return;
   }

   const fpsDisplay = document.createElement('div');
   fpsDisplay.id = 'fpsDisplay';
   fpsDisplay.className = 'zoom-display';
   fpsDisplay.style.bottom = '130px';
   fpsDisplay.style.right = '20px';
   fpsDisplay.style.position = 'fixed';
   fpsDisplay.textContent = '0';
   fpsDisplay.title = 'Frames Per Second';

   document.body.appendChild(fpsDisplay);

   console.log('📊 FPS Display created');
}

function closeAllMenusOnMove() {
    const filterMenu = document.getElementById('filterControlMenu');
    const filterButton = document.getElementById('filterButton');
    if (filterMenu && filterMenu.classList.contains('active')) {
        filterMenu.classList.remove('active');
        filterButton.classList.remove('filterButton-active');
    }
    
    const layerMenu = document.getElementById('layerControlMenu');
    const layerButton = document.getElementById('layerControlButton');
    if (layerMenu && layerMenu.classList.contains('active')) {
        layerMenu.classList.remove('active');
        layerButton.classList.remove('layerButton-active');
    }
    
    const areasMenu = document.getElementById('areasControlMenu');
    const areasButton = document.getElementById('areasButton');
    if (areasMenu && areasMenu.classList.contains('active')) {
        areasMenu.classList.remove('active');
        areasButton.classList.remove('areasButton-active');
    }
    
    const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (shipInfo) {
        shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
    }
    
    map.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';

    const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');
    if (resultsContainer) {
        //resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

function updateLastUpdateTime() {
   const now = new Date();
   //console.log('[Last Update]', now.toLocaleTimeString());
}

function hasMapMoved() {
   const currentBounds = map.getBounds();
   if (!lastBounds) {
       lastBounds = currentBounds;
       return true;
   }

   const threshold = 0.01;
   const moved = Math.abs(currentBounds.getNorth() - lastBounds.getNorth()) > threshold ||
                Math.abs(currentBounds.getSouth() - lastBounds.getSouth()) > threshold ||
                Math.abs(currentBounds.getEast() - lastBounds.getEast()) > threshold ||
                Math.abs(currentBounds.getWest() - lastBounds.getWest()) > threshold;

   if (moved) {
       lastBounds = currentBounds;
   }

   return moved;
}

function setLoadingState(loading) {
   isLoading = loading;
}

function calculateDistance(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
   const R = 6371000;
   const dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * Math.PI / 180;
   const dLon = (lon2 - lon1) * Math.PI / 180;
   const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
             Math.cos(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) *
             Math.sin(dLon/2) * Math.sin(dLon/2);
   const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a));
   return R * c;
}

function startAutoRefresh() {
   if (autoRefreshInterval) {
       clearInterval(autoRefreshInterval);
   }

   autoRefreshInterval = setInterval(async function() {
       if (autoRefreshEnabled && !isMapMoving) {
           const now = Date.now();
           const timeSinceLastRefresh = now - lastAutoRefresh;

           if (timeSinceLastRefresh >= 15000) {  
               lastAutoRefresh = now;
               
               // Standard Ship Update (API2)
               if(map.getZoom() >= 11) {
                   console.log('[Auto Refresh] Updating ships after 10 seconds');
                   loadRealShips();
               }
           }
       }
   }, 15100);
}

function stopAutoRefresh() {
   if (autoRefreshInterval) {
       clearInterval(autoRefreshInterval);
       autoRefreshInterval = null;
   }
}

// ZUSÄTZLICHE OPTIMIERUNG: Globe-aware Filterung
function isShipVisibleOnGlobe(ship, center) {
   const projection = map.getProjection();
   
   if (!projection || projection.name !== 'globe') {
       return true; // Bei anderen Projektionen normale Filterung
   }

   const zoom = map.getZoom();
   if (zoom >= 6) {
       return true; // Bei hohem Zoom normale Filterung
   }

   // Bei Globe-Projektion: Prüfe ob Schiff auf der sichtbaren Seite ist
   const shipLng = ship.lng;
   const centerLng = center.lng;

   let lngDiff = Math.abs(shipLng - centerLng);
   if (lngDiff > 180) {
       lngDiff = 360 - lngDiff;
   }

   // Schiffe auf der Rückseite des Globus ausblenden
   return lngDiff <= 90;
}
