// Anfangswerte
let modelOrigin = [6.6068, 55.9190];
let modelAltitude = 0;
let modelRotate = [Math.PI / 2, 0, 0];

// Startwert für Mercator
let modelAsMercatorCoordinate = mapboxgl.MercatorCoordinate.fromLngLat(
    modelOrigin,
    modelAltitude
);

// Transformation speichern
let modelTransform = {
    translateX: modelAsMercatorCoordinate.x,
    translateY: modelAsMercatorCoordinate.y,
    translateZ: modelAsMercatorCoordinate.z,
    rotateX: modelRotate[0],
    rotateY: modelRotate[1],
    rotateZ: modelRotate[2],
    scale: modelAsMercatorCoordinate.meterInMercatorCoordinateUnits()
};

// 🟩 Funktion: direkt neue Koordinaten und Kurs setzen
function updateModelFromCoordinates(lng, lat, course) {
    // Neue Ursprungskoodinaten speichern
    modelOrigin = [lng, lat];
    modelAsMercatorCoordinate = mapboxgl.MercatorCoordinate.fromLngLat(
        modelOrigin,
        modelAltitude
    );

    // Transform aktualisieren
    modelTransform.translateX = modelAsMercatorCoordinate.x;
    modelTransform.translateY = modelAsMercatorCoordinate.y;
    modelTransform.translateZ = modelAsMercatorCoordinate.z;
    modelTransform.rotateY = -course * Math.PI / 270;

    // Map neu rendern
    map.triggerRepaint();
}


// Custom Layer Definition
const customLayer = {
    id: '3d-ship-model',
    type: 'custom',
    renderingMode: '3d',
    onAdd: function (map, gl) {
        this.map = map;
        this.camera = new THREE.Camera();
        this.scene = new THREE.Scene();
        this.ship3DModels = ship3DModels; // Referenz auf globale Map

        // Lichter
        const directionalLight1 = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff);
        directionalLight1.position.set(0, -70, 100).normalize();
        this.scene.add(directionalLight1);

        const directionalLight2 = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff);
        directionalLight2.position.set(0, 70, 100).normalize();
        this.scene.add(directionalLight2);

        // Renderer
        this.renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({
            canvas: map.getCanvas(),
            context: gl,
            antialias: true
        });
        this.renderer.autoClear = false;

        // GLTF Loader
        const loader = new THREE.GLTFLoader();
        loader.load(
            'https://marinetraffic.live/3d-models/aidaprima/scene.gltf',
            (gltf) => {
                this.scene.add(gltf.scene);
                this.ship3DModels.set('3683399', gltf.scene);
                console.log('3D-Modell geladen und gespeichert');
            },
            undefined,
            (error) => {
                console.error('GLTF Load Error:', error);
            }
        );
    },
    render: function (gl, matrix) {
        const rotationX = new THREE.Matrix4().makeRotationAxis(
            new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0),
            modelTransform.rotateX
        );
        const rotationY = new THREE.Matrix4().makeRotationAxis(
            new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0),
            modelTransform.rotateY
        );
        const rotationZ = new THREE.Matrix4().makeRotationAxis(
            new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1),
            modelTransform.rotateZ
        );

        const m = new THREE.Matrix4().fromArray(matrix);
        const l = new THREE.Matrix4()
            .makeTranslation(
                modelTransform.translateX,
                modelTransform.translateY,
                modelTransform.translateZ
            )
            .scale(
                new THREE.Vector3(
                    modelTransform.scale,
                    modelTransform.scale,
                    modelTransform.scale
                )
            )
            .multiply(rotationX)
            .multiply(rotationY)
            .multiply(rotationZ);

        this.camera.projectionMatrix = m.multiply(l);

        this.renderer.resetState();
        this.renderer.render(this.scene, this.camera);
        this.map.triggerRepaint();
    }
};

// Layer auf der Map hinzufügen
map.on('style.load', () => {
    //map.addLayer(customLayer);
});

// Beispiel: updatePosition aufrufen, wenn sich Schiff bewegt
function updateShipModelPosition(lng, lat, course) {
    if (map.getLayer('3d-model')) {
        customLayer.updatePosition(lng, lat, course);
    }
}

async function loadRealShips() {
	
    if (currentRequestController) {
        console.log('Request already in progress, aborting previous');
        currentRequestController.abort();
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 50)); // Kurz warten
    }
	
    currentRequestController = new AbortController();
    const signal = currentRequestController.signal;

    setLoadingState(true);

    try {
        const center = map.getCenter();
        const bounds = map.getBounds();
        const real_zoom = map.getZoom();

        // Angepasste Zoom-Logik für API-Calls
        let api_zoom = Math.floor(real_zoom);
        let tile_zoom = Math.floor(real_zoom);

        // NEU: Spezielle API2 Zoom-Logik
		if (real_zoom >= 2 && real_zoom < 3) {
            api_zoom = 1;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 3 && real_zoom < 4) {
            api_zoom = 3;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 4 && real_zoom < 5) {
            api_zoom = 4;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 5 && real_zoom < 6) {
            api_zoom = 5;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 6 && real_zoom < 7) {
            api_zoom = 6;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 7 && real_zoom < 8) {
            api_zoom = 7;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 8 && real_zoom < 9) {
            api_zoom = 8;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 9 && real_zoom < 10) {
            api_zoom = 9;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 10 && real_zoom < 11) {
            api_zoom = 9;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 11 && real_zoom < 12) {
            api_zoom = 10;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 12 && real_zoom < 13) {
            api_zoom = 11;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 13 && real_zoom < 14) {
            api_zoom = 12;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 14 && real_zoom < 15) {
            api_zoom = 12;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } else if (real_zoom >= 15 && real_zoom < 16) {
            api_zoom = 12;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        }  else if (real_zoom >= 16 && real_zoom < 17) {
            api_zoom = 12;
            console.log(`🔧 API2 Zoom adjusted: real_zoom ${real_zoom} → api_zoom ${api_zoom}`);
        } 

        // WICHTIG: Wenn api_zoom gecapped oder angepasst wurde, 
        // müssen wir die Tiles auch mit api_zoom berechnen!
        let effective_tile_zoom = api_zoom;
        
        // Nur bei sehr niedrigen Zoom-Levels den originalen tile_zoom verwenden
        if (real_zoom < 2) {
            effective_tile_zoom = tile_zoom;
        }

        // NEU: Force API2 für SAT-AIS wenn Zoom >= 8
        let forceAPI2 = false;
        if (real_zoom >= 11) {
            // Prüfe ob SAT-AIS Schiffe in der Ansicht sind
            const hasSatAIS = ships.some(ship => ship.name && ship.name.includes('[SAT-AIS]'));
            if (hasSatAIS) {
                forceAPI2 = true;
                console.log('🛰️ SAT-AIS detected - forcing API2 usage');
            }
        }

        // Modifiziere die API1 Promise Bedingung:
        if (USE_API1 && real_zoom >= 11 && !forceAPI2) {
            // Warte auf vorheriges Promise falls noch läuft
            if (api1Promise) {
                try {
                    await api1Promise;
                } catch (e) {
                    console.log('Previous API1 call failed/aborted');
                }
            }
            // Starte neuen API1 Call
            api1Promise = loadAPI1Data(bounds, signal);
        } else if (!USE_API1 && real_zoom >= 11) {
            console.log('📡 API1 disabled - using API2 only');
        }

        console.log(`📊 Zoom levels: real_zoom=${real_zoom}, api_zoom=${api_zoom}, effective_tile_zoom=${effective_tile_zoom}`);
    
        // n für Tile-Berechnung basiert jetzt auf effective_tile_zoom
        const n = Math.pow(2, effective_tile_zoom);
        
        const tileCoords = [];
        
        var tileNW = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getWest() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };
        
        var tileNE = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getEast() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };
        
        var tileSW = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getWest() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };
        
        var tileSE = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getEast() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };

        let priority = 1;
        let extraTiles = 0;
        
        const minX = Math.max(0, Math.min(tileNW.x, tileNE.x, tileSW.x, tileSE.x) - extraTiles);
        const maxX = Math.max(tileNW.x, tileNE.x, tileSW.x, tileSE.x) + extraTiles;
        const minY = Math.max(0, Math.min(tileNW.y, tileNE.y, tileSW.y, tileSE.y) - extraTiles);
        const maxY = Math.max(tileNW.y, tileNE.y, tileSW.y, tileSE.y) + extraTiles;
        
        const centerX = (minX + maxX) / 2;
        const centerY = (minY + maxY) / 2;
        
        const tileRangeX = maxX - minX;
        const tileRangeY = maxY - minY;
        const totalTiles = tileRangeX * tileRangeY;

        if (totalTiles > 100) {
            const center = map.getCenter();
            // Verwende api_zoom für die Fallback-Berechnung (bleibt gleich)
            const n_api = Math.pow(2, api_zoom);
            const fallbackX = Math.floor((center.lng + 180) / 360 * n_api / 2);
            const fallbackY = Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(center.lat * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(center.lat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n_api / 2);
            
            tileCoords.push({ 
                x: fallbackX, 
                y: fallbackY, 
                priority: 0,
                isCore: true
            });
        } else {
            for (let x = minX; x <= maxX; x++) {
                for (let y = minY; y <= maxY; y++) {
                    const distance = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - centerX, 2) + Math.pow(y - centerY, 2));
                    const isCore = x >= Math.min(tileNW.x, tileSE.x) && x <= Math.max(tileNW.x, tileSE.x) && 
                                   y >= Math.min(tileNW.y, tileSE.y) && y <= Math.max(tileNW.y, tileSE.y);
                    
                    tileCoords.push({ 
                        x, 
                        y, 
                        priority: isCore ? Math.round(distance * 10) : 100 + Math.round(distance * 10),
                        isCore
                    });
                }
            }
        }
        
        tileCoords.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);

        var maxTiles = isLowEndDevice ? 14 : 14
        const limitedTiles = tileCoords.slice(0, maxTiles);
		
		var batchSize = isLowEndDevice ? 4 : (isMobile ? 4 : 6);
			
        const batches = [];
        
        for (let i = 0; i < limitedTiles.length; i += batchSize) {
            batches.push(limitedTiles.slice(i, i + batchSize));
        }

        for (const batch of batches) {
            // Prüfe ob Request abgebrochen wurde
            if (signal.aborted) {
                console.log('⚠️ Ship loading cancelled');
                return;
            }
			
            const batchPromises = batch.map(async function(coord) {
                // DIESE VARIABLEN MÜSSEN HIER DRIN SEIN - FÜR JEDEN REQUEST EINZELN!
                let tileData = null;
                let retryCount = 0;
                const maxRetries = 1;
   
				const mtUrl = `https://marinetraffic.com/getData/get_data_json_4/z:${api_zoom}/X:${coord.x}/Y:${coord.y}`;
				const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
				const baseUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/ship_api/?getData=AIS/z:${api_zoom}/X:${coord.x}/Y:${coord.y}`;
                 
                let urls = [generateFilterURL(baseUrl)];
                
                while (!tileData && retryCount < maxRetries && !signal.aborted) {
                    for (const url of urls) {
                        if (signal.aborted) {
                            return null;
                        }
                        
                        try {
                            const response = await fetch(url, {
                                signal: signal,
                                cache: 'default',
            method: 'GET',
            headers: {
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest'
            },
            timeout: 10000
        }); 
                            
                            if (response.status === 429) {
                                console.warn('Rate limit erreicht (429) - warte länger');
                                retryCount = maxRetries;
                                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10000));
                                break;
                            }
                            
                            if (response.status >= 500) {
                                console.warn(`Server Error: ${response.status}`);
                                retryCount++;
                                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
                                break;
                            }
							
                            if (response.status === 403) {
                                retryCount = maxRetries;
                                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 5000));
                                break;
                            }
                            
                            if (response.status === 404) {
                                console.warn('Tile nicht gefunden (404)');
                                return null;
                            }
                            
                            if (!response.ok) {
                                console.warn(`HTTP Error: ${response.status}`);
                                retryCount++;
                                break;
                            }
                            
                            const responseText = await response.text();
                            
                            if (responseText.trim().startsWith('<!DOCTYPE') || 
                                responseText.trim().startsWith('<html')) {
                                console.warn('HTML statt JSON erhalten');
                                retryCount++;
                                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
                                break;
                            }
                            
                            try {
                                tileData = JSON.parse(responseText);
                                break;
                            } catch (parseError) {
                                console.warn('JSON Parse Error:', parseError);
                                retryCount++;
                                break;
                            }
                            
                        } catch (e) {
                            if (e.name === 'AbortError') {
                                console.log('Request abgebrochen');
                                return null;
                            }
                            
                            console.warn('Fetch error:', e);
                            retryCount++;
                            
                            if (retryCount < maxRetries && !signal.aborted) {
                                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
                            }
                            
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    if (!tileData && retryCount < maxRetries && !signal.aborted) {
                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
                    }
                }
                
                // Rückgabe am Ende
                if (tileData && !signal.aborted) {
                    let shipData = [];
                    if (Array.isArray(tileData)) {
                        shipData = tileData;
                    } else if (tileData.data && tileData.data.rows && Array.isArray(tileData.data.rows)) {
                        shipData = tileData.data.rows;
                    } else if (tileData.rows && Array.isArray(tileData.rows)) {
                        shipData = tileData.rows;
                    }
                    return { coord: coord, shipData: shipData, priority: coord.priority };
                }
                return null;
            });

            var batchResults = await Promise.all(batchPromises);
            var isSatAIS = true;
			
            // Verarbeite Results nur wenn nicht abgebrochen
            if (!signal.aborted) {
                for (const result of batchResults) {
                    if (result && result.shipData) {
                        successCount++;
						
                        result.shipData.forEach(async function(shipData, index) {
                            let lat, lng, speed = 0, course = 0, heading = 0, name = '', type = '', destination = '', mmsi = '', shipId = '', length = 0;
                            let elapsed = 'N/A';
                            

                            if (typeof shipData === 'object' && shipData.LAT && shipData.LON) {
                                lat = parseFloat(shipData.LAT);
                                lng = parseFloat(shipData.LON);
                                speed = parseFloat(shipData.SPEED) / 10 || 0;
                                course = parseFloat(shipData.COURSE) || 0;
                                heading = parseFloat(shipData.HEADING) || course;
                                name = shipData.SHIPNAME || 'Ship ' + (incomingShips.size + index + 1);
                                isSatAIS = name && name.includes('[SAT-AIS]');
                                type = shipData.SHIPTYPE || 'N/A';
                                destination = shipData.DESTINATION || 'N/A';
                                mmsi = shipData.MMSI || '';
                                shipId = shipData.SHIP_ID || '';
                                length = parseFloat(shipData.LENGTH) || parseFloat(shipData.VSL_LENGTH) || 50;
                                
                                if (shipData.ELAPSED && shipData.ELAPSED !== null && shipData.ELAPSED !== 'N/A') {
                                    elapsed = parseInt(shipData.ELAPSED);
                                    if (isNaN(elapsed)) {
                                        elapsed = 'N/A';
                                    }
                                }
                                
                            } else if (Array.isArray(shipData) && shipData.length >= 4) {
                                lat = parseFloat(shipData[0]);
                                lng = parseFloat(shipData[1]);
                                speed = parseFloat(shipData[2]) || 0;
                                course = parseFloat(shipData[3]) || 0;
                                heading = course;
                                name = shipData[6] || 'Ship ' + (incomingShips.size + index + 1);
                                isSatAIS = name && name.includes('[SAT-AIS]');
                                mmsi = shipData[4] || '';
                                shipId = shipData[5] || '';
                                length = parseFloat(shipData[7]) || parseFloat(shipData[8]) || parseFloat(shipData[9]) || 50;
                                
                                if (shipData.length > 10 && shipData[10] && shipData[10] !== null && shipData[10] !== 'N/A') {
                                    elapsed = parseInt(shipData[10]);
                                    if (isNaN(elapsed)) {
                                        elapsed = 'N/A';
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            const shipType = type || '0';
                            const isTypeActive = activeShipTypeFilters[shipType];
                            
                            if (isTypeActive !== true) {
                                return;
                            }

                            if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
                                if (lat < bounds.getSouth() || lat > bounds.getNorth() ||
                                    lng < bounds.getWest() || lng > bounds.getEast()) {
                                    return;
                                }

                                const shipKey = mmsi || shipId || `${name}_${Math.round(lat*1000)}_${Math.round(lng*1000)}`;
                                const existingShip = masterShipList.get(shipKey);

                                if (existingShip) {
                                    // Verwende die verbesserte Update-Logik
                                    const updatedShip = updateShipData(existingShip, {
                                        lat, lng, speed, course, heading, destination, elapsed, shipData
                                    }, api_zoom);
                                    incomingShips.set(shipKey, updatedShip);
                                } else {
                                    // Neues Schiff erstellen
                                    const hasDetailedData = !!(destination && destination !== 'N/A');
                                    const newShip = {
                                        lat: lat,
                                        lng: lng,
                                        speed: speed,
                                        course: course,
                                        heading: heading,
                                        name: name,
                                        type: type,
                                        destination: destination,
                                        mmsi: mmsi,
                                        shipId: shipId,
                                        length: length,
                                        vsl_length: length,
                                        elapsed: elapsed,
                                        isLiveAPI1: false,
                                        signalAge: elapsed === 'N/A' ? 999 : parseInt(elapsed),
                                        lastSeen: Date.now(),
                                        lastPositionUpdate: Date.now(),
                                        lastZoom: real_zoom,
                                        lastApiZoom: api_zoom,
                                        isSatAIS: isSatAIS,
                                        dataQuality: getDataQuality(api_zoom, elapsed, hasDetailedData)
                                    };

                                    masterShipList.set(shipKey, newShip);
                                    incomingShips.set(shipKey, newShip);
									
                                }
if (parseInt(shipId) === 3683399) {
    const shipModel = ship3DModels.get('3683399');
    if (shipModel) {
		updateModelFromCoordinates(lng, lat, course);
		const mercCoord = mapboxgl.MercatorCoordinate.fromLngLat([lng, lat], 0);
        shipModel.position.set(mercCoord.x, mercCoord.y, mercCoord.z);
        shipModel.rotation.y = -course * Math.PI * 180;
    } else {
        console.log('3D-Modell noch nicht geladen, Update wird übersprungen');
        // Optional: einmal später versuchen oder setTimeout/retry
    }
}
                            }

                        });
                    }
                }
            }
            
            if (batch !== batches[batches.length - 1] && !signal.aborted) {
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10));
            }
        }
		

        // Finale Verarbeitung nur wenn nicht abgebrochen
        if (!signal.aborted && successCount > 0 && incomingShips.size > 0) {
            const now = Date.now();
            
            // Cleanup
            for (const [key, ship] of masterShipList.entries()) {
                if (now - ship.lastSeen > 60000) {
                    masterShipList.delete(key);
                }
            }

            for (const [key, ship] of incomingShips.entries()) {
                if (now - ship.lastSeen > 60000) {
                    incomingShips.delete(key);
                }
            }

            const previousHoveredShipKey = lastHoveredShipKey;
				
            let allShips = Array.from(incomingShips.values());
            
            const zoom = map.getZoom();
            let MaxShips = 1000;
            if (isMobile) MaxShips = 800;
            if (isLowEndDevice) MaxShips = 300;
            
            ships = allShips.length > MaxShips ? 
                filterShipsByPerformanceOnly(allShips, MaxShips) : 
                allShips;
				
            updateSearchMarkerToShipPosition();

            // API1 Updates
            try {
                if(USE_API1 && real_zoom >= 8) {
                    await api1Promise;
                    console.log('applying API1 updates...');
                    wasUpdated = updateShipsWithAPI1(incomingShips);
                    
                    if (wasUpdated) {
                        // Ships Array neu aus incomingShips aufbauen
                        let allShips = Array.from(incomingShips.values());
                        
                        const zoom = map.getZoom();
                        let MaxShips = 1000;
                        if (isMobile) MaxShips = 800;
                        if (isLowEndDevice) MaxShips = 300;
                        
                        ships = allShips.length > MaxShips ? 
                            filterShipsByPerformanceOnly(allShips, MaxShips) : 
                            allShips;
                        
                        console.log(`✅ Ships array rebuilt with ${ships.length} ships after API1 updates`);
                        
                        needsRedraw = true;
                        if (!isMapMoving) {
                            drawShips();
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (error) {
                if (error.name !== 'AbortError') {
                    console.warn('API1 failed:', error);
                }
            }

            // Rest des hoveredShip Updates...
            if (previousHoveredShipKey && hoveredShip) {
                const newHoveredShip = findShipByKey(previousHoveredShipKey);
                if (newHoveredShip) {
                    hoveredShip = newHoveredShip;
                } else {
                    hoveredShip = null;
                    lastHoveredShipKey = null;
                }
            }

            updateLastUpdateTime();
            
            // Nur wenn KEIN API1-Update
            if (!wasUpdated) {
                needsRedraw = true;
            }

            if (isLowEndDevice && !wasUpdated) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    drawShips();
                }, 100);
            }
        } else if (successCount === 0 && !signal.aborted) {
            throw new Error('Could not reach API for any tiles. Check api.php path.');
        } else if (!signal.aborted) {
            setStatus('No ships found in this area', 'error');
        }

    } catch (error) {
        if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
            console.log('Ship loading was aborted');
        } else {
            console.warn('Error:', error);
            setStatus('Error: ' + error.message, 'error');
        }
    } finally {
        setLoadingState(false);
        
        // Controller zurücksetzen wenn fertig
        if (currentRequestController === currentRequestController) {
            currentRequestController = null;
        }
    }
}

async function loadRealShips2() {
	
}

setInterval(() => {
if(map.getZoom() >=8)
updateFleetTrackingPositions();
}, 5000);

function removeSatAISDuplicates(shipsMap) {
    if (!shipsMap || shipsMap.size === 0) return shipsMap;
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    if (zoom >= 6) return shipsMap; // Nur bei niedrigem Zoom bereinigen
    
    const satAISGroups = new Map();
    const cleanedShips = new Map();
    
    // Gruppiere SAT-AIS Schiffe nach Name
    for (const [key, ship] of shipsMap.entries()) {
        if (ship.name && ship.name.includes('[SAT-AIS]')) {
            const groupKey = ship.mmsi || ship.name;
            if (!satAISGroups.has(groupKey)) {
                satAISGroups.set(groupKey, []);
            }
            satAISGroups.get(groupKey).push({ key, ship });
        } else {
            // Nicht-SAT-AIS Schiffe direkt übernehmen
            cleanedShips.set(key, ship);
        }
    }
    
    // Für jede SAT-AIS Gruppe: Nehme nur das neueste
    for (const [groupKey, ships] of satAISGroups.entries()) {
        if (ships.length === 1) {
            cleanedShips.set(ships[0].key, ships[0].ship);
        } else {
            // Mehrere SAT-AIS mit gleichem Namen - nimm das mit bestem Signal
            const bestShip = ships.reduce((best, current) => {
                const bestElapsed = parseInt(best.ship.elapsed) || 999999;
                const currentElapsed = parseInt(current.ship.elapsed) || 999999;
                return currentElapsed < bestElapsed ? current : best;
            });
            
            console.log(`🛰️ Consolidated ${ships.length} SAT-AIS duplicates for: ${groupKey}`);
            cleanedShips.set(bestShip.key, bestShip.ship);
        }
    }
    
    return cleanedShips;
}

// Globale Variablen für smoothe Animation
let lastUpdateTime = performance.now();
let animationFrame = null;

function startContinuousShipUpdates() {
    // Verwende requestAnimationFrame statt setInterval für smoothere Animation
    function animate(currentTime) {
        // Delta-Zeit berechnen für frame-unabhängige Bewegung
        const deltaTime = (currentTime - lastUpdateTime) / 1000; // in Sekunden
        lastUpdateTime = currentTime;
        
        if (map.getZoom() >= 11 && !isMapMoving) {  // Changed from == 0 to >= 8
            // Filter für bewegende Schiffe MIT LIVE/RECENT ELAPSED
            const movingShips = ships.filter(ship => {
                // Prüfe Geschwindigkeit
                if (ship.speed <= 5) return false;
				if (ship.speed >= 41) return false;
                
                // NEUE PRÜFUNG: Nur Schiffe mit recentem Signal animieren
                if (ship.elapsed !== undefined && ship.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
                    const elapsedMinutes = parseInt(ship.elapsed);
                    if (!isNaN(elapsedMinutes)) {
                        // Nur animieren wenn Signal < 15 Minuten alt ist
                        return elapsedMinutes <= 2.1;
                    }
                }
                
                // Wenn kein elapsed vorhanden, nicht animieren
                return false;
            });
            
            if (movingShips.length > 0) {
                let needsUpdate = false;
                
                movingShips.forEach(ship => {
                    if (ship.speed && ship.course !== undefined) {
                        // Smoothe Interpolation der Position
                        if (!ship.targetLat) {
                            ship.targetLat = ship.lat;
                            ship.targetLng = ship.lng;
                            ship.displayLat = ship.lat;
                            ship.displayLng = ship.lng;
                        }
                        
                        // Geschwindigkeit: Knoten zu m/s
                        const speedMs = ship.speed * 0.514444;
                        
                        // Distanz basierend auf tatsächlicher Frame-Zeit
                        const distanceM = speedMs * deltaTime;
                        
                        // Neue Zielposition berechnen
                        const courseRad = ship.course * Math.PI / 180;
                        const latChange = (distanceM * Math.cos(courseRad)) / 111320;
                        const lngChange = (distanceM * Math.sin(courseRad)) / 
                                         (111320 * Math.cos(ship.targetLat * Math.PI / 180));
                        
                        ship.targetLat += latChange;
                        ship.targetLng += lngChange;
                        
                        // Smoothe Interpolation zur Zielposition (Lerp)
                        const lerpFactor = Math.min(1, deltaTime * 10); // Anpassbare Smoothness
                        ship.displayLat = ship.displayLat + (ship.targetLat - ship.displayLat) * lerpFactor;
                        ship.displayLng = ship.displayLng + (ship.targetLng - ship.displayLng) * lerpFactor;
                        
                        // Für die eigentliche Position (für Berechnungen)
                        ship.lat = ship.targetLat;
                        ship.lng = ship.targetLng;
                        
                        needsUpdate = true;
                    }
                });
                
                if (needsUpdate) {
                    // Batch-Update für bessere Performance
                    requestIdleCallback(() => {
                        drawShips();
                    }, { timeout: 16 }); // Max 16ms für ~60fps
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Nächsten Frame anfordern
        animationFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    }
    
    // Animation starten
    animationFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}

// Korrigierte loadAPI1Data Funktion mit automatischem Update-Trigger
const loadAPI1Data = async (bounds, signal) => {
    try {
        // Bounds-Korrektur (wie gehabt)
        let adjustedBounds = {
            sw: { lat: bounds.getSouth(), lng: bounds.getWest() },
            ne: { lat: bounds.getNorth(), lng: bounds.getEast() }
        };
        
        const extendedBounds = boundingExtend(adjustedBounds.sw, adjustedBounds.ne, 500);
        const apiZoom = Math.round(map.getZoom()) - 2;
        
        const api1Url = `/realtime_ais.php?type=json&minlat=${extendedBounds.swLat}&maxlat=${extendedBounds.neLat}&minlon=${extendedBounds.swLng}&maxlon=${extendedBounds.neLng}&zoom=${apiZoom}&selid=0&seltype=0&timecode=-1&filters=${encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify({}))}`;
        
        const response = await fetch(`https://marinetraffic.live${api1Url}`, {
            signal: signal,
            cache: 'default'
        });
        
        if (!response.ok) return;
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data && data.data && data.data.rows && Array.isArray(data.data.rows)) {
            api1PositionUpdates.clear();
            
            data.data.rows.forEach(ship => {
                if (ship.SHIPNAME && ship.LAT && ship.LON && ship.ELAPSED) {
                    const shipName = ship.SHIPNAME.trim().toUpperCase()
                    // KORRIGIERT: Verwende die tatsächlichen API1 Felder
                    api1PositionUpdates.set(shipName, {
                        lat: parseFloat(ship.LAT),
                        lng: parseFloat(ship.LON),
                        elapsed: ship.ELAPSED || 999999, // Verwende ELAPSED aus API1
                        mmsi: ship.MMSI || '',
                        speed: ship.SPEED ? parseFloat(ship.SPEED) / 10 : undefined, // Speed in Zehntel-Knoten
                        course: ship.COURSE ? parseFloat(ship.COURSE) : undefined,
                        heading: ship.HEADING ? parseFloat(ship.HEADING) : undefined,
                        destination: ship.DESTINATION || undefined,
                        shiptype: ship.SHIPTYPE || undefined,
                        rot: ship.ROT ? parseFloat(ship.ROT) : undefined
                    });
                }
            });
            
            console.log(`API1: ${api1PositionUpdates.size} position updates prepared`);
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        if (error.name !== 'AbortError') {
            console.warn('API1 load failed:', error);
        }
    }
};

const updateShipsWithAPI1 = (shipsMap) => {
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    
    if (currentZoom < 8) {
        console.log(`Skipping API1 updates - zoom too low: ${currentZoom.toFixed(1)} < 8`);
        return false;
    }
    
    if (api1PositionUpdates.size === 0) {
        console.log('No API1 updates available');
        return false;
    }
    
    if (!shipsMap || shipsMap.size === 0) {
        console.log('No ships to update');
        return false;
    }
    
    console.log(`🔍 API1: Checking ${shipsMap.size} ships against ${api1PositionUpdates.size} updates`);
    
    let updatedCount = 0;
    let checkedCount = 0;
    let matchCount = 0;
    
    // Debug: Zeige alle API1 Updates
    for (const [name, update] of api1PositionUpdates.entries()) {
        console.log(`API1 has: ${name}, elapsed: ${update.elapsed}`);
    }
    
    // Durchlaufe ALLE Schiffe
    for (const [shipKey, ship] of shipsMap.entries()) {
        if (ship.name) {
            checkedCount++;
            const shipNameKey = ship.name.trim().toUpperCase();
            
            console.log(`Checking ship: ${ship.name} -> ${shipNameKey}`);
            
            if (api1PositionUpdates.has(shipNameKey)) {
                matchCount++;
                const api1Update = api1PositionUpdates.get(shipNameKey);
                const api1Elapsed = api1Update.elapsed;
                
                //console.log(`MATCH FOUND: ${ship.name}, API1 elapsed: ${api1Elapsed}`);
                
                // NUR wenn Signal frisch genug ist (<=15 Min)
                if (api1Elapsed <= 60) {
                    console.log(`✅ UPDATING: ${ship.name} - ${ship.elapsed} with API1 data`);
                    
                    // WICHTIG: Update sowohl incomingShips als auch ships Array
                    ship.lat = api1Update.lat;
                    ship.lng = api1Update.lng;
                    ship.elapsed = api1Elapsed;
                    ship.lastPositionUpdate = Date.now();
                    
                    if (api1Update.speed !== undefined) ship.speed = api1Update.speed;
                    if (api1Update.course !== undefined) ship.course = api1Update.course;
                    if (api1Update.heading !== undefined) ship.heading = api1Update.heading;
                    
                    updatedCount++;
                } else {
                    console.log(`❌ Signal too old: ${api1Elapsed} > 60`);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    console.log(`API1 Results: ${checkedCount} checked, ${matchCount} matches, ${updatedCount} updated`);
    
    // WICHTIG: Return true wenn Updates gemacht wurden
    return updatedCount > 0;
};

// Helper-Funktion für Bounds-Erweiterung (wie im Original)
function boundingExtend(sw, ne, meters) {
    const latDegPerMeter = 1 / 111000;
    const lngDegPerMeter = 1 / (111000 * Math.cos(((sw.lat + ne.lat) / 2) * Math.PI / 180));
    
    return {
        swLat: sw.lat - (meters * latDegPerMeter),
        neLat: ne.lat + (meters * latDegPerMeter),
        swLng: sw.lng - (meters * lngDegPerMeter),
        neLng: ne.lng + (meters * lngDegPerMeter)
    };
}

// Funktion zur Berechnung der Positionsdistanz
function calculatePositionDistance(lat1, lng1, lat2, lng2) {
    const R = 6371000; // Erdradius in Metern
    const dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * Math.PI / 180;
    const dLng = (lng2 - lng1) * Math.PI / 180;
    const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
              Math.cos(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) *
              Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2);
    const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a));
    return R * c; // Distanz in Metern
}

// Funktion zur Bewertung der Datenqualität basierend auf Zoom-Level und Elapsed-Zeit
function getDataQuality(apiZoom, elapsed, hasDetailedData) {
    let qualityScore = 0;
    
    // Zoom-basierte Qualität (höhere Zoom = bessere Auflösung)
    if (apiZoom >= 14) qualityScore += 100;
    else if (apiZoom >= 11) qualityScore += 75;
    else if (apiZoom >= 8) qualityScore += 50;
    else qualityScore += 25;
    
    // Elapsed-Zeit basierte Qualität (neuere Daten = bessere Qualität)
    if (elapsed !== 'N/A' && typeof elapsed === 'number') {
        if (elapsed <= 60) qualityScore += 50;      // Sehr aktuell (≤1 Min)
        else if (elapsed <= 300) qualityScore += 35; // Aktuell (≤5 Min)
        else if (elapsed <= 900) qualityScore += 20; // Mäßig aktuell (≤15 Min)
        else qualityScore += 10;                      // Alt (>15 Min)
    } else {
        qualityScore += 5; // Unbekanntes Alter
    }
    
    // Bonus für detaillierte Daten (mehr Felder verfügbar)
    if (hasDetailedData) qualityScore += 25;
    
    return qualityScore;
}

// Verbesserte Ship-Update Logik
function updateShipData(existingShip, newData, apiZoom) {
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    
        const shipNameKey = existingShip.name ? existingShip.name.trim().toUpperCase() : '';
        
        if (api1PositionUpdates.has(shipNameKey)) {
            const api1Data = api1PositionUpdates.get(shipNameKey);
            
            if (api1Data.elapsed <= 60) {
                return existingShip;
            }
        }

    const { lat, lng, speed, course, heading, destination, elapsed, shipData } = newData;
    
    // Bewerte Datenqualität
    const hasDetailedData = shipData && (shipData.SHIPNAME || shipData.DESTINATION || shipData.SHIPTYPE);
    const newQuality = getDataQuality(apiZoom, elapsed, hasDetailedData);
    const existingQuality = getDataQuality(
        existingShip.lastApiZoom || apiZoom, 
        existingShip.elapsed, 
        !!(existingShip.destination && existingShip.destination !== 'N/A')
    );
    
    // Berechne Positionsdistanz wenn beide Positionen vorhanden
    const positionDistance = calculatePositionDistance(
        existingShip.lat, existingShip.lng, lat, lng
    );
    
    // Entscheide ob Position aktualisiert werden soll
    let shouldUpdatePosition = false;
    
    if (newQuality > existingQuality + 10) {
        shouldUpdatePosition = true;
    } else if (newQuality >= existingQuality - 5) {
        if (elapsed !== 'N/A' && typeof elapsed === 'number') {
            const existingElapsed = existingShip.elapsed;
            if (existingElapsed === 'N/A' || elapsed < existingElapsed) {
                shouldUpdatePosition = true;
            }
        } else if (positionDistance < 1000) {
            shouldUpdatePosition = true;
        }
    }
    
    // Plausibilitätsprüfung für große Positionssprünge
    if (shouldUpdatePosition && positionDistance > 5000) {
        const timeSinceLastUpdate = Date.now() - existingShip.lastPositionUpdate;
        const maxPossibleDistance = (existingShip.speed || 20) * 0.514444 * (timeSinceLastUpdate / 1000);
        
        if (positionDistance > maxPossibleDistance * 3) {
            if (newQuality <= existingQuality + 25) {
                shouldUpdatePosition = false;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Aktualisiere Schiffsdaten
    if (shouldUpdatePosition) {
        existingShip.lat = lat;
        existingShip.lng = lng;
        existingShip.lastPositionUpdate = Date.now();
        existingShip.lastApiZoom = apiZoom;
        
    }
	
    // Andere Daten immer aktualisieren wenn besser oder ähnlich
    if (newQuality >= existingQuality - 10) {
        existingShip.speed = speed;
        existingShip.course = course;
        existingShip.heading = heading;
        
        if (destination && destination !== 'N/A') {
            existingShip.destination = destination;
        }
        
        if (elapsed !== 'N/A') {
            existingShip.elapsed = elapsed;
        }
    }
    
    existingShip.lastSeen = Date.now();
    existingShip.dataQuality = Math.max(existingShip.dataQuality || 0, newQuality);
    
    return existingShip;
}

function filterShipsByPerformanceOnly(allShips, MaxShips) {
    if (allShips.length <= MaxShips) {
        return allShips;
    }
	
	const center = map.getCenter();
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
	
    // Canvas Center Berechnung (aus den Rendering-Funktionen)
    var canvasCenter = {
        x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
        y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1)))
    };
    
    if(isLowEndDevice){
        canvasCenter = {
            x: shipCanvas.width / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1))),
            y: shipCanvas.height / (2 * (isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 0.5) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1)))
        };
    }

    const prioritizedShips = allShips.map(ship => {
        const point = ship._projectedPoint || map.project([ship.lng, ship.lat]);
        const distanceFromCenter = Math.sqrt(
            Math.pow(point.x - canvasCenter.x, 2) +
            Math.pow(point.y - canvasCenter.y, 2)
        );

        
		let priority = 0;

        // Höchste Priorität: Selected/Hovered ships (aus allen Funktionen)
        if (ship === selectedShip) priority += 10000;
        if (ship === hoveredShip) priority += 5000;

        // Bewegende Schiffe (aus Rendering-Funktionen)
        if (ship.speed > 1) priority += 500;

        // Große Schiffe (vereinfacht aus Original und Rendering)
        const shipLength = parseFloat(ship.length) || parseFloat(ship.vsl_length) || 50;
        if (shipLength > 300) priority += 800;
        else if (shipLength > 200) priority += 500;
        else if (shipLength > 100) priority += 200;

        // Schiffstyp-Priorität (aus Original)
        const shipType = ship.type || '0';
        switch(shipType) {
			case '1': priority += 1000; break; // Navigation
			case '2': priority += 300; break; // Fishing
			case '3': priority += 500; break; // Tug
			case '4': priority += 300; break; // Speedboat
			case '6': priority += 400; break; // Passenger
			case '7': priority += 400; break; // Cargo
			case '8': priority += 400; break; // Tanker
			case '9': priority += 300; break; // Yacht
            default: priority += 100;
        }

        // Zoom-abhängige Priorität (aus Rendering-Funktionen)
        if (zoom > 8) {
            priority += 300; // Bei hohem Zoom: Alle Schiffe wichtig
        } else {
            if (ship.speed < 0.1) priority += 200; // Stationäre Schiffe bei niedrigem Zoom wichtiger
        }

        // Signal-Alter (aus Original)
        if (ship.elapsed !== undefined && ship.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
            const elapsedMinutes = parseInt(ship.elapsed) || 0;
            if (elapsedMinutes < 5) priority += 200; // Live signals
            else if (elapsedMinutes < 30) priority += 100; // Recent signals
            else if (elapsedMinutes > 120) priority -= 200; // Old signals
        }

        ship._filterPriority = priority;
        return ship;
    });

    // Sortiere nach Priorität und nimm die besten
    prioritizedShips.sort((a, b) => b._filterPriority - a._filterPriority);
    const result = prioritizedShips.slice(0, MaxShips);
    
    // Cleanup
    result.forEach(ship => {
        delete ship._filterPriority;
    });
    
    return result;
}

    // KRITISCH: Alle Schiffslisten komplett leeren
    ships = [];
    masterShipList.clear();
    incomingShips.clear();
    api1PositionUpdates.clear();
    
    // Canvas sofort leeren für visuelles Feedback
    if (shipCanvas && shipCtx) {
        const pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
        shipCtx.clearRect(0, 0, shipCanvas.width, shipCanvas.height);
    }
    
    // Prüfe ob alle Filter deaktiviert sind
    const allFiltersDisabled = Object.values(activeShipTypeFilters).every(value => value === false);
    
    if (allFiltersDisabled) {
        console.log('🔍 Alle Filter deaktiviert - keine Schiffe anzeigen');
        needsRedraw = true;
        drawShips();
        return;
    }
    
        loadRealShips();
        needsRedraw = true;
        drawShips();
}

// Event Listeners Setup - KORRIGIERT
function setupFilterEventListeners() {
    // BESTEHENDE LOGIK FÜR ALLE FILTER-CHECKBOXEN (inkl. Status-Filter!)
    document.querySelectorAll('.filter-checkbox').forEach(checkbox => {
        // Entferne alte Event Listeners
        checkbox.removeEventListener('change', handleFilterChange);
        
        // Füge neuen Event Listener hinzu
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
            handleFilterChange(this);
        });
    });

    // Menu schließen wenn außerhalb geklickt wird
    document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
        const layerMenu = document.getElementById('layerControlMenu');
        const layerButton = document.getElementById('layerControlButton');
        
        if (layerMenu && layerButton && !layerMenu.contains(event.target) && !layerButton.contains(event.target)) {
            layerMenu.classList.remove('active');
            layerButton.classList.remove('layerButton-active');
        }
    });
    
    console.log('🎛️ Filter Event Listeners eingerichtet (inkl. Status-Filter)');
}

// Filter Menu Toggle
function toggleFilterMenu() {
    const menu = document.getElementById('filterControlMenu');
    const button = document.getElementById('filterButton');
    
    if (menu && button) {
        const isActive = menu.classList.toggle('active');
        
        // NUR diesen Button stylen
        if (isActive) {
            button.classList.add('filterButton-active');
        } else {
            button.classList.remove('filterButton-active');
        }
        
        console.log('🎛️ Filter Menu', isActive ? 'geöffnet' : 'geschlossen');
    }
}
