    };
}

// FIXED: Sichere updateHoverDisplay Funktion mit Null-Checks
function updateHoverDisplay(ship, isLoading = false) {
   // KRITISCHE NULL-CHECKS
   if (!ship || typeof ship !== 'object') {
       console.log('updateHoverDisplay: Invalid ship object');
       return;
   }
   
   const currentShipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
   if (!currentShipInfo || currentShipInfo.style.display === 'none') {
       return; // Hover-Info ist nicht mehr sichtbar
   }
   
   // Prüfe ob das noch das gleiche gehöverte Schiff ist
   if (!hoveredShip || 
       (ship.mmsi && hoveredShip.mmsi !== ship.mmsi) ||
       (ship.shipId && hoveredShip.shipId !== ship.shipId) ||
       (!ship.mmsi && !ship.shipId && hoveredShip.name !== ship.name)) {
       return; // Anderes Schiff wird jetzt gehövert
   }
   
   // FIXED: Sichere String-Formatierung mit Fallbacks
   var shipName = ship.name || 'N/A Ship';
   const shipSpeed = (ship.speed !== undefined && ship.speed !== null) ? parseFloat(ship.speed).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
   const shipCourse = (ship.course !== undefined && ship.course !== null) ? parseInt(ship.course) : 0;
   const shipType = getShipTypeName(ship.type) || 'N/A';
   const destination = formatDestination(ship.destination) || 'Unbekannt';
         signalAge = 'LIVE';
   
   try {
       currentShipInfo.innerHTML = 
           '<strong>' + shipName + '</strong><br>' +
           'Tempo: ' + shipSpeed + ' kn<br>' +
           'Kurs: ' + shipCourse + '°<br>' +
           'Typ: ' + shipType + '<br>' +
           'Ziel: ' + destination + '<br>' +
           'Signal: ' + signalAge + '';
           
   } catch (error) {
       console.error('Error updating hover display:', error);
   }}0

// FIXED: Erweiterte mousemove Handler mit besserer Fehlerbehandlung
map.on('mousemove', function(e) {
    // Existing movement checks...
    if (isMapMoving || isZoomTransition) {
        return;
    }

    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    let REDRAW_THROTTLE = currentZoom <= 3 ? 250 : 150;

    const point = e.point;
    const shipAtPosition = getShipAtPosition(point.x, point.y);

    let newHoveredShipKey = null;
    if (shipAtPosition) {
        newHoveredShipKey = shipAtPosition.mmsi || shipAtPosition.shipId ||
            `${shipAtPosition.name}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lat*1000)}_${Math.round(shipAtPosition.lng*1000)}`;
    }

    if (newHoveredShipKey !== lastHoveredShipKey) {
        const previousHoveredShip = hoveredShip;
        hoveredShip = shipAtPosition;
        lastHoveredShipKey = newHoveredShipKey;

        const now = performance.now();
        if (now - lastRedrawTime > REDRAW_THROTTLE) {
            if (hoveredShip !== previousHoveredShip) {
                needsRedraw = true;
                lastRedrawTime = now;
            }
        }

        if (hoveredShip) {
            map.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';
        } else {
           map.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';
        }
    }

    // VEREINFACHT: Hover-Info DIREKT anzeigen ohne API Call
    const shipInfo = document.getElementById('ship-info');
    if (shipInfo && hoveredShip && window.innerWidth >= 1200) {
        try {
            // DIREKT anzeigen mit verfügbaren Daten
            updateHoverDisplay(hoveredShip);
            
            // Tooltip positionieren
            shipInfo.style.display = 'block';
            shipInfo.style.left = (e.originalEvent.clientX + 10) + 'px';
            shipInfo.style.top = (e.originalEvent.clientY - 10) + 'px';
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error in mousemove hover handling:', error);
            if (shipInfo) {
                shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    } else if (shipInfo) {
        shipInfo.style.display = 'none';
    }
});

let markerShipDetailsPosition = null;
let updatePosition = false;
let firstFlyTo = false;
let flyToZoom = 8.1;
let flyToZoom2 = 8.1;
let check = false;
let satShip = null;
let currentShip = null;
let trackingPosition = null;
let shouldCenterMap = false;

function isAtSea(lat, lon) {
    if (lat < -60 || lat > 80) return true;
    if (lon < -170 || lon > 170) return true;
    if (Math.abs(lat) < 60 && Math.abs(lon) > 20) return true;
    return false;
}

function areEqual(var1, var2, isAtSea) {
    const s1 = parseFloat(var1);
    const s2 = parseFloat(var2);
    const tolerance = isAtSea ? 0.5	: 0.001;
	flyToZoom = isAtSea ? Math.max(map.getZoom(), 8.1) : Math.max(map.getZoom(), 11.1);
	flyToZoom2 = isAtSea ? Math.max(map.getZoom(), 8.1) : Math.max(map.getZoom(), 11.1);
    const difference = Math.abs(s1 - s2);
    //console.log(`🌊 areEqual(): ${s1} vs ${s2}, diff=${difference}, tol=${tolerance}, isAtSea=${isAtSea}`);
    return difference <= tolerance;
}

function areEqual2(var1, var2, isAtSea) {
    const s1 = parseFloat(var1);
    const s2 = parseFloat(var2);
    const tolerance = isAtSea ? 0.5	: 0.05;
	flyToZoom = isAtSea ? Math.max(map.getZoom(), 8.1) : Math.max(map.getZoom(), 11.1);
	flyToZoom2 = isAtSea ? Math.max(map.getZoom(), 8.1) : Math.max(map.getZoom(), 11.1);
    const difference = Math.abs(s1 - s2);
    //console.log(`🌊 areEqual(): ${s1} vs ${s2}, diff=${difference}, tol=${tolerance}, isAtSea=${isAtSea}`);
    return difference <= tolerance;
}

function areEqualSpeed(var1, var2, tolerance = 10.0) {
    const s1 = parseFloat(var1);
    const s2 = parseFloat(var2);
    
    const difference = Math.abs(s1 - s2);
    
    return difference <= tolerance;
}

async function loadShipDetailsFromAPI(ship, shouldCenterMap = false) {
    console.log('=== loadShipDetailsFromAPI CALLED ===');
    console.log('Ship object:', ship);
    console.log('shouldCenterMap:', shouldCenterMap); // DEBUG
	
    const content = document.getElementById('shipDetailContent');
    if (!content) {
        console.error('Ship detail content element not found');
        return;
    }

    try {
        let apiData = null;
        let shipId = ship.shipId;

        // API Daten laden (wie gehabt)...
        if (!shipId && ship.mmsi) {
            console.log('NO shipId found, calling getShipIdFromMMSI...');
            try {
                shipId = await getShipIdFromMMSI(ship.mmsi);
                console.log('getShipIdFromMMSI returned:', shipId);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error getting shipId from MMSI:', error);
            }
        }

        if (shipId) {
		if(shipId.length >= 15 && localStorage.getItem('shipId') >=1)
		shipId = localStorage.getItem('shipId');
		
            try {
        const originalUrl = `https://marinetraffic.com/de/ais/get_info_window_json?asset_type=ship&id=${shipId}`;
        const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
        const detailUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
        
        const response = await fetch(detailUrl, {
			headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
            }
        });

                if (response.ok) {
                    const responseText = await response.text();
                    
                    if (responseText && !responseText.trim().startsWith('<')) {
                        try {
                            apiData = JSON.parse(responseText);
                            console.log('Ship details loaded successfully for Ship-ID:', shipId);
                        } catch (parseError) {
                            console.error('JSON parse error:', parseError);
                            apiData = null;
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.error('Received HTML instead of JSON');
                    }
                } else {
                    console.error('Ship details API error:', response.status, response.statusText);
                }
            } catch (detailError) {
                console.error('Error fetching ship details:', detailError);
            }
        }	

        // Ship object mit API Daten erweitern
        if (apiData && apiData.values) {	
            const values = apiData.values;
            satShip = await getSatShipPositionFromDetails(values.mmsi);	
			satShip2 = await getSatShipPositionFromDetails2(shipId);
            let calculatedElapsed = 'N/A';
            if (ship.elapsed && values.elapsed !== 'N/A') {
                const elapsedTimestamp = parseInt(ship.elapsed);
                if (!isNaN(elapsedTimestamp)) {
                    const currentTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                    const elapsedMinutes = Math.floor((currentTime - elapsedTimestamp) / 60);
                    calculatedElapsed = elapsedMinutes >= 0 ? elapsedMinutes : 'N/A';
                }
            }
            
            if (calculatedElapsed === 'N/A' && values.last_pos && values.last_pos !== 'N/A') {
                const lastPosTimestamp = parseInt(values.last_pos);
                if (!isNaN(lastPosTimestamp)) {
                    const currentTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                    const elapsedMinutes = Math.floor((currentTime - lastPosTimestamp) / 60);
                    calculatedElapsed = elapsedMinutes >= 0 ? elapsedMinutes : 'N/A';
                }
            }
			
			shipData = [];
		
		if(satShip && satShip2 && satShip[0].elapsed <= satShip2[0].elapsed) {
            ship = Object.assign({}, ship, {
                lat: satShip[0].lat || parseFloat(values.ship_lat),
                lng: satShip[0].lng || parseFloat(values.ship_lon),
                speed: satShip[0].speed / 10 || parseFloat(values.speed) || ship.speed || 0,
                course: satShip[0].course|| parseFloat(values.course) || ship.course || 0,
                heading: parseFloat(values.heading) || ship.heading || ship.course || 0,
                name: values.shipname || ship.name,
                type: values.ship_type || ship.type,
                destination: values.dest_rep || values.destination || ship.destination,
                shipId: shipId,
                imo: values.imo,
				mmsi:values.mmsi,
                flag: values.flag,
                length: values.vsl_length || ship.length,
                dwt: values.dwt,
                draught: values.draught || values.draft,
                last_pos: values.last_pos,
                elapsed: satShip[0].elapsed || calculatedElapsed
            });
		} else if(satShip && satShip2 && satShip[0].elapsed >= satShip2[0].elapsed) {
			
            ship = Object.assign({}, ship, {
                lat: satShip2[0].lat || parseFloat(values.ship_lat),
                lng: satShip2[0].lng || parseFloat(values.ship_lon),
                speed: satShip2[0].speed / 10 || parseFloat(values.speed) || ship.speed || 0,
                course: satShip2[0].course|| parseFloat(values.course) || ship.course || 0,
                heading: parseFloat(values.heading) || ship.heading || ship.course || 0,
                name: values.shipname || ship.name,
                type: values.ship_type || ship.type,
                destination: values.dest_rep || values.destination || ship.destination,
                shipId: shipId,
                imo: values.imo,
				mmsi:values.mmsi,
                flag: values.flag,
                length: values.vsl_length || ship.length,
                dwt: values.dwt,
                draught: values.draught || values.draft,
                last_pos: values.last_pos,
                elapsed: satShip2[0].elapsed || calculatedElapsed
            });
		} else {
            ship = Object.assign({}, ship, {
                lat: parseFloat(values.ship_lat) || ship.lat,
                lng: parseFloat(values.ship_lon) || ship.lng,
                speed: parseFloat(values.speed) || ship.speed || 0,
                course: parseFloat(values.course) || ship.course || 0,
                heading: parseFloat(values.heading) || ship.heading || ship.course || 0,
                name: values.shipname || ship.name,
                type: values.ship_type || ship.type,
                destination: values.dest_rep || values.destination || ship.destination,
                shipId: shipId,
                imo: values.imo,
                flag: values.flag,
                length: values.vsl_length || ship.length,
                dwt: values.dwt,
                draught: values.draught || values.draft,
                last_pos: values.last_pos,
                elapsed: calculatedElapsed
            });
		}
			
			shipData.push(ship);

				markerShipDetailsPosition = {
					lat: ship.lat,
					lng: ship.lng 
				};
				
            console.log('Updated ship object with Ship-ID:', shipId);
            console.log('💾 Ship Details Position gespeichert:', markerShipDetailsPosition);
        } else {
            markerShipDetailsPosition = {
                lat: ship.lat,
                lng: ship.lng
            };
            console.log('💾 Fallback Position gespeichert:', markerShipDetailsPosition);
        }

        let shipLat = ship.lat;
        let shipLng = ship.lng;
        
        selectedShip = ship;
        
        if (searchSelectedShip) {
            searchSelectedShip.lat = shipLat;
            searchSelectedShip.lng = shipLng;
            searchSelectedShip.speed = ship.speed;
            searchSelectedShip.course = ship.course;
            searchSelectedShip.heading = ship.heading;
            searchSelectedShip.destination = ship.destination;
            searchSelectedShip.type = ship.type;
            searchSelectedShip.shipId = shipId;
            searchSelectedShip.imo = ship.imo;
            searchSelectedShip.mmsi = ship.mmsi;
			searchSelectedShip.elapsed = ship.elapsed;
        }
        
		
        searchSelectedPosition = {
            lat: shipLat,
            lng: shipLng
        };
		
		if(apiData)
		localStorage.setItem('shipName', apiData.values.shipname.toUpperCase());
		localStorage.setItem('shipId', shipId);
		localStorage.setItem('mmsi', ship.mmsi);
		localStorage.setItem('imo', ship.imo);
		localStorage.setItem('type', ship.imo);
		localStorage.setItem('destination', ship.destination);
		localStorage.setItem('speed', ship.speed);
		localStorage.setItem('speed2', parseFloat(apiData.values.speed));
		localStorage.setItem('course', ship.course);
		localStorage.setItem('length', apiData.values.vsl_length)
		
		if(satShip)
		localStorage.setItem('speed', satShip[0].speed);
		localStorage.setItem('speed2', ship.speed);
		localStorage.setItem('course', satShip[0].course);
		localStorage.setItem('elapsed', satShip[0].elapsed);
		localStorage.setItem('elapsed2', satShip[0].elapsed);
		localStorage.setItem('length', apiData.values.vsl_length);	
		
    const trackingShip = searchSelectedShip || clickedShip || selectedShip;
		  trackingPosition = searchSelectedPosition;
    
    if (!trackingShip || !trackingPosition) {
        return false;
    }
    
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    // Live Position aus ships array verwenden
    currentShip = ships.find(ship => {
		const sea = isAtSea(ship.lat, ship.lng);
        // FIX: Erweiterte Suche mit mehreren Kriterien
        if (ship.shipId && ship.shipId === trackingShip.shipId && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === trackingShip.mmsi && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship.shipId && ship.shipId === (selectedShip?.shipId) && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === (selectedShip?.mmsi) && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
		if (areEqual(trackingShip.lat.toFixed(4), ship.lat.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqual(trackingShip.lng.toFixed(4), ship.lng.toFixed(4), sea) && trackingShip.type == ship.type && trackingShip.name == ship.name) {
			return true;
		}
        if (satShip && areEqual(satShip[0].lat.toFixed(4), ship.lat.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqual(satShip[0].lng.toFixed(4), ship.lng.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqualSpeed(trackingShip.speed, ship.speed) && trackingShip.name != ship.name && trackingShip.type == ship.type && ship.name === '[SAT-AIS]') {
			trackingPosition.lat = ship.lat;
			trackingPosition.lng = ship.lng;		
			searchSelectedShip.name = localStorage.getItem('shipName');
			searchSelectedShip.speed = localStorage.getItem('speed');	
			searchSelectedShip.course = localStorage.getItem('course');
			searchSelectedShip.elapsed = localStorage.getItem('elapsed');	
			searchSelectedShip.length = localStorage.getItem('length');
			searchSelectedShip.destination = localStorage.getItem('destination');			
			return true;
        }	
        return false;
    });

    if (currentShip) {
        // FIX: Aktualisiere IMMER die Position für Marker-Anzeige
        trackingPosition.lat = currentShip.lat;
        trackingPosition.lng = currentShip.lng;
	}
	
        // KRITISCH: Nur FlyTo wenn shouldCenterMap = true
        if (shouldCenterMap) {		
            console.log('✈️ FlyTo wird ausgeführt - shouldCenterMap = true');
            isFlying = true; 
			    map.flyTo({
                center: [shipLng, shipLat],
                zoom: flyToZoom,
                duration: 1000,
            });
			
			setTimeout(function() {
			updatePosition = true;	
			check = true;
			clearTimeout(timeout);
			timeout = setTimeout(function() {
			updatePosition = false;
			check = false;
			}, 6000);
			}, 1000);
        } else{
            console.log('🚫 FlyTo übersprungen - shouldCenterMap = false');		
			updatePosition = false;
		}
			
		
        
        // Ship Details anzeigen
        displayShipDetails(ship, apiData);
		
        // Hafendaten laden - hole MMSI und IMO aus dem DOM
        const detailItems = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-item');
        let mmsi = '';
        let imo = '';
        
        detailItems.forEach(item => {
            const label = item.querySelector('.detail-label')?.textContent;
            if (label === 'MMSI') {
                mmsi = item.querySelector('.detail-value')?.textContent || '';
            }
            if (label === 'IMO') {
                imo = item.querySelector('.detail-value')?.textContent || '';
            }
        });
        
        console.log('📋 MMSI aus DOM:', mmsi, 'IMO:', imo);
        
        if (mmsi) {
            // Erst alte Ports-Section entfernen falls vorhanden
            const oldPortsSection = document.querySelector('.ports-section');
            if (oldPortsSection) {
                oldPortsSection.remove();
            }
            
            const portsHtml = await loadLastPorts(mmsi);
            const detailContent = document.getElementById('shipDetailContent');
            if (detailContent && portsHtml) {
                // Finde die ship-details-grid Section
                const shipDetailsSection = detailContent.querySelector('.ship-detail-section:has(.ship-details-grid)');
                if (shipDetailsSection) {
                    shipDetailsSection.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', portsHtml);
                } else {
                    // Fallback: nach voyage-section oder am Ende
                    const voyageSection = detailContent.querySelector('.voyage-section');
                    if (voyageSection) {
                        voyageSection.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', portsHtml);
                    } else {
                        detailContent.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', portsHtml);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
		
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error in loadShipDetailsFromAPI:', error);
        displayShipDetails(ship, null);
    }
}

async function loadLastPorts(mmsi) {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`https://marinetraffic.live/sat_api.php/pro/pcext/v4/${mmsi}`);
        const ports = await response.json();
        
        if (!ports || ports.length === 0) {
            return '<p style="padding: 10px; color: #7f8c8d; text-align: center;">Keine Hafendaten verfügbar</p>';
        }
        
        let html = '<div class="ship-detail-section ports-section" style="padding-top: 20px;">';
        html += '<h4 style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-weight: 500; color:#2c3e50;">Letzte Häfen</h4>';
        html += '<div class="ports-table">';
        
        // Zeige ALLE Häfen an (nicht mehr auf 5 begrenzt)
        for (const port of ports) {
			var portName = port.dp;
            // Erstelle die Port-URL (entferne die Zahlen am Ende)
            const portCode = port.l.replace(/\d+$/, '').toLowerCase(); // Entfernt 001, 200, 300 etc.
            const portNameUrl = portName
                .toLowerCase()
                .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
                .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '');
            
            const portUrl = '/ports/' + portNameUrl.toLowerCase() + '-port/' + portCode
                                                                         
            // Hole die Flagge des Landes
            const countryCode = getCountryCode(port.c);
            const flagUrl = countryCode !== 'UN' 
                ? `https://www.marinetraffic.com/img/flags/png40/${countryCode}.png`
                : 'https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png';
            
            // Prüfe ob Hafen verlinkt werden soll (s: 3 bedeutet nicht verlinken)
            const isLinkable = port.s !== 3;
            const portNameHtml = isLinkable 
                ? `<a onclick="isLoadingShipFromURL= false; handleURLShip('0','${portCode}', '${portName}');"  class="port-name">${port.dp}</a>`
                : `<span class="port-name-static">${port.dp}</span>`;
            
            html += `
                <div class="port-row">
                    <div class="port-info2 notranslate">
                        <img loading="lazy" class="port-flag" src="${flagUrl}" alt="${port.c}">
                        ${portNameHtml}
                    </div>
                    <div class="port-time">
                        <span class="port-ata">${port.a}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        html += '</div></div>';

        // Füge Smooth Scroll Handler hinzu nachdem HTML eingefügt wurde
        setTimeout(() => {
            const portsTable = document.getElementById('portsTableScroll');
            if (portsTable) {
                let isScrolling = false;
                let startY = 0;
                let scrollTop = 0;
                
                portsTable.addEventListener('wheel', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    // Reduziere die Scroll-Geschwindigkeit (0.3 = 30% der normalen Geschwindigkeit)
                    const delta = e.deltaY * 0.3;
                    portsTable.scrollTop += delta;
                }, { passive: false });
            }
        }, 100);
        
        return html;
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.warn('Fehler beim Laden der Hafendaten:', error);
        return '';
    }
}

// Hilfsfunktion um Ländercodes zu ermitteln
function getCountryCode(countryName) {
    const countryCodes = {
        'Netherlands': 'NL',
        'Norway': 'NO',
        'United Kingdom (UK)': 'GB',
        'Germany': 'DE',
        'Denmark': 'DK',
        'Sweden': 'SE',
        'Belgium': 'BE',
        'France': 'FR',
        'Spain': 'ES',
        'Italy': 'IT',
        'Poland': 'PL',
        'Finland': 'FI',
        'Portugal': 'PT',
        'Greece': 'GR',
        'Ireland': 'IE',
        'Estonia': 'EE',
        'Latvia': 'LV',
        'Lithuania': 'LT',
        'Iceland': 'IS',
        'Malta': 'MT',
        'Cyprus': 'CY',
        'Croatia': 'HR',
        'Slovenia': 'SI',
        'Romania': 'RO',
        'Bulgaria': 'BG',
        'Turkey': 'TR',
        'Russia': 'RU',
        'USA': 'US',
        'Canada': 'CA',
        'China': 'CN',
        'Japan': 'JP',
        'South Korea': 'KR',
        'Singapore': 'SG',
        'United Arab Emirates': 'AE',
        'Saudi Arabia': 'SA',
        'India': 'IN',
        'Australia': 'AU',
        'New Zealand': 'NZ',
        'Brazil': 'BR',
        'Argentina': 'AR',
        'Chile': 'CL',
        'Mexico': 'MX',
        'South Africa': 'ZA',
        'Egypt': 'EG',
        'Morocco': 'MA',
        'Algeria': 'DZ',
        'Tunisia': 'TN',
        'Israel': 'IL',
        'Ukraine': 'UA'
    };
    
    return countryCodes[countryName] || 'UN';
}

let lastUpdateSearchMarker = 0;
async function updateSearchMarkerToShipPosition() {	
    const now = Date.now();
    if (now - lastUpdateSearchMarker < 1000) {
        return false;
    }
    lastUpdateSearchMarker = now;
    
    // FIX: Prüfe sowohl searchSelectedShip als auch clickedShip
    const trackingShip = searchSelectedShip || clickedShip || selectedShip;
		  trackingPosition = searchSelectedPosition;
    
    if (!trackingShip || !trackingPosition) {
        return false;
    }
	
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    // Live Position aus ships array verwenden
    currentShip = ships.find(ship => {
		const sea = isAtSea(ship.lat, ship.lng);
        // FIX: Erweiterte Suche mit mehreren Kriterien
        if (ship && satShip && ship.shipId && ship.shipId === trackingShip.shipId && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship && satShip && ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === trackingShip.mmsi && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship && satShip && ship.shipId && ship.shipId === (selectedShip?.shipId) && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
        if (ship && satShip && ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === (selectedShip?.mmsi) && satShip[0].elapsed >= ship.elapsed && ship.name != '[SAT-AIS]') {
            return true;
        }
		if (ship && trackingShip && areEqual2(trackingShip.lat.toFixed(4), ship.lat.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqual2(trackingShip.lng.toFixed(4), ship.lng.toFixed(4), sea) && ship.name == trackingShip.name) {
			return true;
		}
		if (ship && trackingShip && areEqual(trackingShip.lat.toFixed(4), ship.lat.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqual(trackingShip.lng.toFixed(4), ship.lng.toFixed(4), sea) && trackingShip.type == ship.type && trackingShip.name == ship.name) {
			return true;
		}
        if (satShip && areEqual(satShip[0].lat.toFixed(4), ship.lat.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqual(satShip[0].lng.toFixed(4), ship.lng.toFixed(4), sea) && areEqualSpeed(trackingShip.speed, ship.speed) && trackingShip.name != ship.name && trackingShip.type == ship.type && ship.name === '[SAT-AIS]') {
			trackingPosition.lat = ship.lat;
			trackingPosition.lng = ship.lng;	
			searchSelectedShip.name = localStorage.getItem('shipName');
			searchSelectedShip.speed = localStorage.getItem('speed');	
			searchSelectedShip.course = localStorage.getItem('course');
			searchSelectedShip.elapsed = localStorage.getItem('elapsed');	
			searchSelectedShip.length = localStorage.getItem('length');
			searchSelectedShip.destination = localStorage.getItem('destination');			
			return true;
        }
        return false;
    });
        
    if (currentShip) {
        // FIX: Aktualisiere IMMER die Position für Marker-Anzeige
        trackingPosition.lat = currentShip.lat;
        trackingPosition.lng = currentShip.lng;

 		if (updatePosition == true) {		
        map.flyTo({
			center: [currentShip.lng, currentShip.lat],
			zoom: flyToZoom2,
			duration: 1000,
            });		
		if(check == true) {
		setTimeout(function() {
		updatePosition = false;
		check = false;
		localStorage.setItem('elapsed2', 999999);
		}, 1500);	
		}
		}

        if (searchSelectedShip) {
            searchSelectedShip.lat = currentShip.lat;
            searchSelectedShip.lng = currentShip.lng;
            searchSelectedShip.speed = currentShip.speed;
            searchSelectedShip.course = currentShip.course;
            searchSelectedShip.heading = currentShip.heading;
            searchSelectedShip.destination = currentShip.destination;
			searchSelectedShip.length = currentShip.length;
			searchSelectedShip.name = currentShip.name;
			searchSelectedShip.elapsed = currentShip.elapsed;
			searchSelectedShip.shipId = localStorage.getItem('shipId');
			searchSelectedShip.mmsi = localStorage.getItem('mmsi');
		}
		
        needsRedraw = true;
        return true;		
		
    } else {
        return false;
    }
}

// Touch events for mobile
let touchHoldTimer = null;
let touchStartTime = 0;
let touchStartPos = null;

map.on('touchstart', function(e) {
        if (typeof isDistanceMeasureActive !== 'undefined' && isDistanceMeasureActive) {
            return
        }

        if (typeof isRoutingMode !== 'undefined' && isRoutingMode) {
            return;
        }
   if (e.originalEvent.touches.length === 1) {
       const touch = e.originalEvent.touches[0];
       const rect = map.getCanvas().getBoundingClientRect();
       const touchPoint = {
           x: touch.clientX - rect.left,
           y: touch.clientY - rect.top
       };

       const shipAtPosition = getShipAtPosition(touchPoint.x, touchPoint.y);

       if (shipAtPosition) {
           touchStartTime = Date.now();
           touchStartPos = touchPoint;

       }
   }
});

map.on('touchend', function(e) {
   if (touchHoldTimer) {
       clearTimeout(touchHoldTimer);
       touchHoldTimer = null;
   }

   if (touchStartPos && e.originalEvent.changedTouches.length > 0) {
       const touchDuration = Date.now() - touchStartTime;
       const touch = e.originalEvent.changedTouches[0];
       const rect = map.getCanvas().getBoundingClientRect();
       const touchEndPoint = {
           x: touch.clientX - rect.left,
           y: touch.clientY - rect.top
       };

       const touchDistance = Math.sqrt(
           Math.pow(touchEndPoint.x - touchStartPos.x, 2) +
           Math.pow(touchEndPoint.y - touchStartPos.y, 2)
       );

       if (touchDuration < 300 && touchDistance < 10) {
           const tappedShip = getShipAtPosition(touchEndPoint.x, touchEndPoint.y);
           if (tappedShip) {
               selectedShip = tappedShip;
               showShipDetails(tappedShip);

               if (navigator.vibrate) {
                   navigator.vibrate(30);
               }
           }
       }
   }

   touchStartPos = null;
});

function formatDestination(destination) {
   if (!destination || destination === 'N/A' || destination.trim() === '') {
       return 'Unbekannt';
   }
   
   // Kürzen falls zu lang
   if (destination.length > 20) {
       return destination.substring(0, 17) + '...';
   }
   
   return destination;
}

// Ship details functions
async function getShipIdFromMMSI(identifier) {
    try {
        console.log('=== getShipIdFromIdentifier START ===');
        console.log('Identifier parameter:', identifier, 'Type:', typeof identifier);
        
        // Bestimme ob es MMSI (9 Ziffern) oder IMO (7 Ziffern) ist
        let searchTerm = '';
        if (identifier && identifier.length === 7) {
            searchTerm = identifier;
            console.log('Searching by IMO:', identifier);
        } else {
            searchTerm = identifier;
            console.log('Searching by MMSI:', identifier);
        }
        
        const originalUrl = 'https://www.marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search/?types=1,3,7,9,2&dataset=full&term=' + searchTerm.toUpperCase();
        const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
        const searchUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
        
        const response = await fetch(searchUrl, {
            headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
            }
        });
        
        const data = await response.json();
        console.log('Response data:', data);
        
        if (data.results && data.results.length > 0) {
            const firstResult = data.results[0];
            console.log('First result:', firstResult);
            
            // Prüfe ob Result-Type passt oder einfach ID vorhanden ist
            if (firstResult.id) {
                console.log('=== SHIP ID FOUND: ' + firstResult.id + ' ===');
                return firstResult.id.toString();
            }
        }
        
        console.log('=== NO SHIP ID FOUND ===');
        return null;
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('=== ERROR in getShipIdFromIdentifier:', error);
        return null;
    }
}

function toggleMinimize() {
   const detailWindow = document.getElementById('shipDetailWindow');
   const minimizeButton = document.getElementById('minimizeButton');

   if (detailWindow && minimizeButton) {
       if (detailWindow.classList.contains('minimized')) {
           detailWindow.classList.remove('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '−';
           localStorage.setItem('shipDetailMinimized', 'false');
       } else {
           detailWindow.classList.add('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '+';
           localStorage.setItem('shipDetailMinimized', 'true');
       }
   }
}

function loadMinimizedState() {
   const isMinimized = localStorage.getItem('shipDetailMinimized');
   const detailWindow = document.getElementById('shipDetailWindow');
   const minimizeButton = document.getElementById('minimizeButton');

   if (detailWindow && minimizeButton) {
       if (isMinimized === 'false') {
           detailWindow.classList.remove('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '−';
       } else {
           detailWindow.classList.add('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '+';
       }
   }
}

function getCurrentShipFromDetailWindow() {
    const shipDetailWindow = document.getElementById('shipDetailWindow');
    if (!shipDetailWindow || shipDetailWindow.style.display === 'none') {
        return null;
    }
    
    // ERST: Prüfe selectedShip
    if (selectedShip && selectedShip.mmsi) {
        return selectedShip;
    }
    
    // DANN: Prüfe window.searchSelectedShip (hat oft die MMSI)
    if (window.searchSelectedShip && window.searchSelectedShip.mmsi) {
        return window.searchSelectedShip;
    }
    
    // FALLBACK: Original-Logik aus main.js
    const shipName = document.getElementById('shipDetailTitle')?.textContent || '';
    const detailItems = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-item');
    let mmsi = '';
    let imo  = '';
    
    detailItems.forEach(item => {
        const label = item.querySelector('.detail-label')?.textContent;
        if (label === 'MMSI') {
            mmsi = item.querySelector('.detail-value')?.textContent || '';
        }
        if (label === 'IMO') {
            imo = item.querySelector('.detail-value')?.textContent || '';
        }
    });
    
    return {
        name: shipName,
        mmsi: mmsi,
		imo: imo,
        shipId: window.currentShipId || '',
        type: '0'
    };
}

// API FUNCTIONS
// =================================================================

async function updateSingleShipPosition(ship) {
    try {        
        // Schritt 1: Hole Ship ID über Search API
        let shipId = ship.shipId;
             
        // Schritt 2: Hole aktuelle Position über Ship Details API
        const position = await getShipPositionFromDetails(shipId);
        
        if (position) {
            // Speichere Position mit Metadaten
            fleetShipPositions.set(ship.mmsi || ship.name, {
                ...position,
                name: ship.name,
                fleetName: ship.fleetName,
                fleetId: ship.fleetId,
                mmsi: ship.mmsi,
                shipId: shipId,
                lastUpdate: Date.now(),
                type: ship.type || '0'
            });
            
        } else {
            console.warn(`⚠️ Keine Position erhalten für: ${ship.name}`);
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`❌ Fehler beim Laden von ${ship.name}:`, error);
        throw error;
    }
}

// Wartezeit zwischen Requests (in ms)
const DELAY_BETWEEN_REQUESTS = 500; // 2 Sekunden
const MAX_REQUESTS_PER_MINUTE = 99999;
let requestCount = 0;
let lastResetTime = Date.now();

async function getShipPositionFromDetails(shipId) {
    try {
        // Rate Limiting: Max 30 Requests pro Minute
        const now = Date.now();
        if (now - lastResetTime > 60000) { // 1 Minute vorbei
            requestCount = 0;
            lastResetTime = now;
        }
        
        if (requestCount >= MAX_REQUESTS_PER_MINUTE) {
            // Zu viele Requests, warte bis zur nächsten Minute
            const waitTime = 60000 - (now - lastResetTime);
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, waitTime + 1000));
            requestCount = 0;
            lastResetTime = Date.now();
        }
        
        requestCount++;
        
        // Wartezeit zwischen Requests
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, DELAY_BETWEEN_REQUESTS));
        
        const originalUrl = `https://marinetraffic.com/de/ais/get_info_window_json?asset_type=ship&id=${shipId}`;
        const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
        const detailUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&ttl=1800&key=94f3f2c0`;
        
        const response = await fetch(detailUrl, {
            headers: {
                'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
                'Referer': 'https://marinetraffic.com/'
            }
        });
        
        if (response.status === 429) {
            // Rate limit erreicht, warte länger
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10000)); // 10 Sekunden
            return getShipPositionFromDetails(shipId); // Retry
        }
        
        if (!response.ok) {
            throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
        }
        
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data && data.values) {
            const values = data.values;
            
            const lat = parseFloat(values.ship_lat);
            const lng = parseFloat(values.ship_lon);
            
            if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
                return {
                    lat: lat,
                    lng: lng,
                    speed: parseFloat(values.speed) || 0,
                    course: parseFloat(values.course) || 0,
                    lastPos: values.last_pos || null
                };
            }
        }
        
        return null;
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Error fetching ship ${shipId}:`, error.message);
        // Bei Fehler 1 Minute warten
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 60000));
        return false;
    }
}

let satData = null;

async function getSatShipPositionFromDetails(mmsi, name) {
    try {
        const originalUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/pasttrack/?getData=https://marinetraffic.live/sat_api.php/pro/track/${mmsi}/1`;

        // AbortController für Timeout erstellen
        const controller = new AbortController();
        const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 0);

        const response = await fetch(originalUrl, {
            method: 'GET',
            headers: {
                'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
                'x-access-token': 'eyJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCIsImtpZCI6ImtyRU03TTJKZDY5NWZRZ3dsOG4tYyJ9.eyJodHRwczovL21hcmluZXRyYWZmaWMuY29tL3VzZXJJZCI6Nzk1ODk3OCwiaHR0cHM6Ly9tYXJpbmV0cmFmZmljLmNvbS9lbWFpbCI6InNjaHVsemVlbnJpY28yMTRAZ21haWwuY29tIiwiaXNzIjoiaHR0cHM6Ly9hdXRoLmtwbGVyLmNvbS8iLCJzdWIiOiJnb29nbGUtb2F1dGgyfDEwMjA5Nzk2MTIzNDc1NjQyOTkzMSIsImF1ZCI6WyJodHRwczovL21hcmluZXRyYWZmaWMuY29tIiwiaHR0cHM6Ly9rcGxlci1wcm9kLmV1LmF1dGgwLmNvbS91c2VyaW5mbyJdLCJpYXQiOjE3NjAwMDgwMzcsImV4cCI6MTc2MDAwODYzNywic2NvcGUiOiJvcGVuaWQgcHJvZmlsZSBlbWFpbCBvZmZsaW5lX2FjY2VzcyIsImF6cCI6IkQyRmg2cFlpWUFTYWhNdE1XNXhTYWhFclpCa0xmMTF3In0.KXHUNIXveYaYepxXmrsHLvPcEcCffxRJGjVOA-HrKNKqZ7X_nCEx50GnHCmTEM4eaaIobkuGjSHweSWa72_bw9kZHDZHr1y40-iEFaFGR9mfgzJ8Wt_kQp5m6AvQQvHJBTUxxfsxLOzil2yOvy6dWTr9rwGJNU_Vba8e_m_CtnC_0y-1UuxG0nH8KfPVVmfW9HueZXPlwTonCXv-AWJh4HNTJ1cbfT-ygsDsgGcjM_VpdL4qjimHF3wUQkzYDKgy7u-6YBweQ0d_G8HuDOZhEFTpL7f2o5n8aJYOHQu-CY8Mk9Jzq-uTpSJNvjxEQQaoyAcDG_pwg2fgdpmcAUZTMQ'
            },
            signal: controller.signal
        });

        clearTimeout(timeoutId); // Timeout aufheben, wenn Request erfolgreich war

        if (!response.ok) {
            throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
        }

        const data = await response.json();

        if (data && data.data && data.data.length > 0) {
            const lastEntry = data.data[data.data.length - 1];
            const { latitude, longitude, course, speed, index } = lastEntry;

            const timeEnd = data.summary?.time_end || lastEntry.datetime;
            const now = new Date();
            const endTime = new Date(timeEnd);
            const elapsedMinutes = Math.round((now - endTime) / 60000);

            const result = [{
                lat: longitude*10,
                lng: latitude*10,
                course,
                speed,
                index,
                elapsed: elapsedMinutes
            }];

            return result;
        }

        // Wenn keine Daten vorhanden sind:
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            index: 0,
            elapsed: 999999
        }];

    } catch (error) {
        if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
            //console.error('❌ getSatShipPositionFromDetails Request abgebrochen (Timeout nach 5s)');
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            index: 0,
            elapsed: 999999
        }];
        } else {
            //console.error('❌ Fehler bei getSatShipPositionFromDetails:', error);
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            index: 0,
            elapsed: 999999
        }];
        }
        
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            index: 0,
            elapsed: 999999
        }];
    }
}

async function getSatShipPositionFromDetails2(shipId) {
    try {
        // Neue URL (Proxy über dein getSatPos/)
        const apiUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/getSatPos/?getData=satAIS/trackedshipid:${shipId}`;
		// AbortController für Timeout erstellen
		const controller = new AbortController();
		const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 3500);
		
        const response = await fetch(apiUrl, {
            method: 'GET',
            headers: {
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest'
            },
            timeout: 10000
        });
			
		clearTimeout(timeoutId);
	
        if (!response.ok) {
            throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
        }

        const data = await response.json();

        // Prüfen, ob Daten vorhanden sind
        if (data && data.data && Array.isArray(data.data.rows) && data.data.rows.length > 0) {
            const ship = data.data.rows[0];

            const latitude = parseFloat(ship.LAT);
            const longitude = parseFloat(ship.LON);
            const speed = parseFloat(ship.SPEED) || 0;
            const course = parseFloat(ship.COURSE) || 0;
            const elapsed = parseFloat(ship.ELAPSED);
            const shipId = parseFloat(ship.SHIP_ID);
            const status = ship.STATUS_NAME || "Unknown";

            const result = [{
                lat: latitude,
                lng: longitude,
                course,
                speed,
                status,
                elapsed,
				shipId,
            }];

            return result;
        }

        // Wenn keine Daten vorhanden sind
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            status: "No data",
            elapsed: 999999
        }];

    } catch (error) {
        return [{
            lat: 0,
            lng: 0,
            course: 0,
            speed: 0,
            status: "Error",
            elapsed: 999999
        }];
    }
}

function truncateString(str, num) {
if (str.length > num) {
return str.slice(0, num) + "...";
} else {
return str;
}
}

            '</div>';
    }

    content.innerHTML = html;

    // WICHTIG: AdSense neu laden nach DOM-Update
    setTimeout(() => {
        // Port-Code Update
        document.querySelectorAll('.port-code').forEach(el => {
            if (el.textContent.toLowerCase().includes('destination port not recognized')) {
                el.innerHTML = '🏃‍♂️ Unterwegs';
            }
        });
        
        // AdSense neu initialisieren
        try {
            // Prüfe ob Pro-User
            if (localStorage.getItem('pro') != 1 && adLoad5 <= 20) {
				if (!window.AdFraudProtection || window.AdFraudProtection.botScore < 70) {
					(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
					console.log('✅ AdSense Werbeblöcke initialisiert');
				} else {
					console.warn('Ads blocked: Bot detected');
				}            
				} else {
                // Verstecke Ad-Container für Pro-User
                const adContainer = document.getElementById('ad3');
                if (adContainer) {
                    adContainer.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.log('AdSense load error:', e);
        }
    }, 100);
}

function formatTimeSince(totalMinutes) {
    const totalSeconds = Math.floor(totalMinutes * 60);
    const days = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 86400);
    const hours = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 86400) / 3600);
    const minutes = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60);
    const seconds = totalSeconds % 60;
    
    const parts = [];
    
    if (days > 0) {
        const dayText = days === 1 ? 'Tag' : 'Tage';
        parts.push(`${days} ${dayText}`);
    }
    
    if (hours > 0) {
        const hourText = hours === 1 ? 'Stunde' : 'Stunden';
        parts.push(`${hours} ${hourText}`);
    }
    
    if (minutes > 0) {
        const minuteText = minutes === 1 ? 'Minute' : 'Minuten';
        parts.push(`${minutes} ${minuteText}`);
    }
    
    if (seconds > 0) {
        const secondText = seconds === 1 ? 'Sekunde' : 'Sekunden';
        parts.push(`${seconds} ${secondText}`);
    }
    
    if (parts.length === 0) {
        return 'vor 0 Sekunden';
    }
    
    if (parts.length === 1) {
        return `vor ${parts[0]}`;
    } else if (parts.length === 2) {
        return `vor ${parts[0]} und ${parts[1]}`;
    } else {
        const last = parts.pop();
        return `vor ${parts.join(', ')} und ${last}`;
    }
}

    window.originalLoadShipDetailsFromAPI = loadShipDetailsFromAPI;
    
    window.loadShipDetailsFromAPI = async function(ship, shouldCenterMap = false) {
        await window.originalLoadShipDetailsFromAPI(ship, shouldCenterMap);
    };
}

if (typeof window.originalShowShipDetails === 'undefined' && typeof showShipDetails !== 'undefined') {
    window.originalShowShipDetails = showShipDetails;
    
    window.showShipDetails = function(ship, fromURL = false) {
        window.originalShowShipDetails(ship, fromURL);
    };
}

// Erweitere die bestehende displayShipDetails Funktion
if (typeof window.originalDisplayShipDetails === 'undefined') {
    window.originalDisplayShipDetails = window.displayShipDetails;
}

window.displayShipDetails = function(ship, apiData) {
    // Rufe ursprüngliche Funktion auf
    if (window.originalDisplayShipDetails) {
        window.originalDisplayShipDetails(ship, apiData);
    }
};

function updatePageMetaTags(ship, values) {
    const shipName = ship.name || values.shipname || 'N/A Ship';
    
    // FIXED: Better handling of MMSI and IMO - prioritize actual values over N/A
    let shipIdentifier = '';
    let mmsi = values.mmsi || ship.mmsi || '';
    let imo = values.imo || ship.imo || '';
    
    // Clean up N/A values
    if (mmsi === 'N/A' || mmsi === 'null' || mmsi === null) mmsi = '';
    if (imo === 'N/A' || imo === 'null' || imo === null) imo = '';
    
    // Build identifier string - prefer IMO over MMSI, avoid showing N/A
    if (imo && imo !== '') {
        shipIdentifier = 'IMO: ' + imo;
    } else if (mmsi && mmsi !== '') {
        shipIdentifier = 'MMSI: ' + mmsi;
    } else {
        // Fallback: try to get from shipId or use ship type
        const shipType = getShipTypeNameFromCode(ship.type || values.ship_type) || 'Schiff';
        shipIdentifier = shipType;
    }
    
	if (ship || values) {
    const lat = (parseFloat(values.ship_lat) || ship.lat).toFixed(4);
    const lng = (parseFloat(values.ship_lon) || ship.lng).toFixed(4);
    const country = values.country || '';
    const destination = values.next_port_name || 'N/A';
	const lastdestination = values.last_port_name || 'N/A';
    const speed = (parseFloat(values.speed) || ship.speed || 0).toFixed(1);
    const status = speed < 0.1 ? 'stationär' : 'in Fahrt mit ' + speed + ' kn';
    const shipType = getShipTypeNameFromCode(ship.type || values.ship_type) || 'Schiff';
	
    // FIXED: Use clean identifier in title
    document.title = shipName + ' (' + shipIdentifier + ') - Aktuelle Position | MarineTraffic';

    let metaDescription = document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]');
    if (!metaDescription) {
        metaDescription = document.createElement('meta');
        metaDescription.name = 'description';
        document.head.appendChild(metaDescription);
    }
    
    // FIXED: Use ship type in description when identifiers are missing
    metaDescription.content = 'Das ' + shipType + ' ' + shipName +
        (country ? ' (' + country + ')' : '') +
        ' kommt von dem Hafen ' + lastdestination + ', befindet sich aktuell auf Position ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '° und ist ' + status +
        '. Der Ziehafen des Schiffes ist ' + destination + '.';

    // FIXED: Open Graph tags with better identifier handling
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:title', shipName + ' (' + shipIdentifier + ') - Aktuelle Position | MarineTraffic');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:description', 'Live Tracking von ' + shipName + 
        (shipIdentifier.includes('IMO:') || shipIdentifier.includes('MMSI:') ? ' (' + shipIdentifier + ')' : '') + 
        ' - ' + shipType + '. Aktuelle Position: ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '°. Status: ' + status);
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:type', 'website');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:url', window.location.href);

    // FIXED: Twitter tags
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:card', 'summary');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:title', shipName + ' (' + shipIdentifier + ') - Aktuelle Position');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:description', 'Live AIS Tracking: ' + shipName + ' (' + shipType + ') - Position: ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '°');

    // FIXED: Structured Data with proper identifier
    let jsonLdScript = document.querySelector('script[type="application/ld+json"]');
    if (!jsonLdScript) {
        jsonLdScript = document.createElement('script');
        jsonLdScript.type = 'application/ld+json';
        document.head.appendChild(jsonLdScript);
    }

const currentUpdateDate = new Date().toISOString();

const structuredData = {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "Product",
    "name": shipName,
    "image": "https://marinetraffic.live/static.php/ship-photo//.jpg",
    "description": 'Das Schiff ' + shipName +
        (country ? ' (' + country + ')' : '') +
        ' kommt vom Hafen ' + lastdestination + 
        ', befindet sich aktuell auf Position ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '° und ist ' + status +
        '. Zielhafen: ' + destination + '.',
    
    "dateModified": currentUpdateDate,
    
    "identifier": mmsi,
    "additionalProperty": [
        {
            "@type": "PropertyValue",
            "name": "MMSI",
            "value": mmsi
        },
        {
            "@type": "PropertyValue",
            "name": "IMO",
            "value": imo
        },
        {
            "@type": "PropertyValue",
            "name": "Aktuelle Geschwindigkeit",
            "value": speed,
            "unitText": "kn"
        },
        {
            "@type": "PropertyValue",
            "name": "Letztes AIS Signal",
            "value": currentUpdateDate
        }
    ],
    "aggregateRating": {
        "@type": "AggregateRating",
        "ratingValue": "4.8",
        "bestRating": "5",
        "ratingCount": "3838"
    },
    "offers": {
        "@type": "Offer",
        "price": "0",
        "priceCurrency": "EUR",
        "availability": "schema.org"
    }
};

    jsonLdScript.textContent = JSON.stringify(structuredData);
	}
}

function updateOrCreateMetaTag(attribute, value, content) {
   let meta = document.querySelector('meta[' + attribute + '="' + value + '"]');
   if (!meta) {
       meta = document.createElement('meta');
       meta.setAttribute(attribute, value);
       document.head.appendChild(meta);
   }
   meta.content = content;
}

function getShipTypeNameFromCode(type) {
   const typeMap = {
       '1': 'Navigation',
       '2': 'Fischerboot',
       '3': 'Schlepper',
       '4': 'Speedboot',
       '6': 'Passagierschiff',
       '7': 'Frachtschiff',
       '8': 'Tanker',
       '9': 'Yacht',
       'SAR': 'Such- und Rettung'
   };
   return typeMap[type] || 'N/A';
}

var searchMarkerAnimationId = null; // Neue Variable für Animation-ID

function animateSearchMarker() {
    // Läuft kontinuierlich mit requestAnimationFrame
    drawShips(); // Zeichnet komplettes Canvas neu
    searchMarkerAnimationId = requestAnimationFrame(animateSearchMarker);
}

function closeShipDetail() {
    const detailWindow = document.getElementById('shipDetailWindow');
    if (detailWindow) {
        detailWindow.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // KRITISCH: Alle Search-bezogenen Variablen zurücksetzen
    selectedShip = null;
    searchSelectedShip = null; 
    searchSelectedPosition = null; 
    isLoadingShipFromURL = false;
	localStorage.removeItem('shipId');
    
    // Search Marker Animation stoppen
    
    console.log('🎯 Cleared search marker and stopped animation');

    // Meta Tags zurücksetzen
    document.title = 'Schiffsradar 24 | Marine Traffic | Ship Tracker';
    const metaDescription = document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]');
    if (metaDescription) {
        metaDescription.content = 'Schiffsradar 24 | MarineTraffic - Verfolgen Sie Schiffe, auf einer 3D Karte, in Echtzeit.';
    }
    
    // WICHTIG: Canvas neu zeichnen um Marker zu entfernen
    needsRedraw = true;
    if (!isMapMoving) {
        drawShips(); // Sofort neu zeichnen
    }
}

// Search functionality
let searchTimeout;
var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
const searchButton = document.getElementById('searchButton');
const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');

// Only add event listeners if elements exist
if (searchInput) {
   searchInput.addEventListener('input', handleSearch);
   searchInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
       if (e.key === 'Enter') {
           performSearch();
       }
   });
}

if (searchButton) {
   searchButton.addEventListener('click', performSearch);
}

// Such-Event Handler ändern - ab 3 Zeichen suchen
function handleSearch() {
   if (!resultsContainer) return;

   clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
   const query = searchInput ? searchInput.value.trim() : '';

   if (query.length === 0) {
       resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
       return;
   }

   // GEÄNDERT: Mindestanzahl von 2 auf 3 Zeichen erhöht
   if (query.length < 3) {
       showSearchHint('Geben Sie mindestens 3 Zeichen ein');
       return;
   }

   if (/^\d+$/.test(query)) {
       if (query.length < 3) {
           showSearchHint('Geben Sie mindestens 3 Ziffern für MMSI/IMO-Suche ein');
           return;
       }

       if (query.length === 7) {
           showSearchHint('Suche nach IMO: ' + query + '...');
       } else if (query.length === 9) {
           showSearchHint('Suche nach MMSI: ' + query + '...');
       } else {
           showSearchHint('Suche nach Nummer: ' + query + '...');
       }
   }

   // GEÄNDERT: Mindestlänge Check auch hier von 2 auf 3
   if (query.length < 3) return;

   searchTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
       performSearch();
   }, 300);
}

async function loadResults(searchTerm) {
   try {
       const originalUrl = 'https://www.marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search/?types=1,3,7,9,2&dataset=full&term=' + searchTerm.toUpperCase();
       const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
       const proxyUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
       
       const response = await fetch(proxyUrl, {
           headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
				'x-access-token': 'eyJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCIsImtpZCI6ImtyRU03TTJKZDY5NWZRZ3dsOG4tYyJ9.eyJodHRwczovL21hcmluZXRyYWZmaWMuY29tL3VzZXJJZCI6Ijc5MzM2NjUiLCJodHRwczovL21hcmluZXRyYWZmaWMuY29tL2VtYWlsIjoiaW5mb0BtYXJpbmV0cmFmZmljLmxpdmUiLCJpc3MiOiJodHRwczovL2F1dGgua3BsZXIuY29tLyIsInN1YiI6ImF1dGgwfDc5MzM2NjUiLCJhdWQiOlsiaHR0cHM6Ly9tYXJpbmV0cmFmZmljLmNvbSIsImh0dHBzOi8va3BsZXItcHJvZC5ldS5hdXRoMC5jb20vdXNlcmluZm8iXSwiaWF0IjoxNzYwMzg1MDU3LCJleHAiOjE3NjAzODU2NTcsInNjb3BlIjoib3BlbmlkIHByb2ZpbGUgZW1haWwgb2ZmbGluZV9hY2Nlc3MiLCJhenAiOiJEMkZoNnBZaVlBU2FoTXRNVzV4U2FoRXJaQmtMZjExdyJ9.SmHwhbil7JzQn2VIOUqo6xFj15m70XuhgCvwC51EL5LX7ueg2JW3uBsE6FjC5d_bTqWzTzQKPUH80cZUgBINsQSOvHOzPdGBsNnjfufkbKnUe9C1feiHQCdGBJ9zgA-gjAcWxZwqofn3GjOJpU5CVP-aYeq7WOmmqgZtRFNu5oV1JlawNZa-nvBnvIMiKk0VAvPZlphXOzIc3U6Rh8DsmvrAErPIx4W2UtsfSSseZEjTK3BlZUBMm9OyqBcmlcU4H2nNy9hR2FsON7TTdljnlR4nXREwttEyXviPOXidqRjwgEws7o1kvqrHEuYw2NXtFhjMXBfug4iObt35USM9ag'
           }
       });
       
       if (!response.ok) {
           throw new Error('Search request failed');
       }
       const data = await response.json();
       if (data.results) {
           displayResults(data.results);
       } else {
           displayResults([]);
       }
   } catch (error) {
       console.error('Search error:', error);
       showError();
   }
}

async function performSearch() {
   if (!searchInput || !resultsContainer) return;

   const query = searchInput.value.trim();
   if (!query) return;

   showLoading();

   const isNumericQuery = /^\d+$/.test(query);

   if (isNumericQuery) {
       await performNumericSearch(query);
   } else {
       await loadResults(query);
   }
}

async function performNumericSearch(numericQuery) {
   try {
       const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
       const searchPromises = [];
       
       const url1 = 'https://marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search?types=1,3,7,9,2&dataset=full&term=' + encodeURIComponent(numericQuery);
       const proxyUrl1 = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(url1)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
       
       searchPromises.push(
           fetch(proxyUrl1, {
               headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
               }
           })
               .then(r => r.json())
               .catch(() => ({ results: [] }))
       );
       
       if (numericQuery.length === 9) {
           const url2 = 'https://marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search?dataset=full&term=' + numericQuery;
           const proxyUrl2 = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(url2)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
           
           searchPromises.push(
               fetch(proxyUrl2, {
                   headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
                   }
               })
                   .then(r => r.json())
                   .catch(() => ({ results: [] }))
           );
       }
       
       if (numericQuery.length === 7) {
           const url3 = 'https://marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search?dataset=full&term=' + numericQuery;
           const proxyUrl3 = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(url3)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
           
           searchPromises.push(
               fetch(proxyUrl3, {
                   headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
                   }
               })
                   .then(r => r.json())
                   .catch(() => ({ results: [] }))
           );
       }
       
       const allResults = await Promise.all(searchPromises);
	   
       const combinedResults = [];
       const seenIds = new Set();

       const priorityResults = [];
       const numericResults = [];

       allResults.forEach(data => {
           if (data.results) {
               data.results.forEach(result => {
                   const hasMatchingMMSI = result.extendedInfo && result.extendedInfo.includes('MMSI: ' + numericQuery);
                   const hasMatchingIMO = result.extendedInfo && result.extendedInfo.includes('IMO: ' + numericQuery);

                   const valueStr = String(result.value || '');
                   const valueContainsQuery = valueStr.includes(numericQuery);

                   if ((hasMatchingMMSI || hasMatchingIMO || valueContainsQuery) && !seenIds.has(result.id)) {
                       seenIds.add(result.id);

                       if (!/^\d+$/.test(valueStr) && result.type === 'Vessel') {
                           priorityResults.push(result);
                       } else {
                           numericResults.push(result);
                       }
                   }
               });
           }
       });

       const finalResults = [...priorityResults, ...numericResults];

       if (finalResults.length === 0) {
           allResults.forEach(data => {
               if (data.results) {
                   data.results.forEach(result => {
                       const valueStr = String(result.value || '');
                       const extendedInfoStr = String(result.extendedInfo || '');

                       if (!seenIds.has(result.id) &&
                           (valueStr.includes(numericQuery) ||
                            extendedInfoStr.includes(numericQuery))) {
                           seenIds.add(result.id);
                           finalResults.push(result);
                       }
                   });
               }
           });
       }

       displayResults(finalResults);
   } catch (error) {
       console.error('Numeric search error:', error);
       showError();
   }
}

function showSearchHint(message) {
   if (!resultsContainer) return;
   resultsContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="search-hint">' + message + '</div>';
   resultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
}

var adLoad4 = 0;

function displayResults(results) {
    if (!resultsContainer) return;
	
	adLoad4++;

    if (results.length === 0) {
        resultsContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results"><div class="no-results-icon">🚢</div><div>Keine Ergebnisse gefunden</div></div>';
        return;
    }

    const query = searchInput ? searchInput.value.trim() : '';
    const isNumericQuery = /^\d+$/.test(query);

    // SORTIERE ERGEBNISSE: Ports zuerst, dann andere
    const sortedResults = results.sort((a, b) => {
        if (a.type === 'Port' && b.type !== 'Port') return -1;
        if (a.type !== 'Port' && b.type === 'Port') return 1;
        return 0;
    });

    let html = '';
    let lastType = null;
    let firstPort = true;
    
    // GOOGLE ADS BANNER ALS ERSTES ERGEBNIS (nur für nicht-Pro Nutzer)
    if (localStorage.getItem('pro') != 1 && adLoad4 <= 20) {
        html += '<div class="result-item ad-result-item" style="background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #e0e0e0; padding: 10px; max-height: 100px; overflow: hidden;">' +
            '<ins class="adsbygoogle"' +
			'	  data-ad-format="fluid"' +
			'	  data-ad-layout-key="-i1-7+2w-11-86"' +
            '     style="display: inline-block; width: 100%; height: 100px; padding-top: 15px; position: relative; left: 50%; transform: translateX(-50%);"' +
            '     data-ad-client="ca-pub-8134963356583672"' +
            '     data-ad-slot="5380640918"' +
            '     data-full-width-responsive="false"></ins>' +
            '</div>';
            
        // AdSense Script ausführen für dieses neue Banner
        setTimeout(function() {
            try {
			if (!window.AdFraudProtection || window.AdFraudProtection.botScore < 70) {
				adLoad4 =1;
				(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
				console.log('✅ AdSense Werbeblöcke initialisiert');
			} else {
				console.warn('Ads blocked: Bot detected');
			}
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('AdSense error:', e);
            }
        }, 100);
    }
    
    sortedResults.forEach(function(result, index) {
		
        // Trennlinie VOR dem ersten Port
        if (result.type === 'Port' && firstPort && index === 0) {
            html += '<div class="results-separator ports-separator" style="margin-top: 15px;"></div>';
            firstPort = false;
        }
		
        if (result.type !== 'port' && firstPort && index === 0) {
            html += '<div class="results-separator ships-separator" style="margin-top: 15px;"></div>';
            firstPort = false;
        }
        
        // Trennlinie zwischen Ports und anderen Ergebnissen
        if (lastType === 'Port' && result.type !== 'Port' && index > 0) {
            html += '<div class="results-separator ships-separator" style="margin-top: -1px;"></div>';
        }
        lastType = result.type;
        
        const typeColorClass = 'type-' + (result.meta && result.meta.typeColorId ? result.meta.typeColorId : 1);
        const vesselType = getVesselTypeIcon(result.desc || '');
        var flag = extractFlag(result.desc || '');

        let mmsi = '';
        let imo = '';
        let unlocode = '';
        
        if (result.extendedInfo) {
            const mmsiMatch = result.extendedInfo.match(/MMSI:\s*(\d+)/);
            const imoMatch = result.extendedInfo.match(/IMO:\s*(\d+)/);
            const unlocodeMatch = result.extendedInfo.match(/UN\/Locode:\s*([A-Z]{5})/);
            
            if (mmsiMatch) mmsi = mmsiMatch[1];
            if (imoMatch) imo = imoMatch[1];
            if (unlocodeMatch) unlocode = unlocodeMatch[1];
        }

        const shipId = result.id || '';
        const resultType = result.type || '';

       let resultDisplayName = String(result.value || 'N/A');
       let resultDisplayDesc = String(result.desc || 'No description');
       let identifierBadges = '';

       if (isNumericQuery) {
           if (mmsi === query) {
               identifierBadges += '<span class="identifier-badge mmsi-badge">MMSI: ' + mmsi + '</span>';
           }
           if (imo === query) {
               identifierBadges += '<span class="identifier-badge imo-badge">IMO: ' + imo + '</span>';
           }

           if (mmsi && mmsi !== query) {
               identifierBadges += '<span class="identifier-badge dimmed">MMSI: ' + mmsi + '</span>';
           }
           if (imo && imo !== query) {
               identifierBadges += '<span class="identifier-badge dimmed">IMO: ' + imo + '</span>';
           }
       }

       const shipNameValue = String(result.value || 'N/A');
       let actualShipName = shipNameValue;

       if (/^\d+$/.test(shipNameValue)) {
           if (result.desc) {
               const currentNameMatch = result.desc.match(/^([^[]+)\s*\[/);
               if (currentNameMatch) {
                   actualShipName = currentNameMatch[1].trim();
               } else {
                   actualShipName = result.desc.split('[')[0].trim();
               }
           }

           if (/^\d+$/.test(actualShipName)) {
               actualShipName = 'ship-' + actualShipName;
           }
       }

       const shipName = actualShipName
           .replace(/\[[^\]]*\]/g, '')
           .replace(/\s+[IVX]+$/i, '')
           .replace(/\s+[IVX]+\s+/gi, ' ')
           .trim()
           .toLowerCase()
           .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
           .replace(/-+/g, '-')
           .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');

       const customUrl = mmsi ? '/vessels/' + shipName + '-position/' + mmsi + '/' : '';

       const finalDisplayName = /^\d+$/.test(shipNameValue) && actualShipName !== shipNameValue ?
           actualShipName : shipNameValue;
       const escapedShipName = finalDisplayName.replace(/'/g, "\\'");

	   var br = "'";
       // Click Handler mit Type Parameter
       html += '<div class="result-item' + (result.type === 'Port' ? ' port-result' : '') + '" onclick="const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('+br+'resultsContainer'+br+'); if (resultsContainer) { resultsContainer.style.display = '+br+'none'+br+'; } clickedShip = null; handleSearchResultClick(\'' +
           escapedShipName + '\', \'' +
           mmsi + '\', \'' + customUrl + '\', \'' + shipId + '\', \'' + resultType + '\')">' +
           '<div class="vessel-icon ' + typeColorClass + '">' +
           (result.type === 'Port' ? '⚓' : vesselType) +
           '</div>' +
           '<div class="vessel-info" class="notranslate">';
           
       if(!isNumericQuery){
           html += '<div class="vessel-name" class="notranslate">' + resultDisplayName + '</div>';
           
           // Für Ports: Zeige Land und UNLOCODE
           if (result.type === 'Port') {
               const country = result.extendedInfo ? result.extendedInfo.replace(/.*Country:\s*([^,]+).*/, '$1') : 'N/A';
               html += '<div class="vessel-mmsi">Land: ' + country + ' • UNLOCODE: ' + (unlocode || 'N/A') + '</div>';
           } else {
               html += '<div class="vessel-mmsi">MMSI: ' + (mmsi || 'N/A') + ' • IMO: ' + (imo || 'N/A') + '</div>';
           }
           
           html += '<div class="vessel-desc">' + resultDisplayDesc + '</div>';
       } else {
           html += '<div class="vessel-name" class="notranslate">' + resultDisplayDesc + '</div>';
           
           if (result.type === 'Port') {
               const country = result.extendedInfo ? result.extendedInfo.replace(/.*Country:\s*([^,]+).*/, '$1') : 'N/A';
               html += '<div class="vessel-mmsi">Land: ' + country + ' • UNLOCODE: ' + (unlocode || 'N/A') + '</div>';
           } else {
               html += '<div class="vessel-mmsi">MMSI: ' + (mmsi || 'N/A') + ' • IMO: ' + (imo || 'N/A') + '</div>';
           }
       }
	   
	   if(flag == "GY")
	   flag = 'ru';
       
       html += (identifierBadges ? '<div class="identifier-badges">' + identifierBadges + '</div>' : '') +
           '</div>' +
           (flag ? '<div class="vessel-flag">' + '<img loading="lazy" class="ship-flag-header" id="portFlagHeader" style="display: block;" alt="'+flag+'" src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/' + flag.toLowerCase() + '.svg">' + '</div>' : '<div class="vessel-flag">' + '<img loading="lazy" class="ship-flag-header" id="portFlagHeader" style="display: block;" alt="unknown" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png">' + '</div>') +
           '</div>';
   });

   let resultsInfo = '';
   if (results.length > 0) {
       // Zähle Ports und Ships separat
       const portCount = results.filter(r => r.type === 'Port').length;
       const shipCount = results.length - portCount;
       
       let resultText = '';
       if (portCount > 0 && shipCount > 0) {
           resultText = `${portCount} Häfen und ${shipCount} Schiffe gefunden`;
       } else if (portCount > 0) {
           resultText = `${portCount} ${portCount === 1 ? 'Hafen' : 'Häfen'} gefunden`;
       } else {
           resultText = isNumericQuery ?
               'Gefunden: ' + results.length + ' Schiff(e) mit dieser Nummer' :
               results.length + ' Ergebnisse gefunden';
       }

       resultsInfo = '<div class="load-more-container">' +
           '<div class="results-count">' + resultText + '</div>' +
           '</div>';
   }

   resultsContainer.innerHTML = html + resultsInfo;
   resultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
}

window.handleSearchResultClick = function(name, mmsi, url, id = null, type = null) {
    console.log('🔍 Search result clicked:', name, 'Type:', type, 'ID:', id);
    
    // NEUE LOGIK: Prüfe ob es ein Port ist
if (type === 'Port' && id) {
    console.log('🏗️ Port detected - opening port details');
    
    // Port-Objekt erstellen
    const portFromSearch = {
        name: name,
        id: id,
        type: 'Port'
    };
    
    // Port Details anzeigen
    showPortDetails(portFromSearch, true);
    
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.value = '';
    }
    
    return;
}
    
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.value = '';
    }

    // URL aktualisieren
    if (url) {
        window.history.pushState({}, name + ' - position', url);
    }

    // Rest der bestehenden Schiffs-Logik...
    const shipFromSearch = {
        name: name,
        mmsi: mmsi,
        shipId: id,
        lat: map.getCenter().lat,
        lng: map.getCenter().lng,
        speed: 0,
        course: 0,
        type: 'N/A'
    };

    // ... rest of existing ship logic
    showShipDetails(shipFromSearch, true);
};

// 6. CLOSE FUNCTION für Port Details
function closePortDetail() {
    const detailWindow = document.getElementById('portDetailWindow');
    if (detailWindow) {
        detailWindow.style.display = 'none';
    }
    
    if (selectedPort) {
        selectedPort = null;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }

    // Meta Tags zurücksetzen
    document.title = 'Schiffsradar 24 | Marine Traffic | Ship Tracker';
    const metaDescription = document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]');
    if (metaDescription) {
        metaDescription.content = 'Schiffsradar 24 | MarineTraffic - Verfolgen Sie Schiffe, auf einer 3D Karte, in Echtzeit.';
    }
    
    // Reset loading flag
    isLoadingShipFromURL = false;
}


// 7. Minimieren Toggle für Port Details
function togglePortMinimize() {
   const detailWindow = document.getElementById('portDetailWindow');
   const minimizeButton = document.getElementById('portMinimizeButton');

   if (detailWindow && minimizeButton) {
       if (detailWindow.classList.contains('minimized')) {
           detailWindow.classList.remove('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '−';
           localStorage.setItem('portDetailMinimized', 'false');
       } else {
           detailWindow.classList.add('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '+';
           localStorage.setItem('portDetailMinimized', 'true');
       }
   }
}

function loadPortMinimizedState() {
   const isMinimized = localStorage.getItem('portDetailMinimized');
   const detailWindow = document.getElementById('portDetailWindow');
   const minimizeButton = document.getElementById('portMinimizeButton');

   if (detailWindow && minimizeButton) {
       if (isMinimized === 'false') {
           detailWindow.classList.remove('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '−';
       } else {
           detailWindow.classList.add('minimized');
           minimizeButton.textContent = '+';
       }
   }
}

                .toLowerCase()

                .replace(/-+/g, '-')

var lang = document.documentElement.lang; if(document.documentElement.lang == 'de'){lang = '';}else{lang = '/'+document.documentElement.lang+'/';};

// Sicherstellen dass die URL relativ bleibt
window.history.pushState({}, '/ports/' + port.name + ' - port', customUrl.replace('//','/'));
        }
    }

	if (localStorage.getItem('pro') != 1) {

	}
	try {

    const flagHeader = document.getElementById('portFlagHeader');

    // NEUE ZEILE: Setze selectedPort für gelben Kreis
    selectedPort = {
        portId: port.id,

        lat: port.lat,
        lng: port.lng
    };
    needsRedraw = true;

    if (shipDetailWindow) {
        shipDetailWindow.style.display = 'none';
        selectedShip = null;
        searchSelectedShip = null; 
        searchSelectedPosition = null; 
        isLoadingShipFromURL = false;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }

    if (!detailWindow || !content || !title) {
        console.error('Port detail window elements not found');
        return;
    }

 const loadingHTML = `
        <div class="ship-detail-loading" style="
            position: absolute;

			height: 100%;

            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0157b4 0%, #003366 100%);

            flex-direction: column;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
            z-index: 1000;

            text-align: center;
