    // Minimized state
    loadPortMinimizedState();

    // API Daten laden
    await loadPortDetailsFromAPI(port, flyToPort);
}

// NEUE Hilfsfunktion zur ID-Validierung
async function validatePortId(portName, currentId, countryCode = null) {
    console.log('=== validatePortId CALLED ===');
    console.log('Port Name:', portName);
    console.log('Current ID:', currentId);
    console.log('Country Code:', countryCode);
    
    try {
	   const originalUrl = 'https://www.marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search/?types=2,12,21&dataset=full&term='+ encodeURIComponent(portName.toUpperCase());
       const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
       const proxyUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
       
       const response = await fetch(proxyUrl, {
           headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
           }
       });
       
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data.results && data.results.length > 0) {
            // Filter nur Ports
            const portResults = data.results.filter(result => result.type === 'Port' || result.type === 'Marina');
            
            if (portResults.length === 0) {
                return currentId;
            }
            
            // Strategie 1: Exakter Name + Country Code Match
            if (countryCode) {
                const exactMatchWithFlag = portResults.find(result => 
                    result.value && 
                    result.value.toLowerCase() === portName.toLowerCase() && 
                    result.flag === countryCode
                );
                
                if (exactMatchWithFlag && exactMatchWithFlag.id) {
                    console.log('✅ Found exact match with country code:', exactMatchWithFlag.value, exactMatchWithFlag.flag);
                    return exactMatchWithFlag.id.toString();
                }
            }
            
            // Strategie 2: Prüfe ob aktuelle ID in den Ergebnissen ist
            const currentIdMatch = portResults.find(result => 
                (result.id === currentId || result.id === parseInt(currentId)) &&
                result.value && 
                result.value.toLowerCase() === portName.toLowerCase()
            );
            
            if (currentIdMatch) {
                console.log('✅ Current ID is valid');
                return currentId;
            }
            
            // Strategie 3: Exakter Name Match
            const exactMatch = portResults.find(result => 
                result.value && result.value.toLowerCase() === portName.toLowerCase()
            );
            
            if (exactMatch && exactMatch.id) {
                console.log('✅ Found exact name match:', exactMatch.value, exactMatch.flag || 'no flag');
                return exactMatch.id.toString();
            }
            
            // Strategie 4: Erster Port als Fallback
            const firstPort = portResults[0];
            if (firstPort && firstPort.id) {
                console.log('⚠️ Using first port as fallback:', firstPort.value);
                return firstPort.id.toString();
            }
        }
        
        return currentId; // Behalte aktuelle ID
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Port ID validation failed:', error);
        return currentId;
    }
}

async function loadPortDetailsFromAPI(port, shouldFlyTo = false) {
    console.log('=== loadPortDetailsFromAPI CALLED ===');
    console.log('Port ID:', port.id);
    console.log('Should fly to:', shouldFlyTo);	   

    try {
        // Schritt 1: Port Details laden
        const originalUrl = `https://marinetraffic.com/de/ais/get_info_window_json?asset_type=port&id=${port.id}`;
        const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
        const detailUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
        
        const response = await fetch(detailUrl, {
			headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
            }
        });

        if (!response.ok) {
            console.error('Port details API error:', response.status, response.statusText);
            displayPortDetails(port, null);
            return;
        }

        const responseText = await response.text();
        
        if (!responseText || responseText.trim().startsWith('<')) {
            console.error('Received HTML instead of JSON');
            displayPortDetails(port, null);
            return;
        }

        let apiData;
        try {
            apiData = JSON.parse(responseText);
            console.log('Port details loaded successfully');
        } catch (parseError) {
            console.error('JSON parse error:', parseError);
            displayPortDetails(port, null);
            return;
        }

        // Port Daten erweitern
        if (apiData && apiData.values) {
            const values = apiData.values;
            
            port.unlocode = values.unlocode || 'N/A';
            port.country = values.country || 'N/A';
            port.countryCode = values.country_code || '';
            port.timezone = values.timezone || 'UTC';
            port.localTime = values.local_time || 'N/A';
            port.shipsInPort = values.shipcount || 0;
            port.expectedArrivals = values.expected_count || 0;
            port.recentPortCalls = values.recent_port_calls || 0;
		}
		
    // URL AKTUALISIEREN (mit korrigierter ID)
    if (port.name && port.id) {
        var urlFriendlyName = port.name
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '')
            .replace(/-+/g, '-')
            .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');

var lang = document.documentElement.lang; if(document.documentElement.lang == 'de'){lang = '';}else{lang = '/'+document.documentElement.lang+'/';};

// Lang bereinigen - entferne führende/trailing slashes
const cleanLang = lang.replace(/^\/+|\/+$/g, '');

// URL korrekt aufbauen
const customUrl = '/' + (cleanLang ? cleanLang + '/ports/' : 'ports/') + urlFriendlyName + '-port/' + port.unlocode.toLowerCase() + '/';

// Sicherstellen dass die URL relativ bleibt
window.history.pushState({}, '/ports/' + port.name + ' - port', customUrl.replace('//','/'));
    }

        // Schritt 2: Koordinaten über Search API holen (da nicht in Details)
        if (shouldFlyTo || !port.lat || !port.lng) {
            console.log('📍 Fetching port coordinates via search API...');
			const originalUrl = `https://www.marinetraffic.com/de/global_search/search/?types=2,12,21&dataset=full&term=${encodeURIComponent(port.name.toUpperCase())}`;
			const corsProxyKey = '22fa65f1';
			const proxyUrl = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=${encodeURIComponent(originalUrl)}&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;            
            
            try {
				const searchResponse = await fetch(proxyUrl, {
					headers: {
			    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                'Accept': 'application/json',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
				'x-requested-with': 'XMLHttpRequest',
					}
				});
				
                const searchData = await searchResponse.json();
                
                if (searchData.results && searchData.results.length > 0) {
                    // Finde den Port mit der passenden ID
                    let matchingPort;

                    // Prüfe ob es eine Marina ist (andere ID-Range)
                    if (parseInt(port.id) > 5000) {
                        // Marina - nimm einfach den ersten Treffer
                        matchingPort = searchData.results[0];
                        console.log('🚢 Marina detected - using first result');
                    } else {
                        // Normaler Port - ID-Match
                        matchingPort = searchData.results.find(result => 
                            result.id === port.id || result.id === parseInt(port.id)
                        );
                    }

                    if (!matchingPort && searchData.results.length > 0) {
                        // Fallback
                        matchingPort = searchData.results[0];
                    }
                    
                    if (matchingPort && matchingPort.meta) {
                        port.lat = matchingPort.meta.lat;
                        port.lng = matchingPort.meta.lon;
                        console.log('✅ Port coordinates found:', port.lat, port.lng);
                        
                        // Update selectedPort mit korrekten Koordinaten
                        if (selectedPort) {
                            selectedPort.lat = port.lat;
                            selectedPort.lng = port.lng;
                        }
                        
                        // FlyTo ausführen wenn gewünscht
                        if (shouldFlyTo && port.lat && port.lng) {
                            console.log('✈️ Flying to port location:', port.lat, port.lng);
                            map.flyTo({
                                center: [port.lng, port.lat],
                                zoom: Math.max(map.getZoom(),13),
                                duration: 1000,
                                curve: 1.2,
                                easing: (t) => t * (2 - t)
                            });
                            
                            // Redraw nach FlyTo
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                needsRedraw = true;
                                drawShips(); // Zeichnet auch POIs neu
                            }, 1100);
                            
                            if (map.getZoom() > 8 && !isMapMoving && Object.values(poiFilters).some(active => active)) {
                                setTimeout(function() {
                                    loadStaticAssets();
                                }, 1500);
                            }
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.warn('⚠️ No matching port found in search results');
                    }
                }
            } catch (searchError) {
                console.error('Error fetching port coordinates:', searchError);
            }
        }

	//await Promise.all([
		   await loadPortExpected(apiData.values.unlocode);
		   await loadPortArrivals(apiData.values.unlocode);
		   await loadPortDepartures(apiData.values.unlocode);
		   await loadPortInPort(apiData.values.unlocode);
		   await loadPortWeather(apiData.values.unlocode)
	//]);
		
	// Port Details anzeigen
	await displayPortDetails(port, apiData);  
	
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error in loadPortDetailsFromAPI:', error);
        displayPortDetails(port, null);
    }
}

var adLoad3 = 0;
    
function displayPortDetails(port, apiData) {
    const content = document.getElementById('portDetailContent');
    const title = document.getElementById('portDetailTitle');
    const titleSection = document.querySelector('.port-detail-title-section');
	
	adLoad3++;

    if (!content || !title || !titleSection) return;

    const data = apiData || {};
    const values = data.values || {};
    const text = data.text || {};

    // Port Name & Country Code
    const portName = port.name || values.port_name || 'N/A Port';
    const countryCodeRaw = (values.country_code || port.country_code || '').toLowerCase();

    // Mapping für Sonderfälle
    const codeMap = { uk: 'gb', el: 'gr', fx: 'fr', gy: 'ru' };
    const countryCode = codeMap[countryCodeRaw] || countryCodeRaw;
    const countryName = values.country || port.country || 'N/A';

    // Titel aktualisieren
    title.textContent = portName;

    // Alte Flaggen entfernen (alle!)
    document.querySelectorAll('.port-flag-header').forEach(flag => flag.remove());

    // Neue Flagge erstellen
    const flagImg = document.createElement('img');
    flagImg.className = 'port-flag-header';
    flagImg.src = `https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/${countryCode}.svg`;
    flagImg.alt = countryName;
    flagImg.style.display = 'block';
    flagImg.onerror = function () {
        this.src = 'https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png';
    };

    // Flagge vor dem Titel einfügen
    titleSection.insertBefore(flagImg, title);

    // Meta-Tags aktualisieren
    if (typeof updatePortMetaTags === 'function') {
        updatePortMetaTags(port, values);
    }

    // Ab hier: restliche Details
    let html = '';
	   $('.ship-detail-loading').css('display', 'block');
	   html += ` <div class="ship-detail-loading" style="
            position: absolute;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100%;
			height: 100%;
			max-height: calc(-140px + 100vh);
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0157b4 0%, #003366 100%);
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
            z-index: 1000;
            color: white;
            text-align: center;
            padding: 20px;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        ">
		<div style=" margin-top: -30px;">
            <div style="margin-bottom: 15px; font-size: 3em;">
                <i class="fas fa-ship"></i>
            </div>
            <a href="https://marinetraffic.live" class="nav-brand" style="
                color: white;
                text-decoration: none;
                font-size: 1.5em;
                margin-bottom: 20px;
                font-weight: bold;
            ">
                MarineTraffic.live
            </a>
            <div style="font-size: 1.2em; opacity: 0.9; margin-top: 10px;">
                Lade Daten...
            </div>
		</div>
    </div>` 
   setTimeout(function() {
		$('.ship-detail-loading').css('display', 'none');
   }, 500);
   
    // Port Foto
if (text.img_medium) {
    const highResImage = text.img_medium.replace(/photo_size=\d+/, "photo_size=800").replace("www.marinetraffic.com/", "marinetraffic.live/static2.php/").replace("getAssetDefaultPhoto", ""+portName.replace(/\s+/g, '-').toLowerCase()+".jpg");
    html += `
        <div class="ship-photo-section">
            <img loading="lazy" src="${highResImage}" alt="${portName}" class="port-photo"
            onerror="this.src='/no-image.jpg'">
			<div style="position: absolute; width: 100%;height: 30px;background: linear-gradient(135deg, #066edf 0%, #004691 100%);margin-top: -30px;color: #fff;display: flex;align-items: center;justify-content: right;">MarineTraffic.live&nbsp;&nbsp;</div>
        </div>
    `;
} else {
    html += `
        <div class="ship-photo-section">
            <img loading="lazy" src="/no-image.jpg" alt="Kein Bild verfügbar" class="port-photo">
			<div style="position: absolute; width: 100%;height: 30px;background: linear-gradient(135deg, #066edf 0%, #004691 100%);margin-top: -30px;color: #fff;display: flex;align-items: center;justify-content: right;">MarineTraffic.live&nbsp;&nbsp;</div>
        </div>
    `;
}

	html += '<div class="ship-detail-section">';	
	html += '<center id="ad4" style="user-select:none;overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:5px;">' +
		'<ins class="adsbygoogle" id="ad-mobile4"' +
		'data-ad-format="fluid"'+
		'data-ad-layout-key="-i0-4+2d-1u-4h"'+
		'style="user-select: none; position:relative !important; margin-top: 0px; display:inline-block; max-width:calc(100vw - 60px) !important; height:92px; padding:0px; background: #fff !important; text-align: center;"' +
		'data-ad-client="ca-pub-8134963356583672"' +
		'data-full-width-responsive="false"' +
		'data-ad-slot="4924333584"></ins>' +
		'</center>';
    html += `<h4 style="margin-top:0px;font-weight:500;color:#2c3e50;margin-bottom:5px;">Hafendetails</h4>
            <div class="port-details-grid">
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">Typ</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${values.port_type || 'Hafen'}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">UNLOCODE</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${values.unlocode || port.unlocode || 'N/A'}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">Land</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${countryName}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">Schiffe im Hafen</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${values.shipcount || port.shipsInPort || '0'}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">Erwartete Ankünfte</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${values.expected_count || port.expectedArrivals || '0'}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label">Letzte Hafenanläufe</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">${values.recent_port_calls || port.recentPortCalls || '0'}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    // Lokale Zeit
    if (values.current_local_time) {
        const utcSign = values.current_local_offset >= 0 ? '+' : '';
        html += `
            <div class="port-detail-section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; border-top: 1px solid #eee; padding-bottom: 15px; margin-top: 10px;">
                <div class="detail-item">
                    <div class="detail-label" style="padding-top: 0px;">Lokale Zeit</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">
                        ${values.current_local_time} (UTC ${utcSign}${values.current_local_offset || ''})
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    // Expected, falls vorhanden
	if (window.portExpectedData && window.portExpectedData.list && window.portExpectedData.list.length > 0 && typeof generateExpectedSection === 'function') {
		html += generateExpectedSection(window.portExpectedData.list);
	}
	
	// Arrivals, falls vorhanden
	if (window.portArrivalsData && window.portArrivalsData.list && window.portArrivalsData.list.length > 0 && typeof generateArrivalsSection === 'function') {
		html += generateArrivalsSection(window.portArrivalsData.list);
	}
	
	// Depatures, falls vorhanden
	if (window.portDeparturesData && window.portDeparturesData.list && window.portDeparturesData.list.length > 0 && typeof generateDeparturesSection === 'function') {
		html += generateDeparturesSection(window.portDeparturesData.list);
	}
	// im Port, falls vorhanden
	if (window.portInPortData && window.portInPortData.list && window.portInPortData.list.length > 0 && typeof generateInPortSection === 'function') {
		html += generateInPortSection(window.portInPortData.list);
	}

    // Wetter, falls vorhanden
    if (window.portWeatherData && window.portWeatherData.length > 0 && typeof generateWeatherSection === 'function') {
        html += generateWeatherSection(window.portWeatherData);
    }
	
    setTimeout(() => {
        // AdSense neu initialisieren
        try {
            // Prüfe ob Pro-User
            if (localStorage.getItem('pro') != 1 && adLoad3 <= 20) {
				if (!window.AdFraudProtection || window.AdFraudProtection.botScore < 70) {
					(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
					console.log('✅ AdSense Werbeblöcke initialisiert');
				} else {
					console.warn('Ads blocked: Bot detected');
				}
            } else {
                // Verstecke Ad-Container für Pro-User
                const adContainer = document.getElementById('ad4');
                if (adContainer) {
                    adContainer.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.log('AdSense load error:', e);
        }
    }, 100);
	
    // Inhalt einsetzen
    content.innerHTML = html;
	
}

async function loadPortWeather(unlocode) {
    if (!unlocode) return null;
    if (unlocode == '-') return null;
    
    // Definiere mögliche UNLOCODE-Suffixe
    const suffixes = ['001'];
    let weatherData = null;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < suffixes.length; i++) {
        const suffix = suffixes[i];
        if (unlocode == 'CNSZP') unlocode = 'CNSZX';
        const modifiedUnlocode = unlocode + suffix;
        
        try {
            const weatherUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/pub_api.php/pub/weather-forecast/v4/${modifiedUnlocode}`;
            console.log(`📍 Trying weather data for: ${modifiedUnlocode}`);
  
			// AbortController für Timeout erstellen
			const controller = new AbortController();
			const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 3500);
			
            const response = await fetch(weatherUrl);
			
            clearTimeout(timeoutId);
			
            if (!response.ok) {
                console.log(`Weather API returned ${response.status} for ${modifiedUnlocode}`);
                // Versuche nächsten Suffix nur wenn 001 leer war
                if (suffix === '001') continue;
                else break;
            }
            
            const responseText = await response.text();
            
            // Prüfe ob Response valides JSON ist
            try {
                weatherData = JSON.parse(responseText);
                
                // Prüfe ob Daten vorhanden sind
                if (weatherData && weatherData.length > 0) {
                    console.log(`✅ Weather data loaded with ${modifiedUnlocode}:`, weatherData.length, 'entries');
                    
                    // Speichere Wetterdaten für Anzeige
                    window.portWeatherData = weatherData;
                    return weatherData;
                }
                
            } catch (parseError) {
            }
            
        } catch (error) {
        }
    }
    
    console.warn('⚠️ Could not load weather data for any UNLOCODE variant');
    window.portWeatherData = null;
    return null;
}

async function loadPortExpected(unlocode) {
    if (!unlocode || unlocode === '-') {
        window.portExpectedData = null;
        return null;
    }

    const suffixes = ['001'];
    for (let suffix of suffixes) {
        if (unlocode == 'CNSZP') unlocode = 'CNSZX';
        const modifiedUnlocode = unlocode + suffix;
        
        try {
            const expectedUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/sat_api.php/expl/port/${modifiedUnlocode}/expv4?pageId=1&rpp=100&sortBy=6&dir=1&type=-1`;
            console.log(`📍 Loading expected for ${modifiedUnlocode}...`);

			// AbortController für Timeout erstellen
			const controller = new AbortController();
			const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 3500);

            const response = await fetch(expectedUrl, {
                headers: {
                    'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
                    'Accept': 'application/json',
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                }
            });

            clearTimeout(timeoutId);

            if (!response.ok) {
                console.warn(`⚠️ API returned ${response.status} for ${modifiedUnlocode}`);
                if (suffix === '001') continue;
                else break;
            }

            const responseText = await response.text();

            let jsonData;
            try {
                jsonData = JSON.parse(responseText);
            } catch (err) {
                console.warn(`Invalid JSON for ${modifiedUnlocode}:`, err);
                if (suffix === '001') continue;
                else break;
            }

            if (jsonData && jsonData.list && jsonData.list.length > 0) {
                console.log(`✅ Expected data loaded for ${modifiedUnlocode}: ${jsonData.list.length} entries`);
                window.portExpectedData = jsonData;
                return jsonData;
            }

        } catch (err) {
        }
    }

    console.warn('⚠️ Could not load expected data for any UNLOCODE variant');
    window.portExpectedData = null;
    return null;
}

function generateWeatherSection(weatherData) {
    let html = '<div class="port-weather-section">';
    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 0px; font-weight: 500;color:#2c3e50; margin-bottom:5px; padding-top: 5px; border-top: 0px solid #eee;">Wetter</h4>';
    
    // Tabellen-Header für 3 Spalten
    html += '<div class="weather-table" style="max-height: 145px; margin-bottom: 10px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += '<div class="weather-header-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Datum</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Temperatur</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Wind</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    
    // Zeige die ersten 8 Einträge
    const entriesToShow = weatherData.slice(0, 8);
    
    entriesToShow.forEach(entry => {
        html += generateWeatherEntry(entry);
    });
    
    html += '</div></div>';
    return html;
}

function generateWeatherEntry(entry) {
    const windSpeedKnots = (parseFloat(entry.WSPD) * 1.94384).toFixed(1);
    const tempCelsius = parseInt(entry.TMP);
    const tempFahrenheit = Math.round((tempCelsius * 9/5) + 32);
    
    // Wind-Pfeil Rotation berechnen
    const rotation = parseInt(entry.WDIR) - 180;
    
    let html = '<div class="weather-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date" style="display: flex; align-items: center;">' + entry.TS + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date" style="display: flex; align-items: center;">';
    html += '<span class="temp-primary">' + tempCelsius + '°C</span> ';
    html += '<span class="temp-secondary">(' + tempFahrenheit + '°F)</span>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date" style="display: flex; align-items: center;">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">';
    
    // Wind-Pfeil SVG direkt hier
    html += '<svg width="10" height="12" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="transform: rotateZ(' + rotation + 'deg);">';
    html += '<path d="M.06 11.934c-.055-.045-.074-.111-.05-.17L4.82.103C4.848.043 4.922 0 5.005 0s.157.042.186.105l4.79 11.658c.03.075.03.16-.05.201-.08.04-.222.055-.29 0L5 7.984l-4.643 3.98c-.068.055-.173.035-.26-.005l-.037-.025z" fill="#065785" fill-rule="nonzero"></path>';
    html += '</svg>';
    
    html += ' ' + entry.WDIR + '° - ';
    html += windSpeedKnots + ' kn';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    return html;
}

function generateExpectedSection(expectedList) {
    if (!expectedList || !Array.isArray(expectedList) || expectedList.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    let html = '<div class="port-weather-section">';
    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 0px; font-weight: 500; color: #2c3e50; margin-bottom: 5px; padding-top: 15px;">Erwartet</h4>';

    html += '<div class="weather-table" style="max-height: 161px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += '<div class="expected-header-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">ETA</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Schiff</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Letzter Hafen</div>';
    html += '</div>';

	expectedList.forEach(entry => {
    const next = entry.next || {};
    const prev = entry.prev || {};

    // Distanz in NM
    let distanceNM = 'N/A';
    if (next.rtd != null && !isNaN(next.rtd)) {
        distanceNM = (next.rtd / 1852).toFixed(1) + ' NM';
    }

    // Flagge mit Fallback
    let flagHTML = '';
    if (entry.a2) {
        const code = entry.a2.toLowerCase();
        flagHTML = `<img loading="lazy" class="port-flag-header" src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/${code}.svg" alt="${entry.country || ''}" 
            style="display: inline-block; width: 28px; height: 21px; margin-right: 10px; margin-top: 3px; align-content: center; justify-content: center; border: 1px solid #000; box-shadow: unset;"
            onerror="this.src='https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png'">`;
    }

    // ATD Zeit formatieren - verwende rpatd statt rpatd
    let atdString = '';
    if (prev.rpatd && !isNaN(prev.rpatd) && prev.rpatd > 0) {
        const atdDate = new Date(prev.rpatd * 1000); // Timestamp in ms
        const options = { year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', timeZone: 'UTC', hour12: false };
        atdString = `<br><div style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #888; width: 105px;">${atdDate.toLocaleString('de-DE', options)}</div>`;
    }

    // Schiff mit oder ohne Link
    const shipName = entry.name || 'N/A';
    let shipHTML = '';
    if (shipName !== 'N/A' && entry.mmsi) {
        shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer; padding-top: 2px;" onclick="handleURLShip('${entry.mmsi}',0,'${shipName}')" class="weather-col-date notranslate">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
    } else {
        shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500;" class="weather-col-date notranslate">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
    }

    // Letzter Hafen mit oder ohne Link - KORREKTUR: Verwende prev.rpna und prev.rpid
    const lastPort = prev.rpna || 'N/A';
    let lastPortHTML = '';
    if (lastPort !== 'N/A') {
        // Hafen ist immer verlinkt, solange er nicht N/A ist
        const portId = prev.rpid || ''; // rpid aus den Daten verwenden
        lastPortHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate"><span style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer;" onclick="isLoadingShipFromURL= false; handleURLShip(0,'${portId}','${lastPort}')">${truncateString(lastPort,13)}</span>${atdString}</div>`;
    } else {
        lastPortHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate"><p style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500; margin-top: 0px;">${lastPort}</p>${atdString}</div>`;
    }

    html += '<div class="expected-row">';
    html += `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate" style="margin-top: -1px;">${next.ceta || entry.formattedETA || 'N/A'}</div>`;
    html += shipHTML;
    html += lastPortHTML;
    html += '</div>';
	});

    html += '</div>'; // weather-table
    html += '</div>'; // port-weather-section

    return html;
}

function generateArrivalsSection(arrivalsList) {
    if (!arrivalsList || !Array.isArray(arrivalsList) || arrivalsList.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    let html = '<div class="port-weather-section">';
    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 0px; font-weight: 500; color: #2c3e50; margin-bottom: 5px; padding-top: 15px; border-top: 0px solid #eee;">Ankünfte</h4>';

    html += '<div class="weather-table" style="max-height: 161px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += '<div class="expected-header-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Ankunft (LT)</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Schiff</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Letzter Hafen</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    arrivalsList.forEach(entry => {
        const prev = entry.prev || {};

        // Flagge mit Fallback
        let flagHTML = '';
        if (entry.a2) {
            const code = entry.a2.toLowerCase();
            flagHTML = `<img loading="lazy" class="port-flag-header" src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/${code}.svg" alt="${entry.country || ''}" 
                style="display: inline-block; width: 28px; height: 21px; margin-right: 10px; margin-top: 3px; align-content: center; justify-content: center; border: 1px solid #000; box-shadow: unset;"
                onerror="this.src='https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png'">`;
        }

        // ATD Zeit formatieren (rpdatd = Reported Port ATD)
        let atdString = '';
        if (prev.rpdatd && !isNaN(prev.rpdatd) && prev.rpdatd > 0) {
            const atdDate = new Date(prev.rpdatd * 1000); // Timestamp in ms
            const options = { 
                year: 'numeric', 
                month: 'short', 
                day: 'numeric', 
                hour: '2-digit', 
                minute: '2-digit', 
                timeZone: 'UTC', 
                hour12: false 
            };
            atdString = `<br><div style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #888; width: 105px;">${atdDate.toLocaleString('de-DE', options)}</div>`;
        }

        // Schiff mit oder ohne Link
        const shipName = entry.name || 'N/A';
        let shipHTML = '';
        if (shipName !== 'N/A' && entry.mmsi) {
            shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer; padding-top: 2px;" onclick="handleURLShip('${entry.mmsi}',0,'${shipName}')" class="weather-col-date notranslate">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
        } else {
            shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500;" class="weather-col-date notranslate">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
        }

        // Letzter Hafen mit oder ohne Link
        const lastPort = prev.rpdna || 'N/A';
        let lastPortHTML = '';
        if (lastPort !== 'N/A' && prev.rpdid) {
            lastPortHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate"><span style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer;" onclick="isLoadingShipFromURL= false; handleURLShip(0,'${prev.rpdid}','${lastPort}')">${truncateString(lastPort,13)}</span>${atdString}</div>`;
        } else {
            lastPortHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate"><p style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500; margin-top: -1px;">${lastPort}</p>${atdString}</div>`;
        }

        html += '<div class="expected-row">';
        html += `<div class="weather-col-date notranslate" style="margin-top: -1px;">${entry.formattedETA || 'N/A'}</div>`;
        html += shipHTML;
        html += lastPortHTML;
        html += '</div>';
    });

    html += '</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    return html;
}

function generateDeparturesSection(departuresList) {
    if (!departuresList || !Array.isArray(departuresList) || departuresList.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    let html = '<div class="port-weather-section">';
    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 0px; font-weight: 500; color: #2c3e50; margin-bottom: 5px; padding-top: 15px; border-top: 0px solid #eee;">Abfahrten</h4>';

    html += '<div class="weather-table" style="max-height: 161px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += '<div class="expected-header-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Abfahrt (LT)</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Schiff</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Ziel</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    departuresList.forEach(entry => {
        const next = entry.next || {};

        // Flagge mit Fallback
        let flagHTML = '';
        if (entry.a2) {
            const code = entry.a2.toLowerCase();
            flagHTML = `<img loading="lazy" class="port-flag-header" src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/${code}.svg" alt="${entry.country || ''}" 
                style="display: inline-block; width: 28px; height: 21px; margin-right: 10px; margin-top: 3px; align-content: center; justify-content: center; border: 1px solid #000; box-shadow: unset;"
                onerror="this.src='https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png'">`;
        }

        // Schiff mit oder ohne Link
        const shipName = entry.name || 'N/A';
        let shipHTML = '';
        if (shipName !== 'N/A' && entry.mmsi) {
            shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer; padding-top: 2px;" onclick="handleURLShip('${entry.mmsi}',0,'${shipName}')" class="weather-col-date">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
        } else {
            shipHTML = `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500;" class="weather-col-date">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(entry.type || '', 15)}</p></div>`;
        }

        // Zielhafen mit oder ohne Link
        const destination = next.npna || 'N/A';
        let destinationHTML = '';
        if (destination !== 'N/A' && next.npid) {
            destinationHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date"><p style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer; margin-top: 10px; height: 10px;" onclick="isLoadingShipFromURL= false; handleURLShip(0,'${next.npid}','${destination}')">${truncateString(destination,15)}</p></div>`;
        } else {
            destinationHTML = `<div class="weather-col-date"><p style="font-size: 13px; color: #333; font-weight: 500; margin-top: -1px; height: 10px;">${destination}</p></div>`;
        }

        html += '<div class="expected-row">';
        html += `<div class="weather-col-date" style="margin-top: -1px; height: 10px;">${entry.formattedETA || 'N/A'}</div>`;
        html += shipHTML;
        html += destinationHTML;
        html += '</div>';
    });

    html += '</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    return html;
}

function generateInPortSection(inPortList) {
    if (!inPortList || !Array.isArray(inPortList) || inPortList.length === 0) {
        return '';
    }

    // Fallback truncateString Funktion falls nicht vorhanden
    const truncateString = (str, maxLength) => {
        if (typeof str !== 'string') return '';
        if (str.length <= maxLength) return str;
        return str.substring(0, maxLength) + '...';
    };

    let html = '<div class="port-weather-section" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">';
    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 0px; font-weight: 500; color: #2c3e50; margin-bottom: 5px; padding-top: 15px; border-top: 0px solid #eee;">Im Hafen</h4>';

    html += '<div class="weather-table" style="max-height: 163px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += '<div class="expected-header-row">';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Bericht</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Schiff</div>';
    html += '<div class="weather-col-date">Terminal</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    inPortList.forEach(entry => {
        // Flagge mit Fallback
        let flagHTML = '';
        if (entry.a2) {
            const code = entry.a2.toLowerCase();
            flagHTML = `<img loading="lazy" class="port-flag-header" src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/flag-icon-css/3.3.0/flags/4x3/${code}.svg" alt="${entry.country || ''}" 
                style="display: inline-block; width: 28px; height: 21px; margin-right: 10px; margin-top: 3px; align-content: center; justify-content: center; border: 1px solid #000; box-shadow: unset;"
                onerror="this.src='https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Flag_of_None.svg/225px-Flag_of_None.svg.png'">`;
        }

        // Letzten Bericht formatieren (verwende formattedETA oder ähnliches Feld)
        let lastReport = 'N/A';
        if (entry.formattedETA) {
            lastReport = entry.formattedETA;
        }

        // Sicherstellen, dass die Werte definiert sind
        const shipName = entry.name || 'N/A';
        const shipType = entry.type || '';
        const terminal = entry.term || 'N/A';

        html += '<div class="expected-row">';
        html += `<div class="weather-col-date" style="margin-top: -1px; height: 10px;">${lastReport}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #0a84f1; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer; margin-top: 0px;" onclick="handleURLShip('${entry.mmsi}',0,'${shipName}')" class="weather-col-date">${flagHTML}${truncateString(shipName, 8)}<br><p style="font-size: 0.8em; color:#666;  margin-top: 0px;">${truncateString(shipType, 15)}</p></div>`;
        html += `<div class="weather-col-date" style="font-size: 13px; margin-top: -1px; font-weight: 500; height: 10px;">${truncateString(terminal, 13)}</div>`;
        html += '</div>';
    });

    html += '</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    return html;
}

function updatePortMetaTags(port, values) {
    const portName = port.name || values.port_name || 'N/A Port';
    const country = values.country || port.country || '';
    const unlocode = values.unlocode || port.unlocode || '';
    const lat = port.lat ? port.lat.toFixed(4) : 'N/A';
    const lng = port.lng ? port.lng.toFixed(4) : 'N/A';
    const shipsInPort = values.shipcount || port.shipsInPort || 0;

    // Titel
    document.title = 'Schiffsradar ' + portName + ' ('+unlocode.toUpperCase()+') - Aktuelle Informationen | MarineTraffic';

    // Meta Description
    let metaDescription = document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]');
    if (!metaDescription) {
        metaDescription = document.createElement('meta');
        metaDescription.name = 'description';
        document.head.appendChild(metaDescription);
    }
    metaDescription.content = 'Hafen ' + portName + 
        (country ? ' in ' + country : '') +
        '. UNLOCODE: ' + unlocode +
        '. Aktuelle Position: ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '°' +
        '. ' + shipsInPort + ' Schiffe im Hafen. Live AIS Tracking auf MarineTraffic.';

    // Open Graph Tags
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:title', 'Schiffsradar ' + portName + ' ('+unlocode.toUpperCase()+') - Aktuelle Informationen | MarineTraffic');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:description', 'Live Hafen-Tracking von ' + portName +  ' (' + unlocode.toUpperCase() + ')' +  (country ? ' (' + country + ')' : '') + '. Position: ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '°. ' + shipsInPort + ' Schiffe im Hafen.');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:type', 'website');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('property', 'og:url', window.location.href);

    // Twitter Tags
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:card', 'summary');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:title', 'Schiffsradar ' + portName + ' ('+unlocode.toUpperCase()+') - Aktuelle Informationen | MarineTraffic');
    updateOrCreateMetaTag('name', 'twitter:description', 'Live Hafen-Tracking: ' + portName + 
        ' (UNLOCODE: ' + unlocode + ') - Position: ' + lat + '°, ' + lng + '°');

    // Structured Data
    let jsonLdScript = document.querySelector('script[type="application/ld+json"]');
    if (!jsonLdScript) {
        jsonLdScript = document.createElement('script');
        jsonLdScript.type = 'application/ld+json';
        document.head.appendChild(jsonLdScript);
    }

const structuredData = {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "LocalBusiness", // GEÄNDERT: Dies steht in der Liste der unterstützten Typen für Sterne
    "name": portName,
    "image": "https://marinetraffic.live/app-logo.png", // PFLICHT: Für LocalBusiness wird ein Bild benötigt
    "address": {
        "@type": "PostalAddress",
        "addressCountry": country
    },
    "geo": {
        "@type": "GeoCoordinates",
        "latitude": lat,
        "longitude": lng
    },
    "aggregateRating": {
        "@type": "AggregateRating",
        "ratingValue": "4.6",
        "bestRating": "5",
        "ratingCount": "3543"
    },
    "identifier": unlocode
};

    jsonLdScript.textContent = JSON.stringify(structuredData);
}

// 2. NEUE FUNKTION: Schiff eindeutig finden
function findExistingShipById(mmsi, shipName, shipId) {
    if (!ships || ships.length === 0) return null;

    // Priorität 1: Ship-ID Match (eindeutigste Identifikation)
    if (shipId) {
        const shipByShipId = ships.find(ship => 
            ship.shipId && ship.shipId === shipId
        );
        if (shipByShipId) {
            console.log('✅ Ship found by Ship-ID:', shipId);
            return shipByShipId;
        }
    }

    // Priorität 2: MMSI Match (sehr zuverlässig)
    if (mmsi) {
        const shipByMMSI = ships.find(ship => 
            ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === mmsi
        );
        if (shipByMMSI) {
            console.log('✅ Ship found by MMSI:', mmsi);
            return shipByMMSI;
        }
    }

    // Priorität 3: Name Match (nur als letzter Ausweg)
    if (shipName) {
        const shipsByName = ships.filter(ship => 
            ship.name && ship.name.toLowerCase().trim() === shipName.toLowerCase().trim()
        );
        
        if (shipsByName.length === 1) {
            console.log('✅ Ship found by unique name:', shipName);
            return shipsByName[0];
        } else if (shipsByName.length > 1) {
            console.warn('⚠️ Multiple ships with same name found:', shipName, shipsByName.length);
            // Wenn Ship-ID verfügbar ist, verwende sie als Tiebreaker
            if (shipId) {
                const exactMatch = shipsByName.find(ship => ship.shipId === shipId);
                if (exactMatch) {
                    console.log('✅ Ship found by name + shipId combination');
                    return exactMatch;
                }
            }
            // Sonst nimm das erste (kann falsch sein)
            console.warn('⚠️ Taking first ship with matching name - might be wrong!');
            return shipsByName[0];
        }
    }

    console.log('❌ No ship found for:', { mmsi, shipName, shipId });
    return null;
}

function showLoading() {
   if (!resultsContainer) return;
   resultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
   resultsContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">🔍 Suche läuft...</div>';
}

function showError() {
   if (!resultsContainer) return;
   resultsContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results"><div class="no-results-icon">⚠️</div><div>Fehler beim Laden der Suchergebnisse</div></div>';
}

function extractFlag(desc) {
   if (!desc || typeof desc !== 'string') {
       return null;
   }
   const match = desc.match(/\[([A-Z]{2})\]/);
   return match ? match[1] : null;
}

function getVesselTypeIcon(desc) {
   return '';
}

// URL handling functions
async function handleURLShip(mmsi, port, name) {
    if (isLoadingShipFromURL) {
        flytime = 1000;
        console.log('Already loading ship from URL, skipping...');
        return;
    }


    const path = window.location.pathname;
    console.log('=== handleURLShip CALLED with path:', path);

    const shipUrlPattern = /\/([^\/]+)-position\/(\d+)\/?$/;
    const portUrlPattern = /\/([^\/]+)-port\/([a-zA-Z0-9]+)\/?$/;
    const portUrlPattern2 = /\/([^\/]+)-port\//;
	
    const shipMatch = path.match(shipUrlPattern);
    const portMatch = path.match(portUrlPattern);
    const portMatch2 = path.match(portUrlPattern2);	

    if (shipMatch && !port) {
        isLoadingShipFromURL = true;
        const shipNameFromURL = shipMatch[1] || name;
        const identifier = shipMatch[2] || ship;
        
        const shipName = ucwords(shipNameFromURL.replace(/-/g, ' '));

        // Verwende identifier als MMSI - getShipIdFromMMSI erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
        console.log('Found ship in URL:', shipName, 'Identifier:', identifier);

        const shipFromURL = {
            name: shipName,
            mmsi: identifier, // Funktion erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
            imo: identifier, // Funktion erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
            lat: map.getCenter().lat,
            lng: map.getCenter().lng,
            speed: 0,
            course: 0,
            type: 'N/A',
            shipId: null
        };

        flytime = 3000;
        showShipDetails(shipFromURL, true);
        
    } else if (mmsi && !port) {
        isLoadingShipFromURL = true;
        const shipNameFromURL = name;
        const identifier = mmsi;
        
        const shipName = ucwords(shipNameFromURL.replace(/-/g, ' '));

        // Verwende identifier als MMSI - getShipIdFromMMSI erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
        console.log('Found ship in URL:', shipName, 'Identifier:', identifier);

        const shipFromURL = {
            name: shipName,
            mmsi: identifier, // Funktion erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
            imo: identifier, // Funktion erkennt automatisch ob es IMO ist
            lat: map.getCenter().lat,
            lng: map.getCenter().lng,
            speed: 0,
            course: 0,
            type: 'N/A',
            shipId: null
        };

        flytime = 3000;
        showShipDetails(shipFromURL, true);
        
    } else if (portMatch || port) {
        // PORT URL HANDLING (bleibt unverändert)
        isLoadingShipFromURL = true;

        var portNameFromURL;
        var portIdOrCode; 
        var portName;
        
		if(port) {
        portNameFromURL = name;
        portIdOrCode = port; 
        portName = name;
		
		console.log('Found port:', name, 'portIdOrCode',port);	
		}else {	
        portNameFromURL = portMatch[1];
        portIdOrCode = portMatch[2]; 
        portName = ucwords(portNameFromURL.replace(/-/g, ' '));
		console.log('Found port in URL:', portName, 'portIdOrCode',portIdOrCode)
		}
		
        const portFromURL = {
            name: portName || name,
            id: portIdOrCode || port,
            type: 'Port'
        };

        selectedPort = {
            portId: portIdOrCode || port,
            portName: portName || name,
            lat: null,
            lng: null
        };

        needsRedraw = true;

        flytime = 3000;
		
        showPortDetails(portFromURL, true);
	} else if (portMatch2) {
        portNameFromURL = portMatch2[1];
        portName = ucwords(portNameFromURL.replace(/-/g, ' '));
		const validate = await validatePortId(portName);

		const portFromURL = {
            name: portName,
            id: validate,
            type: 'Port'
        };	
		
        selectedPort = {
            portId: validate,
            portName: portName,
            lat: null,
            lng: null
        };

		showPortDetails(portFromURL, true);
	 } else {
        console.log('No ship or port pattern found in URL:', path);
    }
}

function ucwords(str) {
    return str.toLowerCase().replace(/\b[a-z]/g, function(letter) {
        return letter.toUpperCase();
    });
}

       handleURLShip();
   }
});

   stopAutoRefresh();
});

let tabInactiveTimer = null;

document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
    if (document.hidden) {
        console.log('[Auto Refresh] Tab hidden - pausing auto refresh');
        stopAutoRefresh();
        // NEU: Animation stoppen
        if (animationId) {
            cancelAnimationFrame(animationId);
            animationId = null;
        }
    } else {
        console.log('[Auto Refresh] Tab visible - resuming auto refresh');
        
        // NEU: Sanfter Neustart mit Verzögerung
        setTimeout(() => {
            // Canvas einmal neu zeichnen statt viele aufgestaute Updates
            if (shipCanvas && shipCtx) {
                shipCtx.clearRect(0, 0, shipCanvas.width, shipCanvas.height);
            }
            
            // Schiffe neu laden
			masterShipList.clear();
            incomingShips.clear();
            loadRealShips();
            
            // Animation verzögert starten
            setTimeout(() => {
                startAutoRefresh();
                animate();
                needsRedraw = true;
            }, 0);
        }, 0);
    }
});

function CanvasFixOnLowEndDevice() {
   const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
	   // Sanfter Zoom (weniger merkbar)
	   //map.setZoom(currentZoom + 1);
       map.setZoom(currentZoom+0.0001);
       // Schiffe neu laden falls noch keine da
       loadRealShips();
	   needsRedraw: true;
	   drawShips();
}

// Vollbild Funktionalität
let isFullscreen = false;

function toggleFullscreen() {
    const fullscreenButton = document.getElementById('fullscreenButton');
    const fullscreenIcon = document.getElementById('fullscreenIcon');
    
    if (!isFullscreen) {
        enterFullscreen();
    } else {
        exitFullscreen();
    }
}

function enterFullscreen() {
    const element = document.documentElement;
    
    if (element.requestFullscreen) {
        element.requestFullscreen();
    } else if (element.webkitRequestFullscreen) {
        element.webkitRequestFullscreen();
    } else if (element.mozRequestFullScreen) {
        element.mozRequestFullScreen();
    } else if (element.msRequestFullscreen) {
        element.msRequestFullscreen();
    }
}

function exitFullscreen() {
    if (document.exitFullscreen) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
    } else if (document.webkitExitFullscreen) {
        document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    } else if (document.mozCancelFullScreen) {
        document.mozCancelFullScreen();
    } else if (document.msExitFullscreen) {
        document.msExitFullscreen();
    }
}

function updateFullscreenButton() {
    const fullscreenButton = document.getElementById('fullscreenButton');
    const fullscreenIcon = document.getElementById('fullscreenIcon');
    
    isFullscreen = !!(document.fullscreenElement || 
                     document.webkitFullscreenElement || 
                     document.mozFullScreenElement || 
                     document.msFullscreenElement);
    
    if (isFullscreen) {
        fullscreenButton.classList.add('fullscreen-active');
        fullscreenButton.title = 'Vollbild verlassen';
        
        // Icon zu "Minimize" ändern
        fullscreenIcon.innerHTML = '<path d="M8 3v3a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H3m18 0h-3a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V3m0 18v-3a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h3M3 16h3a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v3"/>';
    } else {
        fullscreenButton.classList.remove('fullscreen-active');
        fullscreenButton.title = 'Vollbild';
        
        // Icon zu "Expand" zurück ändern
        fullscreenIcon.innerHTML = '<path d="M8 3H5a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v3m18 0V5a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-3m0 18h3a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-3M3 16v3a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h3"/>';
    }
    
    console.log('📺 Vollbild Status:', isFullscreen ? 'Aktiv' : 'Inaktiv');
}

// Event Listeners für Vollbild-Änderungen
document.addEventListener('fullscreenchange', updateFullscreenButton);
document.addEventListener('webkitfullscreenchange', updateFullscreenButton);
document.addEventListener('mozfullscreenchange', updateFullscreenButton);
document.addEventListener('MSFullscreenChange', updateFullscreenButton);

// Hilfsfunktion: Filter aus localStorage laden
function loadFilterPreferences() {
    try {
        console.log('📂 === LOAD FILTER PREFERENCES START ===');
        
        const saved = localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences');
        if (saved) {
            const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);
            console.log('📂 Geladene Preferences:', parsed);
            
            // Schiffstyp-Filter laden
            if (parsed.shipTypes) {
                Object.assign(activeShipTypeFilters, parsed.shipTypes);
                console.log('📂 Ship types loaded:', activeShipTypeFilters);
            }
            
            // STATUS-FILTER LADEN - VORSICHTIG!
            if (parsed.shipStatus) {
                console.log('📂 Status-Filter aus localStorage:', parsed.shipStatus);
                
                // NUR überschreiben wenn gültige Werte vorhanden sind
                if (typeof parsed.shipStatus.CheckMoving === 'boolean') {
                    window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckMoving != parsed.shipStatus.CheckMoving;
                }
                if (typeof parsed.shipStatus.CheckStopped === 'boolean') {
                    window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckStopped != parsed.shipStatus.CheckStopped;
                }
                
                console.log('📂 Status-Filter nach Laden:', JSON.stringify(window.activeShipStatusFilters));
            } else {
                console.log('📂 Keine Status-Filter in localStorage - behalte aktuelle Werte');
                // NICHT überschreiben wenn nicht vorhanden!
            }
            
            // Schiffstyp-Checkboxen setzen
            Object.keys(activeShipTypeFilters).forEach(type => {
                const checkbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-' + type);
                if (checkbox) {
                    checkbox.checked = activeShipTypeFilters[type];
                }
            });
            
            // STATUS-CHECKBOXEN SETZEN - NACH dem Laden!
            setTimeout(() => {
                console.log('📂 Setze Status-Checkboxen basierend auf:', window.activeShipStatusFilters);
                
                const stoppedCheckbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-CheckStopped');
                if (stoppedCheckbox) {
                    // API false = Schiffe anzeigen = Checkbox checked
                    const shouldBeChecked = window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckStopped;
                    stoppedCheckbox.checked = shouldBeChecked;
                    console.log('📂 CheckStopped Checkbox gesetzt auf:', shouldBeChecked);
                }
                
                const movingCheckbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-CheckMoving');
                if (movingCheckbox) {
                    // API false = Schiffe anzeigen = Checkbox checked
                    const shouldBeChecked = window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckMoving;
                    movingCheckbox.checked = shouldBeChecked;
                    console.log('📂 CheckMoving Checkbox gesetzt auf:', shouldBeChecked);
                }
            }, 100);
            
            if (typeof updateToggleAllButton === 'function') {
                updateToggleAllButton();
            }
        } else {
            console.log('📂 Keine gespeicherten Preferences gefunden');
        }
        
        console.log('📂 Final activeShipStatusFilters:', JSON.stringify(window.activeShipStatusFilters));
        console.log('📂 === LOAD FILTER PREFERENCES END ===');
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Fehler beim Laden der Filter Preferences:', error);
    }
}

// Hilfsfunktion: Filter in localStorage speichern
function saveFilterPreferences() {
    try {
        console.log('💾 === SAVE FILTER PREFERENCES START ===');
        console.log('Saving activeShipStatusFilters:', JSON.stringify(window.activeShipStatusFilters));
        
        const preferences = {
            overlays: [],
            shipTypes: activeShipTypeFilters,
            shipStatus: window.activeShipStatusFilters  // EXPLIZIT window.activeShipStatusFilters verwenden
        };

        // Overlay-Layer sammeln
        document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox:checked').forEach(function(checkbox) {
            const layerName = checkbox.id.replace('layer-', '');
            preferences.overlays.push(layerName);
        });

        localStorage.setItem('layerPreferences', JSON.stringify(preferences));
        console.log('💾 Preferences gespeichert:', JSON.stringify(preferences));
        console.log('💾 === SAVE FILTER PREFERENCES END ===');
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Fehler beim Speichern der Filter Preferences:', error);
    }
}

// ============================================
// GLOBALE FILTER-VARIABLEN
// ============================================
let speedRangeFilter = [0, 100];
let yobRangeFilter = [1950, 2025];
let loRangeFilter = [0, 500];
let navstatusFilter = "";

// ============================================
// FRÜHE INITIALISIERUNG - Läuft SOFORT beim Script-Load
// ============================================
(function initializeFiltersEarly() {
    console.log('🔄 === EARLY FILTER INIT ===');
    
    // Initialisiere globale Filter-Objekte mit Defaults
    if (!window.activeShipTypeFilters) {
        window.activeShipTypeFilters = {
            '0': true, '1': true, '2': true, '3': true,
            '4': true, '6': true, '7': true, '8': true, '9': true
        };
    }
    
    if (!window.activeShipStatusFilters) {
        window.activeShipStatusFilters = {CheckMoving: true, CheckStopped: true};
    }
    
    // Lade gespeicherte Filter aus localStorage
    try {
        const masterSaved = localStorage.getItem('masterShipFilters');
        if (masterSaved) {
            const filters = JSON.parse(masterSaved);
            console.log('📂 Loading saved filters:', filters);
            
            // Setze alle Filter-Variablen
            if (filters.speedFilter) speedRangeFilter = filters.speedFilter;
            if (filters.yobFilter) yobRangeFilter = filters.yobFilter;
            if (filters.loFilter) loRangeFilter = filters.loFilter;
            if (filters.navstatusFilter !== undefined) navstatusFilter = filters.navstatusFilter;
            
            if (filters.shipTypes) {
                Object.assign(window.activeShipTypeFilters, filters.shipTypes);
            }
            
            if (filters.shipStatus) {
                if (typeof filters.shipStatus.CheckMoving === 'boolean') {
                    window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckMoving = filters.shipStatus.CheckMoving;
                }
                if (typeof filters.shipStatus.CheckStopped === 'boolean') {
                    window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckStopped = filters.shipStatus.CheckStopped;
                }
            }
            
            console.log('✅ Filters loaded from storage');
        }
        
        // LEGACY: Lade auch aus altem Format falls vorhanden
        const legacySaved = localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences');
        if (!masterSaved && legacySaved) {
            const legacy = JSON.parse(legacySaved);
            if (legacy.shipTypes) {
                Object.assign(window.activeShipTypeFilters, legacy.shipTypes);
            }
            if (legacy.shipStatus) {
                Object.assign(window.activeShipStatusFilters, legacy.shipStatus);
            }
            console.log('📂 Loaded from legacy format');
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading filters:', error);
    }
    
    console.log('Filter state after init:', {
        shipTypes: window.activeShipTypeFilters,
        shipStatus: window.activeShipStatusFilters
    });
})();

// ============================================
// SPEICHER-FUNKTIONEN
// ============================================
function saveAllFilters() {
    try {
        const allFilters = {
            speedFilter: speedRangeFilter,
            yobFilter: yobRangeFilter,
            loFilter: loRangeFilter,
            navstatusFilter: navstatusFilter,
            shipTypes: window.activeShipTypeFilters || {},
            shipStatus: window.activeShipStatusFilters || {CheckMoving: true, CheckStopped: true},
            savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        
        localStorage.setItem('masterShipFilters', JSON.stringify(allFilters));
        console.log('💾 Filters saved');
        
        // Legacy format für Kompatibilität
        const legacyPreferences = {
            overlays: [],
            shipTypes: allFilters.shipTypes,
            shipStatus: allFilters.shipStatus
        };
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.layer-checkbox:checked').forEach(function(checkbox) {
            const layerName = checkbox.id.replace('layer-', '');
            legacyPreferences.overlays.push(layerName);
        });
        
        localStorage.setItem('layerPreferences', JSON.stringify(legacyPreferences));
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error saving filters:', error);
    }
}

// UI-Update Funktion (ohne Filter anzuwenden)
function updateUIFromSavedFilters() {
    try {
        // Speed Range UI
        const speedMin = document.getElementById('speedMin');
        const speedMax = document.getElementById('speedMax');
        if (speedMin && speedMax) {
            speedMin.value = speedRangeFilter[0];
            speedMax.value = speedRangeFilter[1];
            updateSliderDisplay('speed', 'minValueDisplay', 'maxValueDisplay');
        }
        
        // Year of Build UI
        const yobMin = document.getElementById('yobMin');
        const yobMax = document.getElementById('yobMax');
        if (yobMin && yobMax) {
            yobMin.value = yobRangeFilter[0];
            yobMax.value = yobRangeFilter[1];
            updateSliderDisplay('yob', 'yobMinValueDisplay', 'yobMaxValueDisplay');
        }
        
        // Length Overall UI
        const loMin = document.getElementById('loMin');
        const loMax = document.getElementById('loMax');
        if (loMin && loMax) {
            loMin.value = loRangeFilter[0];
            loMax.value = loRangeFilter[1];
            updateSliderDisplay('lo', 'loMinValueDisplay', 'loMaxValueDisplay');
        }
        
        // Navigation Status UI
        const navSelect = document.getElementById('nav-status');
        if (navSelect) {
            navSelect.value = navstatusFilter;
        }
        
        // Schiffstyp-Checkboxen UI
        Object.keys(window.activeShipTypeFilters).forEach(type => {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-' + type);
            if (checkbox) {
                checkbox.checked = window.activeShipTypeFilters[type];
            }
        });
        
        // Status-Checkboxen UI
        const movingCheckbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-CheckMoving');
        const stoppedCheckbox = document.getElementById('filter-type-CheckStopped');
        if (movingCheckbox) {
            movingCheckbox.checked = window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckMoving;
        }
        if (stoppedCheckbox) {
            stoppedCheckbox.checked = window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckStopped;
        }
        
        // Toggle-Button aktualisieren
        if (typeof updateToggleAllButton === 'function') {
            updateToggleAllButton();
        }
        
        console.log('📂 UI updated from saved filters');
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error updating UI:', error);
    }
}

// ============================================
// SLIDER DISPLAY FUNKTIONEN
// ============================================
function updateSliderDisplay(sliderId, minValueId, maxValueId) {
    const minSlider = document.getElementById(sliderId + 'Min');
    const maxSlider = document.getElementById(sliderId + 'Max');
    const minDisplay = document.getElementById(minValueId);
    const maxDisplay = document.getElementById(maxValueId);
    
    if (!minSlider || !maxSlider) return;
    
    let minVal = parseInt(minSlider.value);
    let maxVal = parseInt(maxSlider.value);
    
    if (minVal > maxVal) {
        [minVal, maxVal] = [maxVal, minVal];
        minSlider.value = minVal;
        maxSlider.value = maxVal;
    }
    
    if (minDisplay) minDisplay.textContent = minVal;
    if (maxDisplay) maxDisplay.textContent = maxVal;
    
    return [minVal, maxVal];
}

// ============================================
// FILTER APPLY FUNKTIONEN (beim Release)
// ============================================
let applyTimeout = null;

function applyFiltersWithDebounce() {
    // Clear existing timeout
    if (applyTimeout) {
        clearTimeout(applyTimeout);
    }
    
    // Debounce - warte 300ms
    applyTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        console.log('🔄 Applying filters...');
        
        if (typeof applyFiltersDirectAPI === 'function') {
            applyFiltersDirectAPI();
        } else if (typeof loadRealShips === 'function') {
            loadRealShips();
        }
        
        // Redraw nach kurzer Verzögerung
        setTimeout(() => {
            needsRedraw = true;
            if (typeof drawShips === 'function') {
                drawShips();
            }
        }, 50);
        
    }, 100);
}

function applySpeedFilter() {
    const values = updateSliderDisplay('speed', 'minValueDisplay', 'maxValueDisplay');
    if (!values) return;
    
    speedRangeFilter = values;
    console.log('Speed filter:', speedRangeFilter);
    
    saveAllFilters();
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

function applyYOBFilter() {
    const values = updateSliderDisplay('yob', 'yobMinValueDisplay', 'yobMaxValueDisplay');
    if (!values) return;
    
    yobRangeFilter = values;
    console.log('YOB filter:', yobRangeFilter);
    
    saveAllFilters();
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

function applyLOFilter() {
    const values = updateSliderDisplay('lo', 'loMinValueDisplay', 'loMaxValueDisplay');
    if (!values) return;
    
    loRangeFilter = values;
    console.log('LO filter:', loRangeFilter);
    
    saveAllFilters();
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

function updateNavStatus() {
    const navSelect = document.getElementById('nav-status');
    if (!navSelect) return;
    
    navstatusFilter = navSelect.value;
    console.log('Nav status:', navstatusFilter);
    
    saveAllFilters();
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

// ============================================
// INTEGRATION MIT EXISTIERENDEN FUNKTIONEN
// ============================================
function toggleAllShipTypes() {
    if (!window.activeShipTypeFilters) return;
    
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.filter-checkbox');
    const allChecked = Object.values(window.activeShipTypeFilters).every(value => value === true);
    
    const newState = !allChecked;
    
    Object.keys(window.activeShipTypeFilters).forEach(type => {
        window.activeShipTypeFilters[type] = newState;
    });
    
    checkboxes.forEach(checkbox => {
        checkbox.checked = newState;
    });
    
    saveAllFilters();
    
    if (typeof updateToggleAllButton === 'function') {
        updateToggleAllButton();
    }
    
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

function handleFilterChange(checkbox) {
    const fullId = checkbox.id;
    const isChecked = checkbox.checked;
    
    // Initialisiere falls nötig
    if (!window.activeShipStatusFilters) {
        window.activeShipStatusFilters = {CheckMoving: true, CheckStopped: true};
    }
    if (!window.activeShipTypeFilters) {
        window.activeShipTypeFilters = {
            '0': true, '1': true, '2': true, '3': true,
            '4': true, '6': true, '7': true, '8': true, '9': true
        };
    }
    
    // Update filter
    if (fullId === 'filter-type-CheckStopped') {
        window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckStopped = isChecked;
    } 
    else if (fullId === 'filter-type-CheckMoving') {
        window.activeShipStatusFilters.CheckMoving = isChecked;
    }
    else {
        const type = fullId.replace('filter-type-', '');
        window.activeShipTypeFilters[type] = isChecked;
    }
    
    saveAllFilters();
    
    if (typeof updateToggleAllButton === 'function') {
        updateToggleAllButton();
    }
    
    applyFiltersWithDebounce();
}

function updateToggleAllButton() {
    const toggleButton = document.querySelector('.filter-toggle-all');
    if (toggleButton && window.activeShipTypeFilters) {
        const allChecked = Object.values(window.activeShipTypeFilters).every(value => value === true);
        toggleButton.textContent = allChecked ? 'Keine' : 'Alle';
    }
}

function setupSpeedSlider() {
    const minSlider = document.getElementById('speedMin');
    const maxSlider = document.getElementById('speedMax');
    
    if (minSlider && maxSlider) {
        minSlider.step = '1';
        maxSlider.step = '1';
        
        minSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
            updateSliderDisplay('speed', 'minValueDisplay', 'maxValueDisplay');
        });
        maxSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
            updateSliderDisplay('speed', 'minValueDisplay', 'maxValueDisplay');
        });
        
        minSlider.addEventListener('change', applySpeedFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('change', applySpeedFilter);
        minSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applySpeedFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applySpeedFilter);
        
        console.log('✅ Speed slider setup');
    }
}

    const minSlider = document.getElementById('yobMin');
    const maxSlider = document.getElementById('yobMax');
    
    if (minSlider && maxSlider) {
        minSlider.step = '1';
        maxSlider.step = '1';
        
        minSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
            updateSliderDisplay('yob', 'yobMinValueDisplay', 'yobMaxValueDisplay');
        });
        maxSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
            updateSliderDisplay('yob', 'yobMinValueDisplay', 'yobMaxValueDisplay');
        });
        
        minSlider.addEventListener('change', applyYOBFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('change', applyYOBFilter);
        minSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applyYOBFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applyYOBFilter);
        
        console.log('✅ YOB slider setup');
    }
}

function setupLOSlider() {
    const minSlider = document.getElementById('loMin');
    const maxSlider = document.getElementById('loMax');

        minSlider.step = '1';
        maxSlider.step = '1';

            updateSliderDisplay('lo', 'loMinValueDisplay', 'loMaxValueDisplay');

            updateSliderDisplay('lo', 'loMinValueDisplay', 'loMaxValueDisplay');
        });
        
        minSlider.addEventListener('change', applyLOFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('change', applyLOFilter);
        minSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applyLOFilter);
        maxSlider.addEventListener('touchend', applyLOFilter);

    }

    setupYOBSlider();
    setupLOSlider();
    
    const navSelect = document.getElementById('nav-status');
    if (navSelect) {
        navSelect.addEventListener('change', updateNavStatus);
        console.log('✅ Nav status dropdown setup');
    }
}

// ============================================
// URL GENERATION
// ============================================


function generateFilterURL(baseUrl) {
    const allShipTypes = ['0', '1', '2', '3', '4', '6', '7', '8', '9'];
    
    const disabledTypes = {};
    allShipTypes.forEach(type => {
        if (window.activeShipTypeFilters && window.activeShipTypeFilters[type] === false) {
            disabledTypes[type] = false;
        }
    });
    
    const filters = {
        type: disabledTypes,
        subtype: {},
        CheckMoving: window.activeShipStatusFilters?.CheckMoving,
        CheckStopped: window.activeShipStatusFilters?.CheckStopped
    };
    
    if (speedRangeFilter[0] !== 0 || speedRangeFilter[1] !== 100) {
        filters.csFilter = speedRangeFilter;
    }
    
    if (yobRangeFilter[0] !== 1950 || yobRangeFilter[1] !== 2025) {
        filters.yobFilter = yobRangeFilter;
    }
    
    if (loRangeFilter[0] !== 0 || loRangeFilter[1] !== 500) {
        filters.loFilter = loRangeFilter;
    }
    
    if (navstatusFilter && navstatusFilter !== "") {
        filters.navstatusFilter = navstatusFilter;
    }
    
    filters.paFilter = [0, 10080];
    
    const activeTypesCount = allShipTypes.filter(type => 
        window.activeShipTypeFilters && window.activeShipTypeFilters[type] === true
    ).length;
    
    if (activeTypesCount === 0) {
        return null;
    }
    
    try {
        const filterString = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(filters));
        return baseUrl + '/filters:' + filterString + '&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0';
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('URL-Encoding Error:', error);
        return baseUrl;
    }
}
