// Projektions-Status verwalten
var currentProjection = 'mercator'; // 'mercator', '3d', 'globe'
let projectionTransitioning = false;

// Text für verschiedene Modi
const projectionTexts = {
    mercator: '2D',
    '3d': '3D',
    globe: '⊕'
};

// Tooltip Texte
const projectionTooltips = {
    mercator: 'Aktuell: 2D Ansicht - Klicken für 3D',
    '3d': 'Aktuell: 3D Ansicht - Klicken für Globus',
    globe: 'Aktuell: Globus - Klicken für 2D'
};

// Hauptfunktion: Projektion wechseln
// EINFACHSTE LÖSUNG: Nur Projektion ändern ohne Map neu zu erstellen

function toggleProjection() {
    if (projectionTransitioning) {
        console.log('🌍 Projektion wechselt bereits - warten...');
        return;
    }
    
    const button = document.getElementById('projectionButton');
    const text = document.getElementById('projectionText');
    
    if (!button || !text) {
        console.error('Projection Button oder Text nicht gefunden');
        return;
    }
    
    projectionTransitioning = true;
    
    // Nächste Projektion bestimmen
    let nextProjection;
    switch(currentProjection) {
        case 'mercator':
            nextProjection = '3d';
            break;
        case '3d':
            nextProjection = 'globe';
            break;
        case 'globe':
            nextProjection = 'mercator';
            break;
        default:
            nextProjection = 'mercator';
    }
    
    console.log(`🔄 Projektionswechsel: ${currentProjection} → ${nextProjection}`);
    
    // Button visuell deaktivieren
    button.style.opacity = '0.5';
    button.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    
    try {
        changeMapProjection(nextProjection).then(() => {
            // Canvas neu dimensionieren
            if (shipCanvas) {
                resizeShipCanvas();
            }
            
            // Performance-Optimierungen anwenden
            applyProjectionOptimizations(nextProjection);
            
            // Animation wieder starten
            animate();
            
            // Schiffe neu laden
                needsRedraw = true;
                if (!isMapMoving) {
                    loadRealShips();
                }
            
            // UI aktualisieren
            updateProjectionButton();
            
            // FINAL SAVE
            setTimeout(() => {
                saveMapState();
                console.log('🔄 Final projection save completed');
            }, 2000);
            
            // Button wieder aktivieren
            button.style.opacity = '1';
            button.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
            projectionTransitioning = false;
            
            console.log(`✅ Projektionswechsel abgeschlossen: ${nextProjection}`);
            showNotification(getProjectionDisplayName(nextProjection));
            
        }).catch(error => {
            console.error('❌ Fehler beim Projektionswechsel:', error);
            
            // Bei Fehler: Button wieder aktivieren
            button.style.opacity = '1';
            button.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
            projectionTransitioning = false;
        });
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Fehler beim Projektionswechsel:', error);
        
        // Button wieder aktivieren bei Fehler
        button.style.opacity = '1';
        button.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
        projectionTransitioning = false;
    }
}

// Performance-Optimierungen je nach Projektion
function applyProjectionOptimizations(projection) {
    const isGlobe = (projection === 'globe');
    
    if (isGlobe) {
        console.log('🌍 Aktiviere Globe-Optimierungen...');
        
        // Weniger Schiffe für Globe
        if (!window.originalMaxShips) {
            window.originalMaxShips = window.MaxShips || 1500;
        }
        
        if (isMobile) {
            window.MaxShips = 800;
		if (isLowEndDevice) { 
	        window.MaxShips = 300;	
		} 
        }else {
            window.MaxShips = 1000;
        }
        
        // Canvas-Qualität für Globe reduzieren
        if (shipCtx) {
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
		} else if (shipCtx && isLowEndDevice) {
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
			shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
		} 
        
    } else {
        console.log('🗺️ Normale Performance-Einstellungen...');
        
        // Normale Einstellungen wiederherstellen
        if (window.originalMaxShips) {
            window.MaxShips = window.originalMaxShips;
        }
        
        // Canvas-Qualität wiederherstellen
        if (shipCtx && !isMobile) {
            shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
            shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';
        } else if (shipCtx && isLowEndDevice) {
		    shipCtx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
		    shipCtx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'low';
		} 
    }
    
    console.log(`🎯 Max Ships für ${projection}:`, window.MaxShips);
}

// Map Projektion tatsächlich ändern
async function changeMapProjection(projection) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        try {
            const currentCenter = map.getCenter();
            const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
            const currentPitch = map.getPitch();
            const currentBearing = map.getBearing();
            
            switch(projection) {
                case 'mercator':
                    map.setProjection({ name: 'mercator' });
                    map.easeTo({
                        pitch: 0,
                        bearing: 0,
                        zoom: Math.max(currentZoom, 3),
                        duration: 1000
                    });
                    break;
                    
                case '3d':
                    map.setProjection({ name: 'mercator' });
                    map.easeTo({
                        pitch: 55,
                        zoom: Math.max(currentZoom, 5),
                        duration: 1000
                    });
                    break;
                    
                case 'globe':          
                    map.setProjection({ name: 'globe' });
                    map.easeTo({
                        pitch: 0,
                        bearing: 0,
                        zoom: Math.min(currentZoom, 1),
                        duration: 1000
                    });
                    break;
                    
                default:
                    throw new Error('Unbekannte Projektion: ' + projection);
            }
            
            // KRITISCH: currentProjection SOFORT setzen (nicht erst nach setTimeout)
            currentProjection = projection;
            console.log('🌍 Current projection set to:', currentProjection);
            
            // MEHRFACHES SPEICHERN für Robustheit
            // 1. Sofort speichern
            saveMapState();
            
            // 2. Nach easeTo-Animation speichern
            setTimeout(() => {
                saveMapState();
                resolve();
            }, 1200);
            
            // 3. Zusätzlicher Save nach weiterer Verzögerung (für Low-End-Geräte)
            setTimeout(() => {
                saveMapState();
                console.log('🔄 Additional save for low-end devices');
            }, 2000);
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error in changeMapProjection:', error);
            reject(error);
        }
    });
}

// Button Text aktualisieren
function updateProjectionButton() {
    const button = document.getElementById('projectionButton');
    const text = document.getElementById('projectionText');
    
    if (!button || !text) return;
    
    // Text aktualisieren
    const buttonText = projectionTexts[currentProjection];
    if (buttonText) {
        text.textContent = buttonText;
    }
    
    // Tooltip aktualisieren
    const tooltip = projectionTooltips[currentProjection];
    if (tooltip) {
        button.title = tooltip;
    }
    
    console.log(`🔄 Button aktualisiert für Projektion: ${currentProjection}`);
}

// Projektions-Namen für Anzeige
function getProjectionDisplayName(projection) {
    const names = {
        mercator: '2D Kartenansicht',
        '3d': '3D Kartenansicht', 
        globe: 'Globus-Ansicht'
    };
    return names[projection] || projection;
}

let isMenuVisible = true; // Wird beim Laden überschrieben

// Menu Status aus localStorage laden
function loadMenuState() {
    try {
        const savedState = localStorage.getItem('menuToggleState');
        if (savedState !== null) {
            isMenuVisible = JSON.parse(savedState);
            console.log('📂 Menu Status geladen:', isMenuVisible ? 'sichtbar' : 'versteckt');
        } else {
            isMenuVisible = true; // Standard: sichtbar
            console.log('🚢 Menu Status Standard: sichtbar');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Fehler beim Laden des Menu Status:', error);
        isMenuVisible = true; // Fallback
    }
}

// Menu Status in localStorage speichern
function saveMenuState() {
    try {
        localStorage.setItem('menuToggleState', JSON.stringify(isMenuVisible));
        console.log('💾 Menu Status gespeichert:', isMenuVisible ? 'sichtbar' : 'versteckt');
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Fehler beim Speichern des Menu Status:', error);
    }
}

// Menu visuell aktualisieren basierend auf isMenuVisible
function updateMenuVisual() {
    const menu = document.getElementById('menu');
    const toggleButton = document.getElementById('menuToggleButton');
    
    if (!menu || !toggleButton) return;
    
    if (isMenuVisible) {
        menu.style.display = 'block';
       if (localStorage.getItem('pro') !=1)
		toggleButton.classList.remove('active');
	
       if (localStorage.getItem('pro') ==1)
		toggleButton.classList.remove('active2');
    } else {
        menu.style.display = 'none';
		
       if (localStorage.getItem('pro') !=1)		
        toggleButton.classList.add('active');

       if (localStorage.getItem('pro') ==1)		
        toggleButton.classList.add('active2');
    }
}

function toggleMenu() {
    // Status umschalten
    isMenuVisible = !isMenuVisible;
    
    // Visuell aktualisieren
    updateMenuVisual();
    
    // Status speichern
    saveMenuState();
    
    console.log('🎮 Menu', isMenuVisible ? 'angezeigt' : 'versteckt');
}

// Menu beim Laden der Seite korrekt initialisieren
function initializeMenu() {
    loadMenuState(); // Status laden
    updateMenuVisual(); // Visuell anwenden
    console.log('🎮 Menu initialisiert mit Status:', isMenuVisible ? 'sichtbar' : 'versteckt');
}

// Beim Laden der Seite initialisieren
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Kurze Verzögerung um sicherzustellen dass alle Elemente geladen sind
    setTimeout(initializeMenu, 100);
});

// Fallback falls DOMContentLoaded bereits ausgeführt wurde
if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeMenu);
} else {
    setTimeout(initializeMenu, 100);
}

console.log('💡 Funktionen: window.getMenuStatus(), window.resetMenuState()');

function drawTrackMarker() {
    if (!trackMarker) {
        return;
    }
    
    if (!shipCanvas || !shipCtx) {
        console.error('❌ Canvas nicht verfügbar für Track Marker');
        return;
    }
    
    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    
    // Track Position projizieren
    const point = map.project([trackMarker.lng, trackMarker.lat]);
    
    // Sichtbarkeitsprüfung
    if (point.x < -100 || point.x > canvasWidth + 100 || 
        point.y < -100 || point.y > canvasHeight + 100) {
        return;
    }
    
    shipCtx.save();
    
    const time = Date.now() / 1000;
    
    // ===== EXAKT GLEICHE FARBEN WIE GPS MARKER =====
    
    // Mehrere pulsierende Ringe für bessere Sichtbarkeit
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    
    // Äußerster pulsierender Ring (GLEICHE BLAUE FARBE)
    const outerPulse = 1 + Math.sin(time * 3) * 0.4;
    const outerRadius = 20 * outerPulse;
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#3b82f6'; // GLEICHE BLAUE FARBE wie GPS
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 2;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.3 / outerPulse;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, outerRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    // Mittlerer pulsierender Ring
    const middlePulse = 1 + Math.sin(time * 4 + 1) * 0.3;
    const middleRadius = 15 * middlePulse;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.4 / middlePulse;
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, middleRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    // Track Marker Hauptkörper (GLEICHE STRUKTUR WIE GPS)
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    
    // Schatten-Effekt
    shipCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x + 1, point.y + 1, 12, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    // Äußerer weißer Kreis (GLEICHE GRÖßE WIE GPS)
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#e5e7eb';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 12, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    // Innerer blauer Kreis (GLEICHE BLAUE FARBE)
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#3b82f6'; // GLEICHE BLAUE FARBE wie GPS
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    // Kleiner weißer Punkt in der Mitte
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    // ===== RICHTUNGSANZEIGE (GRÖßER) =====
    // Ermittele Richtung aus Track-Daten
    let heading = null;
    
    if (playbackTrack && playbackIndex < playbackTrack.trackPoints.length) {
        const currentPoint = playbackTrack.trackPoints[playbackIndex];
        
        // 1. Versuche heading aus trackPoint
        if (currentPoint.heading !== undefined && currentPoint.heading !== null) {
            heading = currentPoint.heading;
        }
        // 2. Berechne Richtung aus vorherigem/nächstem Punkt
        else if (playbackIndex > 0 && playbackTrack.coordinates) {
            const prevCoord = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex - 1];
            const currCoord = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex];
            
            if (prevCoord && currCoord && 
                prevCoord[0] !== null && prevCoord[1] !== null &&
                currCoord[0] !== null && currCoord[1] !== null) {
                
                const deltaLng = currCoord[0] - prevCoord[0];
                const deltaLat = currCoord[1] - prevCoord[1];
                
                if (deltaLng !== 0 || deltaLat !== 0) {
                    // Berechne Winkel in Grad (0° = Norden)
                    heading = Math.atan2(deltaLng, deltaLat) * 180 / Math.PI;
                    if (heading < 0) heading += 360;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Richtungsanzeige zeichnen (falls verfügbar und Track läuft)
    if (heading !== null && isPlayingTrack) {
        const headingRad = (heading * Math.PI) / 180;
        const arrowLength = 28; // GRÖßER: 28 statt 20
        const arrowEndX = point.x + Math.sin(headingRad) * arrowLength;
        const arrowEndY = point.y - Math.cos(headingRad) * arrowLength;
        
        shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#1d4ed8'; // GLEICHE BLAUE FARBE für Pfeil
        shipCtx.lineWidth = 4; // GRÖßER: 4 statt 3
        shipCtx.lineCap = 'round';
        shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.9;
        
        // Pfeil-Linie
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(point.x, point.y);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.stroke();
        
        // Pfeilspitze (GRÖßER)
        const arrowSize = 8; // GRÖßER: 8 statt 6
        const angle1 = headingRad + (Math.PI * 0.8);
        const angle2 = headingRad - (Math.PI * 0.8);
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle1) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle1) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle2) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle2) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.stroke();
    }
    
    shipCtx.restore();
    
    // Kontinuierliche Animation triggern wenn Track abgespielt wird
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
}

function setcookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure) {
    let cookieString = encodeURIComponent(name) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value);
    if (expires) {
        // Konvertiere Unix Timestamp zu Date Object
        let expiryDate;
        if (typeof expires === 'number') {
            // Unix timestamp (wie von PHP time() + seconds)
            expiryDate = new Date(expires * 1000);
        } else {
            // Bereits ein Date Object
            expiryDate = expires;
        }
        cookieString += '; expires=' + expiryDate.toUTCString();
    }
    if (path) {
        cookieString += '; path=' + path;
    } else {
        cookieString += '; path=/';
    }
    if (domain) {
        cookieString += '; domain=' + domain;
    }
    if (secure) {
        cookieString += '; secure';
    }
    // SameSite für moderne Browser
    cookieString += '; SameSite=Lax';
    document.cookie = cookieString; 
}

// PHP time() Equivalent (Unix Timestamp in Sekunden)
function time() {
    return Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
}

function getQueryStrings() { 
  var assoc  = {};
  var decode = function (s) { return decodeURIComponent(s.replace(/\+/g, " ")); };
  var queryString = location.search.substring(1); 
  var keyValues = queryString.split('&'); 

  for(var i in keyValues) { 
    var key = keyValues[i].split('=');
    if (key.length > 1) {
      assoc[decode(key[0])] = decode(key[1]);
    }
  } 

  return assoc; 
} 

////////////////////////////////////////////

if (!window.shipDetailHookManager) {
    window.shipDetailHookManager = {
        buttonAddCallbacks: [],
        closeCallbacks: [],
        originalFunctions: {},
        
        // Registriere Button-Add Callback
        registerButtonCallback: function(callback) {
            this.buttonAddCallbacks.push(callback);
        },
        
        // Registriere Close Callback
        registerCloseCallback: function(callback) {
            this.closeCallbacks.push(callback);
        },
        
        // Führe alle Button-Callbacks aus
        executeButtonCallbacks: function() {
            this.buttonAddCallbacks.forEach(callback => {
                try {
                    callback();
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Button Callback Fehler:', error);
                }
            });
        },
        
        // Führe alle Close-Callbacks aus
        executeCloseCallbacks: function() {
            this.closeCallbacks.forEach(callback => {
                try {
                    callback();
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('❌ Close Callback Fehler:', error);
                }
            });
        },
        
        // Setup einmaliger Hooks
        setupUnifiedHooks: function() {
            if (this.hooksSetup) return;
            this.hooksSetup = true;
            
            // Hook loadShipDetailsFromAPI
            if (typeof loadShipDetailsFromAPI !== 'undefined' && !this.originalFunctions.loadShipDetailsFromAPI) {
                this.originalFunctions.loadShipDetailsFromAPI = loadShipDetailsFromAPI;
                
                window.loadShipDetailsFromAPI = async function(ship, shouldCenterMap = false) {
                    await window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.loadShipDetailsFromAPI(ship, shouldCenterMap);
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.shipDetailHookManager.executeButtonCallbacks();
                    }, 200);
                };
            }
            
            // Hook showShipDetails
            if (typeof showShipDetails !== 'undefined' && !this.originalFunctions.showShipDetails) {
                this.originalFunctions.showShipDetails = showShipDetails;
                
                window.showShipDetails = function(ship, fromURL = false) {
                    window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.showShipDetails(ship, fromURL);
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.shipDetailHookManager.executeButtonCallbacks();
                    }, 500);
                };
            }
            
            // Hook displayShipDetails
            if (!this.originalFunctions.displayShipDetails) {
                this.originalFunctions.displayShipDetails = window.displayShipDetails;
                
                window.displayShipDetails = function(ship, apiData) {
                    if (window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.displayShipDetails) {
                        window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.displayShipDetails(ship, apiData);
                    }
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.shipDetailHookManager.executeButtonCallbacks();
                    }, 100);
                };
            }
            
            // Hook closeShipDetail
            if (!this.originalFunctions.closeShipDetail) {
                this.originalFunctions.closeShipDetail = window.closeShipDetail;
                
                window.closeShipDetail = function() {
                    window.shipDetailHookManager.executeCloseCallbacks();
                    
                    if (window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.closeShipDetail) {
                        window.shipDetailHookManager.originalFunctions.closeShipDetail();
                    }
                };
            }
            
            console.log('✅ Unified Hook System aktiviert');
        }
    };
}

// Tracking ob Button bereits eingerichtet wurde
let shipPositionButtonSetup = false;
// Ship Position Button - Verwendet die gleiche Logik wie handleSearchResultClick
function flyToShipPosition() {
    if (!selectedShip) {
        console.log('❌ Kein Schiff ausgewählt');
        return;
    }
    
    const shipName = selectedShip.name || 'Unknown Ship';
    const mmsi = selectedShip.mmsi || '';
    const shipId = selectedShip.shipId || '';
    
    console.log('🚢 Position Button clicked:', shipName, 'MMSI:', mmsi, 'ShipID:', shipId);
    
    // Search-Interface schließen (falls offen)
    const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');
    if (resultsContainer) {
        resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
    }
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.value = '';
    }

    // URL erstellen wie in handleSearchResultClick
    let customUrl = '';
    if (mmsi) {
        const urlFriendlyName = shipName
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '')
            .replace(/-+/g, '-')
            .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
        customUrl = '/vessels/' + urlFriendlyName + '-position/' + mmsi + '/';
    }

    // URL aktualisieren
    if (customUrl) {
        window.history.pushState({}, shipName + ' - Position', customUrl);
    }

    // Basis-Schiffsobjekt erstellen (wie in handleSearchResultClick)
    const shipFromSearch = {
        name: shipName,
        mmsi: mmsi,
        lat: selectedShip.lat || map.getCenter().lat,
        lng: selectedShip.lng || map.getCenter().lng,
        speed: selectedShip.speed || 0,
        course: selectedShip.course || 0,
        type: selectedShip.type || 'N/A',
        shipId: shipId, // WICHTIG: shipId mitführen
        destination: selectedShip.destination || 'N/A',
		elapsed: selectedShip.elapsed || 'N/A'
    };

    // WICHTIG: Tracking-Setup mit ALLEN Identifikatoren (wie in handleSearchResultClick)
    searchSelectedShip = {
        mmsi: mmsi,
        shipId: shipId, // KRITISCH: shipId für eindeutige Identifikation
        name: shipName,
        lat: selectedShip.lat || map.getCenter().lat,
        lng: selectedShip.lng || map.getCenter().lng,
        speed: selectedShip.speed || 0,
        course: selectedShip.course || 0,
        heading: selectedShip.heading || selectedShip.course || 0,
        destination: selectedShip.destination || 'N/A',
        type: selectedShip.type || 'N/A',
		elapsed: selectedShip.elapsed || 'N/A'
    };

    console.log('🎯 Ship tracking setup completed with unique identifiers:', {
        searchSelectedShip: searchSelectedShip,
        searchSelectedPosition: searchSelectedPosition
    });

    // KORRIGIERT: Eindeutige Schiffssuche - Priorität: shipId > MMSI > Name+Position
    const existingShip = findExactShipMatch(shipId, mmsi, shipName, selectedShip.lat, selectedShip.lng);

    if (existingShip) {
        console.log('🎯 EXACT ship found in existing data:', existingShip.name, 'MMSI:', existingShip.mmsi, 'ShipID:', existingShip.shipId);
        
        // Aktualisiere mit echten Daten ABER behalte die ursprünglichen IDs
        searchSelectedPosition.lat = existingShip.lat;
        searchSelectedPosition.lng = existingShip.lng;
        searchSelectedShip.lat = existingShip.lat;
        searchSelectedShip.lng = existingShip.lng;
        searchSelectedShip.speed = existingShip.speed;
        searchSelectedShip.course = existingShip.course;
        searchSelectedShip.heading = existingShip.heading;
        searchSelectedShip.destination = existingShip.destination;
        searchSelectedShip.type = existingShip.type;
        searchSelectedShip.elapsed = existingShip.elapsed;
		
        // KRITISCH: Übernehme die Daten vom gefundenen Schiff, aber behalte die Original-IDs
        Object.assign(shipFromSearch, existingShip);
        // Falls das gefundene Schiff andere IDs hat, behalte die ursprünglichen
        shipFromSearch.mmsi = mmsi || existingShip.mmsi;
        shipFromSearch.shipId = shipId || existingShip.shipId;
    } else {
        console.log('⚠️ Exact ship not found in current data, using selected ship data');
    }

	updatePosition = true;	
    // Schiffsdetails anzeigen (wird flyTo durchführen und API-Daten laden)
    showShipDetails(shipFromSearch, true); // true = fromURL (triggert flyTo + API Korrektur)
}

// NEUE FUNKTION: Eindeutige Schiffssuche mit mehreren Kriterien
function findExactShipMatch(targetShipId, targetMMSI, targetName, targetLat, targetLng) {
    if (!ships || ships.length === 0) {
        console.log('🔍 Keine Schiffe zum Durchsuchen verfügbar');
        return null;
    }

    console.log('🔍 Suche exaktes Schiff:', {
        targetShipId: targetShipId,
        targetMMSI: targetMMSI, 
        targetName: targetName,
        targetPosition: `${targetLat}, ${targetLng}`
    });

    // PRIORITÄT 1: Ship-ID Match (eindeutigste Identifikation)
    if (targetShipId) {
        const shipByShipId = ships.find(ship => 
            ship.shipId && ship.shipId === targetShipId
        );
        if (shipByShipId) {
            console.log('✅ EXACT match by Ship-ID:', targetShipId);
            return shipByShipId;
        }
    }

    // PRIORITÄT 2: MMSI Match (sehr zuverlässig)
    if (targetMMSI) {
        const shipByMMSI = ships.find(ship => 
            ship.mmsi && ship.mmsi === targetMMSI
        );
        if (shipByMMSI) {
            console.log('✅ EXACT match by MMSI:', targetMMSI);
            return shipByMMSI;
        }
    }

    // PRIORITÄT 3: Name + Position Match (für Schiffe ohne MMSI/shipId)
    if (targetName && targetLat && targetLng) {
        const shipsByName = ships.filter(ship => 
            ship.name && ship.name.toLowerCase().trim() === targetName.toLowerCase().trim()
        );
        
        if (shipsByName.length === 1) {
            console.log('✅ EXACT match by unique name:', targetName);
            return shipsByName[0];
        } else if (shipsByName.length > 1) {
            console.log(`⚠️ Multiple ships (${shipsByName.length}) with name "${targetName}", using position matching`);
            
            // Bei mehreren Schiffen mit gleichem Namen: Finde das nächstgelegene
            const POSITION_TOLERANCE = 0.01; // ~1km Toleranz
            
            const shipByPosition = shipsByName.find(ship => 
                Math.abs(ship.lat - targetLat) < POSITION_TOLERANCE &&
                Math.abs(ship.lng - targetLng) < POSITION_TOLERANCE
            );
            
            if (shipByPosition) {
                console.log('✅ EXACT match by name + position:', targetName, 'at', `${shipByPosition.lat}, ${shipByPosition.lng}`);
                return shipByPosition;
            } else {
                // Letzter Ausweg: Das erste Schiff mit dem Namen (kann falsch sein)
                console.warn('⚠️ Taking first ship with matching name - might be wrong!');
                console.warn('Available positions for', targetName + ':', 
                    shipsByName.map(s => `${s.lat}, ${s.lng} (MMSI: ${s.mmsi || 'N/A'})`));
                return shipsByName[0];
            }
        }
    }

    console.log('❌ No exact ship match found for:', { targetShipId, targetMMSI, targetName });
    return null;
}

// Event Handler für den Position Button einrichten
function setupShipPositionButton() {
    // Verhindere mehrfaches Setup
    if (shipPositionButtonSetup) {
        return true;
    }
    
    const positionButton = document.getElementById('shipDetailPositionBtn');
    
    if (positionButton) {
        // Prüfe ob Button bereits Event Listener hat
        if (positionButton.hasAttribute('data-position-setup')) {
            shipPositionButtonSetup = true;
            return true;
        }
        
        // Markiere Button als eingerichtet
        positionButton.setAttribute('data-position-setup', 'true');
        
        // Füge Event Listener hinzu
        positionButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            flyToShipPosition(); // Rufe unsere neue Funktion auf
        });
        
        shipPositionButtonSetup = true;
        console.log('✅ Ship Position Button eingerichtet (verwendet handleSearchResultClick Logik)');
        return true;
    }
    
    return false;
}

// Reset Setup Status wenn Ship Detail geschlossen wird
function resetShipPositionButtonSetup() {
    shipPositionButtonSetup = false;
}

// Hook in das Ship Detail System (nur einmal)
if (window.shipDetailHookManager) {
    if (!window.shipDetailHookManager.positionButtonRegistered) {
        window.shipDetailHookManager.registerButtonCallback(setupShipPositionButton);
        window.shipDetailHookManager.registerCloseCallback(resetShipPositionButtonSetup);
        window.shipDetailHookManager.positionButtonRegistered = true;
        console.log('🔗 Position Button Hook registriert');
    }
}

// Fallback-Setup für den Fall dass Hook Manager nicht verfügbar ist
function setupPositionButtonFallback() {
    if (shipPositionButtonSetup) return;
    
    let attempts = 0;
    const maxAttempts = 3;
    
    const trySetup = () => {
        attempts++;
        
        if (setupShipPositionButton()) {
            console.log('✅ Position Button Fallback Setup erfolgreich');
            return;
        }
        
        if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
            setTimeout(trySetup, 500);
        }
    };
    
    trySetup();
}

// Hook in bestehende Ship Detail Funktionen (nur wenn noch nicht gehookt)
if (!window.shipPositionButtonHooksInstalled) {
    window.shipPositionButtonHooksInstalled = true;
    
    // Hook showShipDetails
    if (typeof showShipDetails !== 'undefined' && !window.originalShowShipDetailsPosition) {
        window.originalShowShipDetailsPosition = showShipDetails;
        
        window.showShipDetails = function(ship, fromURL = false) {
            resetShipPositionButtonSetup(); // Reset bei neuem Schiff
            window.originalShowShipDetailsPosition(ship, fromURL);
            
            setTimeout(setupPositionButtonFallback, 500);
        };
    }
    
    // Hook displayShipDetails
    if (typeof displayShipDetails !== 'undefined' && !window.originalDisplayShipDetailsPosition) {
        window.originalDisplayShipDetailsPosition = displayShipDetails;
        
        window.displayShipDetails = function(ship, apiData) {
            if (window.originalDisplayShipDetailsPosition) {
                window.originalDisplayShipDetailsPosition(ship, apiData);
            }
            
            if (!shipPositionButtonSetup) {
                setTimeout(setupPositionButtonFallback, 100);
            }
        };
    }
    
    // Hook closeShipDetail
    if (typeof closeShipDetail !== 'undefined' && !window.originalCloseShipDetailPosition) {
        window.originalCloseShipDetailPosition = closeShipDetail;
        
        window.closeShipDetail = function() {
            resetShipPositionButtonSetup();
            
            if (window.originalCloseShipDetailPosition) {
                window.originalCloseShipDetailPosition();
            }
        };
    }
    
}

// DOM Ready Setup
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        if (!shipPositionButtonSetup) {
            setupPositionButtonFallback();
        }
    }, 1000);
});

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    setTimeout(() => {
        if (map && map.loaded()) {
            startContinuousRedrawCheck();
        }
    }, 2000);
});

// Global verfügbare Funktionen
window.flyToShipPosition = flyToShipPosition;
window.setupShipPositionButton = setupShipPositionButton;

function copyToClipboard() {
    // Versuche Daten aus verschiedenen Quellen zu holen
    let shipname = '';
    let mmsi = '';
    
    // 1. Aus selectedShip (falls verfügbar)
    if (selectedShip) {
        shipname = selectedShip.name || '';
        mmsi = selectedShip.mmsi || '';
    }
    
    // 2. Fallback: Aus Ship Detail Window DOM extrahieren
    if (!shipname || !mmsi) {
        // Schiffsname aus Title
        const titleElement = document.getElementById('shipDetailTitle');
        if (titleElement) {
            shipname = titleElement.textContent.trim();
        }
        
        // MMSI aus Detail Items suchen
        const detailItems = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-item');
        detailItems.forEach(item => {
            const label = item.querySelector('.detail-label');
            const value = item.querySelector('.detail-value');
            
            if (label && value && label.textContent.trim() === 'MMSI') {
                mmsi = value.textContent.trim();
            }
        });
    }
    
    // 3. Fallback: Aus aktueller URL extrahieren (falls Schiff über URL geladen)
    if (!mmsi && window.location.pathname.includes('-position/')) {
        const urlMatch = window.location.pathname.match(/\/([^\/]+)-position\/(\d+)\/?$/);
        if (urlMatch) {
            if (!shipname) shipname = urlMatch[1].replace(/-/g, ' ');
            mmsi = urlMatch[2];
        }
    }
    
    // Validierung
    if (!shipname || !mmsi) {
        alert('Schiffsdaten nicht verfügbar. Bitte öffnen Sie zuerst ein Schiff.');
        return;
    }
    
    // URL erstellen
    const urlFriendlyName = shipname
        .toLowerCase()
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '')
        .replace(/-+/g, '-')
        .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
    
    const url = `https://marinetraffic.live/vessels/${urlFriendlyName}-position/${mmsi}/`;
    
    // In Zwischenablage kopieren (mit Fallback auf Prompt)
    if (navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext) {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => {
            console.log('✅ URL in Zwischenablage kopiert:', url);
            // Optional: Erfolgs-Benachrichtigung anzeigen
            if (typeof showNotification === 'function') {
                showNotification('Link kopiert!', 'success');
            }
        }).catch(() => {
            // Fallback auf Prompt
            window.prompt('Link kopieren:', url);
        });
    } else {
        // Fallback für ältere Browser
        window.prompt('Link kopieren:', url);
    }
}

function copyToClipboard2() {
    // Versuche Daten aus verschiedenen Quellen zu holen
    let portName = '';
    let portId = '';
    
    // 1. Aus selectedPort (falls verfügbar)
    if (selectedPort) {
        portName = selectedPort.portName || selectedPort.name || '';
        portId = selectedPort.portId || selectedPort.id || '';
    }
    
    // 2. Fallback: Aus Port Detail Window DOM extrahieren
    if (!portName || !portId) {
        // Port Name aus Title (ohne Country Code)
        const titleElement = document.getElementById('portDetailTitle');
        if (titleElement) {
            let titleText = titleElement.textContent.trim();
            // Entferne Country Code [XX] falls vorhanden
            portName = titleText.replace(/\s*\[[A-Z]{2}\]\s*$/, '').trim();
        }
        
        // Port ID aus URL extrahieren (falls Port über URL geladen)
        if (!portId && window.location.pathname.includes('-port/')) {
            const urlMatch = window.location.pathname.match(/\/([^\/]+)-port\/(\d+)\/?$/);
            if (urlMatch) {
                portId = urlMatch[2];
            }
        }
        
        // Alternativ: Aus Detail Items suchen (falls ID irgendwo angezeigt wird)
        if (!portId) {
            const detailItems = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-item');
            detailItems.forEach(item => {
                const label = item.querySelector('.detail-label');
                const value = item.querySelector('.detail-value');
                
                if (label && value && label.textContent.trim() === 'Port ID') {
                    portId = value.textContent.trim();
                }
            });
        }
    }
    
    // 3. Letzte Möglichkeit: Aus globalen Variablen
    if (!portId) {
        // Durchsuche currentAssets.ports nach dem Port Namen
        if (currentAssets && currentAssets.ports && portName) {
            const foundPort = currentAssets.ports.find(port => 
                port[1] && port[1].toLowerCase() === portName.toLowerCase()
            );
            if (foundPort) {
                portId = foundPort[0]; // Port ID ist das erste Element
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Validierung
    if (!portName || !portId) {
        alert('Hafendaten nicht verfügbar. Bitte öffnen Sie zuerst einen Hafen.');
        return;
    }
    
    // URL erstellen
    const urlFriendlyName = portName
        .toLowerCase()
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '')
        .replace(/-+/g, '-')
        .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
    
    const url = `https://marinetraffic.live/ports/${urlFriendlyName}-port/${portId}/`;
    
    // In Zwischenablage kopieren (mit Fallback auf Prompt)
    if (navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext) {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => {
            console.log('✅ Port URL in Zwischenablage kopiert:', url);
            // Optional: Erfolgs-Benachrichtigung anzeigen
            if (typeof showNotification === 'function') {
                showNotification('Hafen-Link kopiert!', 'success');
            } else {
                // Fallback Notification
                showNotification('Hafen-Link kopiert!');
            }
        }).catch(() => {
            // Fallback auf Prompt
            window.prompt('Hafen-Link kopieren:', url);
        });
    } else {
        // Fallback für ältere Browser
        window.prompt('Hafen-Link kopieren:', url);
    }
}

function shareShipPosition() {
    // Versuche Daten aus verschiedenen Quellen zu holen
    let shipname = '';
    let mmsi = '';
    
    // 1. Aus selectedShip (falls verfügbar)
    if (selectedShip) {
        shipname = selectedShip.name || '';
        mmsi = selectedShip.mmsi || '';
    }
    
    // 2. Fallback: Aus Ship Detail Window DOM extrahieren
    if (!shipname || !mmsi) {
        // Schiffsname aus Title
        const titleElement = document.getElementById('shipDetailTitle');
        if (titleElement) {
            shipname = titleElement.textContent.trim();
        }
        
        // MMSI aus Detail Items suchen
        const detailItems = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-item');
        detailItems.forEach(item => {
            const label = item.querySelector('.detail-label');
            const value = item.querySelector('.detail-value');
            
            if (label && value && label.textContent.trim() === 'MMSI') {
                mmsi = value.textContent.trim();
            }
        });
    }
    
    // 3. Fallback: Aus aktueller URL extrahieren (falls Schiff über URL geladen)
    if (!mmsi && window.location.pathname.includes('-position/')) {
        const urlMatch = window.location.pathname.match(/\/([^\/]+)-position\/(\d+)\/?$/);
        if (urlMatch) {
            if (!shipname) shipname = urlMatch[1].replace(/-/g, ' ');
            mmsi = urlMatch[2];
        }
    }
    
    // Validierung
    if (!shipname || !mmsi) {
        alert('Schiffsdaten nicht verfügbar. Bitte öffnen Sie zuerst ein Schiff.');
        return;
    }
    
    // URL erstellen
    const urlFriendlyName = shipname
        .toLowerCase()
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '')
        .replace(/-+/g, '-')
        .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
    
    const shipUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/vessels/${urlFriendlyName}-position/${mmsi}`;
    
    // Benutzer Name aus localStorage (mit Fallback)
    const userName = localStorage.getItem('Name') || 'einem Nutzer';
    
    // Share-App URL erstellen (NUR die Message encoden, URL roh lassen)
    const shareMessage = `Aktuelle Schiffsposition von ${shipname} `;
    const shareUrl = `shareapp://message?=${encodeURIComponent(shareMessage)}&url=${shipUrl}`;
    
    console.log('📤 Teile Schiffsposition:', {
        shipname: shipname,
        mmsi: mmsi,
        userName: userName,
        shipUrl: shipUrl,
        shareUrl: shareUrl
    });
    
    // Zur Share-App weiterleiten
    try {
        location.replace(shareUrl);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Fehler beim Öffnen der Share-App:', error);
        
        // Fallback: Normal teilen falls Share-App nicht verfügbar
        if (navigator.share) {
            navigator.share({
                title: `Schiffsposition: ${shipname}`,
                text: shareMessage,
                url: shipUrl
            }).catch(err => {
                console.log('Native Share fehlgeschlagen:', err);
                // Letzter Fallback: URL in Zwischenablage
                if (navigator.clipboard) {
                    navigator.clipboard.writeText(shipUrl);
                    alert('Share-App nicht verfügbar. URL wurde in die Zwischenablage kopiert.');
                } else {
                    window.prompt('Share-App nicht verfügbar. Kopiere den Link:', shipUrl);
                }
            });
        } else {
            // Kein natives Teilen verfügbar
            if (navigator.clipboard) {
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(shipUrl);
                alert('Share-App nicht verfügbar. URL wurde in die Zwischenablage kopiert.');
            } else {
                window.prompt('Share-App nicht verfügbar. Kopiere den Link:', shipUrl);
            }
        }
    }
}

        portName: portName,

        shareUrl: shareUrl
    });

///////////////////////////////////////////
////////////POI-MODUL/////////////////////
/////////////////////////////////////////

// 1. GLOBALE VARIABLEN (ganz oben im Script hinzufügen)
let currentAssets = { ports: [], marinas: [], lights: [] };
let assetsLoaded = false;

// 1. GLOBALE POI FILTER VARIABLEN (bei anderen globalen Variablen hinzufügen)
let poiFilters = {
    ports: true,
    marinas: true,
    lights: true
};

// 2. POI FILTER SPEICHERN/LADEN
function savePOIFilters() {
    try {
        localStorage.setItem('poiFilters', JSON.stringify(poiFilters));
        console.log('POI filters saved:', poiFilters);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error saving POI filters:', error);
    }
}

function loadPOIFilters() {
    try {
        const saved = localStorage.getItem('poiFilters');
        if (saved) {
            const parsedFilters = JSON.parse(saved);
            poiFilters = parsedFilters; // DIREKTE Zuweisung statt Merge!
            console.log('📂 POI filters loaded from storage:', poiFilters);
        } else {
            // ERSTE BENUTZUNG: Speichere Standardwerte (alle aktiv)
            console.log('🆕 First time - saving default POI filters:', poiFilters);
            savePOIFilters();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Error loading POI filters:', error);
        // Fallback zu Standardwerten
        poiFilters = { ports: true, marinas: true, lights: true };
        savePOIFilters();
    }
}

// NEUE FUNKTION: Checkboxen korrekt setzen - AGGRESSIVER ANSATZ
function syncCheckboxesToFilters() {
    console.log('🔄 AGGRESSIVE checkbox sync - filters:', poiFilters);
    
    Object.keys(poiFilters).forEach(filterId => {
        const checkbox = document.getElementById('poi-filter-' + filterId);
        if (checkbox) {
            const oldValue = checkbox.checked;
            checkbox.checked = poiFilters[filterId];
            
            console.log(`✅ Checkbox ${filterId}: ${oldValue} → ${checkbox.checked}`);
            
            // ZUSÄTZLICH: Trigger change event falls nötig
            if (oldValue !== checkbox.checked) {
                console.log(`🔥 Triggering change event for ${filterId}`);
            }
        } else {
            console.error(`❌ Checkbox NOT FOUND: poi-filter-${filterId}`);
        }
    });
    
    // DEBUGGING: Prüfe alle POI Checkboxen
    const allPOICheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.poi-filter-checkbox');
    console.log(`🔍 Found ${allPOICheckboxes.length} POI checkboxes:`);
    allPOICheckboxes.forEach(cb => {
        console.log(`  - ${cb.id}: checked=${cb.checked}`);
    });
    
    // DEBUGGING: Prüfe localStorage Inhalt
    console.log('💾 Current localStorage poiFilters:', localStorage.getItem('poiFilters'));
    console.log('💾 Current layerPreferences:', localStorage.getItem('layerPreferences'));
}

// KORRIGIERTE anyActive Berechnung
function isAnyPOIActive() {
    return Object.values(poiFilters).some(active => active);
}

// 3. POI FILTER INITIALISIERUNG - SOFORT AUSFÜHREN
function initializePOIFilters() {
    console.log('🚀 POI System initialization...');
    
    // 1. Lade gespeicherte Filter
    loadPOIFilters();
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        console.log('🔄 Third sync attempt (1000ms)...');
        syncCheckboxesToFilters();
        
        // 3. JETZT erst Event Listeners hinzufügen
        const poiCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.poi-filter-checkbox');
        console.log(`📋 Adding event listeners to ${poiCheckboxes.length} checkboxes...`);
        
        if (poiCheckboxes.length === 0) {
            console.error('❌ NO POI CHECKBOXES FOUND! Check HTML structure!');
            // Versuche alle möglichen Selektoren
            console.log('🔍 Trying alternative selectors...');
            console.log('- .poi-filter-checkbox:', document.querySelectorAll('.poi-filter-checkbox').length);
            console.log('- input[id^="poi-filter-"]:', document.querySelectorAll('input[id^="poi-filter-"]').length);
            console.log('- .layer-item input:', document.querySelectorAll('.layer-item input').length);
        }
        
        poiCheckboxes.forEach(checkbox => {
            console.log(`📎 Adding listener to: ${checkbox.id}`);
            
            checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
                const filterId = this.id.replace('poi-filter-', '');
                poiFilters[filterId] = this.checked;
                
                console.log('POI Filter changed:', filterId, this.checked);
                console.log('Current POI filters:', poiFilters);
                
                // Speichere Filter sofort
                savePOIFilters();
                
                // KORRIGIERTE anyActive Berechnung
                const anyActive = isAnyPOIActive();
                
                if (anyActive && map.getZoom() > 8) {
                    console.log('Reloading assets with new filters...');
                    loadStaticAssets();
                } else if (!anyActive) {
                    // Alle deaktiviert - lösche Assets
                    currentAssets = { ports: [], marinas: [], lights: [] };
                    assetsLoaded = false;
                    needsRedraw = true;
                    console.log('All POI filters disabled - clearing assets');
                }
            });
        });
        
        // 4. Assets laden
        setTimeout(() => {
            const anyActive = isAnyPOIActive();
            console.log(`🎯 Final check - anyActive: ${anyActive}, zoom: ${map.getZoom()}`);
            if (anyActive && map.getZoom() > 8) {
                console.log('Initial POI assets load...');
                loadStaticAssets();
            }
        }, 500);
        
    }, 1000); // Längere Verzögerung für schwere Seiten
}

// SCHUTZ VOR ÜBERSCHREIBUNG DURCH ANDERE SYSTEME
function protectPOIFilters() {
    // Überwache localStorage für Änderungen an poiFilters
    const originalSetItem = localStorage.setItem;
    localStorage.setItem = function(key, value) {
        // Falls jemand versucht poiFilters zu überschreiben, verhindere es
        if (key === 'poiFilters') {
            console.log('🛡️ POI Filters write detected:', value);
        }
        return originalSetItem.apply(this, arguments);
    };
    
    // Überwache auch layerPreferences um Konflikte zu vermeiden
    const originalGetItem = localStorage.getItem;
    localStorage.getItem = function(key) {
        const result = originalGetItem.apply(this, arguments);
        if (key === 'layerPreferences' && result) {
            console.log('📂 layerPreferences loaded - checking for POI conflicts...');
        }
        return result;
    };
}

// SOFORTIGE AUSFÜHRUNG - BEIDE VARIANTEN + SCHUTZ
if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    // DOM lädt noch
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        protectPOIFilters();
        initializePOIFilters();
    });
} else {
    // DOM bereits geladen - sofort ausführen
    console.log('🚀 DOM already loaded - initializing POI filters immediately');
    protectPOIFilters();
    initializePOIFilters();
}

async function loadStaticAssets() {
    
    // Prüfe ob überhaupt Filter aktiv sind
    const anyActive = Object.values(poiFilters).some(active => active);
    if (!anyActive) {
        console.log('No POI filters active - skipping load');
        currentAssets = { ports: [], marinas: [], lights: [] };
        assetsLoaded = false;
        return;
    }
    
    try {
        const bounds = map.getBounds();
        const zoom = Math.floor(map.getZoom());
        const n = Math.pow(2, zoom);
        
        console.log('Loading assets at zoom:', zoom, 'with filters:', poiFilters);
        
        // KORREKTE Tile-Berechnung (wie bei <= 2) {hips)
        const tileNW = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getWest() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getNorth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };
        
        const tileSE = {
            x: Math.floor((bounds.getEast() + 180) / 360 * n / 2),
            y: Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180) + 
                  1 / Math.cos(bounds.getSouth() * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * n / 2)
        };

        const minX = Math.max(0, Math.min(tileNW.x, tileSE.x));
        const maxX = Math.max(tileNW.x, tileSE.x);
        const minY = Math.max(0, Math.min(tileNW.y, tileSE.y));
        const maxY = Math.max(tileNW.y, tileSE.y);
        
        console.log('Tile range:', minX, maxX, minY, maxY);
        
        let allAssets = { ports: [], marinas: [], lights: [] };
        let loadedTiles = 0;
        
        // Maximal 12 Tiles laden
        const maxTiles = 14;
        let tilesProcessed = 0;
        
        for (let x = minX; x <= maxX && tilesProcessed < maxTiles; x++) {
            for (let y = minY; y <= maxY && tilesProcessed < maxTiles; y++) {
                
                // URL mit Filtern generieren
                const portParam = poiFilters.ports ? 1 : 0;
                const marinaParam = poiFilters.marinas ? 1 : 0;
                const lightsParam = poiFilters.lights ? 1 : 0;
                
                const url = `https://corsproxy.io/?url=https://marinetraffic.com/map/getStaticAssetsjson_v3/z:${zoom}/X:${x}/Y:${y}/port:${portParam}/marina:${marinaParam}/lights:${lightsParam}/&reqHeaders=x-requested-with%3AXMLHttpRequest&reqHeaders=content-type%3Aapplication%2Fjson&key=94f3f2c0`;
                                
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(url);
                    const data = await response.json();
                    
                    // Nur hinzufügen wenn Filter aktiv ist UND POI im sichtbaren Bereich
                    if (data.ports && poiFilters.ports) {
                        const visiblePorts = data.ports.filter(port => {
                            const lat = parseFloat(port[3]);
                            const lng = parseFloat(port[2]);
                            return lat >= bounds.getSouth() && lat <= bounds.getNorth() && 
                                   lng >= bounds.getWest() && lng <= bounds.getEast();
                        });
                        allAssets.ports.push(...visiblePorts);
                    }
                    
                    if (data.marinas && poiFilters.marinas) {
                        const visibleMarinas = data.marinas.filter(marina => {
                            const lat = parseFloat(marina.CENTERY);
                            const lng = parseFloat(marina.CENTERX);
                            return lat >= bounds.getSouth() && lat <= bounds.getNorth() && 
                                   lng >= bounds.getWest() && lng <= bounds.getEast();
                        });
                        allAssets.marinas.push(...visibleMarinas);
                    }
                    
                    if (data.lights && poiFilters.lights) {
                        const visibleLights = data.lights.filter(light => {
                            const lat = parseFloat(light.LAT);
                            const lng = parseFloat(light.LON);
                            return lat >= bounds.getSouth() && lat <= bounds.getNorth() && 
                                   lng >= bounds.getWest() && lng <= bounds.getEast();
                        });
                        allAssets.lights.push(...visibleLights);
                    }
                    
                    loadedTiles++;
                    
                } catch (error) {
                    console.log('Error loading tile:', x, y, error);
                }
                
                tilesProcessed++;
            }
        }
        
        currentAssets = allAssets;
        assetsLoaded = true;
                
        // Sofort anzeigen
        needsRedraw = true;
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading static assets:', error);
    }
}

let hoveredPort = null;
let selectedPort = null;
let hoveredMarina = null;
let selectedMarina = null;

// 2. ERWEITERE drawStaticAssets um Hover/Selection-Effekte zu zeichnen
function drawStaticAssets() {
    if (!assetsLoaded || !currentAssets) return;
    
    const ctx = shipCtx;
    if (!ctx) return;
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    
    // Nur bei hohem Zoom anzeigen
    if (zoom <= 8) return;
    
    // SCHRIFT-ANZEIGE KONFIGURATION
    const SHOW_NAMES_FROM_ZOOM = 11;
    const showNames = zoom >= SHOW_NAMES_FROM_ZOOM;
    
    // Port Click Areas zurücksetzen
    window.portClickAreas = [];
    
    // HÄFEN - Bereits gefiltert beim Laden
    if (poiFilters.ports) {
        currentAssets.ports.forEach(port => {
            const portId = port[0];
            const portName = port[1];
            const lng = parseFloat(port[2]);
            const lat = parseFloat(port[3]);
            
            const point = map.project([lng, lat]);
            
            // Mobile: Doppelte Größe
            const iconSize = isMobile ? 32 : 32;
            const clickRadius = iconSize / 2 + 5; // Etwas größerer Klickbereich
            
            // Speichere Klickbereich
            window.portClickAreas.push({
                x: point.x,
                y: point.y,
                radius: clickRadius,
                portId: portId,
                portName: portName,
                lat: lat,
                lng: lng
            });
            
            // ZEICHNE SELECTION/HOVER EFFEKTE VOR DEM ICON
            ctx.save();
            
            // Selected Port - Gelber Kreis
            if (selectedPort && selectedPort.portId === portId) {
                ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffff00';
                ctx.lineWidth = 2;
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(point.x, point.y, iconSize * 0.8, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.stroke();
            }
            
            // Hovered Port - Weißer Kreis
            if (hoveredPort && hoveredPort.portId === portId) {
                ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
                ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(point.x, point.y, iconSize * 0.7, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.stroke();
            }
            
            ctx.restore();
            
            // Icon zeichnen
            drawPNGIcon(ctx, point.x, point.y, 'ports', iconSize);
            
            // Name nur bei hohem Zoom anzeigen
            if (showNames) {
                drawPOILabel(ctx, point.x, point.y, portName, -20);
            }
        });
    }
	
if (poiFilters.marinas) {
    // Marina Click Areas Array initialisieren
    if (!window.marinaClickAreas) {
        window.marinaClickAreas = [];
    }
    
    currentAssets.marinas.forEach(marina => {
        const lat = parseFloat(marina.CENTERY);
        const lng = parseFloat(marina.CENTERX);
        const name = marina.PORT_NAME || 'Marina';
        const marinaId = marina.ID || marina.PORT_ID || Date.now(); // Fallback ID
        
        const point = map.project([lng, lat]);
        
        const iconSize = isMobile ? 28 : 28;
        const clickRadius = iconSize / 2 + 5;
        
        // Speichere Klickbereich
        window.marinaClickAreas.push({
            x: point.x,
            y: point.y,
            radius: clickRadius,
            marinaId: marinaId,
            marinaName: name,
            lat: lat,
            lng: lng
        });
        
        // ZEICHNE SELECTION/HOVER EFFEKTE
        ctx.save();
        
        // Selected Marina - Gelber Kreis
        if (selectedMarina && selectedMarina.marinaId === marinaId) {
            ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffff00';
            ctx.lineWidth = 2;
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(point.x, point.y, iconSize * 0.8, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.stroke();
        }
        
        // Hovered Marina - Weißer Kreis
        if (hoveredMarina && hoveredMarina.marinaId === marinaId) {
            ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(point.x, point.y, iconSize * 0.7, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.stroke();
        }
        
        ctx.restore();
        
        // Icon zeichnen
        drawPNGIcon(ctx, point.x, point.y, 'marinas', iconSize);
        
        if (showNames) {
            drawPOILabel(ctx, point.x, point.y, name, -20);
        }
    });
}
    
    // MARINAS - Bereits gefiltert beim Laden
    if (poiFilters.marinas) {
        currentAssets.marinas.forEach(marina => {
            const lat = parseFloat(marina.CENTERY);
            const lng = parseFloat(marina.CENTERX);
            const name = marina.PORT_NAME || 'Marina';
            
            const point = map.project([lng, lat]);
            
            // Mobile: Doppelte Größe
            const iconSize = isMobile ? 28 : 28;
            drawPNGIcon(ctx, point.x, point.y, 'marinas', iconSize);
            
            // Name nur bei hohem Zoom anzeigen
            if (showNames) {
                drawPOILabel(ctx, point.x, point.y, name, -20);
            }
        });
    }
    
    // LEUCHTTÜRME - Bereits gefiltert beim Laden
    if (poiFilters.lights) {
        currentAssets.lights.forEach(light => {
            const lat = parseFloat(light.LAT);
            const lng = parseFloat(light.LON);
            const name = light.LIGHT_NAME || 'Lighthouse';
            
            const point = map.project([lng, lat]);
            
            // Mobile: Doppelte Größe
            const iconSize = isMobile ? 28 : 28;
            drawPNGIcon(ctx, point.x, point.y, 'lighthouse', iconSize);
            
            // Name nur bei hohem Zoom anzeigen  
            if (showNames) {
                drawPOILabel(ctx, point.x, point.y, name, -16);
            }
        });
    }
}

function getMarinaAtPosition(x, y) {
    if (!window.marinaClickAreas || window.marinaClickAreas.length === 0) {
        return null;
    }
    
    for (const marinaArea of window.marinaClickAreas) {
        const distance = Math.sqrt(
            Math.pow(x - marinaArea.x, 2) + 
            Math.pow(y - marinaArea.y, 2)
        );
        
        if (distance <= marinaArea.radius) {
            return marinaArea;
        }
    }
    
    return null;
}

function getPortAtPosition(x, y) {
    if (!window.portClickAreas || window.portClickAreas.length === 0) {
        return null;
    }
    
    // Finde Port in Klickbereich
    for (const portArea of window.portClickAreas) {
        const distance = Math.sqrt(
            Math.pow(x - portArea.x, 2) + 
            Math.pow(y - portArea.y, 2)
        );
        
        if (distance <= portArea.radius) {
            return portArea;
        }
    }
    
    return null;
}

// HILFSFUNKTION FÜR POI LABELS
function drawPOILabel(ctx, x, y, name, offsetY) {
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.font = isMobile ? '12px system-ui' : '12px system-ui';
    
    const labelY = y + (isMobile ? offsetY : offsetY);
    
    // Schwarzer Schatten/Rand für bessere Lesbarkeit
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000000';
    ctx.fillText(name, x + 1, labelY);
    ctx.fillText(name, x - 1, labelY);
    ctx.fillText(name, x, labelY + 1);
    ctx.fillText(name, x, labelY - 1);
    
    // Weiße Hauptschrift
    ctx.fillStyle = '#FFFFFF';
    ctx.fillText(name, x, labelY);
}

// PNG ICON ZEICHNEN
let iconCache = {}; // Cache für geladene Icons

function drawPNGIcon(ctx, x, y, type, size) {
    const iconUrls = {
        ports: 'https://marinetraffic.live/ports.png',
        marinas: 'https://marinetraffic.live/marinas.png', 
        lighthouse: 'https://marinetraffic.live/lighthouse.png'
    };
    
    const cacheKey = type + '_' + size;
    
    // Prüfe Cache
    if (iconCache[cacheKey]) {
        const img = iconCache[cacheKey];
        if (img.complete) {
            // Originales Seitenverhältnis beibehalten
            const aspectRatio = img.width / img.height;
            let drawWidth, drawHeight;
            
            if (aspectRatio > 1) {
                // Breiter als hoch - Breite auf size begrenzen
                drawWidth = size;
                drawHeight = size / aspectRatio;
            } else {
                // Höher als breit - Höhe auf size begrenzen
                drawHeight = size;
                drawWidth = size * aspectRatio;
            }
            
            ctx.drawImage(img, x - drawWidth/2, y - drawHeight/2, drawWidth, drawHeight);
        }
        return;
    }
    
    // Lade neues Icon
    const img = new Image();
    img.crossOrigin = 'anonymous'; // Für CORS
    
    img.onload = function() {
        iconCache[cacheKey] = img;
        
        // Originales Seitenverhältnis beibehalten
        const aspectRatio = img.width / img.height;
        let drawWidth, drawHeight;
        
        if (aspectRatio > 1) {
            // Breiter als hoch
            drawWidth = size;
            drawHeight = size / aspectRatio;
        } else {
            // Höher als breit
            drawHeight = size;
            drawWidth = size * aspectRatio;
        }
        
        ctx.drawImage(img, x - drawWidth/2, y - drawHeight/2, drawWidth, drawHeight);
        needsRedraw = true; // Trigger redraw für andere Icons
    };
    
    img.onerror = function() {
        console.log('Failed to load icon:', iconUrls[type]);
        // Fallback: Einfaches Symbol zeichnen
        drawFallbackIcon(ctx, x, y, type, size);
    };
    
    img.src = iconUrls[type];
}

// FALLBACK ICON FUNKTION
function drawFallbackIcon(ctx, x, y, type, size) {
    ctx.save();
    
    const colors = {
        ports: '#4CAF50',      // Grün für Häfen
        marinas: '#2196F3',    // Blau für Marinas
        lighthouse: '#FF9800'  // Orange für Leuchttürme
    };
    
    ctx.fillStyle = colors[type] || '#666666';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(x, y, size/2, 0, 2 * Math.PI);
    ctx.fill();
    
    // Weißer Rand
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#FFFFFF';
   ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.stroke();
    
    ctx.restore();
}

let deferredPrompt;
let userInteracted = false;

function triggerInstallPrompt() {
  if (!deferredPrompt || !userInteracted) {
    console.log('Cannot show prompt - no user interaction');
    return;
  }
  
  console.log('Showing install prompt');
  deferredPrompt.prompt();
  
  deferredPrompt.userChoice.then((choiceResult) => {
    if (choiceResult.outcome === 'accepted') {
      console.log('User accepted the install prompt');
    } else {
      console.log('User dismissed the install prompt');
    }
    deferredPrompt = null;
  });
}

window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', (e) => {
  e.preventDefault();
  deferredPrompt = e;
  console.log('Install prompt ready - waiting for interaction...');
});

const interactionEvents = ['mousemove', 'touchstart', 'touchend', 'touchmove', 'click', 'scroll'];

interactionEvents.forEach(event => {
  document.addEventListener(event, handleFirstInteraction, { 
    once: true,
    passive: true // Wichtig für Performance bei Touch
  });
});

  userInteracted = true;
  console.log('User interaction detected:', event.type);
  
  // Zeige Prompt nach 2-3 Sekunden
  //setTimeout(() => {

      //triggerInstallPrompt();
    //}
 //}, 5000);
}

function isAndroid() {
    // Prüft den User-Agent auf Android-Indikatoren
    return /android/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
}
function isIosPhone() {
    const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
    const platform = navigator.platform;
    
    // Prüfe auf iPhone, iPad, iPod
    const isIOSDevice = /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream;
    
    // Zusätzliche Prüfung für iPad auf Mac mit Touch Support
    const isIPadPro = platform === 'MacIntel' && navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0;
    
    return isIOSDevice || isIPadPro;
}

function getIOSApp() {
    // Geräteerkennung
    const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
    const isIPhone = /iPhone/.test(userAgent);
    const isIPad = /iPad/.test(userAgent);
    const isIOS = /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream;
    
    if (!isIOS) {
        alert('Diese Funktion ist nur für iOS-Geräte verfügbar.');
        return;
    }

    // Gerätetyp bestimmen
    let deviceType = 'iPhone';
    let screenSize = 'klein';
    
    // iPad Erkennung
    if (isIPad || (navigator.platform === 'MacIntel' && navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0)) {
        deviceType = 'iPad';
        screenSize = 'groß';
    }
    
    // iPhone Größen Erkennung
    if (isIPhone) {
        const screenWidth = window.screen.width;
        const screenHeight = window.screen.height;
        
        if (screenWidth >= 414 || screenHeight >= 896) {
            screenSize = 'groß'; // iPhone 12/13/14/15 Pro Max, Plus Modelle
        } else if (screenWidth >= 390 || screenHeight >= 844) {
            screenSize = 'mittel'; // iPhone 12/13/14/15 Pro
        } else {
            screenSize = 'klein'; // Ältere Modelle
        }
    }

    // Installations-Anleitung anzeigen
    showInstallationGuide(deviceType, screenSize);
}

function showInstallationGuide(deviceType, screenSize) {
    // Modal für die Installations-Anleitung erstellen
    const modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.style.cssText = `
        position: fixed;
        top: 0;
        left: 0;
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        background: rgba(0,0,0,0.9);
        z-index: 10000;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: center;
        font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif;
    `;

    const content = document.createElement('div');
    content.style.cssText = `
        background: #1a1a1a;
        border-radius: 12px;
        padding: 20px;
        max-width: 80%;
        max-height: 90%;
        overflow-y: auto;
        color: white;
        text-align: center;
        border: 2px solid rgb(1 85 176);
    `;

    // Titel
    const title = document.createElement('h2');
    title.textContent = 'App Installation - iOS';
    title.style.cssText = `
        color: rgb(38 142 255);
        margin-bottom: 20px;
        font-size: 1.5rem;
    `;

    // Geräte-Info
    const deviceInfo = document.createElement('p');
    deviceInfo.textContent = `Erkanntes Gerät: ${deviceType} (${screenSize}er Bildschirm)`;
    deviceInfo.style.cssText = `
        margin-bottom: 20px;
        color: #ccc;
    `;

    // Installations-Schritte
    const steps = document.createElement('div');
    steps.style.cssText = `
        text-align: left;
        margin: 20px 0;
        line-height: 1.6;
    `;

    const installationSteps = [
        '1. Tippen Sie auf das "Teilen"-Symbol in der Safari-Menüleiste',
        '2. Scrollen Sie nach unten im Teilen-Menü',
        '3. Wählen Sie "Zum Home-Bildschirm" aus',
        '4. Tippen Sie auf "Hinzufügen" in der oberen rechten Ecke',
        '5. Die App wird nun auf Ihrem Home-Bildschirm installiert'
    ];

    installationSteps.forEach(step => {
        const stepElement = document.createElement('div');
        stepElement.textContent = step;
        stepElement.style.marginBottom = '10px';
        steps.appendChild(stepElement);
    });

    // Visuelle Anleitung basierend auf Gerätetyp
    const visualGuide = document.createElement('div');
    visualGuide.style.cssText = `
        margin: 20px 0;
        padding: 15px;
        background: #2a2a2a;
        border-radius: 5px;
        border-left: 4px solid #4075c1;
    `;

    let guideText = '';
    if (deviceType === 'iPad') {
        guideText = '💡 Tipp: Auf dem iPad finden Sie das Teilen-Symbol in der oberen Menüleiste oder durch langes Drücken auf die Adressleiste.';
    } else if (screenSize === 'klein') {
        guideText = '💡 Tipp: Bei kleineren iPhones ist das Teilen-Symbol das Quadrat mit dem Pfeil nach oben in der unteren Menüleiste.';
    } else {
        guideText = '💡 Tipp: Bei neueren iPhones ist das Teilen-Symbol in der unteren Mitte der Menüleiste (Quadrat mit Pfeil nach oben).';
    }

    visualGuide.textContent = guideText;

    // Schließen-Button
    const closeButton = document.createElement('button');
    closeButton.textContent = 'Verstanden';
    closeButton.style.cssText = `
		background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0157b4 0%, #003366 100%);
		color: white;
		border: none;
		padding: 12px 30px;
		border-radius: 5px;
		font-size: 16px;
		cursor: pointer;
		margin-top: 15px;
		transition: background 0.3s;
    `;

    closeButton.onmouseover = () => closeButton.style.background = '#305a9c';
    closeButton.onmouseout = () => closeButton.style.background = '#4075c1';
    closeButton.onclick = () => document.body.removeChild(modal);

    // Elemente zusammenbauen
    content.appendChild(title);
    content.appendChild(deviceInfo);
    content.appendChild(steps);
    content.appendChild(visualGuide);
    content.appendChild(closeButton);
    modal.appendChild(content);

    // Modal zum Body hinzufügen
    document.body.appendChild(modal);

    // Klick außerhalb des Modals zum Schließen
    modal.onclick = (e) => {
        if (e.target === modal) {
            document.body.removeChild(modal);
        }
    };
}

    <script type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
        // Mobile Menu Funktionen - ANGEPASST FÜR RECHTS
        const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobileMenuBtn');
        const mobileMenuClose = document.getElementById('mobileMenuClose');
        const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobileMenu');
        const mobileMenuOverlay = document.getElementById('mobileMenuOverlay');
        
        function openMobileMenu() {
            mobileMenu.classList.add('open');
            mobileMenuOverlay.classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }
        
        function closeMobileMenu() {
            mobileMenu.classList.remove('open');
            mobileMenuOverlay.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        
        mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', openMobileMenu);
        mobileMenuClose.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
        mobileMenuOverlay.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
        
        // Mobile Dropdown Toggle
        function toggleMobileDropdown(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const dropdownToggle = event.currentTarget;
            const dropdown = dropdownToggle.parentElement.querySelector('.mobile-dropdown');
            const icon = dropdownToggle.querySelector('i');
            
            if (dropdown.style.display === 'block') {
                dropdown.style.display = 'none';
                icon.style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
            } else {
                dropdown.style.display = 'block';
                icon.style.transform = 'rotate(180deg)';
            }
        }
</script>
