<script id="gps-modul" type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
// =================================================================
// GPS TRACKING MODUL MIT DYNAMISCHER GESCHWINDIGKEITSLINIE
// =================================================================

// Globale GPS Variablen
let gpsWatchId = null;
let gpsMarker = null;
let isGPSTracking = false;
let lastGPSPosition = null;
let gpsTrackingStartTime = null;

// GPS Control Bar Variablen
let isFollowingGPS = false;
let isRecordingTrack = false;
let recordedTrack = [];
let recordingStartTime = null;
let playbackTrack = null;
let playbackIndex = 0;
let isPlayingTrack = false;
let playbackSpeed = 5;
let playbackInterval = null;
let trackMarker = null;

// NEUE Variablen für GPS Trail/Linie
let gpsTrail = [];
let playbackTrail = [];
let maxTrailPoints = 9999999999999;
let playbackPointReduction = 1;
let lastPlaybackDrawTime = 0;
let playbackDrawThrottle = 16;

// Rotation Variablen
let isRotatingWithGPS = false;
let lastRotationUpdate = 0;
let rotationInterval = null;

// =================================================================
// HAUPT GPS FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function toggleGPSTracking() {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    
    if (isGPSTracking) {
        stopGPSTracking();
    } else {
        resetGPSControlBarState();
        startGPSTracking();
    }
}

function calculatePlaybackPointReduction() {
    if (!playbackTrail || playbackTrail.length < 100) {
        playbackPointReduction = 1;
        return;
    }
    
    if (playbackTrail.length > 5000) {
        playbackPointReduction = 10;
    } else if (playbackTrail.length > 2000) {
        playbackPointReduction = 5;
    } else if (playbackTrail.length > 1000) {
        playbackPointReduction = 3;
    } else if (playbackTrail.length > 500) {
        playbackPointReduction = 2;
    } else {
        playbackPointReduction = 1;
    }
    
    console.log(`📊 Playback Optimierung: ${playbackTrail.length} Punkte, Reduktion: 1/${playbackPointReduction}`);
}

function startGPSTracking() {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    const routing = document.querySelector('#routingInstructionsPanel');
    const distance = document.querySelector('#measurementInfoPanel');    
    const details = document.querySelector('#shipDetailWindow');
    const details2 = document.querySelector('#portDetailWindow');

    details.style.top = '220px';
    details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 248px) !important';        
    if(isMobile) {
        details.style.top = '214px';    
        details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 290px) !important';    
    }

    details2.style.top = '220px';
    details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 248px) !important';        
    if(isMobile) {
        details2.style.top = '214px';    
        details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 290px) !important';    
    }

    if(isRoutingMode) {
        routing.style.top = '220px';
        if(isMobile)
        routing.style.top = '214px';        
    }

    if(isDistanceMeasureActive) {
        distance.style.top = '220px';    
        if(isMobile)
        distance.style.top = '214px';    
    }
        
    if (!navigator.geolocation) {
        showGPSError('GPS wird von diesem Browser nicht unterstützt');
        return;
    }
    
    console.log('🌍 GPS Tracking gestartet');
    gpsTrackingStartTime = Date.now();
    
    gpsTrail = [];
    
    gpsButton.classList.remove('gps-active', 'gps-error');
    gpsButton.classList.add('gps-searching');
    gpsButton.title = 'GPS Position wird gesucht...';
    
    showGPSSpeedDisplay();
    resetGPSSpeedDisplay();
    showGPSControlBar();
    
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        (position) => handleGPSSuccess(position, true),
        handleGPSError,
        {
            enableHighAccuracy: true,
            timeout: 8000,
            maximumAge: 30000
        }
    );
    
    gpsWatchId = navigator.geolocation.watchPosition(
        (position) => handleGPSSuccess(position, false),
        handleGPSError,
        {
            enableHighAccuracy: true,
            timeout: 15000,
            maximumAge: 30000
        }
    );
    
    isGPSTracking = true;
}

function stopGPSTracking() {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    const routing = document.querySelector('#routingInstructionsPanel');
    const distance = document.querySelector('#measurementInfoPanel');
    
    routing.style.top = '72px';    
    distance.style.top = '72px';    
    
    if (gpsWatchId !== null) {
        navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(gpsWatchId);
        gpsWatchId = null;
    }
    
    removeGPSMarker();
    clearGPSTrail();
    
    hideGPSSpeedDisplay();
    hideGPSControlBar();
    stopAllGPSFunctions();
    
    gpsButton.classList.remove('gps-searching', 'gps-active', 'gps-error');
    gpsButton.title = 'GPS Position';
    
    isGPSTracking = false;
    lastGPSPosition = null;
    gpsTrackingStartTime = null;
    
    console.log('🌍 GPS Tracking gestoppt - Alle GPS Funktionen deaktiviert');
}

function handleGPSSuccess(position, shouldFlyTo = false) {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    const latitude = position.coords.latitude;
    const longitude = position.coords.longitude;
    const accuracy = position.coords.accuracy;
    const heading = position.coords.heading;
    const speed = position.coords.speed || 0;
    
    console.log('🌍 GPS Position erhalten:', {
        lat: latitude,
        lng: longitude,
        accuracy: Math.round(accuracy) + 'm'
    });
    
    gpsButton.classList.remove('gps-searching', 'gps-error');
    gpsButton.classList.add('gps-active');
    gpsButton.title = `GPS aktiv ±${Math.round(accuracy)}m • ${(speed * 3.6).toFixed(1)} km/h`;
    
    if (shipCanvas) {
        const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
        const containerRect = mapContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
        const canvasRect = shipCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
        
        const positionDrift = Math.abs(canvasRect.left - containerRect.left) > 2 ||
                             Math.abs(canvasRect.top - containerRect.top) > 2;
        
        if (positionDrift) {
            console.log('🔧 GPS: Canvas Position korrigiert');
            resizeShipCanvas();
        }
    }
    
    lastGPSPosition = {
        lat: latitude,
        lng: longitude,
        accuracy: accuracy,
        heading: heading,
        speed: speed,
        timestamp: Date.now()
    };
    
    updateGPSSpeedDisplay(position);
    
    showGPSPosition(latitude, longitude, accuracy, heading);
    
    if (isRecordingTrack) {
        addTrackPoint(position.coords);
    }
    
    if (isFollowingGPS && !shouldFlyTo) {
        map.setCenter([longitude, latitude]);
    }
    
    if (shouldFlyTo || !gpsMarker) {
        flyToGPSPosition(longitude, latitude, accuracy);
    }
    
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function handleGPSError(error) {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    let errorMessage = 'GPS Fehler';
    
    switch(error.code) {
        case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:
            errorMessage = 'GPS Zugriff verweigert - Bitte Standortberechtigung erteilen';
            break;
        case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:
            errorMessage = 'GPS Position nicht verfügbar - Bitte GPS aktivieren';
            break;
        case error.TIMEOUT:
            errorMessage = 'GPS Timeout - Versuche es erneut';
            break;
        default:
            errorMessage = 'Unbekannter GPS Fehler';
            break;
    }
    
    console.error('🌍 GPS Fehler:', errorMessage, error);
    
    gpsButton.classList.remove('gps-searching', 'gps-active');
    gpsButton.classList.add('gps-error');
    gpsButton.title = errorMessage;
    
    hideGPSSpeedDisplay();
    hideGPSControlBar();
    stopAllGPSFunctions();
    
    showNotification(errorMessage, 'error');
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        if (gpsButton.classList.contains('gps-error')) {
            stopGPSTracking();
        }
    }, 4000);
}

// =================================================================
// GPS TRAIL FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function addPlaybackTrailPoint(lng, lat, speed) {
    if (typeof lng !== 'number' || typeof lat !== 'number') {
        console.error('❌ Ungültige Playback Trail Koordinaten:', { lng, lat });
        return;
    }
    
    const speedKnots = speed || 0;
    
    const trailPoint = {
        lng: lng,
        lat: lat,
        speed: speedKnots,
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        type: 'playback'
    };
    
    playbackTrail.push(trailPoint);
    
    if (playbackTrail.length % 100 === 0) {
        calculatePlaybackPointReduction();
    }    
    
    if (playbackTrail.length > maxTrailPoints) {
        playbackTrail.shift();
    }
    
    console.log('🎬 Playback Trail Punkt hinzugefügt:', {
        position: [lng, lat],
        speed: speedKnots.toFixed(1) + ' kn',
        trailLength: playbackTrail.length
    });
    
    const now = Date.now();
    if (now - lastPlaybackDrawTime > playbackDrawThrottle) {
        lastPlaybackDrawTime = now;
        needsRedraw = true;
        
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            if (typeof drawShips === 'function') {
                drawShips();
            }
        });
    }

    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (typeof drawShips === 'function') {
            drawShips();
        }
    });
}

function clearGPSTrail() {
    gpsTrail = [];
    console.log('🧹 GPS Trail geleert');
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function clearPlaybackTrail() {
    playbackTrail = [];
    console.log('🧹 Playback Trail geleert');
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function getSpeedColor(speedKnots) {
    if (speedKnots <= 0) {
        return '#ef4444';
    } else if (speedKnots <= 5) {
        const factor = speedKnots / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#ef4444', '#f97316', factor);
    } else if (speedKnots <= 10) {
        const factor = (speedKnots - 5) / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#f97316', '#eab308', factor);
    } else if (speedKnots <= 15) {
        const factor = (speedKnots - 10) / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#eab308', '#84cc16', factor);
    } else if (speedKnots <= 20) {
        const factor = (speedKnots - 15) / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#84cc16', '#22c55e', factor);
    } else {
        return '#22c55e';
    }
}

function interpolateColor(color1, color2, factor) {
    const hex1 = color1.replace('#', '');
    const hex2 = color2.replace('#', '');
    
    const r1 = parseInt(hex1.substr(0, 2), 16);
    const g1 = parseInt(hex1.substr(2, 2), 16);
    const b1 = parseInt(hex1.substr(4, 2), 16);
    
    const r2 = parseInt(hex2.substr(0, 2), 16);
    const g2 = parseInt(hex2.substr(2, 2), 16);
    const b2 = parseInt(hex2.substr(4, 2), 16);
    
    const r = Math.round(r1 + (r2 - r1) * factor);
    const g = Math.round(g1 + (g2 - g1) * factor);
    const b = Math.round(b1 + (b2 - b1) * factor);
    
    return `#${r.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')}${g.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')}${b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')}`;
}

function drawGPSTrail() {
    if (!shipCanvas || !shipCtx) return;
    
    const pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    
    if (playbackTrail.length > 1 && isPlayingTrack) {
        drawTrailSegments(playbackTrail, 'Playback');
    }
}

function drawTrailSegments(trail, type) {
    if (!trail || trail.length < 2) return;
    
    shipCtx.save();
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    const lineWidth = Math.max(2, Math.min(6, zoom / 3));
    
    let skipFactor = 1;
    if (trail.length > 5000) {
        skipFactor = 10;
    } else if (trail.length > 2000) {
        skipFactor = 5;
    } else if (trail.length > 1000) {
        skipFactor = 3;
    } else if (trail.length > 500) {
        skipFactor = 2;
    }
    
    for (let i = 0; i < trail.length - 1; i += skipFactor) {
        const nextIndex = Math.min(i + skipFactor, trail.length - 1);
        
        const point1 = trail[i];
        const point2 = trail[nextIndex];
        
        const screenPoint1 = map.project([point1.lng, point1.lat]);
        const screenPoint2 = map.project([point2.lng, point2.lat]);
        
        const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width;
        const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height;
        
        if ((screenPoint1.x < -100 && screenPoint2.x < -100) ||
            (screenPoint1.x > canvasWidth + 100 && screenPoint2.x > canvasWidth + 100) ||
            (screenPoint1.y < -100 && screenPoint2.y < -100) ||
            (screenPoint1.y > canvasHeight + 100 && screenPoint2.y > canvasHeight + 100)) {
            continue;
        }
        
        const avgSpeed = (point1.speed + point2.speed) / 2;
        const segmentColor = getSpeedColor(avgSpeed);
        
        shipCtx.strokeStyle = segmentColor;
        shipCtx.lineWidth = lineWidth;
        shipCtx.lineCap = 'round';
        shipCtx.lineJoin = 'round';
        
        const age = Date.now() - point1.timestamp;
        const maxAge = 300000;
        const alpha = Math.max(0.3, 1 - (age / maxAge));
        shipCtx.globalAlpha = alpha;
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(screenPoint1.x, screenPoint1.y);
        shipCtx.lineTo(screenPoint2.x, screenPoint2.y);
        shipCtx.stroke();
    }
    
    shipCtx.restore();
}

// =================================================================
// GPS MARKER FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function showGPSPosition(lat, lng, accuracy, heading = null) {
    gpsMarker = {
        lat: lat,
        lng: lng,
        accuracy: accuracy,
        heading: heading,
        timestamp: Date.now()
    };
    
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function removeGPSMarker() {
    gpsMarker = null;
    needsRedraw = true;
}

function drawGPSMarker() {
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        return;
    }
    
    if (!gpsMarker || !shipCanvas || !shipCtx) return;
    
    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    
    const point = map.project([gpsMarker.lng, gpsMarker.lat]);
    
    if (point.x < -100 || point.x > canvasWidth + 100 || 
        point.y < -100 || point.y > canvasHeight + 100) {
        return;
    }
    
    shipCtx.save();
    
    const zoom = map.getZoom();
    const time = Date.now() / 1000;
    
    if (gpsMarker.accuracy && gpsMarker.accuracy < 2000) {
        const metersPerPixel = 40075016.686 * Math.abs(Math.cos(gpsMarker.lat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.pow(2, zoom + 8);
        const accuracyRadius = Math.max(5, Math.min(300, gpsMarker.accuracy / metersPerPixel));
        
        if (accuracyRadius >= 5) {
            const pulseAlpha = 0.1 + Math.sin(time * 2) * 0.05;
            
            shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#3b82f6';
            shipCtx.fillStyle = `rgba(59, 130, 246, ${pulseAlpha})`;
            shipCtx.lineWidth = 1.5;
            shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.7;
            
            shipCtx.beginPath();
            shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, accuracyRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            shipCtx.fill();
            shipCtx.stroke();
        }
    }
    
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    
    const outerPulse = 1 + Math.sin(time * 3) * 0.4;
    const outerRadius = 20 * outerPulse;
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#3b82f6';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 2;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.3 / outerPulse;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, outerRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    const middlePulse = 1 + Math.sin(time * 4 + 1) * 0.3;
    const middleRadius = 15 * middlePulse;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.4 / middlePulse;
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, middleRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x + 1, point.y + 1, 12, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#e5e7eb';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 12, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#3b82f6';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    if (gpsMarker.heading !== undefined && gpsMarker.heading !== null) {
        const gpsHeadingRad = (gpsMarker.heading * Math.PI) / 180;
        const mapBearing = map.getBearing();
        const absoluteHeadingRad = gpsHeadingRad - (mapBearing * Math.PI / 180);
        
        const arrowLength = 35;
        const arrowEndX = point.x + Math.sin(absoluteHeadingRad) * arrowLength;
        const arrowEndY = point.y - Math.cos(absoluteHeadingRad) * arrowLength;
        
        shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#1d4ed8';
        shipCtx.lineWidth = 3;
        shipCtx.lineCap = 'round';
        shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.9;
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(point.x, point.y);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.stroke();
        
        const arrowSize = 12;
        const angle1 = absoluteHeadingRad + (Math.PI * 0.8);
        const angle2 = absoluteHeadingRad - (Math.PI * 0.8);
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle1) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle1) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle2) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle2) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.stroke();
    }
    
    shipCtx.restore();
    
    if (isGPSTracking) {
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
}

// =================================================================
// TRACK PLAYBACK FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function updateTrackMarker(lng, lat) {
    console.log('📍 Aktualisiere Track Marker auf:', { lng, lat });
    
    if (typeof lng !== 'number' || typeof lat !== 'number') {
        console.error('❌ Ungültige Koordinaten für Track Marker:', { lng, lat });
        return;
    }
    
    const currentTrackPoint = getCurrentTrackPoint();
    let heading = null;
    
    if (currentTrackPoint) {
        if (currentTrackPoint.heading !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.heading !== null) {
            heading = currentTrackPoint.heading;
        } else if (currentTrackPoint.course !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.course !== null) {
            heading = currentTrackPoint.course;
        } else {
            heading = calculateCOGFromMovement();
        }
    }
    
    trackMarker = {
        lng: lng,
        lat: lat,
        heading: heading,
        type: 'track-playback',
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        visible: true
    };
    
    let speed = 0;
    
    if (currentTrackPoint && currentTrackPoint.speed !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.speed !== null) {
        speed = currentTrackPoint.speed * 1.94384;
    }
    
    addPlaybackTrailPoint(lng, lat, speed);
    
    updateGPSSpeedDisplayFromTrack();
    
    console.log('✅ Track Marker gesetzt:', {
        position: [lng, lat],
        heading: heading ? heading.toFixed(1) + '°' : 'N/A',
        speed: speed.toFixed(1) + ' kn'
    });
    
    needsRedraw = true;

    if (typeof drawShips === 'function') {
        drawShips();
    }
}

function drawTrackMarker() {
    if (!trackMarker || !shipCanvas || !shipCtx || !isPlayingTrack) return;
    
    var pixelRatio = isMobile ? Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.0) : (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
    const canvasWidth = shipCanvas.width / pixelRatio;
    const canvasHeight = shipCanvas.height / pixelRatio;
    
    const point = map.project([trackMarker.lng, trackMarker.lat]);
    
    if (point.x < -100 || point.x > canvasWidth + 100 || 
        point.y < -100 || point.y > canvasHeight + 100) {
        return;
    }
    
    shipCtx.save();
    
    const time = Date.now() / 1000;
    
    const outerPulse = 1 + Math.sin(time * 3) * 0.4;
    const outerRadius = 20 * outerPulse;
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#3b82f6';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 2;
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.3 / outerPulse;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, outerRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    shipCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x + 1, point.y + 1, 10, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#3b82f6';
    shipCtx.lineWidth = 1;
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 10, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    shipCtx.stroke();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#3b82f6';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 7, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    shipCtx.beginPath();
    shipCtx.arc(point.x, point.y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    shipCtx.fill();
    
    if (trackMarker.heading !== undefined && trackMarker.heading !== null) {
        const trackHeadingRad = (trackMarker.heading * Math.PI) / 180;
        const mapBearing = map.getBearing();
        const absoluteHeadingRad = trackHeadingRad - (mapBearing * Math.PI / 180);
        
        const arrowLength = 35;
        const arrowEndX = point.x + Math.sin(absoluteHeadingRad) * arrowLength;
        const arrowEndY = point.y - Math.cos(absoluteHeadingRad) * arrowLength;
        
        shipCtx.strokeStyle = '#1d4ed8';
        shipCtx.lineWidth = 3;
        shipCtx.lineCap = 'round';
        shipCtx.globalAlpha = 0.9;
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(point.x, point.y);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.stroke();
        
        const arrowSize = 12;
        const angle1 = absoluteHeadingRad + (Math.PI * 0.8);
        const angle2 = absoluteHeadingRad - (Math.PI * 0.8);
        
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle1) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle1) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.moveTo(arrowEndX, arrowEndY);
        shipCtx.lineTo(arrowEndX + Math.sin(angle2) * arrowSize, arrowEndY - Math.cos(angle2) * arrowSize);
        shipCtx.stroke();
    } else {
        shipCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
        shipCtx.beginPath();
        shipCtx.moveTo(point.x - 2, point.y - 3);
        shipCtx.lineTo(point.x + 3, point.y);
        shipCtx.lineTo(point.x - 2, point.y + 3);
        shipCtx.closePath();
        shipCtx.fill();
    }
    
    shipCtx.restore();
    
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
}

// =================================================================
// ERWEITERTE DRAW-FUNKTION
// =================================================================

function drawGPSElements() {
    if (shipCanvas && shipCtx) {
        const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
        const expectedWidth = mapContainer.offsetWidth;
        const expectedHeight = mapContainer.offsetHeight;
        const actualStyleWidth = parseInt(shipCanvas.style.width) || 0;
        const actualStyleHeight = parseInt(shipCanvas.style.height) || 0;
        
        if (Math.abs(expectedWidth - actualStyleWidth) > 5 || 
            Math.abs(expectedHeight - actualStyleHeight) > 5) {
            
            console.log('🔧 GPS Draw: Canvas Dimensionen-Mismatch erkannt - korrigiere');
            resizeShipCanvas();
            return;
        }
    }
    
    drawGPSTrail();
    
    if (!isPlayingTrack) {
        drawGPSMarker();
    }
    
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        drawTrackMarker();
    }
}

// =================================================================
// PLAYBACK FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function startPlayback() {
    if (!playbackTrack || !playbackTrack.coordinates || playbackIndex >= playbackTrack.coordinates.length) {
        console.error('❌ Kann Playback nicht starten - ungültige Daten');
        return;
    }
    
    console.log('▶️ Starte Playback von Index:', playbackIndex, 'mit Geschwindigkeit:', playbackSpeed + 'x');
    
    if (playbackIndex === 0) {
        clearPlaybackTrail();
    }

    calculatePlaybackPointReduction();
    
    if (!isGPSTracking) {
        showGPSSpeedDisplay();
        console.log('📊 GPS Speed Display für Track-Playback aktiviert');
    }
    
    let baseIntervalMs = Math.max(50, (playbackTrack.totalDuration * 1000) / playbackTrack.coordinates.length);
    let intervalMs = Math.max(25, baseIntervalMs / playbackSpeed);
    
    console.log('⏱️ Playback Interval:', intervalMs, 'ms (Speed:', playbackSpeed + 'x)');
 
    if (playbackIndex < playbackTrack.coordinates.length) {
        const point = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex];
        updateTrackMarker(point[0], point[1]);
    
        needsRedraw = true;
        if (typeof drawShips === 'function') {
            drawShips();
        }
    }
 
    playbackInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (playbackIndex >= playbackTrack.coordinates.length) {
            console.log('🏁 Playback Ende erreicht');
            stopTrack();
            return;
        }
        
        const point = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex];
        
        if (playbackSpeed <= 25 || playbackIndex % Math.floor(playbackSpeed / 10) === 0) {
            console.log('📍 Playback Punkt:', playbackIndex, '/', playbackTrack.coordinates.length, point);
        }
        
        updateTrackMarker(point[0], point[1]);
        
        if (isFollowingGPS) {
            if (playbackSpeed <= 25 || playbackIndex % Math.floor(playbackSpeed / 25) === 0) {
                map.setCenter([point[0], point[1]]);
            }
        }
        
        playbackIndex++;
        
        if (playbackSpeed <= 25 || playbackIndex % Math.floor(playbackSpeed / 10) === 0) {
            updatePlaybackUI();
        }
        
    }, intervalMs);
}

function stopTrack() {
    isPlayingTrack = false;
    if (playbackInterval) {
        clearInterval(playbackInterval);
        playbackInterval = null;
    }
    
    playbackIndex = 0;
    const playPauseBtn = document.getElementById('playPauseBtn');
    if (playPauseBtn) {
        playPauseBtn.textContent = '▶';
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-size', '16px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('line-height', '1px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-weight', 'bold');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('background', 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)');
    }
    
    clearPlaybackTrail();
    trackMarker = null;
    
    if (!isGPSTracking) {
        hideGPSSpeedDisplay();
        console.log('📊 GPS Speed Display für Track-Playback deaktiviert');
    } else {
        if (lastGPSPosition) {
            const mockPosition = { coords: lastGPSPosition };
            updateGPSSpeedDisplay(mockPosition);
            console.log('📊 GPS Speed Display zurück zu echten GPS-Werten');
        }
    }
    
    updatePlaybackUI();
    needsRedraw = true;
    console.log('⏹️ Track gestoppt - Trail geleert');
}

function closePlayback() {
    const controls = document.getElementById('gpsPlaybackControls');
    const routing = document.querySelector('#routingInstructionsPanel');
    const distance = document.querySelector('#measurementInfoPanel');
    const details = document.querySelector('#shipDetailWindow');
    const details2 = document.querySelector('#portDetailWindow');

    setTimeout(() => {
        if (isGPSTracking) {    
            routing.style.top = '220px';
            distance.style.top = '220px';    
            details.style.top = '220px';
            details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 140px)';    
            details2.style.top = '220px';
            details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 140px)';    
            if(isMobile) {
                routing.style.top = '214px';        
                distance.style.top = '214px';    
                details.style.top = '214px';;
                details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 280px)';    
                details2.style.top = '214px';;
                details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 280px)';
            }
        }
    }, 100);   

    controls.classList.remove('visible');
    
    stopTrack();
    removeTrackFromMap();
    clearPlaybackTrail();
    
    if (!isGPSTracking) {
        hideGPSSpeedDisplay();
    }
    
    playbackTrack = null;
    console.log('🎬 Playback geschlossen - alle Trails geleert');
}

// =================================================================
// HILFSFUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function flyToGPSPosition(longitude, latitude, accuracy) {
    let targetZoom;
    
    if (accuracy <= 10) {
        targetZoom = 18;
    } else if (accuracy <= 50) {
        targetZoom = 16;
    } else if (accuracy <= 100) {
        targetZoom = 15;
    } else if (accuracy <= 500) {
        targetZoom = 13;
    } else {
        targetZoom = 11;
    }
    
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    const finalZoom = Math.max(targetZoom, Math.min(currentZoom, targetZoom + 2));
    
    console.log(`🌍 Fliege zu GPS Position (Genauigkeit: ${Math.round(accuracy)}m, Zoom: ${finalZoom})`);
    
    map.flyTo({
        center: [longitude, latitude],
        zoom: finalZoom,
        duration: 1000,
        curve: 1.2,
        easing: (t) => t * (2 - t)
    });
}

function showNotification(message, type = 'info') {
    let notification = document.getElementById('gps-notification');
    if (!notification) {
        notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.id = 'gps-notification';
        notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 72px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.9);
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 20px;
            border-radius: 6px;
            font-size: 12px;
            z-index: 8000;
            opacity: 0;
            transition: opacity 0.3s ease;
            width: 390px;
            text-align: center;
            pointer-events: none;
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);
    }
    
    const colors = {
        info: 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.9)',
        error: 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.95)',
        success: 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.95)',
        warning: 'rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.95)'
    };
    
    notification.style.background = colors[type] || colors.info;
    notification.textContent = message;
    notification.style.opacity = '1';
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        notification.style.opacity = '0';
    }, 2000);
}

// =================================================================
// GPS SPEED DISPLAY FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function showGPSSpeedDisplay() {
    const display = document.getElementById('gpsSpeedDisplay');
    if (display) {
        display.style.display = 'block';
        console.log('📊 GPS Speed Display angezeigt');
    }
}

function hideGPSSpeedDisplay() {
    const display = document.getElementById('gpsSpeedDisplay');
    if (display) {
        display.style.display = 'none';
        console.log('📊 GPS Speed Display versteckt');
    }
}

function updateGPSSpeedDisplay(position) {
    if (!position || !position.coords) return;
    
    const coords = position.coords;
    const speedMs = coords.speed || 0;
    const speedKnots = speedMs * 1.94384;
    const sog = speedKnots;
    const cog = coords.heading || 0;
    
    updateGPSValue('gpsSogValue', sog.toFixed(1));
    updateGPSValue('gpsSpeedValue', speedKnots.toFixed(1));
    updateGPSValue('gpsCogValue', Math.round(cog) + '°');
}

function updateGPSValue(elementId, value) {
    const element = document.getElementById(elementId);
    if (element) {
        if (elementId === 'gpsSpeedValue') {
            const unit = element.querySelector('.gps-speed-unit');
            if (unit) {
                element.innerHTML = value + unit.outerHTML;
            } else {
                element.innerHTML = value + '<span class="gps-speed-unit">kn</span>';
            }
        } else {
            element.textContent = value;
        }
    }
}

function resetGPSSpeedDisplay() {
    updateGPSValue('gpsSogValue', '--');
    updateGPSValue('gpsSpeedValue', '--');
    updateGPSValue('gpsCogValue', '--°');
}

function updateGPSSpeedDisplayFromTrack() {
    if (!isPlayingTrack || !playbackTrack || !playbackTrack.trackPoints) {
        return;
    }
    
    const speedDisplay = document.getElementById('gpsSpeedDisplay');
    if (!speedDisplay || speedDisplay.style.display === 'none') {
        return;
    }
    
    const currentTrackPoint = getCurrentTrackPoint();
    
    if (currentTrackPoint) {
        let sog = 0;
        if (currentTrackPoint.speed !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.speed !== null) {
            sog = currentTrackPoint.speed * 1.94384;
        }
        
        let cog = 0;
        if (currentTrackPoint.heading !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.heading !== null) {
            cog = currentTrackPoint.heading;
        } else if (currentTrackPoint.course !== undefined && currentTrackPoint.course !== null) {
            cog = currentTrackPoint.course;
        } else {
            cog = calculateCOGFromMovement();
        }
        
        const speed = sog;
        
        updateGPSValue('gpsSogValue', sog.toFixed(1));
        updateGPSValue('gpsSpeedValue', speed.toFixed(1));
        updateGPSValue('gpsCogValue', Math.round(cog) + '°');
    } else {
        updateGPSValue('gpsSogValue', '0.0');
        updateGPSValue('gpsSpeedValue', '0.0');
        updateGPSValue('gpsCogValue', '0°');
    }
}

function getCurrentTrackPoint() {
    if (!playbackTrack || !playbackTrack.trackPoints || playbackIndex >= playbackTrack.trackPoints.length) {
        return null;
    }
    
    const trackPoint = playbackTrack.trackPoints[playbackIndex];
    
    let processedPoint = {
        coordinates: trackPoint.coordinates,
        timestamp: trackPoint.timestamp,
        speed: null,
        heading: null,
        course: null,
        altitude: trackPoint.altitude,
        accuracy: trackPoint.accuracy
    };
    
    if (trackPoint.speed !== undefined && trackPoint.speed !== null) {
        processedPoint.speed = parseFloat(trackPoint.speed);
    } else if (trackPoint.velocity !== undefined && trackPoint.velocity !== null) {
        processedPoint.speed = parseFloat(trackPoint.velocity);
    }
    
    if (trackPoint.heading !== undefined && trackPoint.heading !== null) {
        processedPoint.heading = parseFloat(trackPoint.heading);
    } else if (trackPoint.bearing !== undefined && trackPoint.bearing !== null) {
        processedPoint.heading = parseFloat(trackPoint.bearing);
    }
    
    if (trackPoint.course !== undefined && trackPoint.course !== null) {
        processedPoint.course = parseFloat(trackPoint.course);
    } else if (trackPoint.cog !== undefined && trackPoint.cog !== null) {
        processedPoint.course = parseFloat(trackPoint.cog);
    }
    
    return processedPoint;
}

function calculateCOGFromMovement() {
    if (!playbackTrack || !playbackTrack.coordinates || playbackIndex <= 0) {
        return 0;
    }
    
    const currentCoord = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex];
    const previousCoord = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex - 1];
    
    if (!currentCoord || !previousCoord || 
        currentCoord[0] === null || currentCoord[1] === null ||
        previousCoord[0] === null || previousCoord[1] === null) {
        return 0;
    }
    
    const deltaLng = currentCoord[0] - previousCoord[0];
    const deltaLat = currentCoord[1] - previousCoord[1];
    
    if (deltaLng === 0 && deltaLat === 0) {
        return 0;
    }
    
    let bearing = Math.atan2(deltaLng, deltaLat) * 180 / Math.PI;
    
    if (bearing < 0) {
        bearing += 360;
    }
    
    return bearing;
}

// =================================================================
// CONTROL BAR FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function showGPSControlBar() {
    const controlBar = document.getElementById('gpsControlBar');
    if (!controlBar) return;
    
    if (shipCanvas) {
        const mapContainer = map.getContainer();
        const expectedWidth = mapContainer.offsetWidth;
        const expectedHeight = mapContainer.offsetHeight;
        const actualWidth = parseInt(shipCanvas.style.width);
        const actualHeight = parseInt(shipCanvas.style.height);
        
        if (Math.abs(expectedWidth - actualWidth) > 5 || 
            Math.abs(expectedHeight - actualHeight) > 5) {
            console.log('🔧 GPS: Canvas Dimensionen korrigiert');
            resizeShipCanvas();
        }
    }

    setTimeout(() => {
        controlBar.classList.add('visible');
        controlBar.style.opacity = '0';
        controlBar.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%) translateY(10px)';
        controlBar.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease';
        setTimeout(() => {
            controlBar.style.opacity = '1';
            controlBar.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%) translateY(0)';
        }, 50);
    }, 150);
    
    console.log('🎮 GPS Control Bar angezeigt');
}

function hideGPSControlBar() {
    const controlBar = document.getElementById('gpsControlBar');
    if (controlBar) {
        controlBar.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease';
        controlBar.style.opacity = '0';
        controlBar.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%) translateY(-10px)';
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            controlBar.classList.remove('visible');
            controlBar.style.transition = '';
            controlBar.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%)';
        }, 300);
        
        console.log('🎮 GPS Control Bar versteckt');
    }
}

function toggleFollow() {
    const followBtn = document.getElementById('followBtn');
    
    if (!isFollowingGPS) {
        isFollowingGPS = true;
        isRotatingWithGPS = true;
        followBtn.classList.add('active');
        followBtn.title = 'GPS Verfolgung';
        
        showNotification('🧭 GPS Verfolgung aktiv', 'success');
        
        if (lastGPSPosition) {
            flyToGPSPosition(lastGPSPosition.lng, lastGPSPosition.lat, lastGPSPosition.accuracy);
        } else if (isPlayingTrack && trackMarker) {
            map.flyTo({
                center: [trackMarker.lng, trackMarker.lat],
                zoom: Math.max(map.getZoom(), 16),
                duration: 1000
            });
        }
        
        startAutoRotation();
        
    } else {
        stopGPSFollow();
    }
}

function toggleRecord() {
    const recordBtn = document.getElementById('recordBtn');
    const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('downloadBtn');
    
    if (isRecordingTrack) {
        isRecordingTrack = false;
        recordBtn.classList.remove('recording');
        recordBtn.title = 'GPS Track aufnehmen';
        recordBtn.querySelector('span').textContent = 'Aufnahme';
        
        downloadBtn.disabled = false;
        
        console.log('🔴 GPS Aufnahme gestoppt. Punkte:', recordedTrack.length);
        
        if (isMobile && recordedTrack.length > 0) {
            console.log('📱 Mobile: Starte automatischen Server-Upload nach Aufnahme-Ende');
            const geojson = createGeoJSONFromTrack(recordedTrack);
            uploadTrackToServer(geojson);
        }
    } else {
        isRecordingTrack = true;
        recordedTrack = [];
        recordingStartTime = Date.now();
        recordBtn.classList.add('recording');
        recordBtn.title = 'Aufnahme läuft - Klicken zum Stoppen';
        recordBtn.querySelector('span').textContent = 'Stop';
        
        downloadBtn.disabled = true;
        
        console.log('🔴 GPS Aufnahme gestartet');
        
        if (lastGPSPosition) {
            addTrackPoint(lastGPSPosition);
        }
    }
}

function addTrackPoint(gpsPosition) {
    if (!isRecordingTrack) return;
    
    let lat, lng;
    
    if (gpsPosition.latitude !== undefined && gpsPosition.longitude !== undefined) {
        lat = gpsPosition.latitude;
        lng = gpsPosition.longitude;
    } else if (gpsPosition.lat !== undefined && gpsPosition.lng !== undefined) {
        lat = gpsPosition.lat;
        lng = gpsPosition.lng;
    } else if (gpsPosition.coords) {
        lat = gpsPosition.coords.latitude;
        lng = gpsPosition.coords.longitude;
    } else {
        console.error('❌ Ungültige GPS Position Struktur:', gpsPosition);
        return;
    }
    
    if (typeof lat !== 'number' || typeof lng !== 'number' || 
        isNaN(lat) || isNaN(lng) || 
        lat === null || lng === null) {
        console.error('❌ Ungültige Koordinaten:', { lat, lng });
        return;
    }
    
    const point = {
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        coordinates: [lng, lat],
        altitude: gpsPosition.altitude || (gpsPosition.coords ? gpsPosition.coords.altitude : null),
        accuracy: gpsPosition.accuracy || (gpsPosition.coords ? gpsPosition.coords.accuracy : null),
        heading: gpsPosition.heading || (gpsPosition.coords ? gpsPosition.coords.heading : null),
        speed: gpsPosition.speed || (gpsPosition.coords ? gpsPosition.coords.speed : null)
    };
    
    recordedTrack.push(point);
    console.log('✅ Track Punkt hinzugefügt:', recordedTrack.length);
}

// =================================================================
// TRACK DOWNLOAD FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function downloadTrack() {
    if (recordedTrack.length === 0) {
        showNotification('Keine Aufnahme zum Download verfügbar', 'warning');
        return;
    }
    
    const geojson = createGeoJSONFromTrack(recordedTrack);
    
    if (isMobile) {
        console.log('📱 Mobile Download - Server Upload');
        uploadTrackToServer(geojson);
    } else {
        console.log('💻 Desktop Download - direkter Download');
        downloadTrackDesktop(geojson);
    }
}

function uploadTrackToServer(geojson) {
    const now = new Date();
    const filename = `gps_track_${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}_${String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}.geojson`;
    
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('geojson', JSON.stringify(geojson, null, 2));
    formData.append('filename', filename);
    
    fetch('save_track.php', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(result => {
        if (result.success) {
            console.log('✅ Track erfolgreich auf Server gespeichert:', result.filename);
            showNotification('Du kannst den Track nun downloaden', 'success');
            
            const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('downloadBtn');
            if (downloadBtn) {
                const downloadUrl = `https://marinetraffic.live/DownloadFile/${result.filename}`;
                
                const downloadLink = document.createElement('a');
                downloadLink.href = '#';
                downloadLink.onclick = function() { location.href = downloadUrl; return false; };
                downloadLink.className = downloadBtn.className;
                downloadLink.title = downloadBtn.title;
                downloadLink.innerHTML = downloadBtn.innerHTML;
                downloadLink.id = 'downloadBtn';
                downloadLink.style.textDecoration = 'none';
                downloadLink.style.display = 'inline-flex';
                downloadLink.style.alignItems = 'center';
                downloadLink.style.justifyContent = 'center';
                downloadLink.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                downloadLink.style.boxSizing = 'border-box';
                downloadLink.style.verticalAlign = 'middle';
                
                const computedStyle = window.getComputedStyle(downloadBtn);
                downloadLink.style.padding = computedStyle.padding;
                downloadLink.style.margin = computedStyle.margin;
                downloadLink.style.border = computedStyle.border;
                downloadLink.style.borderRadius = computedStyle.borderRadius;
                downloadLink.style.backgroundColor = computedStyle.backgroundColor;
                downloadLink.style.color = computedStyle.color;
                downloadLink.style.fontSize = computedStyle.fontSize;
                downloadLink.style.fontFamily = computedStyle.fontFamily;
                downloadLink.style.fontWeight = computedStyle.fontWeight;
                downloadLink.style.lineHeight = computedStyle.lineHeight;
                downloadLink.style.width = computedStyle.width;
                downloadLink.style.height = computedStyle.height;
                downloadLink.style.minWidth = computedStyle.minWidth;
                downloadLink.style.minHeight = computedStyle.minHeight;
                
                downloadBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(downloadLink, downloadBtn);
                
                console.log('🔗 Download Button zu Link konvertiert (gleiches Design):', downloadUrl);
            }
        } else {
            console.error('❌ Server-Upload fehlgeschlagen:', result.error);
            showNotification('Upload-Fehler: ' + result.error, 'error');
            
            downloadTrackDesktop(geojson);
        }
    })
    .catch(error => {
        console.error('❌ Upload-Request fehlgeschlagen:', error);
        showNotification('Netzwerk-Fehler - versuche lokalen Download', 'warning');
        
        downloadTrackDesktop(geojson);
    });
}

function downloadTrackDesktop(geojson) {
    const now = new Date();
    const filename = `gps_track_${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}_${String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}.geojson`;
    
    try {
        if (navigator.share && navigator.canShare) {
            const file = new File([JSON.stringify(geojson, null, 2)], filename, {
                type: 'application/json'
            });
            
            if (navigator.canShare({ files: [file] })) {
                navigator.share({
                    files: [file],
                    title: 'GPS Track',
                    text: 'Gespeicherter GPS Track'
                }).then(() => {
                    console.log('💾 Track erfolgreich geteilt');
                    showNotification('Track erfolgreich geteilt!', 'success');
                }).catch((error) => {
                    console.log('❌ Share API fehlgeschlagen, versuche Fallback:', error);
                    downloadTrackFallback(geojson, filename);
                });
                return;
            }
        }
        
        downloadTrackFallback(geojson, filename);
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Download Fehler:', error);
        showTrackInNewWindow(geojson, filename);
    }
}

function downloadTrackFallback(geojson, filename) {
    try {
        console.log('💾 Verwende Fallback Download Methode...');
        
        const jsonString = JSON.stringify(geojson, null, 2);
        const dataUri = 'data:application/json;charset=utf-8,' + encodeURIComponent(jsonString);
        
        const testLink = document.createElement('a');
        const supportsDownload = 'download' in testLink;
        
        if (supportsDownload) {
            const link = document.createElement('a');
            link.href = dataUri;
            link.download = filename;
            link.style.display = 'none';
            
            document.body.appendChild(link);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                try {
                    link.click();
                    console.log('💾 Track Download gestartet:', filename);
                    showNotification('Track Download gestartet!', 'success');
                } catch (clickError) {
                    console.error('❌ Click Fehler:', clickError);
                    showTrackInNewWindow(geojson, filename);
                } finally {
                    document.body.removeChild(link);
                }
            }, 100);
            
        } else {
            showTrackInNewWindow(geojson, filename);
        }
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Fallback Download fehlgeschlagen:', error);
        showTrackInNewWindow(geojson, filename);
    }
}

function createGeoJSONFromTrack(track) {
    const coordinates = track
        .filter(point => point.coordinates && Array.isArray(point.coordinates) && 
                point.coordinates.length >= 2 && 
                point.coordinates[0] !== null && point.coordinates[1] !== null)
        .map(point => point.coordinates);
    
    const geojson = {
        type: "FeatureCollection",
        features: [
            {
                type: "Feature",
                properties: {
                    name: "GPS Track",
                    description: `Aufgezeichnet am ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('de-DE')}`,
                    recordingStart: recordingStartTime,
                    recordingEnd: Date.now(),
                    pointCount: track.length,
                    creator: "MarineTraffic GPS Tracker"
                },
                geometry: {
                    type: "LineString",
                    coordinates: coordinates
                }
            }
        ],
        properties: {
            trackPoints: track.map(point => ({
                timestamp: point.timestamp,
                coordinates: point.coordinates,
                altitude: point.altitude,
                accuracy: point.accuracy,
                heading: point.heading,
                speed: point.speed
            }))
        }
    };
    
    return geojson;
}

// =================================================================
// TRACK PLAYBACK FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

function openFileUpload() {
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('gpsFileInput');
    fileInput.click();
}

function handleFileUpload(event) {
    const file = event.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(e) {
        try {
            const geojson = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
            loadTrackForPlayback(geojson, file.name);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Fehler beim Laden der GeoJSON Datei:', error);
            showNotification('Fehler beim Laden der Datei', 'error');
        }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
    
    event.target.value = '';
}

function loadTrackForPlayback(geojson, filename) {
    try {
        console.log('🔍 Analysiere GeoJSON:', geojson);
        
        let coordinates = [];
        let trackPoints = [];
        let geometryType = 'unknown';
        
        if (geojson.features && geojson.features.length > 0) {
            const firstFeature = geojson.features[0];
            if (firstFeature && firstFeature.geometry && firstFeature.geometry.type) {
                geometryType = firstFeature.geometry.type;
            } else {
                throw new Error('Ungültige GeoJSON Struktur');
            }
            
            if (geometryType === 'LineString') {
                if (geojson.properties && geojson.properties.trackPoints && Array.isArray(geojson.properties.trackPoints)) {
                    trackPoints = geojson.properties.trackPoints;
                    coordinates = trackPoints
                        .filter(point => point.coordinates && Array.isArray(point.coordinates) && 
                                point.coordinates.length >= 2 && 
                                point.coordinates[0] !== null && point.coordinates[1] !== null)
                        .map(point => point.coordinates);
                } else if (firstFeature.properties && firstFeature.properties.trackPoints && Array.isArray(firstFeature.properties.trackPoints)) {
                    trackPoints = firstFeature.properties.trackPoints;
                    coordinates = trackPoints
                        .filter(point => point.coordinates && Array.isArray(point.coordinates) && 
                                point.coordinates.length >= 2 && 
                                point.coordinates[0] !== null && point.coordinates[1] !== null)
                        .map(point => point.coordinates);
                } else {
                    const lineCoords = firstFeature.geometry.coordinates || [];
                    coordinates = lineCoords.filter(coord => 
                        coord && Array.isArray(coord) && coord.length >= 2 && 
                        coord[0] !== null && coord[1] !== null && 
                        typeof coord[0] === 'number' && typeof coord[1] === 'number'
                    );
                    
                    if (coordinates.length > 0) {
                        trackPoints = coordinates.map((coord, index) => ({
                            timestamp: Date.now() + (index * 1000),
                            coordinates: coord,
                            altitude: null,
                            accuracy: null,
                            heading: null,
                            speed: null
                        }));
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (coordinates.length === 0) {
            throw new Error('Keine gültigen Koordinaten in Track gefunden');
        }
        
        let totalDuration = calculateTrackDuration(trackPoints, coordinates.length);
        
        let trackName = filename;
        if (geojson.features && geojson.features.length > 0 && 
            geojson.features[0].properties && geojson.features[0].properties.name) {
            trackName = geojson.features[0].properties.name;
        }
        
        playbackTrack = {
            name: trackName,
            coordinates: coordinates,
            trackPoints: trackPoints,
            totalDuration: totalDuration,
            originalType: geometryType
        };
        
        playbackIndex = 0;
        
        console.log('✅ Track erfolgreich geladen:', {
            name: playbackTrack.name,
            points: playbackTrack.coordinates.length,
            duration: playbackTrack.totalDuration + ' Sekunden'
        });
        
        showPlaybackControls();
        showTrackOnMap();
                
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌ Fehler beim Verarbeiten der Track Daten:', error);
        showNotification('Fehler beim Laden: ' + error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function calculateTrackDuration(trackPoints, coordinateCount) {
    if (trackPoints && trackPoints.length >= 2) {
        const validTimestamps = trackPoints.filter(point => point.timestamp && point.timestamp > 0);
        
        if (validTimestamps.length >= 2) {
            const startTime = validTimestamps[0].timestamp;
            const endTime = validTimestamps[validTimestamps.length - 1].timestamp;
            const durationMs = endTime - startTime;
            const durationSeconds = Math.floor(durationMs / 1000);
            
            if (durationSeconds > 0) {
                return durationSeconds;
            }
        }
    }
    
    const estimatedSeconds = Math.max(1, coordinateCount);
    return estimatedSeconds;
}

function showPlaybackControls() {
    const controls = document.getElementById('gpsPlaybackControls');
    const trackName = document.getElementById('trackName');
    const trackSlider = document.getElementById('trackSlider');
    const totalTime = document.getElementById('totalTime');
    const currentTime = document.getElementById('currentTime');
    const routing = document.querySelector('#routingInstructionsPanel');
    const distance = document.querySelector('#measurementInfoPanel');
    const details = document.querySelector('#shipDetailWindow');
    const details2 = document.querySelector('#portDetailWindow');

    details.style.top = '360px';
    details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 385px)';    
    if(isMobile) {
        details.style.top = '348px';    
        details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 415px)';
    }
    
    details2.style.top = '360px';
    details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 385px)';    
    if(isMobile) {
        details2.style.top = '348px';    
        details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 415px)';
    }
    
    if(isRoutingMode == true) {
        routing.style.top = '360px';    
        if(isMobile)
        routing.style.top = '348px';    
    }   

    if(isDistanceMeasureActive == true) {
        distance.style.top = '360px';    
        if(isMobile)
        distance.style.top = '348px';    
    }   
    
    if (controls && playbackTrack) {
        controls.classList.add('visible');
        
        trackName.textContent = playbackTrack.name;
        trackSlider.max = playbackTrack.coordinates.length - 1;
        trackSlider.value = 0;
        totalTime.textContent = formatTime(playbackTrack.totalDuration);
        currentTime.textContent = formatTime(0);
    }
}

function showTrackOnMap() {
    if (!playbackTrack || !playbackTrack.coordinates || playbackTrack.coordinates.length === 0) {
        return;
    }
    
    const firstPoint = playbackTrack.coordinates[0];
    
    if (firstPoint && Array.isArray(firstPoint) && firstPoint.length >= 2) {
        const lng = firstPoint[0];
        const lat = firstPoint[1];
        
        map.flyTo({
            center: [lng, lat],
            zoom: Math.max(map.getZoom(), 14),
            duration: 1500
        });
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            updateTrackMarker(lng, lat);
            needsRedraw = true;
        }, 1600);
    }
}

function removeTrackFromMap() {
    if (trackMarker) {
        trackMarker = null;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
}

function playPauseTrack() {
    const playPauseBtn = document.getElementById('playPauseBtn');
    
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        isPlayingTrack = false;
        if (playbackInterval) {
            clearInterval(playbackInterval);
            playbackInterval = null;
        }
        playPauseBtn.textContent = '▶';
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-size', '16px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('line-height', '1px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-weight', 'bold');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('background', 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)');
        console.log('⏸️ Track pausiert');
    } else {
        isPlayingTrack = true;
        playPauseBtn.textContent = '||';
        playPauseBtn.textContent = '▶';
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-size', '16px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('line-height', '1px');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('font-weight', 'bold');
        $('#playPauseBtn').css('background', 'rgb(16 181 126)');
        startPlayback();
        console.log('▶️ Track wird abgespielt');
    }
}

function seekTrack(value) {
    const newIndex = parseInt(value);
    
    if (playbackTrack && newIndex >= 0 && newIndex < playbackTrack.coordinates.length) {
        playbackIndex = newIndex;
        const point = playbackTrack.coordinates[playbackIndex];
        
        updateTrackMarker(point[0], point[1]);
        updatePlaybackUI();
    }
}

function adjustSpeed(direction) {
    const speeds = [5, 10, 25, 50, 100, 150, 200];
    let currentIndex = speeds.indexOf(playbackSpeed);
    
    if (direction > 0 && currentIndex < speeds.length - 1) {
        currentIndex++;
    } else if (direction < 0 && currentIndex > 0) {
        currentIndex--;
    }
    
    playbackSpeed = speeds[currentIndex];
    document.getElementById('speedIndicator').textContent = playbackSpeed + 'x';
    
    if (isPlayingTrack && playbackInterval) {
        clearInterval(playbackInterval);
        startPlayback();
    }
}

function updatePlaybackUI() {
    const trackSlider = document.getElementById('trackSlider');
    const currentTime = document.getElementById('currentTime');
    
    if (trackSlider && playbackTrack && currentTime) {
        trackSlider.value = playbackIndex;
        
        const progress = playbackIndex / Math.max(1, playbackTrack.coordinates.length - 1);
        const currentSeconds = Math.floor(progress * playbackTrack.totalDuration);
        currentTime.textContent = formatTime(currentSeconds);
    }
}

function formatTime(seconds) {
    const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
    const secs = seconds % 60;
    return `${String(mins).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(secs).padStart(2, '0')}`;
}

function resetGPSControlBarState() {
    const followBtn = document.getElementById('followBtn');
    const recordBtn = document.getElementById('recordBtn');
    const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('downloadBtn');
    
    if (followBtn) {
        followBtn.classList.remove('active');
        followBtn.title = 'GPS Position verfolgen';
    }
    
    if (recordBtn) {
        recordBtn.classList.remove('recording');
        recordBtn.title = 'GPS Track aufnehmen';
        recordBtn.querySelector('span').textContent = 'Aufnahme';
    }
    
    if (downloadBtn) {
        downloadBtn.disabled = recordedTrack.length === 0;
    }
    
    isFollowingGPS = false;
    
    if (trackMarker) {
        trackMarker = null;
        needsRedraw = true;
    }
    
    console.log('✅ GPS Control Bar Status zurückgesetzt');
}

function stopAllGPSFunctions() {
    console.log('🛑 Stoppe alle GPS Control Bar Funktionen...');
    const routing = document.querySelector('#routingInstructionsPanel');
    const distance = document.querySelector('#measurementInfoPanel');
    const details = document.querySelector('#shipDetailWindow');
    const details2 = document.querySelector('#portDetailWindow');
    
    routing.style.top = '72px';    
    distance.style.top = '72px';
    details.style.top = '72px';
    details.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 140px)';

    details2.style.top = '72px';
    details2.style.maxHeight = 'calc(100vh - 140px)';
    
    if (isFollowingGPS) {
        isFollowingGPS = false;
        const followBtn = document.getElementById('followBtn');
        if (followBtn) {
            followBtn.classList.remove('active');
            followBtn.title = 'GPS Position verfolgen';
        }
        console.log('📍 GPS Verfolgung automatisch gestoppt');
    }
    
    if (isRecordingTrack) {
        isRecordingTrack = false;
        const recordBtn = document.getElementById('recordBtn');
        const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('downloadBtn');
        
        if (recordBtn) {
            recordBtn.classList.remove('recording');
            recordBtn.title = 'GPS Track aufnehmen';
            recordBtn.querySelector('span').textContent = 'Aufnahme';
        }
        
        if (downloadBtn && recordedTrack.length > 0) {
            downloadBtn.disabled = false;
        }
        
        console.log('🔴 GPS Aufnahme automatisch gestoppt. Punkte:', recordedTrack.length);
        
        if (recordedTrack.length > 0) {
            showNotification(`Aufnahme beendet - ${recordedTrack.length} Punkte gespeichert`, 'info');
        }
    }
    
    if (isPlayingTrack) {
        stopTrack();
        console.log('▶️ Track Playback automatisch gestoppt');
    }
    
    const playbackControls = document.getElementById('gpsPlaybackControls');
    if (playbackControls && playbackControls.classList.contains('visible')) {
        closePlayback();
        console.log('🎬 Playback Controls automatisch geschlossen');
    }
}

function stopGPSFollow() {
    const followBtn = document.getElementById('followBtn');
    
    isFollowingGPS = false;
    isRotatingWithGPS = false;
    
    if (rotationInterval) {
        clearInterval(rotationInterval);
        rotationInterval = null;
    }
    
    followBtn.classList.remove('active');
    followBtn.title = 'GPS Position verfolgen';
    
    showNotification('GPS Verfolgung beendet', 'info');
    
    map.rotateTo(0, { duration: 1000 });
}

function startAutoRotation() {
    performRotation();
    
    if (rotationInterval) clearInterval(rotationInterval);
    
    rotationInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (isRotatingWithGPS) {
            performRotation();
        } else {
            clearInterval(rotationInterval);
            rotationInterval = null;
        }
    }, 500);
}

function performRotation() {
    if (!isRotatingWithGPS) return;
    
    let heading = null;
    let source = '';
    
    if (isGPSTracking && lastGPSPosition) {
        if (lastGPSPosition.heading !== null && lastGPSPosition.heading !== undefined && !isNaN(lastGPSPosition.heading)) {
            heading = lastGPSPosition.heading;
            source = 'GPS Kompass';
        }
        else {
            const cogElement = document.getElementById('gpsCogValue');
            if (cogElement) {
                const cogText = cogElement.textContent;
                const cogValue = parseFloat(cogText);
                if (!isNaN(cogValue)) {
                    heading = cogValue;
                    source = 'GPS COG';
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (heading === null && isPlayingTrack && trackMarker) {
        if (trackMarker.heading !== null && trackMarker.heading !== undefined) {
            heading = trackMarker.heading;
            source = 'Track';
        }
    }
    
    if (heading === null && gpsTrail.length >= 2) {
        const last = gpsTrail[gpsTrail.length - 1];
        const prev = gpsTrail[gpsTrail.length - 2];
        
        const deltaLng = last.lng - prev.lng;
        const deltaLat = last.lat - prev.lat;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(deltaLng * deltaLng + deltaLat * deltaLat);
        
        if (distance > 0.00001) {
            heading = Math.atan2(deltaLng, deltaLat) * 180 / Math.PI;
            if (heading < 0) heading += 360;
            source = 'Berechnet';
        }
    }
    
    if (heading === null && playbackTrail.length >= 2) {
        const last = playbackTrail[playbackTrail.length - 1];
        const prev = playbackTrail[playbackTrail.length - 2];
        
        const deltaLng = last.lng - prev.lng;
        const deltaLat = last.lat - prev.lat;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(deltaLng * deltaLng + deltaLat * deltaLat);
        
        if (distance > 0.00001) {
            heading = Math.atan2(deltaLng, deltaLat) * 180 / Math.PI;
            if (heading < 0) heading += 360;
            source = 'Playback Trail';
        }
    }
    
    if (heading !== null && !isNaN(heading)) {
        const mapRotation = heading;
        const currentBearing = map.getBearing();
        let diff = mapRotation - currentBearing;
        
        if (diff > 180) diff -= 360;
        if (diff < -180) diff += 360;
        
        if (Math.abs(diff) > 2) {
            map.rotateTo(mapRotation, {
                duration: 300,
                easing: (t) => t
            });
        }
    }
}

// =================================================================
// INITIALISIERUNG
// =================================================================

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const gpsButton = document.getElementById('gpsButton');
    if (gpsButton) {
        gpsButton.addEventListener('dblclick', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (lastGPSPosition) {
                copyGPSPosition();
            }
        });
    }
    
    playbackSpeed = 10;
    const speedIndicator = document.getElementById('speedIndicator');
    if (speedIndicator) {
        speedIndicator.textContent = playbackSpeed + 'x';
    }
});

function copyGPSPosition() {
    if (lastGPSPosition) {
        const posText = `${lastGPSPosition.lat.toFixed(6)}, ${lastGPSPosition.lng.toFixed(6)}`;
        
        if (navigator.clipboard) {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(posText).then(() => {
                showNotification('GPS Position kopiert: ' + posText, 'success');
            });
        } else {
            const textArea = document.createElement('textarea');
            textArea.value = posText;
            document.body.appendChild(textArea);
            textArea.select();
            document.execCommand('copy');
            document.body.removeChild(textArea);
            showNotification('GPS Position kopiert: ' + posText, 'success');
        }
    }
}

// =================================================================
// SHIP TRACK VISUALIZATION SYSTEM - MOBILE OPTIMIZED VERSION
// =================================================================

// Global Variables
var currentShipTrack = null;
var trackCanvas = null;
var trackCtx = null;
var isTrackVisible = false;
var trackMarker2 = null;
var trackMarker2 = false;
var playbackTrack2 = null;
var playbackIndex2 = 0;
var playbackSpeed2 = 1000;
var playbackInterval2 = null;

// Performance Variables
let lastDrawTime = 0;
let frameRequestId = null;
let isDrawing = false;
let lastZoom = null;
let trackPath2D = null;
let trackSegments = [];
let mapEventThrottle = null;

// MOBILE-SPEZIFISCHE OPTIMIERUNGEN
var isMobileDevice = /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
let mobileQualityLevel = 'high'; // 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'auto'
let mobileUpdateDelay = isMobileDevice ? 150 : 100; // Längere Delays auf Mobile
let mobilePointLimit = isMobileDevice ? 500 : 500; // Weniger Punkte auf Mobile
let mobileLineWidth = isMobileDevice ? 4 : 4; // Dünnere Linien auf Mobile
let mobileSkipShadows = isMobileDevice; // Schatten deaktivieren auf Mobile
let mobileReduceColors = isMobileDevice; // Farb-Vereinfachung auf Mobile
let lastMobileRedraw = 0;
let mobileRedrawThrottle = isMobileDevice ? 200 : 100; // Weniger häufige Redraws

// Mobile Performance Detection
function detectMobilePerformance() {
    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.width = 100;
    canvas.height = 100;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    
    // Performance Test
    const start = performance.now();
    for (let i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(Math.random() * 100, Math.random() * 100);
        ctx.lineTo(Math.random() * 100, Math.random() * 100);
        ctx.stroke();
    }
    const renderTime = performance.now() - start;
    
    // Auto-detect Quality Level basierend auf Performance
    if (renderTime > 50) {
        mobileQualityLevel = 'low';
        mobileUpdateDelay = 300;
        mobilePointLimit = 100;
        mobileLineWidth = 4;
    } else if (renderTime > 20) {
        mobileQualityLevel = 'medium';
        mobileUpdateDelay = 200;
        mobilePointLimit = 200;
        mobileLineWidth = 4;
    } else {
        mobileQualityLevel = 'high';
        mobileUpdateDelay = 100;
        mobilePointLimit = 500;
        mobileLineWidth = isMobileDevice ? 4 : 4;
    }
    
    console.log(`📱 Mobile Performance: ${mobileQualityLevel} (${renderTime.toFixed(1)}ms)`);
}
