<script id="play-modul" type="d3e3f0b8771c1eaa8a3d3168-text/javascript">
// =================================================================
// TRACK PLAYBACK SYSTEM - KOMPLETT NEUE VARIABLENNAMEN
// =================================================================

// Globale Variablen für Playback - ALLE UMBENANNT
let isPlayingTrackNEW = false;
let playbackSpeedNEW = 0;
let playbackIntervalNEW = null;
let trackMarkerNEW = null;
let playbackTrailNEW = [];
let playbackStartTimeNEW = null;
let playbackIndexNEW = 0;

// KOMPLETT NEUE GESCHWINDIGKEITEN - jetzt mit x100
var PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW = [5, 10, 25, 50]; // 5x -> 10x -> 25x -> 50x -> 100x -> STOP
var currentSpeedStepNEW = 0; // Welcher Schritt in der Geschwindigkeits-Progression

// Persistente Trail-Linie speichern
let persistentTrailPointsNEW = [];

// =================================================================
// ALLE FUNKTIONEN DEFINIEREN BEVOR SIE VERWENDET WERDEN
// =================================================================

/**
 * Calculate heading - NEUE VERSION
 */
function calculateHeadingNEW(lat1, lng1, lat2, lng2) {
    const dLng = (lng2 - lng1) * Math.PI / 180;
    const lat1Rad = lat1 * Math.PI / 180;
    const lat2Rad = lat2 * Math.PI / 180;
    
    const y = Math.sin(dLng) * Math.cos(lat2Rad);
    const x = Math.cos(lat1Rad) * Math.sin(lat2Rad) -
              Math.sin(lat1Rad) * Math.cos(lat2Rad) * Math.cos(dLng);
    
    let bearing = Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI;
    return (bearing + 360) % 360;
}

// 🛰️ Geschwindigkeit in Knoten (sat_api) – für Schiffe - FEINERE STUFEN
function getSpeedColorSatAPI(speed) {
    if (speed <= 1) {
        const factor = speed / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#7f1d1d', '#990a0a', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 2) {
        const factor = (speed - 1) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#990a0a', '#dc2626', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 3) {
        const factor = (speed - 2) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#dc2626', '#f17f37', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 4) {
        const factor = (speed - 3) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#f17f37', '#f59e0b', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 5) {
        const factor = (speed - 4) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#f59e0b', '#eab308', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 6) {
        const factor = (speed - 5) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#eab308', '#d2d231', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 7) {
        const factor = (speed - 6) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#d2d231', '#c8e33f', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 8) {
        const factor = (speed - 7) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#c8e33f', '#a3e635', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 9) {
        const factor = (speed - 8) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#a3e635', '#84d066', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 10) {
        const factor = (speed - 9) / 1;
        return interpolateColor('#84d066', '#68d066', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 12) {
        const factor = (speed - 10) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#68d066', '#22c55e', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 14) {
        const factor = (speed - 12) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#22c55e', '#16a34a', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 16) {
        const factor = (speed - 14) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#16a34a', '#14b593', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 18) {
        const factor = (speed - 16) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#14b593', '#0d9488', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 20) {
        const factor = (speed - 18) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#0d9488', '#00e7b6', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 22) {
        const factor = (speed - 20) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#00e7b6', '#00d4b4', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 24) {
        const factor = (speed - 22) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#00d4b4', '#00c2b2', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 26) {
        const factor = (speed - 24) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#00c2b2', '#00b8ff', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 28) {
        const factor = (speed - 26) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#00b8ff', '#3b82f6', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 30) {
        const factor = (speed - 28) / 2;
        return interpolateColor('#3b82f6', '#2563eb', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 35) {
        const factor = (speed - 30) / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#2563eb', '#6366f1', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 40) {
        const factor = (speed - 35) / 5;
        return interpolateColor('#6366f1', '#8b5cf6', factor);
    } else if (speed > 40) {
        const factor = Math.min((speed - 40) / 20, 1);
        return interpolateColor('#8b5cf6', '#a855f7', factor);
    } else {
        return '#dc2626';
    }
}

// 🚗 Geschwindigkeit in km/h (alte API) - FEINERE STUFEN
function getSpeedColorLegacy(speed) {
    if (speed <= 10) {
        const factor = speed / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#7f1d1d', '#990a0a', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 20) {
        const factor = (speed - 10) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#990a0a', '#dc2626', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 30) {
        const factor = (speed - 20) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#dc2626', '#f17f37', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 40) {
        const factor = (speed - 30) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#f17f37', '#f59e0b', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 50) {
        const factor = (speed - 40) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#f59e0b', '#eab308', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 60) {
        const factor = (speed - 50) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#eab308', '#d2d231', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 70) {
        const factor = (speed - 60) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#d2d231', '#c8e33f', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 80) {
        const factor = (speed - 70) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#c8e33f', '#a3e635', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 90) {
        const factor = (speed - 80) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#a3e635', '#84d066', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 100) {
        const factor = (speed - 90) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#84d066', '#68d066', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 110) {
        const factor = (speed - 100) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#68d066', '#22c55e', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 120) {
        const factor = (speed - 110) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#22c55e', '#16a34a', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 130) {
        const factor = (speed - 120) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#16a34a', '#14b593', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 140) {
        const factor = (speed - 130) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#14b593', '#0d9488', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 150) {
        const factor = (speed - 140) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#0d9488', '#00e7b6', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 160) {
        const factor = (speed - 150) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#00e7b6', '#00d4b4', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 170) {
        const factor = (speed - 160) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#00d4b4', '#00c2b2', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 180) {
        const factor = (speed - 170) / 10;
        return interpolateColor('#00c2b2', '#00b8ff', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 200) {
        const factor = (speed - 180) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#00b8ff', '#3b82f6', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 220) {
        const factor = (speed - 200) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#3b82f6', '#2563eb', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 240) {
        const factor = (speed - 220) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#2563eb', '#6366f1', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 260) {
        const factor = (speed - 240) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#6366f1', '#8b5cf6', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 280) {
        const factor = (speed - 260) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#8b5cf6', '#a855f7', factor);
    } else if (speed <= 300) {
        const factor = (speed - 280) / 20;
        return interpolateColor('#a855f7', '#c026d3', factor);
    } else if (speed > 300) {
        const factor = Math.min((speed - 300) / 100, 1);
        return interpolateColor('#c026d3', '#db2777', factor);
    } else {
        return '#dc2626';
    }
}

// 📊 Automatische Auswahl basierend auf Datenquelle oder Geschwindigkeit
function getColorForSpeed(speed) {
    // Falls keine Quelle angegeben ist, wird anhand der typischen Werte entschieden:
    // <40 → sat_api, >=40 → legacy
    if (speed < 40) {
        return getSpeedColorSatAPI(speed);
    } else {
        return getSpeedColorLegacy(speed);
    }
}

/**
 * Initialize Track Marker - NEUE VERSION
 */
function initializeTrackMarkerNEW() {
    if (!currentShipTrack || currentShipTrack.points.length === 0) return;
    
    // STARTE am ERSTEN Punkt des Arrays (Index 0)
    const firstPoint = currentShipTrack.points[0];
    
    trackMarkerNEW = {
        lat: firstPoint.lat,
        lng: firstPoint.lng,
        heading: firstPoint.course || 0,
        speed: firstPoint.speed || 0,
        color: firstPoint.color || '#3b82f6'
    };
    
    console.log('🚢  Track Marker STARTET am ERSTEN Punkt (Index 0):', {
        index: 0,
        lat: firstPoint.lat,
        lng: firstPoint.lng,
        totalPoints: currentShipTrack.points.length
    });
}

/**
 * Update Playback Progress - NEUE VERSION
 */
function updatePlaybackProgressNEW() {
    if (!currentShipTrack) return;
    
    const progress = (playbackIndexNEW / (currentShipTrack.points.length - 1)) * 100;
    
    if (playbackIndexNEW % 50 === 0) {
        console.log(`📊  Progress: ${progress.toFixed(1)}% (${playbackIndexNEW}/${currentShipTrack.points.length})`);
    }
}

/**
 * Draw Track Marker - NEUE VERSION - VERBESSERT
 */
function drawTrackMarkerNEW() {
    if (!trackMarkerNEW || !isPlayingTrackNEW || !trackCanvas || !trackCtx) {
        console.log('❌ Marker kann nicht gezeichnet werden:', {
            trackMarker: !!trackMarkerNEW,
            isPlaying: isPlayingTrackNEW,
            canvas: !!trackCanvas,
            ctx: !!trackCtx
        });
        return;
    }
    
    // WICHTIG: Prüfe ob map verfügbar ist
    if (!map || typeof map.project !== 'function') {
        console.log('❌ Map nicht verfügbar für Projection');
        return;
    }
    
    const point = map.project([trackMarkerNEW.lng, trackMarkerNEW.lat]);
    
    // Get current zoom level and adjust marker size accordingly
    const currentZoom = map.getZoom();
    var size = currentZoom <= 9 ? 25 : 30; // Smaller size for zoom 1-9, larger for 10+
		  size = size * 0.8;
			
    trackCtx.save();
    trackCtx.translate(point.x, point.y);
    
    const mapBearing = map.getBearing();
    const adjustedHeading = trackMarkerNEW.heading - mapBearing;
    trackCtx.rotate((adjustedHeading * Math.PI) / 180);
    
    trackCtx.shadowColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5)';
    trackCtx.shadowBlur = 4;
    trackCtx.shadowOffsetX = 2;
    trackCtx.shadowOffsetY = 2;
    
    trackCtx.fillStyle = trackMarkerNEW.color;
    trackCtx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
    trackCtx.lineWidth = 1;
    
    // Draw ship marker with dynamic size
    trackCtx.beginPath();
    trackCtx.moveTo(0, -size);
    trackCtx.lineTo(-size * 0.6, size * 0.8);
    trackCtx.lineTo(0, size * 0.6);
    trackCtx.lineTo(size * 0.6, size * 0.8);
    trackCtx.closePath();
    
    trackCtx.fill();
    trackCtx.stroke();
    
    // Center dot - also scaled with marker size
    trackCtx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    trackCtx.beginPath();
    trackCtx.arc(0, 0, size * 0.15, 0, Math.PI * 2); // Proportional to marker size
    trackCtx.fill();
    
    trackCtx.restore();
    
    // Debug Log für Marker Position
    if (playbackIndexNEW % 100 === 0) {
        console.log(`🎯 Marker gezeichnet:`, {
            zoom: currentZoom,
            size: size,
            position: { x: point.x, y: point.y },
            marker: { lat: trackMarkerNEW.lat, lng: trackMarkerNEW.lng }
        });
    }
}

/**
 * Draw Playback Only - NEUE VERSION - VERBESSERT
 */
function drawPlaybackOnlyNEW() {
    if (!trackCanvas || !trackCtx || !isPlayingTrackNEW) {
        console.log('❌ Canvas oder Context nicht verfügbar für Playback Drawing');
        return;
    }
    
    const pixelRatio = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.5);
    
    trackCtx.save();
    trackCtx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
    trackCtx.clearRect(0, 0, trackCanvas.width, trackCanvas.height);
    trackCtx.setTransform(pixelRatio, 0, 0, pixelRatio, 0, 0);
    
    // Trail zeichnen
    if (persistentTrailPointsNEW.length > 1) {
        trackCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
        trackCtx.lineWidth = 5;
        trackCtx.lineCap = 'round';
        trackCtx.lineJoin = 'round';
        
        for (let i = 1; i < persistentTrailPointsNEW.length; i++) {
            const p1 = persistentTrailPointsNEW[i - 1];
            const p2 = persistentTrailPointsNEW[i];
            
            const point1 = map.project([p1.lng, p1.lat]);
            const point2 = map.project([p2.lng, p2.lat]);
            
            trackCtx.strokeStyle = p2.color || getColorForSpeed(p2.speed || 0)
            trackCtx.beginPath();
            trackCtx.moveTo(point1.x, point1.y);
            trackCtx.lineTo(point2.x, point2.y);
            trackCtx.stroke();
        }
        
        trackCtx.globalAlpha = 1;
    }
    
    // WICHTIG: Marker IMMER zeichnen wenn verfügbar
    if (trackMarkerNEW) {
        drawTrackMarkerNEW();
    }
    
    trackCtx.restore();
}

/**
 * Update Playback Button - NEUE VERSION
 */
function updatePlaybackButtonNEW() {
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (!playBtn) return;
    
    console.log(`🔧 BUTTON UPDATE CALLED: Speed=${playbackSpeedNEW}x, Step=${currentSpeedStepNEW}, Array=[${PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW.join(',')}]`);
    
    if (isPlayingTrackNEW) {
        playBtn.innerHTML = `<span style="color:#fff !important; font-size: 10px; font-weight: bold;">${playbackSpeedNEW}x</span>`;
        
        if (currentSpeedStepNEW < PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW.length - 1) {
            const nextSpeed = PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW[currentSpeedStepNEW + 1];
            playBtn.title = `${playbackSpeedNEW}x - Klick für ${nextSpeed}x`;
            console.log(`🔧 BUTTON: Zeige ${playbackSpeedNEW}x, nächste: ${nextSpeed}x`);
        } else {
            playBtn.title = `${playbackSpeedNEW}x - Klick zum Stoppen`;
            console.log(`🔧 BUTTON: Zeige ${playbackSpeedNEW}x, nächste: STOP`);
        }
        
        playBtn.classList.add('playing');
    } else {
        playBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa fa-play" style="color:#fff !important; font-size: 10px;"></i>';
        playBtn.title = 'Track abspielen';
        playBtn.classList.remove('playing');
        console.log(`🔧 BUTTON: Reset zu Play-Icon`);
    }
}

/**
 * Force Canvas Clear - NEUE VERSION
 */
function forceCanvasClearNEW() {
    if (!trackCanvas || !trackCtx) return;
    trackCanvas.width = trackCanvas.width;
    console.log('🧹  Canvas geleert');
}

/**
 * Continue Playback Animation - NEUE VERSION - VERBESSERT
 */
function continuePlaybackAnimationNEW() {
    if (!currentShipTrack || !isPlayingTrackNEW) return;
    
    const baseInterval = Math.max(50, 1000 / playbackSpeedNEW);
    
    playbackIntervalNEW = setInterval(() => {
        if (!isPlayingTrackNEW) {
            return;
        }
        
        // Prüfe ob wir am ENDE des Tracks sind (vorwärts durch das Array)
        if (playbackIndexNEW >= currentShipTrack.points.length - 1) {
            console.log('✅  Track ENDE erreicht (letzter Punkt im Array)');
            
            if (playbackIntervalNEW) {
                clearInterval(playbackIntervalNEW);
                playbackIntervalNEW = null;
            }
            
            showTrackNotification('Wiedergabe beendet', 'success');
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                stopTrackPlaybackNEW();
            }, 100);
            return;
        }
        
        var checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-cemtvector');
        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
            checkbox.checked = false;
            const event = new Event('change');
            checkbox.dispatchEvent(event);
        }
        
        // Gehe zum NÄCHSTEN Punkt (vorwärts im Array)
        playbackIndexNEW++;
        const currentPoint = currentShipTrack.points[playbackIndexNEW];
        const previousPoint = currentShipTrack.points[playbackIndexNEW - 1];
                
        if (!currentPoint) return;
        
        trackMarkerNEW.lat = currentPoint.lat;
        trackMarkerNEW.lng = currentPoint.lng;
        trackMarkerNEW.speed = currentPoint.speed || 0;
        trackMarkerNEW.color = currentPoint.color || '#3b82f6';
        
        if (previousPoint) {
            // Berechne Heading IN FAHRTRICHTUNG (vom vorherigen zum aktuellen Punkt)
            const heading = calculateHeadingNEW(
                previousPoint.lat, previousPoint.lng,
                currentPoint.lat, currentPoint.lng
            );
            trackMarkerNEW.heading = heading;
        }
        
        persistentTrailPointsNEW.push({
            lat: currentPoint.lat,
            lng: currentPoint.lng,
            color: getColorForSpeed(currentPoint.speed || 0)
        });
        
        // WICHTIG: Erzwinge Neuzeichnen nach Marker-Update
        drawPlaybackOnlyNEW();
        
        updatePlaybackProgressNEW();
        
    }, baseInterval);
}

/**
 * Start Playback Animation - NEUE VERSION
 */
function startPlaybackAnimationNEW() {
    if (!currentShipTrack || !isPlayingTrackNEW) return;
    persistentTrailPointsNEW = [];
    continuePlaybackAnimationNEW();
}

/**
 * Stop Track Playback - NEUE VERSION
 */
function stopTrackPlaybackNEW() {
    if (!isPlayingTrackNEW && !trackMarkerNEW && !currentShipTrack) {
        return;
    }
    
    console.log('ℹ️  Stoppe Playback');
    
    isPlayingTrackNEW = false;
    
    if (playbackIntervalNEW) {
        clearInterval(playbackIntervalNEW);
        playbackIntervalNEW = null;
    }
    
    trackMarkerNEW = null;
    playbackTrailNEW = [];
    playbackIndexNEW = 0;
    currentSpeedStepNEW = 0;
    playbackSpeedNEW = PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW[0];
    persistentTrailPointsNEW = [];
    
    console.log(`🔄  Reset: Step=${currentSpeedStepNEW}, Speed=${playbackSpeedNEW}x`);
    
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (playBtn) {
        playBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa fa-play" style="color:#fff !important; font-size: 10px;"></i>';
        playBtn.title = 'Track abspielen';
        playBtn.classList.remove('playing');
    }
    
    isTrackVisible = false;
    forceCanvasClearNEW();
    
    if (typeof map !== 'undefined' && map) {
        map.off('move', drawShipTrackOptimized);
        map.off('zoom', drawShipTrackOptimized);
        map.off('rotate', drawShipTrackOptimized);
        map.off('pitch', drawShipTrackOptimized);
        map.off('move', drawShipTrack);
        map.off('zoom', drawShipTrack);
        map.off('rotate', drawShipTrack);
        map.off('pitch', drawShipTrack);
    }
    
    toggleCEMTLayerSmart();
	loadRealShips();
	needsRedraw = true;
	drawShips();
	
    showTrackNotification('Wiedergabe gestoppt', 'info');
}

/**
 * Start Track Playback - NEUE VERSION
 */
function startTrackPlaybackNEW() {
    if (!currentShipTrack || !currentShipTrack.points || currentShipTrack.points.length < 2) {
        showTrackNotification('Kein Track verfügbar', 'error');
        return;
    }
    
    // PRÜFE: Ist das Array verkehrt herum? Erste vs. letzte Position checken
    const firstPoint = currentShipTrack.points[0];
    const lastPoint = currentShipTrack.points[currentShipTrack.points.length - 1];
    
    console.log('🔍  Track Analyse:');
    console.log('- Erster Punkt (Index 0):', { lat: firstPoint.lat, lng: firstPoint.lng, time: firstPoint.timestamp });
    console.log('- Letzter Punkt (Index', currentShipTrack.points.length - 1, '):', { lat: lastPoint.lat, lng: lastPoint.lng, time: lastPoint.timestamp });
    
    // PRÜFE ob Track nach Zeitstempel sortiert werden muss
    if (firstPoint.timestamp && lastPoint.timestamp && firstPoint.timestamp > lastPoint.timestamp) {
        console.log('⚠️  Track ist RÜCKWÄRTS sortiert! Drehe Array um...');
        currentShipTrack.points.reverse();
        console.log('✅  Track umgedreht - Marker startet jetzt beim grünen S');
    } else {
        console.log('✅  Track ist korrekt sortiert - Marker startet beim grünen S');
    }
    
    isPlayingTrackNEW = true;
    playbackIndexNEW = 0; // START am Anfang des (jetzt korrekten) Arrays
    playbackTrailNEW = [];
    currentSpeedStepNEW = 0;
    playbackSpeedNEW = PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW[0];
    
    console.log(`▶️  Starte mit ${playbackSpeedNEW}x (Schritt ${currentSpeedStepNEW})`);
    console.log(`🎯  Progression: ${PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW.join('x -> ')}x -> STOP`);
    console.log(`🚢  Track Start: Index ${playbackIndexNEW} von ${currentShipTrack.points.length} Punkten`);
    
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (playBtn) {
        playBtn.disabled = false;
    }
    updatePlaybackButtonNEW();
    
    initializeTrackMarkerNEW();
    persistentTrailPointsNEW = [];
    
    // SPRINGE ZUM MARKER beim Start mit Zoom 8
    if (trackMarkerNEW && typeof map !== 'undefined' && map) {
        console.log(`🎯  Springe zum Start-Marker: Lat ${trackMarkerNEW.lat}, Lng ${trackMarkerNEW.lng}, Zoom 8`);
        
        map.flyTo({
            center: [trackMarkerNEW.lng, trackMarkerNEW.lat],
            zoom: map.getZoom(),
            speed: 1, // Geschwindigkeit der Animation
            curve: 1.5, // Kurve der Flugbahn
            essential: true // Reduziert Animationen wenn accessibility-Einstellungen das fordern
        });
    }
    
    startPlaybackAnimationNEW();
    
}

/**
 * Load Track and Start Playback - NEUE VERSION
 */
let loadInProgressNEW = false;

async function loadAndStartPlaybackNEW() {
    if (loadInProgressNEW) return;
    loadInProgressNEW = true;
    
    const currentShip = getCurrentShipFromDetailWindow();
    
    if (!currentShip || (!currentShip.mmsi && !currentShip.shipId && !currentShip.name)) {
        showTrackNotification('Schiffsdaten nicht verfügbar', 'error');
        loadInProgressNEW = false;
        return;
    }
    
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (!playBtn) {
        loadInProgressNEW = false;
        return;
    }
    
    const originalHTML = playBtn.innerHTML;
    playBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin" style="color:#fff !important; font-size: 10px;"></i>';
    playBtn.disabled = true;
    
    showTrackNotification('Track wird geladen...');
    
    try {
        let shipId = currentShip.shipId;
        
        if (!shipId && currentShip.mmsi) {
            shipId = await getShipIdFromMMSI(currentShip.mmsi);
        }
        
        if (!shipId) {
            throw new Error('Ship ID nicht verfügbar');
        }
        
        const trackData = await loadShipTrackData(shipId);
        
        if (!trackData || trackData.length === 0) {
            throw new Error('Keine Track-Daten vorhanden');
        }
        
        currentShipTrack = processTrackData(trackData);
        
        createTrackCanvas();
        isTrackVisible = true;
        
        if (trackCanvas && trackCtx) {
            const pixelRatio = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1.5);
            trackCtx.save();
            trackCtx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
            trackCtx.clearRect(0, 0, trackCanvas.width, trackCanvas.height);
            trackCtx.setTransform(pixelRatio, 0, 0, pixelRatio, 0, 0);
            trackCtx.restore();
        }
        
        setupOptimizedMapEvents();
        
        var checkbox = document.getElementById('layer-cemtvector');
        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
            checkbox.checked = false;
            const event = new Event('change');
            checkbox.dispatchEvent(event);
        }
        
        showTrackNotification(`Track geladen: ${currentShipTrack.points.length} Punkte`, 'success');
        
        const detailWindow = document.getElementById('shipDetailWindow');
        const minimizeButton = document.getElementById('minimizeButton');
        if (detailWindow && minimizeButton) {
            detailWindow.classList.add('minimized');
            minimizeButton.textContent = '+';
            localStorage.setItem('shipDetailMinimized', 'true');
        }
        
        startTrackPlaybackNEW();
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('❌  Fehler beim Laden:', error);
        showTrackNotification('Fehler beim Laden: ' + error.message, 'error');
        playBtn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
        playBtn.disabled = false;
    } finally {
        loadInProgressNEW = false;
    }
}

/**
 * Toggle Track Playback - NEUE VERSION
 */
async function toggleTrackPlaybackNEW() {
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (!playBtn) return;

    console.log(`🚨 CLICK EVENT TRIGGERED! isPlayingTrackNEW=${isPlayingTrackNEW}, currentSpeedStepNEW=${currentSpeedStepNEW}`);
    
    if (window.playbackClickInProgress) {
        console.log(`⚠️ CLICK BLOCKED - bereits in Bearbeitung!`);
        return;
    }
    window.playbackClickInProgress = true;
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        window.playbackClickInProgress = false;
    }, 500);
        
    if (isPlayingTrackNEW && currentShipTrack) {
        if (currentSpeedStepNEW < PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW.length - 1) {
            currentSpeedStepNEW++;
            playbackSpeedNEW = PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW[currentSpeedStepNEW];
            console.log(`⏩  Wechsle zu Geschwindigkeit: ${playbackSpeedNEW}x (Schritt ${currentSpeedStepNEW})`);
            console.log(`🎯  Array: [${PLAYBACK_SPEEDS_NEW.join(', ')}]`);
            
            if (playbackIntervalNEW) {
                clearInterval(playbackIntervalNEW);
                playbackIntervalNEW = null;
            }
            
            updatePlaybackButtonNEW();
            continuePlaybackAnimationNEW();
            
        } else {
            console.log(`🛑  Stoppe Playback nach ${playbackSpeedNEW}x`);
            stopTrackPlaybackNEW();
			hideShipTrack();
        }
    } 
    else if (currentShipTrack && !isPlayingTrackNEW) {
        console.log('🔄  Starte vorhandenen Track neu');
        startTrackPlaybackNEW();
    }
    else {
        console.log('🔥  Lade Track zum ersten Mal');
        await loadAndStartPlaybackNEW();
    }
}

/**
 * Setup Playback Button - NEUE VERSION
 */
function setupPlaybackButtonNEW() {
    const playBtn = document.getElementById('shipDetailPlayBtn');
    if (!playBtn) return;
    
    console.log(`🔧 SETUP BUTTON - Entferne alle alten Event Listener`);
    
    const newButton = playBtn.cloneNode(true);
    playBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newButton, playBtn);
    
    console.log(`🔧 SETUP BUTTON - Füge EINEN neuen Event Listener hinzu`);
    
    newButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        e.stopImmediatePropagation(); 
        
        console.log(`🎯 SINGLE CLICK EVENT - Rufe toggleTrackPlaybackNEW auf`);
        toggleTrackPlaybackNEW();
    }, { once: false, passive: false });
    
    console.log('▶️  Playback Button sauber eingerichtet');
}

/**
 * Handle Ship Detail Close - NEUE VERSION
 */
function handleShipDetailCloseNEW() {
    stopTrackPlaybackNEW();
    forceCanvasClearNEW();
}

// =================================================================
// DRAW FUNCTION HOOK - VERBESSERT
// =================================================================

if (!window.originalDrawShipTrackOptimizedNEW) {
    if (typeof window.drawShipTrackOptimized === 'function') {
        window.originalDrawShipTrackOptimizedNEW = window.drawShipTrackOptimized;
    } else if (typeof window.drawShipTrack === 'function') {
        window.originalDrawShipTrackOptimizedNEW = window.drawShipTrack;
    }
    
    const drawFunctionNEW = function() {
        if (isPlayingTrackNEW) {
            // WICHTIG: Immer Playback-Zeichnung verwenden wenn Track läuft
            drawPlaybackOnlyNEW();
        } else if (window.originalDrawShipTrackOptimizedNEW && isTrackVisible) {
            window.originalDrawShipTrackOptimizedNEW();
        }
    };
    
    window.drawShipTrackOptimized = drawFunctionNEW;
    window.drawShipTrack = drawFunctionNEW;
}

// ZUSÄTZLICHE MAP-EVENT HANDLER FÜR PLAYBACK
if (typeof map !== 'undefined' && map) {
    // Stelle sicher, dass bei Map-Änderungen das Playback neu gezeichnet wird
    map.on('sourcedata', function() {
        if (isPlayingTrackNEW) {
            setTimeout(drawPlaybackOnlyNEW, 100);
        }
    });
    
    map.on('render', function() {
        if (isPlayingTrackNEW) {
            drawPlaybackOnlyNEW();
        }
    });
}

// =================================================================
// HOOK REGISTRATION
// =================================================================

if (!window.playbackHooksRegisteredNEW) {
    if (window.shipDetailHookManager) {
        window.shipDetailHookManager.registerButtonCallback(setupPlaybackButtonNEW);
        window.shipDetailHookManager.registerCloseCallback(handleShipDetailCloseNEW);
    }
    window.playbackHooksRegisteredNEW = true;
    console.log('🔧  Hooks registriert');
}

    if (document.getElementById('playbackStylesNEW')) return;

    style.id = 'playbackStylesNEW';

        .ship-detail-play {
            background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1);

            height: 32px;
            padding: 6px;
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: all 0.2s ease;
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
        }
        
        .ship-detail-play:hover {
            background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.2);
            border-color: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.5);
        }
        
        .ship-detail-play.playing {
            background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.8);
            border-color: rgba(34, 197, 94, 1);
            animation: pulseNEW 2s infinite;
        }
        
        .ship-detail-play.playing:hover {
            background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.9);
        }
        
        @keyframes pulseNEW {
            0% { opacity: 1; }
            50% { opacity: 0.7; }
            100% { opacity: 1; }
        }
        
        #shipDetailPlayBtn span {
            font-family: Arial, system-ui;
            font-weight: bold;
        }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(style);
}
